PRO AI DJ PROJECT SOURCE CODE DUMP
==================================


================================================================================
FILE: ARCHITECTURE.md
================================================================================
   1: # 🦖 AI DJ Autonomous Pipeline - Architecture Diagram
   2: 
   3: This document outlines the system design and data flow for the Autonomous AI DJ Testing & Innovation Pipeline.
   4: 
   5: ## 🏗️ System Overview
   6: 
   7: ```mermaid
   8: graph TD
   9:     User((User Mobile)) -- Feedback/Rating --> UI[Mobile Tester UI]
  10:     UI -- Stores Feedback --> DB[(Logs / Feedback Weights)]
  11:     
  12:     subgraph "Local Swarm (ai_brain/local_swarm)"
  13:         Master[Master Controller] --> Healing[Healing Agent]
  14:         Master --> Logic[Local Logic / Llama3]
  15:         Master --> Selenium[Selenium / Colab Bot]
  16:         Master --> Pre[Preprocessing Agent]
  17:     end
  18: 
  19:     subgraph "AI Brain (ai_brain/agents)"
  20:         Selector[Selector Agent] --> Transition[Transition Agent]
  21:         Transition -- Mutation Mode --> Innovation[Innovation Hook]
  22:         Research[Research Agent] -- Scrapes Web --> Innovation
  23:         Validator[Validation Agent] -- Judges Quality --> Factory
  24:     end
  25:     
  26:     subgraph "Core Factory Loop"
  27:         Factory[Continuous Loop] --> Downloader[Ingestion / Downloader]
  28:         Downloader --> Analyzer[Analysis / Audio Analyzer]
  29:         Analyzer --> Engine[Core / Master Transition Engine]
  30:         Engine --> Mix[test_mix.wav]
  31:     end
  32:     
  33:     Mix -- Local Playback --> UI
  34:     Selenium -- Auto-Reconnect --> Colab((Google Colab Fleet))
  35:     Colab -- Processing Results --> Factory
  36: ```
  37: 
  38: ## 🧩 Components
  39: 
  40: ### 1. Local Swarm (`ai_brain/local_swarm/`) - **CREDIT SAVERS**
  41: - **Master Controller**: Manages the lifecycle of all local bots.
  42: - **Selenium Bot**: Automates Colab re-connections, cell-starts, and Drive approvals.
  43: - **Local Logic (Llama3)**: Handles semantic reasoning and thematic bridges locally via Ollama.
  44: - **Healing Agent**: Automatically fixes code crashes, missing dirs, and dependency issues.
  45: - **Preprocessing Agent**: Background audio analysis using `librosa` to speed up the main loop.
  46: 
  47: ### 2. AI Brain (`ai_brain/agents/`)
  48: - **Transition Agent**: Decides horizontal/vertical mix logic.
  49: - **Research Agent**: Scours the web for new DJ techniques.
  50: - **Validation Agent**: Pre-screens mixes using signal analysis.
  51: 
  52: ### 3. Core Factory
  53: - **Downloader**: Fetches stems and high-quality audio.
  54: - **Analyzer**: Extracts BPM, Key, Energy, and Melodic phrases.
  55: - **Master Engine**: Executes high-fidelity transitions (CSPI, Wordplay Mashups, Echo Out).
  56: 
  57: ### 4. Remote Feedback (`mobile_tester.py`)
  58: - **Pro Interface**: 60s action-slice playback with binary ratings.
  59: - **Public Access**: Tunneled via Cloudflare for remote testing from your phone.
  60: 
  61: ## 🔄 Status & Versioning
  62: - **Git Repo**: [parth33320/DJ](https://github.com/parth33320/DJ)
  63: - **Primary Branch**: `master`
  64: - **Automation**: `local_git_agent` handles automated innovation backups.

FILE: automated_test_transitions.py
================================================================================
   1: import os
   2: import sys
   3: import random
   4: import json
   5: import time
   6: 
   7: # Handle Windows Unicode issues
   8: if sys.platform == "win32":
   9:     try:
  10:         sys.stdout.reconfigure(encoding='utf-8')
  11:     except:
  12:         pass
  13: 
  14: from main import DJApp
  15: 
  16: def run_automated_test():
  17:     print("STARTING AUTOMATED TRANSITION TEST...")
  18:     app = DJApp()
  19:     app.metadata_cache = {}
  20:     
  21:     # 1. Fetch playlist metadata
  22:     playlist_url = app.config['youtube']['playlist_url']
  23:     print(f"Fetching playlist from {playlist_url}...")
  24:     app.playlist = app.downloader.get_playlist_metadata(playlist_url)
  25:     
  26:     if len(app.playlist) < 2:
  27:         print("Need at least 2 songs!")
  28:         return
  29: 
  30:     # 2. Pick from existing metadata
  31:     meta_dir = 'data/metadata'
  32:     meta_files = [f for f in os.listdir(meta_dir) if f.endswith('.json')]
  33:     
  34:     if len(meta_files) < 2:
  35:         print("Need at least 2 metadata files in data/metadata/")
  36:         return
  37:         
  38:     picked_files = random.sample(meta_files, 2)
  39:     song_ids = [f.replace('.json', '') for f in picked_files]
  40:     
  41:     print(f"\n🎧 TEST PAIR (from Metadata):")
  42:     
  43:     # 3. Load metadata
  44:     for sid in song_ids:
  45:         meta_path = os.path.join(meta_dir, f"{sid}.json")
  46:         with open(meta_path, 'r') as f:
  47:             data = json.load(f)
  48:             app.metadata_cache[sid] = data
  49:             print(f"   - {data.get('title', sid)}")
  50: 
  51:     cur_ana = app.metadata_cache[song_ids[0]]
  52:     nxt_ana = app.metadata_cache[song_ids[1]]
  53:     
  54:     # 4. Agent decides transition
  55:     compatibility = random.randint(40, 90)
  56:     technique = app.transition_decider.decide(cur_ana, nxt_ana, compatibility)
  57:     params = app.transition_decider.get_params(cur_ana, nxt_ana, technique)
  58:     
  59:     print(f"\n--- LOGIC REPORT ---")
  60:     print(f"Technique: {technique}")
  61:     print(f"Compatibility Score: {compatibility}")
  62:     
  63:     # Send ntfy summary
  64:     from utils.notifier import send_notification
  65:     msg = f"🧪 TRANSITION TEST\nFROM: {cur_ana.get('title', 'A')}\nTO: {nxt_ana.get('title', 'B')}\nTECH: {technique}"
  66:     send_notification(msg, topic='dj-agent-parth')
  67:     
  68:     print("\n✅ TEST COMPLETE. LOGGED TO NTFY.")
  69: 
  70: if __name__ == "__main__":
  71:     run_automated_test()

FILE: boot.py
================================================================================
   1: import subprocess
   2: import sys
   3: import time
   4: import os
   5: import signal
   6: 
   7: def main():
   8:     print("🚀 Booting DJ God Mode System...")
   9:     processes = []
  10: 
  11:     try:
  12:         # 1. Boot the Standalone UI Server (The Mouth)
  13:         print("🌐 Starting Standalone UI Server (Port 8080)...")
  14:         ui_process = subprocess.Popen([sys.executable, "standalone_ui_server.py"])
  15:         processes.append(ui_process)
  16:         
  17:         # Give the server 2 seconds to bind to the port
  18:         time.sleep(2) 
  19: 
  20:         # 2. Dig the Tunnel (The Network)
  21:         print("🚇 Digging Localtunnel (parth-dj-god-mode-2026)...")
  22:         # shell=True is required on Windows to run npm/npx commands
  23:         tunnel_process = subprocess.Popen("npx localtunnel --port 8080 --subdomain parth-dj-god-mode-2026", shell=True)
  24:         processes.append(tunnel_process)
  25:         
  26:         # Give the tunnel 2 seconds to establish connection
  27:         time.sleep(2)
  28: 
  29:         # 3. Boot the AI DJ Loop (The Brain)
  30:         print("🧠 Waking up AI Brain Queue...")
  31:         brain_process = subprocess.Popen([sys.executable, "test_transitions.py"])
  32:         processes.append(brain_process)
  33: 
  34:         print("\n✅ ALL SYSTEMS ONLINE.")
  35:         print("👉 UI Link: https://parth-dj-god-mode-2026.loca.lt")
  36:         print("🛑 Press [Ctrl + C] here to instantly kill all services.")
  37: 
  38:         # Keep the master script alive and watching
  39:         while True:
  40:             time.sleep(1)
  41: 
  42:     except KeyboardInterrupt:
  43:         print("\n🛑 Shutdown signal received. Terminating all microservices...")
  44:         for p in processes:
  45:             try:
  46:                 p.terminate()
  47:             except:
  48:                 pass
  49:         print("👋 Clean shutdown complete. No zombie processes left behind.")
  50:         sys.exit(0)
  51: 
  52: if __name__ == "__main__":
  53:     main()



================================================================================
FILE: boot_master.py
================================================================================
   1: # boot_master.py
   2: # THE GOD SCRIPT - Launches everything, heals everything, needs no human
   3: 
   4: import subprocess
   5: import threading
   6: import time
   7: import os
   8: import sys
   9: import signal
  10: import requests
  11: 
  12: # ============== CONFIGURATION ==============
  13: FLASK_PORT = 8080
  14: TUNNEL_SUBDOMAIN = "parth-dj-god-mode-2026"
  15: TUNNEL_URL = f"https://{TUNNEL_SUBDOMAIN}.loca.lt"
  16: NTFY_TOPIC = "dj-agent-parth"
  17: HEALTH_CHECK_INTERVAL = 30  # seconds
  18: 
  19: # ============== GLOBAL STATE ==============
  20: processes = {}
  21: shutdown_flag = False
  22: 
  23: def log(emoji, msg):
  24:     print(f"{emoji} [{time.strftime('%H:%M:%S')}] {msg}")
  25: 
  26: def send_notification(msg):
  27:     try:
  28:         requests.post(f"https://ntfy.sh/{NTFY_TOPIC}", data=msg.encode('utf-8'), timeout=5)
  29:     except:
  30:         pass
  31: 
  32: def save_status(status):
  33:     os.makedirs('data/logs', exist_ok=True)
  34:     with open('data/logs/boot_status.json', 'w') as f:
  35:         import json
  36:         json.dump({'status': status, 'url': TUNNEL_URL, 'timestamp': time.time()}, f)
  37: 
  38: # ============== PROCESS LAUNCHERS ==============
  39: 
  40: def run_flask():
  41:     """Flask UI Server - restarts forever until shutdown"""
  42:     global shutdown_flag
  43:     while not shutdown_flag:
  44:         log("🌐", "Starting Flask UI server...")
  45:         proc = subprocess.Popen(
  46:             [sys.executable, 'standalone_ui_server.py'],
  47:             stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
  48:             stderr=subprocess.STDOUT
  49:         )
  50:         processes['flask'] = proc
  51:         
  52:         # Stream output
  53:         for line in iter(proc.stdout.readline, b''):
  54:             if shutdown_flag:
  55:                 break
  56:             line_text = line.decode('utf-8', errors='ignore').strip()
  57:             if line_text:
  58:                 log("🌐", f"[Flask] {line_text}")
  59:         
  60:         proc.wait()
  61:         if not shutdown_flag:
  62:             log("⚠️", "Flask died! Restarting in 3 seconds...")
  63:             time.sleep(3)
  64: 
  65: def run_tunnel():
  66:     """Localtunnel - restarts forever until shutdown"""
  67:     global shutdown_flag
  68:     while not shutdown_flag:
  69:         log("🚇", f"Starting tunnel to {TUNNEL_URL}...")
  70:         proc = subprocess.Popen(
  71:             ['lt', '--port', str(FLASK_PORT), '--subdomain', TUNNEL_SUBDOMAIN],
  72:             stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
  73:             stderr=subprocess.STDOUT
  74:         )
  75:         processes['tunnel'] = proc
  76:         
  77:         for line in iter(proc.stdout.readline, b''):
  78:             if shutdown_flag:
  79:                 break
  80:             line_text = line.decode('utf-8', errors='ignore').strip()
  81:             if line_text:
  82:                 log("🚇", f"[Tunnel] {line_text}")
  83:         
  84:         proc.wait()
  85:         if not shutdown_flag:
  86:             log("⚠️", "Tunnel died! Restarting in 3 seconds...")
  87:             time.sleep(3)
  88: 
  89: def run_transition_engine():
  90:     """Main DJ Brain Loop - restarts forever until shutdown"""
  91:     global shutdown_flag
  92:     time.sleep(10)  # Wait for Flask and Tunnel to stabilize
  93:     
  94:     while not shutdown_flag:
  95:         log("🧠", "Starting DJ Transition Engine...")
  96:         proc = subprocess.Popen(
  97:             [sys.executable, 'test_transitions.py'],
  98:             stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
  99:             stderr=subprocess.STDOUT
 100:         )
 101:         processes['engine'] = proc
 102:         
 103:         for line in iter(proc.stdout.readline, b''):
 104:             if shutdown_flag:
 105:                 break
 106:             line_text = line.decode('utf-8', errors='ignore').strip()
 107:             if line_text:
 108:                 log("🧠", f"[Engine] {line_text}")
 109:         
 110:         proc.wait()
 111:         if not shutdown_flag:
 112:             log("⚠️", "Engine died! Restarting in 5 seconds...")
 113:             time.sleep(5)
 114: 
 115: def run_health_monitor():
 116:     """Check if everything is alive, send status notifications"""
 117:     global shutdown_flag
 118:     time.sleep(15)  # Let everything boot first
 119:     
 120:     last_ok = False
 121:     while not shutdown_flag:
 122:         try:
 123:             # Check if Flask responds
 124:             r = requests.get(f"http://localhost:{FLASK_PORT}/api/queue", timeout=5)
 125:             flask_ok = r.status_code == 200
 126:         except:
 127:             flask_ok = False
 128:         
 129:         try:
 130:             # Check if Tunnel responds
 131:             r = requests.get(TUNNEL_URL, timeout=10, headers={'Bypass-Tunnel-Reminder': 'true'})
 132:             tunnel_ok = r.status_code == 200
 133:         except:
 134:             tunnel_ok = False
 135:         
 136:         engine_ok = 'engine' in processes and processes['engine'].poll() is None
 137:         
 138:         all_ok = flask_ok and tunnel_ok and engine_ok
 139:         
 140:         status = {
 141:             'flask': '✅' if flask_ok else '❌',
 142:             'tunnel': '✅' if tunnel_ok else '❌',
 143:             'engine': '✅' if engine_ok else '❌'
 144:         }
 145:         
 146:         if all_ok and not last_ok:
 147:             msg = f"🟢 DJ AGENT FULLY ONLINE!\n📱 {TUNNEL_URL}\nFlask:{status['flask']} Tunnel:{status['tunnel']} Engine:{status['engine']}"
 148:             log("✅", msg)
 149:             send_notification(msg)
 150:             save_status('ONLINE')
 151:         elif not all_ok and last_ok:
 152:             msg = f"🔴 DJ AGENT DEGRADED!\nFlask:{status['flask']} Tunnel:{status['tunnel']} Engine:{status['engine']}"
 153:             log("❌", msg)
 154:             send_notification(msg)
 155:             save_status('DEGRADED')
 156:         
 157:         last_ok = all_ok
 158:         time.sleep(HEALTH_CHECK_INTERVAL)
 159: 
 160: # ============== GRACEFUL SHUTDOWN ==============
 161: 
 162: def shutdown_handler(signum, frame):
 163:     global shutdown_flag
 164:     log("🛑", "Shutdown signal received! Killing all processes...")
 165:     shutdown_flag = True
 166:     
 167:     for name, proc in processes.items():
 168:         try:
 169:             proc.terminate()
 170:             proc.wait(timeout=5)
 171:             log("🛑", f"Killed {name}")
 172:         except:
 173:             proc.kill()
 174:     
 175:     send_notification("🛑 DJ Agent shut down.")
 176:     save_status('OFFLINE')
 177:     sys.exit(0)
 178: 
 179: # ============== MAIN ==============
 180: 
 181: def main():
 182:     global shutdown_flag
 183:     
 184:     # Handle Ctrl+C gracefully
 185:     signal.signal(signal.SIGINT, shutdown_handler)
 186:     signal.signal(signal.SIGTERM, shutdown_handler)
 187:     
 188:     log("🚀", "=" * 50)
 189:     log("🚀", "   DJ AGENT MASTER BOOT SEQUENCE")
 190:     log("🚀", "=" * 50)
 191:     log("📱", f"Public URL: {TUNNEL_URL}")
 192:     log("📱", f"Notifications: ntfy.sh/{NTFY_TOPIC}")
 193:     log("🚀", "=" * 50)
 194:     
 195:     save_status('BOOTING')
 196:     send_notification(f"🚀 DJ Agent booting...\n📱 {TUNNEL_URL}")
 197:     
 198:     # Launch all services as daemon threads
 199:     threads = [
 200:         threading.Thread(target=run_flask, daemon=True, name="Flask"),
 201:         threading.Thread(target=run_tunnel, daemon=True, name="Tunnel"),
 202:         threading.Thread(target=run_transition_engine, daemon=True, name="Engine"),
 203:         threading.Thread(target=run_health_monitor, daemon=True, name="Monitor"),
 204:     ]
 205:     
 206:     for t in threads:
 207:         t.start()
 208:         log("🧵", f"Started thread: {t.name}")
 209:         time.sleep(2)  # Stagger startup
 210:     
 211:     # Keep main thread alive
 212:     log("✅", "All systems launched! Running forever until Ctrl+C...")
 213:     
 214:     while not shutdown_flag:
 215:         time.sleep(1)
 216: 
 217: if __name__ == "__main__":
 218:     main()

================================================================================
FILE: knowledge_agent.py
================================================================================
   1: import sys, os, json, time, random, yt_dlp
   2: from youtube_transcript_api import YouTubeTranscriptApi
   3: from langchain_ollama import ChatOllama
   4: from langchain_core.messages import HumanMessage
   5: from pydantic import BaseModel, Field
   6: 
   7: KB_FILE = 'data/logs/dj_knowledge_base.json'
   8: COOKIES = 'data/yt_cookies.txt'
   9: 
  10: class TransitionRecipe(BaseModel):
  11:     technique_name: str; suitable_for: str; steps: list; parameters: dict
  12: 
  13: def load_json_safe(fp, default):
  14:     if os.path.exists(fp):
  15:         with open(fp, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: return json.load(f)
  16:     return default
  17: 
  18: def save_json_safe(fp, data):
  19:     os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(fp), exist_ok=True)
  20:     with open(fp, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(data, f, indent=2)
  21: 
  22: class KnowledgeIngestionAgent:
  23:     def __init__(self):
  24:         self.llm = ChatOllama(model="deepseek-r1:8b", temperature=0.1).with_structured_output(TransitionRecipe)
  25: 
  26:     # 🎯 NEW: SNIPER MODE FOR REMEDIATION
  27:     def run_targeted_search(self, query, technique):
  28:         print(f"\n🚨 [KNOWLEDGE AGENT] TARGETED REMEDIATION: Searching YouTube for '{query}'...")
  29:         ydl_opts = {'extract_flat': True, 'quiet': True, 'default_search': 'ytsearch3'}
  30:         
  31:         with yt_dlp.YoutubeDL(ydl_opts) as ydl:
  32:             info = ydl.extract_info(f"ytsearch3:{query}", download=False)
  33:             entries = info.get('entries', [])
  34:             
  35:             for entry in entries:
  36:                 if not entry: continue
  37:                 try:
  38:                     ts = YouTubeTranscriptApi.get_transcript(entry['id'], cookies=COOKIES if os.path.exists(COOKIES) else None)
  39:                     text = " ".join([t['text'] for t in ts])
  40:                     
  41:                     print(f"📚 Found transcript for {entry['title']}! Brain extracting recipe...")
  42:                     recipe = self.llm.invoke([HumanMessage(content=f"Extract step-by-step DJ transition recipe for {technique} from this text. Focus on audio engineering steps: {text[:4000]}")])
  43:                     
  44:                     recipe_dump = recipe.model_dump()
  45:                     
  46:                     # 1. Save specifically for immediate LLM injection
  47:                     save_json_safe(f"data/knowledge/{technique.lower()}_recipe.json", recipe_dump)
  48:                     
  49:                     # 2. Add to general knowledge base
  50:                     self._save(recipe_dump, entry['id'])
  51:                     
  52:                     print(f"✅ [KNOWLEDGE AGENT] Fix for {technique} learned and saved!\n")
  53:                     return # Stop after finding one good tutorial
  54:                 except Exception as e:
  55:                     print(f"  ⚠️ Skip video (no transcript/error): {e}")
  56: 
  57:     def run_mass_harvest(self, playlists):
  58:         processed = set(load_json_safe('data/logs/processed_videos.json', []))
  59:         with yt_dlp.YoutubeDL({'extract_flat': True, 'quiet': True}) as ydl:
  60:             for url in playlists:
  61:                 entries = ydl.extract_info(url, download=False).get('entries', [])
  62:                 for entry in entries:
  63:                     if not entry or entry['id'] in processed: continue
  64:                     print(f"🎬 Harvesting: {entry['title']}")
  65:                     time.sleep(random.uniform(3, 7))
  66:                     try:
  67:                         ts = YouTubeTranscriptApi.get_transcript(entry['id'], cookies=COOKIES if os.path.exists(COOKIES) else None)
  68:                         text = " ".join([t['text'] for t in ts])
  69:                         if len(text.split()) > 100:
  70:                             recipe = self.llm.invoke([HumanMessage(content=f"Extract DJ recipe from: {text}")])
  71:                             self._save(recipe.model_dump(), entry['id'])
  72:                     except Exception as e: print(f"  ⚠️ Error: {e}")
  73:                     processed.add(entry['id']); save_json_safe('data/logs/processed_videos.json', list(processed))
  74: 
  75:     def _save(self, data, vid):
  76:         kb = load_json_safe(KB_FILE, [])
  77:         existing_index = next((i for i, item in enumerate(kb) if item.get('vid') == vid), None)
  78:         data['vid'] = vid
  79:         data['last_updated'] = time.time()
  80:         
  81:         if existing_index is not None: kb[existing_index] = data
  82:         else: kb.append(data)
  83:         save_json_safe(KB_FILE, kb)
  84: 
  85: if __name__ == "__main__":
  86:     agent = KnowledgeIngestionAgent()
  87:     # If called by test_transitions.py with args, use SNIPER MODE
  88:     if len(sys.argv) > 2:
  89:         agent.run_targeted_search(sys.argv[1], sys.argv[2])
  90:     else:
  91:         # Otherwise run mass harvest
  92:         agent.run_mass_harvest([
  93:             "https://www.youtube.com/playlist?list=PLm8kQbauoU-BmyP6EQJXtVLL0xHtfOb_2",
  94:             "https://www.youtube.com/playlist?list=PLm8kQbauoU-Am4wnh58AFiObXjW_43IlT"
  95:         ])

 222:     def _load_metadata_cache(self):
 223:         """Load all existing metadata from disk"""
 224:         meta_dir = self.config['paths']['metadata']
 225:         if os.path.exists(meta_dir):
 226:             for filename in os.listdir(meta_dir):
 227:                 if filename.endswith('.json'):
 228:                     try:
 229:                         filepath = os.path.join(meta_dir, filename)
 230:                         with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
 231:                             data = json.load(f)
 232:                             song_id = filename.replace('.json', '')
 233:                             self.metadata_cache[song_id] = data
 234:                     except Exception as e:
 235:                         print(f"{Fore.YELLOW}⚠️ Failed to load {filename}: {e}{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 236:         
 237:         if self.metadata_cache:
 238:             print(f"{Fore.GREEN}📂 Loaded {len(self.metadata_cache)} songs from cache{Style.RESET_ALL}")

 314:     def initial_setup(self):
 315:         """First time setup - analyze all songs"""
 316:         print(f"\n{Fore.CYAN}📋 INITIAL SETUP{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 317:         print("=" * 50)
 318:         
 319:         playlist_url = self.config['youtube']['playlist_url']
 320:         if not playlist_url:
 321:             playlist_url = input("Enter your YouTube playlist URL: ").strip()
 322:             self.config['youtube']['playlist_url'] = playlist_url
 323:             with open('config.yaml', 'w') as f:
 324:                 yaml.dump(self.config, f)
 325:         
 326:         print(f"\n{Fore.YELLOW}📥 Fetching playlist...{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 327:         self.playlist = self.downloader.get_playlist_metadata(playlist_url)
 328:         
 329:         print(f"Found {len(self.playlist)} songs")
 330:         
 331:         # Process each song
 332:         total = len(self.playlist)
 333:         for i, song in enumerate(self.playlist):
 334:             print(f"\n[{i+1}/{total}] Processing: {song['title'][:50]}")
 335:             self._process_song(song)
 336:         
 337:         # Build word index
 338:         print(f"\n{Fore.YELLOW}🗂️ Building word index...{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 339:         self.wordplay_agent.build_word_index(self.metadata_cache)
 340:         
 341:         print(f"\n{Fore.GREEN}✅ Setup complete! {len(self.metadata_cache)} songs ready{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 342:     
 343:     def _process_song(self, song):
 344:         """Process a single song"""
 345:         try:
 346:             song_id = song['id']
 347:             
 348:             # Check cache first
 349:             meta_path = os.path.join(self.config['paths']['metadata'], f"{song_id}.json")
 350:             if os.path.exists(meta_path):
 351:                 with open(meta_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
 352:                     self.metadata_cache[song_id] = json.load(f)
 353:                 print(f"   ✅ Cached: {song['title'][:40]}")
 354:                 return
 355:             
 356:             # Download
 357:             filepath = self.downloader.download_song(song['url'], song_id)
 358:             if not filepath or not os.path.exists(filepath):
 359:                 print(f"   ❌ Download failed: {song['title'][:40]}")
 360:                 return
 361:             
 362:             # Analyze
 363:             analysis = self.analyzer.analyze_track(filepath, song_id)
 364:             analysis['title'] = song['title']
 365:             analysis['url'] = song.get('url', '')
 366:             analysis['id'] = song_id
 367:             
 368:             # Phrases
 369:             try:
 370:                 phrases = self.phrase_detector.detect_phrases(filepath, song_id)
 371:                 analysis['phrases'] = phrases
 372:             except Exception as e:
 373:                 print(f"   ⚠️ Phrase detection failed: {e}")
 374:                 analysis['phrases'] = []
 375:             
 376:             # Entry points
 377:             try:
 378:                 entry_points = self.entry_finder.find_entry_points(filepath, analysis, song_id)
 379:                 analysis['entry_points'] = entry_points
 380:             except Exception as e:
 381:                 print(f"   ⚠️ Entry point detection failed: {e}")
 382:                 analysis['entry_points'] = []
 383:             
 384:             # Save metadata
 385:             with open(meta_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
 386:                 json.dump(analysis, f, indent=2)
 387:             
 388:             self.metadata_cache[song_id] = analysis
 389:             
 390:             print(f"   ✅ Processed: {song['title'][:40]}")
 391:             
 392:         except Exception as e:
 393:             print(f"{Fore.RED}❌ Error processing {song.get('title', 'unknown')}: {e}{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 394:             import traceback
 395:             traceback.print_exc()
 396:     
 397:     def start_djing(self):
 398:         """Main DJ loop - FIXED"""
 399:         self.is_playing = True
 400:         
 401:         # Signal handlers
 402:         try:
 403:             signal.signal(signal.SIGINT, self._signal_handler)
 404:             signal.signal(signal.SIGTERM, self._signal_handler)
 405:         except ValueError:
 406:             pass  # Not in main thread
 407:         
 408:         # Start services
 409:         if self.audio_engine:
 410:             self.audio_engine.start()
 411:         
 412:         if self.streaming_enabled and self.streamer:
 413:             self.streamer.start()
 414:         
 415:         if self.obs_bridge:
 416:             try:
 417:                 self.obs_bridge.connect()
 418:             except:
 419:                 pass
 420:         
 421:         # Background threads
 422:         threading.Thread(target=self._playlist_watch_loop, daemon=True).start()
 423:         
 424:         print(f"\n{Fore.GREEN}🎧 DJ APP LIVE!{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 425:         
 426:         # Pick first song
 427:         if self.metadata_cache:
 428:             self.current_song = self.selector.pick_first_song(self.metadata_cache)
 429:             if self.current_song:
 430:                 title = self.metadata_cache[self.current_song].get('title', 'Unknown')
 431:                 print(f"{Fore.CYAN}🎵 Starting with: {title}{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 432:         
 433:         # Main loop
 434:         while self.is_playing:
 435:             try:
 436:                 if not self.current_song:
 437:                     print(f"{Fore.YELLOW}⚠️ No current song, waiting...{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 438:                     time.sleep(1)
 439:                     continue
 440:                 
 441:                 self._play_current_song()
 442:                 
 443:             except KeyboardInterrupt:
 444:                 break
 445:             except Exception as e:
 446:                 print(f"{Fore.RED}❌ Error in main loop: {e}{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 447:                 import traceback
 448:                 traceback.print_exc()
 449:                 time.sleep(2)
 450:     
 451:     def _play_current_song(self):
 452:         """Play current song with transition to next"""
 453:         if not self.current_song or self.current_song not in self.metadata_cache:
 454:             self.current_song = self.selector.pick_first_song(self.metadata_cache)
 455:             return
 456:         
 457:         current = self.metadata_cache[self.current_song]
 458:         print(f"\n{Fore.CYAN}▶️  NOW: {current.get('title', 'Unknown')}{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 459:         
 460:         self.update_status(f"playing:{current.get('title', 'Unknown')}")
 461:         
 462:         # Pick next song
 463:         next_song_id, compatibility = self.selector.pick_next_song(
 464:             current, self.metadata_cache
 465:         )
 466:         
 467:         if not next_song_id:
 468:             print(f"{Fore.YELLOW}⚠️ No next song found, picking random...{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 469:             import random
 470:             available = [k for k in self.metadata_cache.keys() if k != self.current_song]
 471:             if available:
 472:                 next_song_id = random.choice(available)
 473:                 compatibility = {'score': 0.5, 'reason': 'random selection'}
 474:             else:
 475:                 time.sleep(5)
 476:                 return
 477:         
 478:         next_analysis = self.metadata_cache.get(next_song_id, {})
 479:         
 480:         # ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 481:         # 🤖 DECIDE TRANSITION (Tree of Thoughts Integration)
 482:         # ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 483:         decide_result = self.transition_decider.decide_transition(
 484:             current.get('title', 'Unknown'), 
 485:             next_analysis.get('title', 'Unknown'), 
 486:             current, 
 487:             next_analysis
 488:         )
 489:         
 490:         if isinstance(decide_result, tuple):
 491:             technique, params = decide_result
 492:         else:
 493:             technique = decide_result
 494:             params = {"duration": 16}
 495:         
 496:         print(f"   {Fore.MAGENTA}⏭️  Next: {next_analysis.get('title', 'Unknown')}{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 497:         print(f"   {Fore.YELLOW}🔀 Technique: {technique}{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 498:         print(f"   {Fore.BLUE}📊 Compatibility: {compatibility.get('score', 0):.2f}{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 499:         
 500:         # Update streaming overlay
 501:         if self.streaming_enabled and self.streamer:
 502:             try:
 503:                 self.streamer.update_song(
 504:                     title=current.get('title', ''),
 505:                     bpm=current.get('bpm', 0),
 506:                     key=current.get('camelot', ''),
 507:                     genre=current.get('genre_hint', ''),
 508:                     next_title=next_analysis.get('title', '')
 509:                 )
 510:             except:
 511:                 pass
 512:         
 513:         # ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 514:         # 🎧 EXECUTE TRANSITION (Headless File Generation Fix)
 515:         # ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 516:         self.update_status(f"transitioning:{current.get('title', '')} -> {next_analysis.get('title', '')}")
 517:         
 518:         output_path = self.transition_engine.generate_transition_mix(
 519:             cur_id=self.current_song,
 520:             nxt_id=next_song_id,
 521:             technique=technique,
 522:             params=params,
 523:             cur_ana=current,
 524:             nxt_ana=next_analysis
 525:         )
 526:         
 527:         if output_path and os.path.exists(output_path):
 528:             print(f"   {Fore.GREEN}✅ Transition generated: {output_path}{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 529:             
 530:             # Upload to Drive for mobile testing
 531:             if self.drive_manager:
 532:                 try:
 533:                     drive_link = self.drive_manager.upload_transition(output_path)
 534:                     if drive_link:
 535:                         print(f"   {Fore.CYAN}📱 Mobile link: {drive_link}{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 536:                         self._save_transition_link(output_path, drive_link, current, next_analysis, technique)
 537:                 except Exception as e:
 538:                     print(f"   {Fore.YELLOW}⚠️ Drive upload failed: {e}{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 539:             
 540:             # Record for quality feedback
 541:             self.transition_history.append({
 542:                 'from': self.current_song,
 543:                 'to': next_song_id,
 544:                 'technique': technique,
 545:                 'output': output_path,
 546:                 'timestamp': time.time()
 547:             })
 548:         else:
 549:             print(f"   {Fore.RED}❌ Transition generation failed{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 550:         
 551:         # Move to next song
 552:         self.current_song = next_song_id
 553:         
 554:         # Small delay before next transition
 555:         time.sleep(2)
 556:     
 557:     def _save_transition_link(self, output_path, drive_link, current, next_analysis, technique):
 558:         """Save transition link for mobile testing"""
 559:         try:
 560:             links_file = os.path.join(self.config['paths']['logs'], 'transition_links.json')
 561:             
 562:             links = []
 563:             if os.path.exists(links_file):
 564:                 with open(links_file, 'r') as f:
 565:                     links = json.load(f)
 566:             
 567:             links.append({
 568:                 'from_title': current.get('title', ''),
 569:                 'to_title': next_analysis.get('title', ''),
 570:                 'technique': technique,
 571:                 'drive_link': drive_link,
 572:                 'local_path': output_path,
 573:                 'timestamp': time.time(),
 574:                 'tested': False,
 575:                 'rating': None
 576:             })
 577:             
 578:             # Keep last 50 transitions
 579:             links = links[-50:]
 580:             
 581:             with open(links_file, 'w') as f:
 582:                 json.dump(links, f, indent=2)
 583:                 
 584:         except Exception as e:
 585:             print(f"   ⚠️ Failed to save transition link: {e}")
 586:     
 587:     def _playlist_watch_loop(self):
 588:         """Background loop to watch for playlist changes"""
 589:         check_interval = self.config['youtube'].get('check_interval_hours', 6) * 3600
 590:         
 591:         while self.is_playing:
 592:             time.sleep(check_interval)
 593:             try:
 594:                 playlist_url = self.config['youtube']['playlist_url']
 595:                 if playlist_url:
 596:                     self.playlist_watcher.check_for_changes(
 597:                         playlist_url,
 598:                         self.playlist,
 599:                         self.metadata_cache,
 600:                         self
 601:                     )
 602:             except Exception as e:
 603:                 print(f"Playlist watch error: {e}")
 604:     
 605:     def test_single_transition(self, song1_id=None, song2_id=None):
 606:         """Test a single transition between two songs"""
 607:         import random
 608:         
 609:         if not self.metadata_cache:
 610:             print(f"{Fore.RED}❌ No songs in cache. Run initial_setup first.{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 611:             return None
 612:         
 613:         # Pick random songs if not specified
 614:         available = list(self.metadata_cache.keys())
 615:         if not song1_id:
 616:             song1_id = random.choice(available)
 617:         if not song2_id:
 618:             remaining = [s for s in available if s != song1_id]
 619:             song2_id = random.choice(remaining) if remaining else song1_id
 620:         
 621:         current = self.metadata_cache.get(song1_id, {})
 622:         next_analysis = self.metadata_cache.get(song2_id, {})
 623:         
 624:         print(f"\n{Fore.CYAN}🧪 TESTING TRANSITION{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 625:         print(f"   From: {current.get('title', 'Unknown')}")
 626:         print(f"   To: {next_analysis.get('title', 'Unknown')}")
 627:         
 628:         # Get compatibility
 629:         compatibility = self.compatibility_scorer.score(current, next_analysis)
 630:         
 631:         # ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 632:         # 🤖 DECIDE TRANSITION (Tree of Thoughts Integration)
 633:         # ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 634:         decide_result = self.transition_decider.decide_transition(
 635:             current.get('title', 'Unknown'),
 636:             next_analysis.get('title', 'Unknown'),
 637:             current,
 638:             next_analysis
 639:         )
 640:         
 641:         if isinstance(decide_result, tuple):
 642:             technique, params = decide_result
 643:         else:
 644:             technique = decide_result
 645:             params = {"duration": 16}
 646:         
 647:         print(f"   Technique: {technique}")
 648:         print(f"   Compatibility: {compatibility.get('score', 0):.2f}")
 649:         
 650:         # ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 651:         # 🎧 EXECUTE TRANSITION (Headless File Generation Fix)
 652:         # ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 653:         output_path = self.transition_engine.generate_transition_mix(
 654:             cur_id=song1_id,
 655:             nxt_id=song2_id,
 656:             technique=technique,
 657:             params=params,
 658:             cur_ana=current,
 659:             nxt_ana=next_analysis
 660:         )
 661:         
 662:         if output_path and os.path.exists(output_path):
 663:             print(f"{Fore.GREEN}✅ Transition saved: {output_path}{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 664:             return output_path
 665:         else:
 666:             print(f"{Fore.RED}❌ Transition failed{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 667:             return None
 668: 
 669: 
 670: def main():
 671:     print_banner()
 672:     
 673:     try:
 674:         app = DJApp()
 675:         
 676:         # Check command line args
 677:         if len(sys.argv) > 1:
 678:             if sys.argv[1] == 'setup':
 679:                 app.initial_setup()
 680:                 return
 681:             elif sys.argv[1] == 'test':
 682:                 # Test single transition
 683:                 result = app.test_single_transition()
 684:                 if result:
 685:                     print(f"\n{Fore.GREEN}Test complete! File: {result}{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 686:                 return
 687:             elif sys.argv[1] == 'test-loop':
 688:                 # Test multiple transitions
 689:                 count = int(sys.argv[2]) if len(sys.argv) > 2 else 5
 690:                 for i in range(count):
 691:                     print(f"\n{'='*50}")
 692:                     print(f"Test {i+1}/{count}")
 693:                     app.test_single_transition()
 694:                 return
 695:         
 696:         # Check if we have songs
 697:         if not app.metadata_cache:
 698:             print(f"\n{Fore.YELLOW}📋 No songs in cache. Running initial setup...{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 699:             app.initial_setup()
 700:         
 701:         app.start_djing()
 702:         
 703:     except KeyboardInterrupt:
 704:         print(f"\n{Fore.YELLOW}👋 Goodbye!{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 705:     except Exception as e:
 706:         print(f"{Fore.RED}❌ Fatal error: {e}{Style.RESET_ALL}")
 707:         import traceback
 708:         traceback.print_exc()
 709: 
 710: 
 711: if __name__ == "__main__":
 712:     main()

   1: # Add this import at the top of mobile_tester.py:
   2: from ai_brain.innovation_engine import InnovationEngine
   3: 
   4: # In the init section, add:
   5: innovation_engine = None
   6: 
   7: # In factory_loop(), after dj is initialized, add:
   8: global innovation_engine
   9: try:
  10:     from utils.drive_manager import DriveManager
  11:     dm = DriveManager(dj.config)
  12:     innovation_engine = InnovationEngine(dj.config, dm)
  13: except:
  14:     innovation_engine = InnovationEngine(dj.config, None)
  15: 
  16: # Replace the feedback() function with this:
  17: @app.route('/feedback', methods=['POST'])
  18: def feedback():
  19:     global innovation_engine
  20:     data = request.json
  21:     is_pass = data.get('pass', False)
  22:     text = data.get('text_feedback', '')
  23:     
  24:     state = current_task.get()
  25:     technique = state.get('technique', '')
  26:     
  27:     # Record feedback for AI learning!
  28:     if technique and innovation_engine:
  29:         try:
  30:             innovation_engine.record_feedback(
  31:                 technique=technique,
  32:                 passed=is_pass,
  33:                 params={},
  34:                 song_a={'title': state.get('cur_title', '')},
  35:                 song_b={'title': state.get('nxt_title', '')},
  36:                 text_feedback=text
  37:             )
  38:         except Exception as e:
  39:             print(f"Learning error: {e}")
  40:     
  41:     # Save feedback weights
  42:     if technique:
  43:         try:
  44:             os.makedirs('data/logs', exist_ok=True)
  45:             weight_file = 'data/logs/feedback_weights.json'
  46:             weights = {}
  47:             if os.path.exists(weight_file):
  48:                 with open(weight_file, 'r') as f:
  49:                     weights = json.load(f)
  50:             weights[technique] = weights.get(technique, 1.0) + (0.3 if is_pass else -0.2)
  51:             with open(weight_file, 'w') as f:
  52:                 json.dump(weights, f, indent=2)
  53:         except Exception as e:
  54:             print(f"Weight save error: {e}")
  55:     
  56:     current_task.update(audio_ready=False, status='idle')
  57:     return jsonify({'status': 'ok'})

FILE: quick_fix.py
================================================================================
   1: import os
   2: 
   3: fixes = {
   4:     'ai_brain/agents/research_agent.py': [
   5:         ('import os\nimport json', 'import os\nimport json\nimport random')
   6:     ],
   7:     'ai_brain/agents/self_improve_agent.py': [
   8:         ('self.whisper_model = whisper.load_model("base")',
   9:          'if whisper is None:\n            print("Whisper missing")\n            return None\n        self.whisper_model = whisper.load_model("base")')
  10:     ],
  11:     'ai_brain/agents/wordplay_agent.py': [
  12:         ('phones = pronouncing.phones_for_word(word)',
  13:          'if pronouncing is None: return None\n        phones = pronouncing.phones_for_word(word)')
  14:     ]
  15: }
  16: 
  17: for path, changes in fixes.items():
  18:     if os.path.exists(path):
  19:         with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
  20:             data = f.read()
  21:         for old, new in changes:
  22:             if old in data:
  23:                 data = data.replace(old, new)
  24:                 print(f"✅ Fixed bug in {path}")
  25:         with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
  26:             f.write(data)



================================================================================
FILE: README.md
================================================================================
   1: # 🎧 AI DJ: Autonomous Innovation Pipeline
   2: 
   3: **AI DJ** is a fully autonomous system designed to discover, invent, and validate next-generation music transitions. It leverages a multi-agent "Brain" to research techniques, mutate them into novel innovations, and pre-validate them before user testing.
   4: 
   5: ## 📌 Index
   6: - [🏗️ System Architecture](ARCHITECTURE.md)
   7: - [📖 Project Wiki](docs/WIKI.md)
   8: - [📱 Mobile Command Terminal](tools/antigravity_mobile.py)
   9: - [🧠 The AI Brain & Agents](docs/WIKI.md#the-ai-brain)
  10: - [🧪 Novel Techniques & Innovation](docs/WIKI.md#novel-techniques--innovation)
  11: - [🛠️ Maintenance & Tools](docs/WIKI.md#maintenance--tools)
  12: 
  13: ---
  14: 
  15: ## 🚀 Core Mission
  16: The goal of this project is to remove the human "middle-man" from the DJ transition workflow. The system identifies track pairs, analyzes their DNA (BPM, Key, Energy), and applies advanced techniques—some learned from YouTube masters, and some invented by the system's own mutation logic.
  17: 
  18: ## 🛠️ Quick Start
  19: 1. **Library**: Add `.mp3` files to `data/library`.
  20: 2. **Run**: Execute `python mobile_tester.py`.
  21: 3. **Test**: Use the public link to rate the generated mixes.
  22: 
  23: ## 🤖 Continuous Innovation Loop
  24: The system runs a background "Factory" that:
  25: 1. Researches new techniques via Google.
  26: 2. Generates 10 candidate "Invention" mixes.
  27: 3. Ranks them using the **Validation Agent**.
  28: 4. Sends the **Top 1** candidate to the user for final approval.
  29: 
  30: ---
  31: *For deep-dives into specific modules, please refer to the [Wiki](docs/WIKI.md).*

   1: """
   2: One-click setup script
   3: Run this ONCE before starting the app:
   4:     python setup.py
   5: """
   6: import os
   7: import sys
   8: import subprocess
   9: import yaml
  10: 
  11: def check_python():
  12:     if sys.version_info < (3, 9):
  13:         print("❌ Python 3.9+ required")
  14:         sys.exit(1)
  15:     print(f"✅ Python {sys.version_info.major}.{sys.version_info.minor}")
  16: 
  17: def check_ffmpeg():
  18:     try:
  19:         subprocess.run(
  20:             ['ffmpeg', '-version'],
  21:             capture_output=True, check=True
  22:         )
  23:         print("✅ FFmpeg found")
  24:     except Exception:
  25:         print("❌ FFmpeg not found!")
  26:         print("   Download from: https://www.gyan.dev/ffmpeg/builds/")
  27:         print("   Add to PATH then re-run setup.py")
  28:         sys.exit(1)
  29: 
  30: def install_requirements():
  31:     print("\n📦 Installing Python packages...")
  32:     subprocess.run(
  33:         [sys.executable, '-m', 'pip', 'install', '-r', 'requirements.txt'],
  34:         check=True
  35:     )
  36:     print("✅ Packages installed")
  37: 
  38: def create_directories():
  39:     dirs = [
  40:         'data/audio_cache',
  41:         'data/stems',
  42:         'data/metadata',
  43:         'data/lyrics',
  44:         'data/phonemes',
  45:         'data/word_index',
  46:         'data/training_data',
  47:         'data/models',
  48:         'data/logs',
  49:         'data/sandbox',
  50:         'transition_engine',
  51:         'ai_brain/agents',
  52:         'ai_brain/training',
  53:         'ai_brain/models',
  54:         'ingestion',
  55:         'analysis',
  56:         'visual_engine',
  57:         'ui/web_ui/templates',
  58:         'ui/web_ui/static',
  59:     ]
  60:     for d in dirs:
  61:         os.makedirs(d, exist_ok=True)
  62: 
  63:     # Create __init__.py files
  64:     packages = [
  65:         'ingestion', 'analysis', 'ai_brain',
  66:         'ai_brain/agents', 'ai_brain/training',
  67:         'transition_engine', 'visual_engine',
  68:         'ui', 'ui/web_ui'
  69:     ]
  70:     for pkg in packages:
  71:         init_file = os.path.join(pkg, '__init__.py')
  72:         if not os.path.exists(init_file):
  73:             open(init_file, 'w').close()
  74: 
  75:     print("✅ Directory structure created")
  76: 
  77: def check_config():
  78:     if not os.path.exists('config.yaml'):
  79:         print("❌ config.yaml not found!")
  80:         print("   Make sure config.yaml is in the project root")
  81:         sys.exit(1)
  82: 
  83:     with open('config.yaml', 'r') as f:
  84:         config = yaml.safe_load(f)
  85: 
  86:     playlist_url = config.get('youtube', {}).get('playlist_url', '')
  87:     if not playlist_url:
  88:         print("\n⚠️  No playlist URL in config.yaml")
  89:         url = input("Enter your YouTube playlist URL now: ").strip()
  90:         config['youtube']['playlist_url'] = url
  91:         with open('config.yaml', 'w') as f:
  92:             yaml.dump(config, f)
  93:         print("✅ Playlist URL saved")
  94:     else:
  95:         print(f"✅ Playlist URL found")
  96:

  98:     print("\n📺 OBS Setup")
  99:     print("   Make sure OBS is running with WebSocket enabled:")
 100:     print("   OBS → Tools → WebSocket Server Settings")
 101:     print("   Enable WebSocket server, port 4455")
 102:     print("   Add password to config.yaml if set")
 103:

  18:     if os.path.exists(filepath):

  20:             with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
  21:                 return json.load(f)

  29:         json.dump(data, f, indent=2)

  70:     <div class="header">
  71:         <h1>DJ God Mode</h1>
  72:         <div class="queue-badge" id="queue-count">Syncing...</div>
  73:     </div>
  74:     <div id="queue-container"></div>
  75:     
  76:     <script>
  77:         let currentItem = null;
  78:         let audioElement = null;
  79:         let isProcessing = false;
  80: 
  81:         async function fetchQueue() {
  82:             if (isProcessing) return; // Don't fetch while processing a rating
  83:             
  84:             const res = await fetch('/api/queue');
  85:             const data = await res.json();
  86:             const container = document.getElementById('queue-container');
  87:             const counter = document.getElementById('queue-count');
  88:             
  89:             counter.innerText = data.length + ' Mixes Pending';
  90:             
  91:             if (data.length === 0) {
  92:                 // Stop any playing audio
  93:                 if (audioElement) {
  94:                     audioElement.pause();
  95:                     audioElement = null;
  96:                 }
  97:                 currentItem = null;
  98:                 container.innerHTML = '<div class="empty"><h3>Queue Empty</h3><p>AI Brain is slicing audio...</p></div>';
  99:                 return;
 100:             }
 101:             
 102:             const newItem = data[0];
 103:             
 104:             // Only rebuild UI if this is a DIFFERENT mix than what's currently showing
 105:             if (currentItem && currentItem.timestamp === newItem.timestamp) {
 106:                 return; // Same item, no need to rebuild
 107:             }
 108:             
 109:             // Stop old audio before switching
 110:             if (audioElement) {
 111:                 audioElement.pause();
 112:                 audioElement.src = '';
 113:                 audioElement = null;
 114:             }
 115:             
 116:             currentItem = newItem;
 117:             
 118:             // Build the UI
 119:             container.innerHTML = `
 120:                 <div class="card" id="focus-card">
 121:                     <div class="tech-badge">* ${currentItem.technique}</div>
 122:                     
 123:                     <div class="track-box track-out">
 124:                         <div class="label-sm label-out">OUTGOING TRACK (A) - Playing First</div>
 125:                         <div class="track-title">${escapeHtml(currentItem.from_title)}</div>
 126:                     </div>
 127:                     
 128:                     <div class="track-box track-in">
 129:                         <div class="label-sm label-in">INCOMING TRACK (B) - Playing Second</div>
 130:                         <div class="track-title">${escapeHtml(currentItem.to_title)}</div>
 131:                     </div>
 132:                     
 133:                     <div class="player-container">
 134:                         <audio id="main-audio" controls preload="auto"></audio>
 135:                         <div id="audio-status" class="status-bar status-loading">Loading audio...</div>
 136:                     </div>
 137:                     
 138:                     <textarea id="feedback-input" placeholder="TEACH THE AI: Why was this mix fire or trash?"></textarea>
 139:                     
 140:                     <div class="btn-row">
 141:                         <button id="btn-trash" class="btn-fail" disabled>* Trash</button>
 142:                         <button id="btn-fire" class="btn-pass" disabled>* Fire</button>
 143:                     </div>
 144:                 </div>`;
 145:             
 146:             // Setup audio element with proper event handling
 147:             audioElement = document.getElementById('main-audio');
 148:             const statusBar = document.getElementById('audio-status');
 149:             const btnTrash = document.getElementById('btn-trash');
 150:             const btnFire = document.getElementById('btn-fire');
 151:             
 152:             // Audio loading events
 153:             audioElement.oncanplaythrough = function() {
 154:                 statusBar.className = 'status-bar status-ready';
 155:                 statusBar.innerText = 'Ready to play - Rate this mix!';
 156:                 btnTrash.disabled = false;
 157:                 btnFire.disabled = false;
 158:             };
 159:             
 160:             audioElement.onerror = function() {
 161:                 statusBar.className = 'status-bar status-error';
 162:                 statusBar.innerText = 'Error loading audio';
 163:             };
 164:             
 165:             audioElement.onplay = function() {
 166:                 statusBar.className = 'status-bar status-ready';
 167:                 statusBar.innerText = 'NOW PLAYING - Listen and rate!';
 168:             };
 169:             
 170:             // Set the source and load
 171:             audioElement.src = '/audio?path=' + encodeURIComponent(currentItem.local_path);
 172:             audioElement.load();
 173:             
 174:             // Attach button handlers
 175:             btnTrash.onclick = function() { rateMix(2); };
 176:             btnFire.onclick = function() { rateMix(8); };
 177:         }
 178: 
 179:         function escapeHtml(text) {
 180:             const div = document.createElement('div');
 181:             div.textContent = text;
 182:             return div.innerHTML;
 183:         }
 184: 
 185:         async function rateMix(ratingScore) {
 186:             if (!currentItem || isProcessing) return;
 187:             
 188:             isProcessing = true;
 189:             
 190:             // Disable buttons and show processing state
 191:             const btnTrash = document.getElementById('btn-trash');
 192:             const btnFire = document.getElementById('btn-fire');
 193:             const statusBar = document.getElementById('audio-status');
 194:             const card = document.getElementById('focus-card');
 195:             
 196:             btnTrash.disabled = true;
 197:             btnFire.disabled = true;
 198:             statusBar.innerText = 'Submitting rating...';
 199:             statusBar.className = 'status-bar status-loading';
 200:             card.style.opacity = '0.5';
 201:             
 202:             // STOP the audio NOW
 203:             if (audioElement) {
 204:                 audioElement.pause();
 205:                 audioElement.src = '';
 206:             }
 207:             
 208:             const feedback = document.getElementById('feedback-input').value;
 209:             
 210:             const payload = {
 211:                 timestamp: currentItem.timestamp,
 212:                 technique: currentItem.technique,
 213:                 rating: ratingScore,
 214:                 feedback: feedback,
 215:                 track_a: currentItem.from_title,
 216:                 track_b: currentItem.to_title,
 217:                 from_id: currentItem.from_id || "unknown",
 218:                 to_id: currentItem.to_id || "unknown"
 219:             };
 220: 
 221:             try {
 222:                 await fetch('/api/rate', {
 223:                     method: 'POST',
 224:                     headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'},
 225:                     body: JSON.stringify(payload)
 226:                 });
 227:             } catch (e) {
 228:                 console.error('Rating failed:', e);
 229:             }
 230:             
 231:             // Clear current item to force reload
 232:             currentItem = null;
 233:             audioElement = null;
 234:             isProcessing = false;
 235:             
 236:             // Small delay to let server update, then fetch new queue
 237:             setTimeout(fetchQueue, 500);
 238:         }
 239: 
 240:         // Initial fetch
 241:         fetchQueue();
 242:         
 243:         // Poll for new items only when not playing/processing
 244:         setInterval(function() {
 245:             if (!isProcessing && (!audioElement || audioElement.paused)) {
 246:                 fetchQueue();
 247:             }
 248:         }, 5000);
 249:     </script>
 250: </body>
 251: </html>
 252: """
 253: 
 254: @app.route('/')
 255: def serve_ui(): return render_template_string(MOBILE_UI_HTML)
 256: 
 257: @app.route('/audio')
 258: def serve_audio():
 259:     path = request.args.get('path')
 260:     if path and os.path.exists(path):
 261:         return send_from_directory(os.path.dirname(path), os.path.basename(path))
 262:     return "Not Found", 404
 263: 
 264: @app.route('/api/queue')
 265: def get_queue():
 266:     links = load_json(LINKS_FILE, [])
 267:     # Sort by timestamp so newest is first, then filter unrated
 268:     unrated = [l for l in links if l.get('rating') is None]
 269:     # Sort by timestamp ASCENDING so oldest unrated is first (FIFO)
 270:     unrated.sort(key=lambda x: x.get('timestamp', 0))
 271:     return jsonify(unrated)
 272: 
 273: @app.route('/api/rate', methods=['POST'])
 274: def rate_transition():
 275:     data = request.json
 276:     ts = data.get('timestamp')
 277:     tech = data.get('technique')
 278:     rating = data.get('rating')
 279:     feedback = data.get('feedback', '').strip()
 280:     
 281:     links = load_json(LINKS_FILE, [])
 282:     for l in links:
 283:         if l.get('timestamp') == ts:
 284:             l.update({'rating': rating, 'tested': True, 'human_feedback': feedback})
 285:             break
 286:     save_json(LINKS_FILE, links)
 287: 
 288:     weights = load_json(WEIGHTS_FILE, {})
 289:     weights[tech] = weights.get(tech, 0) + ((rating - 5) / 10.0)
 290:     save_json(WEIGHTS_FILE, weights)
 291: 
 292:     if feedback:
 293:         mem = load_json(MEMORY_FILE, [])
 294:         mem.append({"timestamp": ts, "technique": tech, "rating": rating, "criticism": feedback})
 295:         save_json(MEMORY_FILE, mem[-50:])
 296:         
 297:     # Trigger REMEDIATION mode on FAIL (Rating < 5)
 298:     if rating < 5:
 299:         state = load_json(STATE_FILE, {})
 300:         
 301:         if data.get('from_id') != "unknown" and data.get('to_id') != "unknown":
 302:             state.update({
 303:                 'mode': 'REMEDIATION',
 304:                 'failed_technique': tech,
 305:                 'failed_from_id': data.get('from_id'),
 306:                 'failed_to_id': data.get('to_id'),
 307:                 'homework_query': f"How to DJ {tech} transition tutorial step by step"
 308:             })
 309:             save_json(STATE_FILE, state)
 310:             print(f"REMEDIATION TRIGGERED: AI will study {tech}")
 311:         else:
 312:             print("FAILED ON OLD MIX: No track IDs available for remediation")
 313: 
 314:     return jsonify({"status": "success"})
 315: 
 316: if __name__ == '__main__':
 317:     print("Flask UI starting on port 8080...")
 318:     app.run(host='0.0.0.0', port=8080, threaded=True, use_reloader=False)

   1: import os, sys, random, json, time, subprocess, librosa, numpy as np
   2: from main import DJApp
   3: from utils.notifier import send_notification
   4: 
   5: MOBILE_UI_URL = "https://parth-dj-god-mode-2026.loca.lt"
   6: MAX_UNRATED_QUEUE = 20
   7: 
   8: def load_json_safe(fp, default):
   9:     if os.path.exists(fp):
  10:         try:
  11:             with open(fp, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: return json.load(f)
  12:         except: pass
  13:     return default
  14: 
  15: def save_json_safe(fp, data):
  16:     os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(fp), exist_ok=True)
  17:     with open(fp, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(data, f, indent=2)
  18: 
  19: def get_unrated_count():
  20:     return len([l for l in load_json_safe('data/logs/transition_links.json', []) if l.get('rating') is None])
  21: 
  22: def get_smart_slice_timestamp(filepath):
  23:     try:
  24:         y, sr = librosa.load(filepath, sr=11025, mono=True)
  25:         rms = librosa.feature.rms(y=y)[0]
  26:         smooth = np.convolve(rms, np.ones(int((sr/512)*5))/int((sr/512)*5), mode='valid')
  27:         drop_time = librosa.frames_to_time(np.argmax(np.diff(smooth)), sr=sr)
  28:         return max(0, drop_time - 30)
  29:     except: return 45.0
  30: 
  31: def test_random_transitions():
  32:     print("🔧 Booting AI DJ Brain (Active Remediation Engine)...")
  33:     app = DJApp(); app.playlist = app.downloader.get_playlist_metadata(app.config['youtube']['playlist_url'])
  34:     blacklist = set(load_json_safe('data/logs/blacklist.json', []))
  35:     session_skips = set(); is_sleeping = False
  36: 
  37:     while True:
  38:         state = load_json_safe('data/logs/system_state.json', {})
  39:         mode = state.get('mode', 'NORMAL')
  40:         ready = []
  41: 
  42:         # 1. REMEDIATION BRANCH (SAME SONGS, NEW KNOWLEDGE)
  43:         if mode == 'REMEDIATION':
  44:             tech = state.get('failed_technique', 'cut')
  45:             print(f"📚 STUDY MODE: Fetching tutorial for {tech}...")
  46:             
  47:             # Call knowledge agent to fetch real steps
  48:             subprocess.run([sys.executable, 'knowledge_agent.py', state['homework_query'], tech])
  49:             
  50:             f_id = state.get('failed_from_id')
  51:             t_id = state.get('failed_to_id')
  52:             
  53:             # Find the exact same songs in playlist
  54:             c_i = next((s for s in app.playlist if s['id'] == f_id), None)
  55:             n_i = next((s for s in app.playlist if s['id'] == t_id), None)
  56:             
  57:             if c_i and n_i:
  58:                 # Load the snips directly (they already exist from last failure)
  59:                 ready = [
  60:                     {'path': os.path.join(app.config['paths']['audio_cache'], f"{c_i['id']}_snip.mp3"), 'info': c_i},
  61:                     {'path': os.path.join(app.config['paths']['audio_cache'], f"{n_i['id']}_snip.mp3"), 'info': n_i}
  62:                 ]
  63:                 print(f"🔄 RETRY MODE: Same songs, new brain! ({c_i['title']} -> {n_i['title']})")
  64:             
  65:             # Reset state immediately so we don't loop forever
  66:             state['mode'] = 'NORMAL'
  67:             save_json_safe('data/logs/system_state.json', state)
  68: 
  69:         # 2. NORMAL ACQUISITION BRANCH
  70:         else:
  71:             unrated = get_unrated_count()
  72:             if unrated >= MAX_UNRATED_QUEUE:
  73:                 if not is_sleeping: print(f"⏸️ Queue full ({unrated}/{MAX_UNRATED_QUEUE}). Paused."); is_sleeping = True
  74:                 time.sleep(10); continue
  75:             is_sleeping = False
  76: 
  77:             drive_index = load_json_safe('data/logs/drive_index.json', {})
  78:             candidates = [s for s in app.playlist if s['id'] not in blacklist and s['id'] not in session_skips]
  79:             
  80:             while len(ready) < 2 and candidates:
  81:                 uncharted = [s for s in candidates if s['id'] not in drive_index]
  82:                 chosen = random.choice(uncharted) if uncharted else random.choice(candidates)
  83:                 candidates = [c for c in candidates if c['id'] != chosen['id']]
  84:                 
  85:                 sid = chosen['id']; snip_id = f"{sid}_snip"; snip_p = os.path.join(app.config['paths']['audio_cache'], f"{snip_id}.mp3")
  86:                 if os.path.exists(snip_p): ready.append({'path': snip_p, 'info': chosen}); continue
  87:                 
  88:                 raw_p = os.path.join(app.config['paths']['audio_cache'], f"{sid}.mp3")
  89:                 if sid in drive_index: 
  90:                     app.drive_manager.download_file(app.downloader._get_account_for_song(sid), drive_index[sid], raw_p)
  91:                 elif app.downloader.download_song(chosen['url'], sid): raw_p = os.path.join(app.config['paths']['audio_cache'], f"{sid}.mp3")
  92:                 else: session_skips.add(sid); continue
  93: 
  94:                 start = get_smart_slice_timestamp(raw_p)
  95:                 subprocess.run(['ffmpeg', '-y', '-i', raw_p, '-ss', str(start), '-t', '90', '-c:a', 'libmp3lame', '-q:a', '2', snip_p], capture_output=True)
  96:                 if sid not in drive_index:
  97:                     did = app.downloader.upload_to_drive(sid, app.drive_manager)
  98:                     if did: drive_index[sid] = did; save_json_safe('data/logs/drive_index.json', drive_index)
  99:                 elif os.path.exists(raw_p): os.remove(raw_p)
 100:                 ready.append({'path': snip_p, 'info': chosen})
 101: 
 102:         if len(ready) < 2: continue
 103:         
 104:         # 3. DECIDE & MIX (Both modes hit this!)
 105:         c_i, n_i = ready[0]['info'], ready[1]['info']
 106:         c_a = app.analyzer.analyze_track(ready[0]['path'], f"{c_i['id']}_snip")
 107:         n_a = app.analyzer.analyze_track(ready[1]['path'], f"{n_i['id']}_snip")
 108:         
 109:         # Force technique if remediation, else let it decide
 110:         if mode == 'REMEDIATION': tech = state.get('failed_technique', 'cut_transition'); params = {}
 111:         else: tech, params = app.transition_decider.decide_transition(c_i['title'], n_i['title'], c_a, n_a)
 112:         
 113:         out_p = app.transition_engine.generate_transition_mix(f"{c_i['id']}_snip", f"{n_i['id']}_snip", tech, params, c_a, n_a)
 114:         if out_p:
 115:             d_l = app.drive_manager.upload_transition(out_p)
 116:             links = load_json_safe('data/logs/transition_links.json', [])
 117:             
 118:             # 🚨 CAVE-MAN FIX: Save from_id and to_id here so UI can access them!
 119:             links.append({
 120:                 'from_id': c_i['id'], 'to_id': n_i['id'],
 121:                 'from_title': c_i['title'], 'to_title': n_i['title'], 
 122:                 'technique': tech, 'drive_link': d_l, 
 123:                 'local_path': out_p, 'timestamp': time.time(), 'rating': None
 124:             })
 125:             save_json_safe('data/logs/transition_links.json', links)
 126:             
 127:             mix_type = "🛠️ REMEDIATION MIX" if mode == 'REMEDIATION' else "🎧 NEW MIX"
 128:             send_notification(f"{mix_type} Ready: {tech}\n{MOBILE_UI_URL}")

  86:         self.btn_generate.config(state=tk.DISABLED)

  89:         self.btn_fail.config(state=tk.DISABLED)

  92:

  94:         
  95:     def _generate_task(self):
  96:         try:
  97:             songs_to_test = random.sample(self.app.playlist, 2)
  98:             cur_song, nxt_song = songs_to_test[0], songs_to_test[1]
  99:             
 100:             for song in [cur_song, nxt_song]:
 101:                 song_id = song['id']
 102:                 
 103:                 # Check for existing metadata cache file
 104:                 meta_path = os.path.join("data", "metadata", f"{song_id}.json")
 105:                 if os.path.exists(meta_path) and song_id not in self.app.metadata_cache:
 106:                     try:
 107:                         with open(meta_path, 'r') as f:
 108:                             self.app.metadata_cache[song_id] = json.load(f)
 109:                     except:
 110:                         pass
 111:                 
 112:                 filepath = os.path.join(self.app.config['paths']['audio_cache'], f"{song_id}.mp3")
 113:                 if not os.path.exists(filepath):
 114:                     self.after(0, lambda s=song: self.lbl_status.config(text=f"Downloading (1 of 2): {s['title'][:30]}..."))
 115:                     filepath = self.app.downloader.download_song(song['url'], song_id)
 116:                 else:
 117:                     self.after(0, lambda s=song: self.lbl_status.config(text=f"Using cached: {s['title'][:30]}"))
 118:                     
 119:                 if song_id not in self.app.metadata_cache:
 120:                     self.after(0, lambda s=song: self.lbl_status.config(text=f"Analyzing: {s['title'][:30]}..."))
 121:                     analysis = self.app.analyzer.analyze_track(filepath, song_id)
 122:                     analysis['title'] = song['title']
 123:                     self.app.metadata_cache[song_id] = analysis
 124: 
 125:             cur_ana = self.app.metadata_cache[cur_song['id']]
 126:             nxt_ana = self.app.metadata_cache[nxt_song['id']]
 127:             
 128:             compatibility = random.randint(40, 80)
 129:             technique = self.app.transition_decider.decide(cur_ana, nxt_ana, compatibility)
 130:             params = self.app.transition_decider.get_params(cur_ana, nxt_ana, technique)
 131:             
 132:             self.after(0, lambda: self.lbl_status.config(text=f"Generating Transition ({technique})..."))
 133:             self.captured_audio = []
 134:             
 135:             self.app.transition_engine.execute(
 136:                 current_id=cur_song['id'], next_id=nxt_song['id'],
 137:                 technique=technique, params=params,
 138:                 current_analysis=cur_ana, next_analysis=nxt_ana
 139:             )
 140:             
 141:             if self.captured_audio:
 142:                 self.audio_arr = np.concatenate(self.captured_audio)
 143:                 max_val = np.max(np.abs(self.audio_arr))
 144:                 if max_val > 0:
 145:                     self.audio_arr = self.audio_arr / max_val * 0.9
 146:             else:
 147:                 self.audio_arr = np.zeros(44100)
 148:                 
 149:             self.current_technique = technique
 150:             
 151:             # ☁️ Now that audio is generated, offload original files to Google Drive
 152:             if os.path.exists('data/tokens/token_account_1.json'):
 153:                 for song in [cur_song, nxt_song]:
 154:                     self.after(0, lambda s=song: self.lbl_status.config(text=f"☁️ Offloading to Drive: {s['title'][:30]}..."))
 155:                     self.app.downloader.upload_to_drive(song['id'], self.app.drive_manager)
 156:             
 157:             song_text = f"From: {cur_song['title'][:40]}\nTo: {nxt_song['title'][:40]}\n\nTechnique: {technique}"
 158:             
 159:             self.after(0, lambda: self.lbl_songs.config(text=song_text))
 160:             self.after(0, lambda: self.lbl_status.config(text="Transition generated! You can now play and rate it."))
 161:             
 162:             self.after(0, lambda: self.btn_generate.config(state=tk.NORMAL))
 163:             self.after(0, lambda: self.btn_play.config(state=tk.NORMAL))
 164:             self.after(0, lambda: self.btn_pass.config(state=tk.NORMAL))
 165:             self.after(0, lambda: self.btn_fail.config(state=tk.NORMAL))
 166:             self.after(0, lambda: self.btn_stop.config(state=tk.NORMAL))
 167:             
 168:             self.after(0, self.play_audio)
 169:             
 170:         except Exception as e:
 171:             self.after(0, lambda: self.lbl_status.config(text=f"Error generating transition: {str(e)}"))
 172:             self.after(0, lambda: self.btn_generate.config(state=tk.NORMAL))
 173: 
 174:     def play_audio(self):
 175:         if self.audio_arr is not None:
 176:             sd.stop()
 177:             sd.play(self.audio_arr, self.app.config['audio']['sample_rate'])
 178:             
 179:     def stop_audio(self):
 180:         sd.stop()
 181:         
 182:     def submit_feedback(self, is_pass):
 183:         if not self.current_technique:
 184:             return
 185:             
 186:         sd.stop()
 187:         rating = 8 if is_pass else 3
 188:         
 189:         weight_file = os.path.join('data', 'logs', 'feedback_weights.json')
 190:         os.makedirs(os.path.join('data', 'logs'), exist_ok=True)
 191:         
 192:         weights = {}
 193:         if os.path.exists(weight_file):
 194:             try:
 195:                 with open(weight_file, 'r') as f:
 196:                     weights = json.load(f)
 197:             except Exception:
 198:                 pass
 199:                 
 200:         # 8 -> 30% positive adjustment, 3 -> 20% negative adjustment
 201:         adjustment = (rating - 5) / 10.0
 202:         current_weight = weights.get(self.current_technique, 0)
 203:         weights[self.current_technique] = current_weight + adjustment
 204:         
 205:         with open(weight_file, 'w') as f:
 206:             json.dump(weights, f, indent=4)
 207:             
 208:         self.lbl_status.config(text=f"Learned! Adjusted '{self.current_technique}' weight by {adjustment:+.2f}")
 209:         self.lbl_songs.config(text="")
 210:         
 211:         self.btn_play.config(state=tk.DISABLED)
 212:         self.btn_pass.config(state=tk.DISABLED)
 213:         self.btn_fail.config(state=tk.DISABLED)
 214:         self.current_technique = None
 215: 
 216: if __name__ == "__main__":
 217:     app = DJUITester()
 218:     app.mainloop()

FILE: ai_brain\innovation_engine.py
