   1: """
   2: Innovation Engine - AI That Learns and Invents New DJ Techniques!
   3: 
   4: This engine:
   5: 1. Stores every transition you rate (pass/fail) on Google Drive
   6: 2. Analyzes patterns in successful vs failed transitions
   7: 3. Mutates and combines techniques to create NEW ones
   8: 4. Tests innovations and keeps the winners
   9: 
  10: This is how AI becomes BETTER than human DJs - it experiments 24/7!
  11: """
  12: 
  13: import os
  14: import json
  15: import random
  16: import time
  17: from datetime import datetime
  18: from typing import Dict, List, Optional
  19: 
  20: class InnovationEngine:
  21:     """
  22:     The brain that never sleeps. Always learning. Always inventing.
  23:     """
  24:     
  25:     def __init__(self, config, drive_manager=None):
  26:         self.config = config
  27:         self.drive = drive_manager
  28:         self.local_feedback_path = 'data/logs/feedback_log.jsonl'
  29:         self.local_innovations_path = 'data/logs/innovations.json'
  30:         self.innovations = self._load_innovations()
  31:         
  32:         # Known base techniques that can be mutated/combined
  33:         self.base_techniques = [
  34:             'beatmatch_crossfade', 'cut_transition', 'echo_out',
  35:             'filter_sweep', 'loop_roll', 'reverb_wash', 'spinback',
  36:             'tempo_ramp', 'white_noise_sweep', 'vinyl_scratch_flourish',
  37:             'tone_play', 'wordplay', 'mashup_short', 'mashup_extended',
  38:             'acapella_layer', 'drum_swap', 'bass_swap', 'stutter_glitch',
  39:             'half_time_transition', 'wordplay_mashup', 'phrasal_interlace'
  40:         ]
  41:         
  42:         # Parameters that can be mutated
  43:         self.mutable_params = {
  44:             'crossfade_bars': [2, 4, 8, 16, 32],
  45:             'mashup_bars': [4, 8, 16, 32],
  46:             'echo_feedback': [0.3, 0.5, 0.7, 0.9],
  47:             'echo_delay_ms': [125, 250, 375, 500],
  48:             'filter_sweep_duration': [4, 8, 12, 16],
  49:             'reverb_room_size': [0.3, 0.5, 0.7, 0.9],
  50:             'pitch_shift_semitones': [-5, -3, -2, 2, 3, 5, 7, 12],
  51:             'interlace_slice_divisions': [4, 8, 16, 32, 64],
  52:             'glitch_density': [4, 8, 16, 32],
  53:             'half_time_ramp_bars': [4, 8, 16],
  54:             'word_repeats': [2, 3, 4, 6, 8],
  55:             'layer_bars': [8, 16, 32],
  56:             'pitch_interpolation_steps': [4, 8, 12, 24],
  57:             'spectral_freeze_duration_ms': [250, 500, 1000, 2000],
  58:         }
  59:     
  60:     def _load_innovations(self) -> Dict:
  61:         """Load existing innovations from disk"""
  62:         if os.path.exists(self.local_innovations_path):
  63:             try:
  64:                 with open(self.local_innovations_path, 'r') as f:
  65:                     return json.load(f)
  66:             except:
  67:                 pass
  68:         return {'techniques': [], 'experiments': [], 'hall_of_fame': []}
  69:     
  70:     def _save_innovations(self):
  71:         """Save innovations to disk and optionally to Drive"""
  72:         os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(self.local_innovations_path), exist_ok=True)
  73:         with open(self.local_innovations_path, 'w') as f:
  74:             json.dump(self.innovations, f, indent=2)
  75:         
  76:         # Upload to Drive for backup
  77:         if self.drive:
  78:             try:
  79:                 self.drive.upload_file('account_1', self.local_innovations_path, 'DJ_Agent_Innovations')
  80:             except:
  81:                 pass
  82:     
  83:     def record_feedback(self, technique: str, passed: bool, params: Dict, 
  84:                         song_a: Dict, song_b: Dict, text_feedback: str = ""):
  85:         """
  86:         Record user feedback for AI learning.
  87:         Every pass/fail teaches the AI what works!
  88:         """
  89:         record = {
  90:             'timestamp': time.time(),
  91:             'datetime': datetime.now().isoformat(),
  92:             'technique': technique,
  93:             'passed': passed,
  94:             'params': params,
  95:             'song_a': {
  96:                 'title': song_a.get('title', 'Unknown'),
  97:                 'bpm': song_a.get('bpm'),
  98:                 'key': song_a.get('camelot'),
  99:                 'energy': song_a.get('energy_mean'),
 100:                 'genre': song_a.get('genre_hint'),
 101:             },
 102:             'song_b': {
 103:                 'title': song_b.get('title', 'Unknown'),
 104:                 'bpm': song_b.get('bpm'),
 105:                 'key': song_b.get('camelot'),
 106:                 'energy': song_b.get('energy_mean'),
 107:                 'genre': song_b.get('genre_hint'),
 108:             },
 109:             'bpm_diff': abs((song_a.get('bpm') or 120) - (song_b.get('bpm') or 120)),
 110:             'text_feedback': text_feedback,
 111:         }
 112:         
 113:         # Append to local log
 114:         os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(self.local_feedback_path), exist_ok=True)
 115:         with open(self.local_feedback_path, 'a') as f:
 116:             f.write(json.dumps(record) + '\n')
 117:         
 118:         # Upload to Drive for long-term storage
 119:         if self.drive:
 120:             try:
 121:                 self.drive.upload_file('account_1', self.local_feedback_path, 'DJ_Agent_Feedback')
 122:             except:
 123:                 pass
 124:         
 125:         print(f"   📝 Feedback recorded: {technique} = {'✅ PASS' if passed else '❌ FAIL'}")
 126:     
 127:     def analyze_patterns(self) -> Dict:
 128:         """
 129:         Analyze all feedback to find patterns.
 130:         What techniques work? When do they fail?
 131:         """
 132:         if not os.path.exists(self.local_feedback_path):
 133:             return {'total': 0, 'patterns': []}
 134:         
 135:         # Load all feedback
 136:         records = []
 137:         with open(self.local_feedback_path, 'r') as f:
 138:             for line in f:
 139:                 try:
 140:                     records.append(json.loads(line))
 141:                 except:
 142:                     continue
 143:         
 144:         if not records:
 145:             return {'total': 0, 'patterns': []}
 146:         
 147:         # Analyze by technique
 148:         technique_stats = {}
 149:         for r in records:
 150:             tech = r['technique']
 151:             if tech not in technique_stats:
 152:                 technique_stats[tech] = {'passes': 0, 'fails': 0, 'contexts': []}
 153:             
 154:             if r['passed']:
 155:                 technique_stats[tech]['passes'] += 1
 156:             else:
 157:                 technique_stats[tech]['fails'] += 1
 158:             
 159:             technique_stats[tech]['contexts'].append({
 160:                 'bpm_diff': r.get('bpm_diff', 0),
 161:                 'passed': r['passed'],
 162:             })
 163:         
 164:         # Find patterns
 165:         patterns = []
 166:         for tech, stats in technique_stats.items():
 167:             total = stats['passes'] + stats['fails']
 168:             if total >= 3:  # Need at least 3 samples
 169:                 success_rate = stats['passes'] / total
 170:                 
 171:                 # Analyze when technique works vs fails
 172:                 pass_bpm_diffs = [c['bpm_diff'] for c in stats['contexts'] if c['passed']]
 173:                 fail_bpm_diffs = [c['bpm_diff'] for c in stats['contexts'] if not c['passed']]
 174:                 
 175:                 avg_pass_bpm = sum(pass_bpm_diffs) / len(pass_bpm_diffs) if pass_bpm_diffs else 0
 176:                 avg_fail_bpm = sum(fail_bpm_diffs) / len(fail_bpm_diffs) if fail_bpm_diffs else 0
 177:                 
 178:                 patterns.append({
 179:                     'technique': tech,
 180:                     'success_rate': success_rate,
 181:                     'total_uses': total,
 182:                     'avg_pass_bpm_diff': avg_pass_bpm,
 183:                     'avg_fail_bpm_diff': avg_fail_bpm,
 184:                     'insight': self._generate_insight(tech, success_rate, avg_pass_bpm, avg_fail_bpm),
 185:                 })
 186:         
 187:         return {
 188:             'total': len(records),
 189:             'patterns': sorted(patterns, key=lambda x: x['success_rate'], reverse=True),
 190:         }
 191:     
 192:     def _generate_insight(self, technique: str, success_rate: float, 
 193:                           avg_pass_bpm: float, avg_fail_bpm: float) -> str:
 194:         """Generate human-readable insight about a technique"""
 195:         if success_rate >= 0.8:
 196:             insight = f"🌟 {technique} is a WINNER! Use it often."
 197:         elif success_rate >= 0.5:
 198:             insight = f"👍 {technique} works OK."
 199:         else:
 200:             insight = f"⚠️ {technique} often fails."
 201:         
 202:         if avg_pass_bpm < avg_fail_bpm and avg_fail_bpm - avg_pass_bpm > 5:
 203:             insight += f" Works better when BPM diff is small (<{int(avg_pass_bpm + 5)})."
 204:         elif avg_pass_bpm > avg_fail_bpm and avg_pass_bpm - avg_fail_bpm > 5:
 205:             insight += f" Works better when BPM diff is large (>{int(avg_fail_bpm)})."
 206:         
 207:         return insight
 208:     
 209:     def invent_new_technique(self) -> Optional[Dict]:
 210:         """
 211:         🧬 MUTATION ENGINE 🧬
 212:         Combines and mutates existing techniques to create NEW ones!
 213:         This is how AI goes beyond human DJ knowledge!
 214:         """
 215:         # Strategy 1: Combine two successful techniques
 216:         patterns = self.analyze_patterns()
 217:         top_techniques = [p['technique'] for p in patterns.get('patterns', [])[:5] if p['success_rate'] >= 0.6]
 218:         
 219:         if len(top_techniques) >= 2:
 220:             # Combine two techniques
 221:             tech_a, tech_b = random.sample(top_techniques, 2)
 222:             
 223:             innovation = {
 224:                 'name': f"hybrid_{tech_a[:4]}_{tech_b[:4]}_{random.randint(100,999)}",
 225:                 'type': 'hybrid',
 226:                 'parents': [tech_a, tech_b],
 227:                 'description': f"Start with {tech_a}, blend into {tech_b}",
 228:                 'created_at': datetime.now().isoformat(),
 229:                 'test_count': 0,
 230:                 'pass_count': 0,
 231:                 'status': 'experimental',
 232:             }
 233:             
 234:             self.innovations['techniques'].append(innovation)
 235:             self._save_innovations()
 236:             
 237:             print(f"   🧬 INVENTED NEW TECHNIQUE: {innovation['name']}")
 238:             print(f"      Parents: {tech_a} + {tech_b}")
 239:             
 240:             return innovation
 241:         
 242:         # Strategy 2: Mutate parameters of a successful technique
 243:         if top_techniques:
 244:             base_tech = random.choice(top_techniques)
 245:             param_key = random.choice(list(self.mutable_params.keys()))
 246:             param_value = random.choice(self.mutable_params[param_key])
 247:             
 248:             innovation = {
 249:                 'name': f"mutant_{base_tech[:6]}_{param_key[:3]}{param_value}",
 250:                 'type': 'mutation',
 251:                 'base': base_tech,
 252:                 'mutation': {param_key: param_value},
 253:                 'description': f"{base_tech} with {param_key}={param_value}",
 254:                 'created_at': datetime.now().isoformat(),
 255:                 'test_count': 0,
 256:                 'pass_count': 0,
 257:                 'status': 'experimental',
 258:             }
 259:             
 260:             self.innovations['techniques'].append(innovation)
 261:             self._save_innovations()
 262:             
 263:             print(f"   🧬 MUTATED TECHNIQUE: {innovation['name']}")
 264:             print(f"      Base: {base_tech}, Mutation: {param_key}={param_value}")
 265:             
 266:             return innovation
 267:         
 268:         # Strategy 3: Random combination
 269:         tech_a, tech_b = random.sample(self.base_techniques, 2)
 270:         innovation = {
 271:             'name': f"experiment_{random.randint(1000,9999)}",
 272:             'type': 'random_experiment',
 273:             'parents': [tech_a, tech_b],
 274:             'description': f"Wild experiment: {tech_a} meets {tech_b}",
 275:             'created_at': datetime.now().isoformat(),
 276:             'test_count': 0,
 277:             'pass_count': 0,
 278:             'status': 'experimental',
 279:         }
 280:         
 281:         self.innovations['techniques'].append(innovation)
 282:         self._save_innovations()
 283:         
 284:         print(f"   🎲 RANDOM EXPERIMENT: {innovation['name']}")
 285:         
 286:         return innovation
 287:     
 288:     def get_experimental_technique(self) -> Optional[Dict]:
 289:         """
 290:         Get an experimental technique to test.
 291:         AI wants to know if its invention works!
 292:         """
 293:         experiments = [t for t in self.innovations.get('techniques', []) 
 294:                        if t.get('status') == 'experimental' and t.get('test_count', 0) < 5]
 295:         
 296:         if experiments:
 297:             return random.choice(experiments)
 298:         return None
 299:     
 300:     def record_experiment_result(self, technique_name: str, passed: bool):
 301:         """Record result of an experimental technique"""
 302:         for tech in self.innovations.get('techniques', []):
 303:             if tech['name'] == technique_name:
 304:                 tech['test_count'] = tech.get('test_count', 0) + 1
 305:                 if passed:
 306:                     tech['pass_count'] = tech.get('pass_count', 0) + 1
 307:                 
 308:                 # Promote to hall of fame if it's proven!
 309:                 if tech['test_count'] >= 5:
 310:                     success_rate = tech['pass_count'] / tech['test_count']
 311:                     if success_rate >= 0.7:
 312:                         tech['status'] = 'proven'
 313:                         self.innovations['hall_of_fame'].append(tech)
 314:                         print(f"   🏆 TECHNIQUE PROVEN: {technique_name} ({success_rate*100:.0f}% success)")
 315:                     else:
 316:                         tech['status'] = 'failed'
 317:                         print(f"   ❌ TECHNIQUE FAILED: {technique_name} ({success_rate*100:.0f}% success)")
 318:                 
 319:                 self._save_innovations()
 320:                 return
 321:     
 322:     def get_hall_of_fame(self) -> List[Dict]:
 323:         """Get all proven AI-invented techniques"""
 324:         return self.innovations.get('hall_of_fame', [])
 325:     
 326:     def print_report(self):
 327:         """Print a report of AI learning progress"""
 328:         patterns = self.analyze_patterns()
 329:         
 330:         print("""
 331:     ╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
 332:     ║              🧠 AI LEARNING REPORT 🧠                      ║
 333:     ╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
 334:         """)
 335:         
 336:         print(f"   📊 Total transitions rated: {patterns['total']}")
 337:         print()
 338:         
 339:         if patterns['patterns']:
 340:             print("   🏆 TOP TECHNIQUES:")
 341:             for p in patterns['patterns'][:5]:
 342:                 bar = "█" * int(p['success_rate'] * 10) + "░" * (10 - int(p['success_rate'] * 10))
 343:                 print(f"      {p['technique'][:20]:<20} [{bar}] {p['success_rate']*100:.0f}%")
 344:                 print(f"         {p['insight']}")
 345:             print()
 346:         
 347:         innovations = self.innovations.get('techniques', [])
 348:         experiments = [t for t in innovations if t.get('status') == 'experimental']
 349:         proven = self.innovations.get('hall_of_fame', [])
 350:         
 351:         print(f"   🧬 INNOVATIONS:")
 352:         print(f"      Experiments in progress: {len(experiments)}")
 353:         print(f"      Proven techniques: {len(proven)}")
 354:         
 355:         if proven:
 356:             print("\n   🏆 HALL OF FAME (AI-Invented Techniques):")
 357:             for t in proven:
 358:                 print(f"      ⭐ {t['name']}: {t['description']}")
 359:         
 360:         print()

FILE: ai_brain\local_brain.py

   1: """
   2: Local AI Brain - Zero API Credits!
   3: Handles all rule-based DJ decisions locally.
   4: Only calls cloud AI for truly creative tasks.
   5: """
   6: 
   7: import random
   8: import os
   9: import json
  10: 
  11: class LocalBrain:
  12:     """
  13:     Caveman-smart DJ brain that uses RULES not API calls!
  14:     Saves your Gemini credits for when you ACTUALLY need creativity.
  15:     """
  16:     
  17:     def __init__(self, config):
  18:         self.config = config
  19:         self.camelot_wheel = self._build_camelot_wheel()
  20:         self.genre_transitions = self._build_genre_rules()
  21:         self.technique_rules = self._build_technique_rules()
  22:         self.feedback_weights = self._load_feedback_weights()
  23:     
  24:     def _build_camelot_wheel(self):
  25:         """Camelot wheel compatibility - no AI needed, just music theory!"""
  26:         # Compatible keys: same number, +1, -1, or switch A/B
  27:         return {
  28:             '1A': ['1A', '1B', '12A', '2A'],
  29:             '1B': ['1B', '1A', '12B', '2B'],
  30:             '2A': ['2A', '2B', '1A', '3A'],
  31:             '2B': ['2B', '2A', '1B', '3B'],
  32:             '3A': ['3A', '3B', '2A', '4A'],
  33:             '3B': ['3B', '3A', '2B', '4B'],
  34:             '4A': ['4A', '4B', '3A', '5A'],
  35:             '4B': ['4B', '4A', '3B', '5B'],
  36:             '5A': ['5A', '5B', '4A', '6A'],
  37:             '5B': ['5B', '5A', '4B', '6B'],
  38:             '6A': ['6A', '6B', '5A', '7A'],
  39:             '6B': ['6B', '6A', '5B', '7B'],
  40:             '7A': ['7A', '7B', '6A', '8A'],
  41:             '7B': ['7B', '7A', '6B', '8B'],
  42:             '8A': ['8A', '8B', '7A', '9A'],
  43:             '8B': ['8B', '8A', '7B', '9B'],
  44:             '9A': ['9A', '9B', '8A', '10A'],
  45:             '9B': ['9B', '9A', '8B', '10B'],
  46:             '10A': ['10A', '10B', '9A', '11A'],
  47:             '10B': ['10B', '10A', '9B', '11B'],
  48:             '11A': ['11A', '11B', '10A', '12A'],
  49:             '11B': ['11B', '11A', '10B', '12B'],
  50:             '12A': ['12A', '12B', '11A', '1A'],
  51:             '12B': ['12B', '12A', '11B', '1B'],
  52:         }
  53:     
  54:     def _build_genre_rules(self):
  55:         """Genre transition compatibility - learned from DJ tutorials, not API!"""
  56:         return {
  57:             'hip-hop': ['hip-hop', 'r&b', 'trap', 'pop'],
  58:             'edm': ['edm', 'house', 'techno', 'pop', 'dubstep'],
  59:             'house': ['house', 'edm', 'disco', 'techno'],
  60:             'pop': ['pop', 'hip-hop', 'edm', 'r&b', 'dance'],
  61:             'rock': ['rock', 'indie', 'alternative', 'metal'],
  62:             'r&b': ['r&b', 'hip-hop', 'soul', 'pop'],
  63:             'latin': ['latin', 'reggaeton', 'pop', 'dance'],
  64:             'bollywood': ['bollywood', 'indian', 'pop', 'dance'],
  65:         }
  66:     
  67:     def _build_technique_rules(self):
  68:         """Transition technique rules - pure logic, no AI!"""
  69:         return {
  70:             'same_bpm_same_key': ['beatmatch_crossfade', 'mashup_short', 'acapella_layer'],
  71:             'same_bpm_diff_key': ['filter_sweep', 'echo_out', 'reverb_wash'],
  72:             'small_bpm_diff': ['tempo_ramp', 'beatmatch_crossfade', 'drum_swap'],
  73:             'large_bpm_diff': ['cut_transition', 'spinback', 'white_noise_sweep'],
  74:             'half_double_bpm': ['half_time_transition', 'loop_roll'],
  75:             'genre_change': ['reverb_wash', 'white_noise_sweep', 'cut_transition'],
  76:             'energy_drop': ['echo_out', 'reverb_wash', 'filter_sweep'],
  77:             'energy_build': ['loop_roll', 'stutter_glitch', 'filter_sweep'],
  78:         }
  79:     
  80:     def _load_feedback_weights(self):
  81:         """Load user feedback to improve decisions over time"""
  82:         weight_file = 'data/logs/feedback_weights.json'
  83:         if os.path.exists(weight_file):
  84:             try:
  85:                 with open(weight_file, 'r') as f:
  86:                     return json.load(f)
  87:             except:
  88:                 pass
  89:         return {}
  90:     
  91:     def is_key_compatible(self, key_a, key_b):
  92:         """Check if two Camelot keys are compatible - NO API CALL!"""
  93:         if not key_a or not key_b:
  94:             return True  # Unknown = compatible
  95:         return key_b in self.camelot_wheel.get(key_a, [key_a])
  96:     
  97:     def calculate_bpm_compatibility(self, bpm_a, bpm_b):
  98:         """Calculate BPM compatibility score - NO API CALL!"""
  99:         if not bpm_a or not bpm_b:
 100:             return 0.5
 101:         
 102:         diff = abs(bpm_a - bpm_b)
 103:         
 104:         # Perfect match
 105:         if diff <= 2:
 106:             return 1.0
 107:         
 108:         # Half/double time (e.g., 70 BPM and 140 BPM)
 109:         ratio = max(bpm_a, bpm_b) / min(bpm_a, bpm_b)
 110:         if 1.95 <= ratio <= 2.05:
 111:             return 0.9
 112:         
 113:         # Small difference (can tempo ramp)
 114:         if diff <= 8:
 115:             return 0.8
 116:         
 117:         # Medium difference
 118:         if diff <= 15:
 119:             return 0.5
 120:         
 121:         # Large difference (need hard cut)
 122:         return 0.2
 123:     
 124:     def calculate_energy_flow(self, energy_a, energy_b):
 125:         """Calculate energy flow score - NO API CALL!"""
 126:         if energy_a is None or energy_b is None:
 127:             return 0.5
 128:         
 129:         diff = energy_b - energy_a
 130:         
 131:         # Slight energy increase = good DJ flow
 132:         if 0 <= diff <= 0.15:
 133:             return 1.0
 134:         
 135:         # Maintaining energy
 136:         if abs(diff) <= 0.1:
 137:             return 0.9
 138:         
 139:         # Moderate change
 140:         if abs(diff) <= 0.3:
 141:             return 0.6
 142:         
 143:         # Drastic change (might be intentional drop/build)
 144:         return 0.4
 145:     
 146:     def score_compatibility(self, song_a, song_b):
 147:         """
 148:         Full compatibility score - ALL LOCAL, ZERO API!
 149:         Returns dict with score and reasons.
 150:         """
 151:         scores = []
 152:         reasons = []
 153:         
 154:         # BPM compatibility (40% weight)
 155:         bpm_score = self.calculate_bpm_compatibility(
 156:             song_a.get('bpm'), song_b.get('bpm')
 157:         )
 158:         scores.append(bpm_score * 0.4)
 159:         if bpm_score >= 0.8:
 160:             reasons.append(f"BPM compatible ({song_a.get('bpm', '?')} → {song_b.get('bpm', '?')})")
 161:         
 162:         # Key compatibility (30% weight)
 163:         key_compat = self.is_key_compatible(
 164:             song_a.get('camelot'), song_b.get('camelot')
 165:         )
 166:         key_score = 1.0 if key_compat else 0.3
 167:         scores.append(key_score * 0.3)
 168:         if key_compat:
 169:             reasons.append(f"Key compatible ({song_a.get('camelot', '?')} → {song_b.get('camelot', '?')})")
 170:         
 171:         # Energy flow (20% weight)
 172:         energy_score = self.calculate_energy_flow(
 173:             song_a.get('energy_mean'), song_b.get('energy_mean')
 174:         )
 175:         scores.append(energy_score * 0.2)
 176:         
 177:         # Genre compatibility (10% weight)
 178:         genre_a = song_a.get('genre_hint', 'unknown').lower()
 179:         genre_b = song_b.get('genre_hint', 'unknown').lower()
 180:         compatible_genres = self.genre_transitions.get(genre_a, [genre_a])
 181:         genre_score = 1.0 if genre_b in compatible_genres else 0.5
 182:         scores.append(genre_score * 0.1)
 183:         
 184:         total_score = sum(scores) * 100  # Convert to 0-100
 185:         
 186:         return {
 187:             'score': total_score,
 188:             'bpm_score': bpm_score,
 189:             'key_score': key_score,
 190:             'energy_score': energy_score,
 191:             'genre_score': genre_score,
 192:             'reasons': reasons,
 193:         }
 194:     
 195:     def decide_technique(self, song_a, song_b, compatibility):
 196:         """
 197:         Decide transition technique - ALL LOCAL, ZERO API!
 198:         Uses rules learned from DJ tutorials.
 199:         """
 200:         bpm_a = song_a.get('bpm', 120)
 201:         bpm_b = song_b.get('bpm', 120)
 202:         bpm_diff = abs(bpm_a - bpm_b)
 203:         bpm_ratio = max(bpm_a, bpm_b) / max(min(bpm_a, bpm_b), 1)
 204:         
 205:         key_a = song_a.get('camelot', '')
 206:         key_b = song_b.get('camelot', '')
 207:         key_compatible = self.is_key_compatible(key_a, key_b)
 208:         
 209:         energy_a = song_a.get('energy_mean', 0.5)
 210:         energy_b = song_b.get('energy_mean', 0.5)
 211:         energy_diff = energy_b - energy_a
 212:         
 213:         # Determine situation
 214:         if bpm_diff <= 3 and key_compatible:
 215:             situation = 'same_bpm_same_key'
 216:         elif bpm_diff <= 3 and not key_compatible:
 217:             situation = 'same_bpm_diff_key'
 218:         elif 1.95 <= bpm_ratio <= 2.05:
 219:             situation = 'half_double_bpm'
 220:         elif bpm_diff <= 10:
 221:             situation = 'small_bpm_diff'
 222:         elif bpm_diff > 20:
 223:             situation = 'large_bpm_diff'
 224:         elif energy_diff < -0.2:
 225:             situation = 'energy_drop'
 226:         elif energy_diff > 0.2:
 227:             situation = 'energy_build'
 228:         else:
 229:             situation = 'small_bpm_diff'
 230:         
 231:         # Get candidate techniques
 232:         candidates = self.technique_rules.get(situation, ['beatmatch_crossfade'])
 233:         
 234:         # Apply user feedback weights
 235:         weighted_candidates = []
 236:         for tech in candidates:
 237:             weight = self.feedback_weights.get(tech, 1.0)
 238:             weight = max(0.1, weight)  # Never fully exclude
 239:             weighted_candidates.append((tech, weight))
 240:         
 241:         # Weighted random selection
 242:         techs = [t[0] for t in weighted_candidates]
 243:         weights = [t[1] for t in weighted_candidates]
 244:         total = sum(weights)
 245:         weights = [w / total for w in weights]
 246:         
 247:         technique = random.choices(techs, weights=weights, k=1)[0]
 248:         
 249:         return technique, {'situation': situation, 'candidates': candidates}
 250:     
 251:     def needs_cloud_ai(self, song_a, song_b):
 252:         """
 253:         Decide if we should call Gemini for creative help.
 254:         Returns True only for tasks that ACTUALLY need AI creativity.
 255:         """
 256:         # Check if both songs have lyrics
 257:         lyrics_a = song_a.get('lyrics', {}).get('text', '')
 258:         lyrics_b = song_b.get('lyrics', {}).get('text', '')
 259:         
 260:         if not lyrics_a or not lyrics_b:
 261:             return False  # No lyrics = no wordplay possible
 262:         
 263:         # Check if languages are different (cross-language wordplay is creative!)
 264:         lang_a = song_a.get('lyrics', {}).get('language', 'unknown')
 265:         lang_b = song_b.get('lyrics', {}).get('language', 'unknown')
 266:         
 267:         if lang_a != lang_b and lang_a != 'unknown' and lang_b != 'unknown':
 268:             return True  # Cross-language wordplay needs AI
 269:         
 270:         # Check compatibility score - if already great, no need for creativity
 271:         compat = self.score_compatibility(song_a, song_b)
 272:         if compat['score'] >= 80:
 273:             return False  # Already compatible, use rules
 274:         
 275:         # Low compatibility + has lyrics = try creative wordplay
 276:         if compat['score'] < 50 and lyrics_a and lyrics_b:
 277:             return True
 278:         
 279:         return False
 280: 
 281: 
 282: class LocalTransitionDecider:
 283:     """
 284:     Drop-in replacement for TransitionAgent that uses LocalBrain.
 285:     ZERO API CALLS for normal transitions!
 286:     """
 287:     
 288:     def __init__(self, config):
 289:         self.config = config
 290:         self.brain = LocalBrain(config)
 291:     
 292:     def decide(self, song_a, song_b, compatibility=None):
 293:         """Decide technique using local rules"""
 294:         if compatibility is None:
 295:             compatibility = self.brain.score_compatibility(song_a, song_b)
 296:         
 297:         technique, info = self.brain.decide_technique(song_a, song_b, compatibility)
 298:         return technique, self.get_params(song_a, song_b, technique)
 299:     
 300:     def get_params(self, song_a, song_b, technique):
 301:         """Get technique parameters based on song analysis"""
 302:         bpm = song_a.get('bpm', 120)
 303:         
 304:         params = {
 305:             'crossfade_bars': 8,
 306:             'mashup_bars': 8,
 307:             'swap_bars': 8,
 308:             'layer_bars': 16,
 309:         }
 310:         
 311:         # Adjust based on BPM (faster songs = shorter transitions)
 312:         if bpm > 140:
 313:             params['crossfade_bars'] = 4
 314:             params['mashup_bars'] = 4
 315:         elif bpm < 90:
 316:             params['crossfade_bars'] = 16
 317:             params['mashup_bars'] = 16
 318:         
 319:         return params

  12: class AnalyzerAgent:
  13:     """
  14:     Agent 1: Master analysis coordinator
  15:     Runs all analysis pipelines on a song
  16:     Orchestrates: audio analysis, phrase detection,
  17:     melody detection, stem separation, lyrics, vocals
  18:     """
  19:     def __init__(self, config):
  20:         self.config = config
  21:         self.metadata_dir = config['paths']['metadata']
  22: 
  23:         # Sub-analyzers
  24:         self.audio_analyzer = AudioAnalyzer(config)
  25:         self.phrase_detector = PhraseDetector(config)
  26:         self.melody_detector = MelodyDetector(config)
  27:         self.entry_finder = EntryPointFinder(config)
  28:         self.vocal_analyzer = VocalAnalyzer(config)
  29:         self.stem_separator = StemSeparator(config)
  30:         self.lyrics_fetcher = LyricsFetcher(config)
  31: 
  32:         self.analysis_queue = []
  33:         self.is_processing = False
  34: 
  35:     def analyze_song_full(self, filepath, song_id, title=''):
  36:         """
  37:         Run complete analysis pipeline on one song
  38:         Returns complete analysis dict
  39:         """
  40:         print(f"\n   🔬 Full analysis: {title or song_id}")
  41: 
  42:         result = {}
  43: 
  44:         # Step 1: Core audio analysis
  45:         try:
  46:             audio_analysis = self.audio_analyzer.analyze_track(
  47:                 filepath, song_id
  48:             )
  49:             audio_analysis['title'] = title
  50:             result.update(audio_analysis)
  51:             print(f"      ✅ Audio: BPM={audio_analysis.get('bpm', 0):.1f} "
  52:                   f"Key={audio_analysis.get('camelot', 'N/A')}")
  53:         except Exception as e:
  54:             print(f"      ❌ Audio analysis failed: {e}")
  55:             result['song_id'] = song_id
  56:             result['title'] = title
  57: 
  58:         # Step 2: Phrase detection
  59:         try:
  60:             phrases = self.phrase_detector.detect_phrases(
  61:                 filepath, song_id
  62:             )
  63:             result['phrases'] = phrases
  64:             total_bars = phrases.get('total_bars', 0)
  65:             print(f"      ✅ Phrases: {total_bars} bars detected")
  66:         except Exception as e:
  67:             print(f"      ❌ Phrase detection failed: {e}")
  68:             result['phrases'] = {}
  69: 
  70:         # Step 3: Melody detection
  71:         try:
  72:             melody = self.melody_detector.detect(filepath, song_id)
  73:             result['melody'] = melody
  74:             note_count = len(melody.get('raw_notes', []))
  75:             print(f"      ✅ Melody: {note_count} notes detected")
  76:         except Exception as e:
  77:             print(f"      ❌ Melody detection failed: {e}")
  78:             result['melody'] = {}
  79: 
  80:         # Step 4: Entry point analysis
  81:         try:
  82:             entries = self.entry_finder.find_entry_points(
  83:                 filepath, result, song_id
  84:             )
  85:             result['entry_points'] = entries
  86:             best = entries.get('best_entry', {})
  87:             print(f"      ✅ Entry: best at "
  88:                   f"{best.get('time', 0):.1f}s "
  89:                   f"(score={best.get('score', 0):.2f})")
  90:         except Exception as e:
  91:             print(f"      ❌ Entry point failed: {e}")
  92:             result['entry_points'] = {}
  93: 
  94:         # Step 5: Stem separation
  95:         try:
  96:             stems = self.stem_separator.separate(filepath, song_id)
  97:             result['stems'] = stems
  98:             available = [k for k, v in stems.items() if v]
  99:             print(f"      ✅ Stems: {available}")
 100:         except Exception as e:
 101:             print(f"      ❌ Stem separation failed: {e}")
 102:             result['stems'] = {}
 103: 
 104:         # Step 6: Lyrics fetching
 105:         try:
 106:             vocals_path = result.get('stems', {}).get('vocals')
 107:             lyrics = self.lyrics_fetcher.fetch(
 108:                 title, song_id, vocals_path
 109:             )
 110:             result['lyrics'] = lyrics
 111:             if lyrics:
 112:                 lang = lyrics.get('language', 'unknown')
 113:                 word_count = len(lyrics.get('timed_words', []))
 114:                 print(f"      ✅ Lyrics: {lang}, {word_count} words")
 115:             else:
 116:                 print(f"      ⚠️  No lyrics found")
 117:         except Exception as e:
 118:             print(f"      ❌ Lyrics fetch failed: {e}")
 119:             result['lyrics'] = None
 120: 
 121:         # Step 7: Vocal/phoneme analysis
 122:         try:
 123:             if result.get('lyrics') and result.get('stems', {}).get('vocals'):
 124:                 phonemes = self.vocal_analyzer.analyze(
 125:                     result['stems']['vocals'],
 126:                     result['lyrics'],
 127:                     song_id
 128:                 )
 129:                 result['phonemes'] = phonemes
 130:                 if phonemes:
 131:                     print(f"      ✅ Phonemes: "
 132:                           f"{phonemes.get('word_count', 0)} words indexed")
 133:             else:
 134:                 result['phonemes'] = None
 135:         except Exception as e:
 136:             print(f"      ❌ Vocal analysis failed: {e}")
 137:             result['phonemes'] = None
 138: 
 139:         # Save complete analysis
 140:         self._save_complete_analysis(song_id, result)
 141: 
 142:         print(f"      ✅ Complete analysis saved: {song_id}")
 143:         return result
 144: 
 145:     def analyze_batch(self, songs, downloader, callback=None):
 146:         """
 147:         Analyze a batch of songs
 148:         songs: list of {'id', 'title', 'url'} dicts
 149:         callback: called after each song with (song_id, analysis)
 150:         """
 151:         total = len(songs)
 152:         results = {}
 153: 
 154:         for i, song in enumerate(songs):
 155:             print(f"\n[{i+1}/{total}] {song['title'][:50]}")
 156: 
 157:             try:
 158:                 filepath = downloader.download_song(
 159:                     song['url'], song['id']
 160:                 )
 161:                 analysis = self.analyze_song_full(
 162:                     filepath, song['id'], song['title']
 163:                 )
 164:                 results[song['id']] = analysis
 165: 
 166:                 if callback:
 167:                     callback(song['id'], analysis)
 168: 
 169:                 # Delete main audio after analysis
 170:                 downloader.delete_audio(song['id'])
 171: 
 172:             except Exception as e:
 173:                 print(f"   ❌ Failed: {e}")
 174:                 continue
 175: 
 176:         return results
 177: 
 178:     def analyze_async(self, filepath, song_id, title,
 179:                       on_complete=None):
 180:         """
 181:         Analyze a song in background thread
 182:         Used for pre-analyzing next song while current plays
 183:         """
 184:         def _run():
 185:             analysis = self.analyze_song_full(filepath, song_id, title)
 186:             if on_complete:
 187:                 on_complete(song_id, analysis)
 188: 
 189:         thread = threading.Thread(target=_run, daemon=True)
 190:         thread.start()
 191:         return thread
 192: 
 193:     def is_analyzed(self, song_id):
 194:         """Check if a song has been fully analyzed"""
 195:         meta_path = os.path.join(
 196:             self.metadata_dir, f"{song_id}.json"
 197:         )
 198:         return os.path.exists(meta_path)
 199: 
 200:     def load_analysis(self, song_id):
 201:         """Load existing analysis from cache"""
 202:         meta_path = os.path.join(
 203:             self.metadata_dir, f"{song_id}.json"
 204:         )
 205:         if os.path.exists(meta_path):
 206:             with open(meta_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
 207:                 return json.load(f)
 208:         return None
 209: 
 210:     def _save_complete_analysis(self, song_id, analysis):
 211:         """Save complete analysis to disk"""
 212:         from utils.json_utils import make_serializable
 213:         meta_path = os.path.join(
 214:             self.metadata_dir, f"{song_id}.json"
 215:         )
 216:         # Convert any non-serializable types
 217:         clean = make_serializable(analysis)
 218:         with open(meta_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
 219:             json.dump(clean, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

FILE: ai_brain\agents\quality_agent.py
================================================================================
   1: import numpy as np
   2: import librosa
   3: import os
   4: 
   5: class QualityAgent:
   6:     """
   7:     Pre-flight quality check before executing transition
   8:     Renders transition silently and scores it
   9:     """
  10:     def __init__(self, config):
  11:         self.config = config
  12:         self.threshold = config['transitions']['quality_threshold']
  13: 
  14:     def check(self, current_analysis, next_analysis,
  15:               technique, params):
  16:         """
  17:         Score how good this transition will sound
  18:         Returns score 0.0 - 1.0
  19:         """
  20:         score = 1.0
  21:         penalties = []
  22: 
  23:         # ---- BPM Check ----
  24:         bpm_diff = abs(
  25:             current_analysis.get('bpm', 120) -
  26:             next_analysis.get('bpm', 120)
  27:         )
  28: 
  29:         if technique == 'beatmatch_crossfade':
  30:             if bpm_diff > 10:
  31:                 penalties.append(('bpm_mismatch', 0.3))
  32:             elif bpm_diff > 5:
  33:                 penalties.append(('bpm_slight', 0.1))
  34: 
  35:         # ---- Key Check ----
  36:         if technique in ['beatmatch_crossfade', 'tone_play',
  37:                          'filter_sweep']:
  38:             camelot_a = current_analysis.get('camelot', '')
  39:             camelot_b = next_analysis.get('camelot', '')
  40: 
  41:             if camelot_a and camelot_b:
  42:                 if camelot_a == camelot_b:
  43:                     pass  # Perfect
  44:                 elif camelot_a[:-1] == camelot_b[:-1]:
  45:                     penalties.append(('key_slight', 0.05))
  46:                 else:
  47:                     penalties.append(('key_mismatch', 0.2))
  48: 
  49:         # ---- Energy Check ----
  50:         energy_diff = abs(
  51:             current_analysis.get('energy_mean', 0) -
  52:             next_analysis.get('energy_mean', 0)
  53:         )
  54:         if energy_diff > 0.1:
  55:             penalties.append(('energy_mismatch', 0.15))
  56: 
  57:         # ---- Technique-specific checks ----
  58:         if technique == 'wordplay':
  59:             if not params.get('word_clip_a'):
  60:                 penalties.append(('no_word_clip', 0.5))
  61: 
  62:         if technique == 'tone_play':
  63:             if not params.get('melody_notes'):
  64:                 penalties.append(('no_melody', 0.4))
  65: 
  66:         # ---- Apply penalties ----
  67:         for reason, penalty in penalties:
  68:             score -= penalty
  69: 
  70:         score = max(0.0, min(1.0, score))
  71: 
  72:         if penalties:
  73:             print(f"   Quality issues: {[p[0] for p in penalties]}")
  74:         print(f"   Quality score: {score:.2f}")
  75: 
  76:         return score

FILE: ai_brain\agents\research_agent.py
================================================================================
   1: import os
   2: import json
   3: import time
   4: try:
   5:     from search_web import search_web
   6:     from read_url_content import read_url_content
   7: except:
   8:     # Fallback for local run
   9:     def search_web(q): return []
  10:     def read_url_content(u): return ""
  11: 
  12: class ResearchAgent:
  13:     """
  14:     Agent that researches new DJ techniques on the web
  15:     and dreams of novel ones by mutating existing ones.
  16:     """
  17:     def __init__(self, config):

  52:     def _dream_of_novel_techniques(self):
  53:         """
  54:         Invent new techniques by mutating/combining existing ones.
  55:         """
  56:         existing = ["spinback", "reverb_wash", "echo_out", "filter_sweep", "loop_roll"]
  57:         novel = []
  58:         
  59:         # Combination: "Echo-Spin" or "Reverb-Roll"
  60:         for _ in range(5):
  61:             t1 = random.choice(existing)
  62:             t2 = random.choice(existing)
  63:             if t1 != t2:
  64:                 name = f"novel_{t1}_{t2}_mutation"
  65:                 novel.append({
  66:                     'name': name,
  67:                     'type': 'innovation',
  68:                     'mutation_parents': [t1, t2],
  69:                     'description': f"A hybrid transition combining {t1} and {t2} with randomized parameters."
  70:                 })
  71:         return novel

================================================================================
FILE: ai_brain\agents\selector_agent.py
================================================================================
   1: import json
   2: import random
   3: import numpy as np
   4: from analysis.compatibility_scorer import CompatibilityScorer
   5: 
   6: class SelectorAgent:
   7:     """
   8:     Decides which song plays next
   9:     Considers: compatibility, energy flow, 
  10:     language bias, genre variety, history
  11:     """
  12:     def __init__(self, config):
  13:         self.config = config
  14:         self.scorer = CompatibilityScorer(config)
  15:         self.play_history = []
  16:         self.max_history = 50
  17: 
  18:     def pick_first_song(self, metadata_cache):
  19:         """Pick a good opening song safely"""
  20:         if not metadata_cache:
  21:             print("⚠️ Cache empty! Cannot pick first song.")
  22:             return None
  23:             
  24:         # FIXED: Use cache keys directly instead of guessing dictionary keys!
  25:         songs = [(sid, data) for sid, data in metadata_cache.items()]
  26: 
  27:         # Sort by energy, pick from middle third
  28:         songs.sort(key=lambda x: x[1].get('energy_mean', 0))
  29:         middle = songs[len(songs)//3: 2*len(songs)//3]
  30: 
  31:         if middle:
  32:             chosen_id = random.choice(middle)[0]
  33:         else:
  34:             chosen_id = songs[0][0]
  35:             
  36:         self.play_history.append(chosen_id)
  37:         return chosen_id
  38: 
  39:     def pick_next_song(self, current_analysis, metadata_cache,
  40:                        exclude=None):
  41:         """
  42:         Pick best next song based on multiple factors
  43:         Returns (song_id, compatibility_dict)
  44:         """
  45:         exclude = exclude or []
  46:         exclude.extend(self.play_history[-5:])  # Avoid recent songs
  47: 
  48:         candidates = []
  49:         
  50:         # FIXED: Safely get current ID (main.py uses 'id', not 'song_id')
  51:         cur_id = current_analysis.get('id', current_analysis.get('song_id', None))
  52: 
  53:         for song_id, analysis in metadata_cache.items():
  54:             if song_id in exclude:
  55:                 continue
  56:             if song_id == cur_id:
  57:                 continue
  58: 
  59:             # Score compatibility
  60:             try:
  61:                 compat = self.scorer.score(current_analysis, analysis)
  62:             except Exception as e:
  63:                 print(f"⚠️ Compatibility scoring failed for {song_id}: {e}")
  64:                 compat = {'score': 50, 'reasons': ['scoring failed']}
  65: 
  66:             # Apply language bias (prefer same language)
  67:             cur_lang = current_analysis.get('lyrics', {})
  68:             nxt_lang = analysis.get('lyrics', {})
  69:             if cur_lang and nxt_lang:
  70:                 cur_l = cur_lang.get('language', '')
  71:                 nxt_l = nxt_lang.get('language', '')
  72:                 if cur_l == nxt_l and cur_l != 'unknown':
  73:                     # FIXED: Safe config fallback
  74:                     bias = self.config.get('transitions', {}).get('same_language_bias', 0.3)
  75:                     compat['score'] += (bias * 100)
  76: 
  77:             # Penalize if played recently
  78:             if song_id in self.play_history:
  79:                 recency = self.play_history[::-1].index(song_id)
  80:                 penalty = max(0, 20 - recency * 2)
  81:                 compat['score'] -= penalty
  82: 
  83:             candidates.append((song_id, compat))
  84: 
  85:         if not candidates:
  86:             # Fallback: pick random not recently played
  87:             available = [
  88:                 sid for sid in metadata_cache.keys()
  89:                 if sid not in self.play_history[-3:] and sid != cur_id
  90:             ]
  91:             if available:
  92:                 chosen_id = random.choice(available)
  93:                 return chosen_id, {'score': 50, 'recommended_transition':
  94:                                    'cut_transition', 'reasons': ['random fallback']}
  95:             elif metadata_cache:
  96:                 # Extreme fallback - just grab anything!
  97:                 chosen_id = list(metadata_cache.keys())[0]
  98:                 return chosen_id, {'score': 50, 'reasons': ['extreme fallback']}
  99:             else:
 100:                 return None, None
 101: 
 102:         # Sort by score
 103:         candidates.sort(key=lambda x: x[1]['score'], reverse=True)
 104: 
 105:         # Add some randomness - pick from top 5
 106:         top_candidates = candidates[:5]
 107:         
 108:         # FIXED: Ensure weights are never negative!
 109:         weights = [max(0.1, c[1]['score']) for c in top_candidates]
 110:         total = sum(weights)
 111:         if total > 0:
 112:             weights = [w/total for w in weights]
 113:         else:
 114:             weights = [1/len(top_candidates)] * len(top_candidates)
 115: 
 116:         chosen = random.choices(top_candidates, weights=weights, k=1)[0]
 117: 
 118:         # Update history
 119:         self.play_history.append(chosen[0])
 120:         if len(self.play_history) > self.max_history:
 121:             self.play_history.pop(0)
 122: 
 123:         return chosen[0], chosen[1]

   1: import os
   2: import json
   3: import time
   4: import subprocess
   5: import requests
   6: from datetime import datetime
   7: 
   8: class SelfImproveAgent:
   9:     """
  10:     Periodically:
  11:     1. Scrapes new DJ tutorial content
  12:     2. Extracts new techniques
  13:     3. Writes/updates code
  14:     4. Tests in sandbox
  15:     5. Deploys if quality improves
  16:     """
  17:     def __init__(self, config):
  18:         self.config = config
  19:         self.improvements_log = "data/logs/improvements.json"
  20:         self.sandbox_dir = "data/sandbox"
  21:         os.makedirs(self.sandbox_dir, exist_ok=True)
  22:         os.makedirs("data/logs", exist_ok=True)
  23: 
  24:         # Use local LLM or OpenAI
  25:         self.use_openai = bool(config['ai'].get('openai_api_key'))
  26:         self.openai_key = config['ai'].get('openai_api_key', '')
  27: 
  28:     def run_improvement_cycle(self):
  29:         """Main improvement cycle - runs weekly"""
  30:         print(f"\n🤖 SELF-IMPROVEMENT CYCLE - {datetime.now()}")
  31:         print("=" * 50)
  32: 
  33:         # Step 1: Scrape new tutorials
  34:         new_techniques = self._scrape_new_tutorials()
  35: 
  36:         # Step 2: Extract technique knowledge
  37:         if new_techniques:
  38:             knowledge = self._extract_knowledge(new_techniques)
  39: 
  40:             # Step 3: Generate code improvements
  41:             if knowledge:
  42:                 new_code = self._generate_improvements(knowledge)
  43: 
  44:                 # Step 4: Test in sandbox
  45:                 if new_code and self._test_in_sandbox(new_code):
  46:                     # Step 5: Deploy
  47:                     self._deploy_improvements(new_code)
  48:                     self._log_improvement(knowledge, new_code)
  49: 
  50:         print("✅ Improvement cycle complete")
  51: 
  52:     def _scrape_new_tutorials(self):
  53:         """Scrape tutorial channels for new content"""
  54:         import yt_dlp
  55: 
  56:         channels = self.config['youtube_channels']['tutorial_sources']
  57:         new_videos = []
  58: 
  59:         # Load previously seen videos
  60:         seen_path = "data/logs/seen_tutorials.json"
  61:         seen_ids = set()
  62:         if os.path.exists(seen_path):
  63:             with open(seen_path, 'r') as f:
  64:                 seen_ids = set(json.load(f))
  65: 
  66:         for channel_url in channels:
  67:             try:
  68:                 ydl_opts = {
  69:                     'quiet': True,
  70:                     'extract_flat': True,
  71:                     'playlistend': 10,  # Check last 10 videos
  72:                 }
  73:                 with yt_dlp.YoutubeDL(ydl_opts) as ydl:
  74:                     info = ydl.extract_info(channel_url, download=False)
  75:                     entries = info.get('entries', [])
  76: 
  77:                     for entry in entries:
  78:                         vid_id = entry.get('id')
  79:                         if vid_id and vid_id not in seen_ids:
  80:                             new_videos.append({
  81:                                 'id': vid_id,
  82:                                 'title': entry.get('title'),
  83:                                 'url': f"https://youtube.com/watch?v={vid_id}",
  84:                                 'channel': channel_url
  85:                             })
  86:                             seen_ids.add(vid_id)
  87: 
  88:             except Exception as e:
  89:                 print(f"❌ Scrape error for {channel_url}: {e}")
  90: 
  91:         # Save updated seen list
  92:         with open(seen_path, 'w') as f:
  93:             json.dump(list(seen_ids), f)
  94: 
  95:         print(f"📺 Found {len(new_videos)} new tutorial videos")
  96:         return new_videos
  97: 
  98:     def _extract_knowledge(self, videos):
  99:         """
 100:         Use Whisper to transcribe tutorials
 101:         Extract technique descriptions
 102:         """
 103:         try:
 104:             import whisper
 105:         except ImportError:
 106:             whisper = None
 107: 
 108: 
 109:         model = whisper.load_model("base")
 110:         knowledge_items = []
 111: 
 112:         for video in videos[:3]:  # Process max 3 at a time
 113:             try:
 114:                 print(f"📝 Transcribing: {video['title']}")
 115: 
 116:                 # Download audio only
 117:                 import yt_dlp
 118:                 audio_path = f"data/sandbox/tutorial_{video['id']}.mp3"
 119: 
 120:                 ydl_opts = {
 121:                     'format': 'bestaudio/best',
 122:                     'outtmpl': audio_path.replace('.mp3', '.%(ext)s'),
 123:                     'postprocessors': [{
 124:                         'key': 'FFmpegExtractAudio',
 125:                         'preferredcodec': 'mp3',
 126:                         'preferredquality': '128',
 127:                     }],
 128:                     'quiet': True,
 129:                 }
 130: 
 131:                 with yt_dlp.YoutubeDL(ydl_opts) as ydl:
 132:                     ydl.download([video['url']])
 133: 
 134:                 # Transcribe
 135:                 result = model.transcribe(audio_path)
 136:                 transcript = result['text']
 137: 
 138:                 # Extract technique mentions
 139:                 techniques_found = self._parse_techniques(transcript)
 140: 
 141:                 if techniques_found:
 142:                     knowledge_items.append({
 143:                         'video_id': video['id'],
 144:                         'title': video['title'],
 145:                         'transcript': transcript[:500],
 146:                         'techniques': techniques_found
 147:                     })
 148: 
 149:                 # Cleanup
 150:                 if os.path.exists(audio_path):
 151:                     os.remove(audio_path)
 152: 
 153:             except Exception as e:
 154:                 print(f"❌ Knowledge extraction failed: {e}")
 155: 
 156:         return knowledge_items
 157: 
 158:     def _parse_techniques(self, transcript):
 159:         """Parse transcript for DJ technique mentions"""
 160:         technique_keywords = [
 161:             'crossfade', 'beatmatch', 'filter', 'echo', 'loop',
 162:             'phrase', 'bar', 'key', 'camelot', 'harmonic',
 163:             'spinback', 'scratch', 'reverb', 'transition',
 164:             'drop', 'build', 'breakdown', 'acapella', 'stems',
 165:             'eq', 'high pass', 'low pass', 'sweep', 'roll'
 166:         ]
 167: 
 168:         found = []
 169:         transcript_lower = transcript.lower()
 170: 
 171:         for keyword in technique_keywords:
 172:             if keyword in transcript_lower:
 173:                 # Get context around keyword
 174:                 idx = transcript_lower.find(keyword)
 175:                 context = transcript[max(0, idx-100):idx+200]
 176:                 found.append({
 177:                     'technique': keyword,
 178:                     'context': context
 179:                 })
 180: 
 181:         return found
 182: 
 183:     def _generate_improvements(self, knowledge):
 184:         """
 185:         Use LLM to generate code improvements
 186:         based on extracted knowledge
 187:         """
 188:         if not self.use_openai:
 189:             print("ℹ️ No OpenAI key - skipping code generation")
 190:             print("   Add openai_api_key to config.yaml for self-improvement")
 191:             return None
 192: 
 193:         try:
 194:             import openai
 195:             client = openai.OpenAI(api_key=self.openai_key)
 196: 
 197:             knowledge_summary = json.dumps(knowledge, indent=2)[:2000]
 198: 
 199:             prompt = f"""
 200: You are improving a Python DJ application.
 201: New techniques learned from DJ tutorials:
 202: 
 203: {knowledge_summary}
 204: 
 205: Current transition techniques in the app:
 206: beatmatch_crossfade, echo_out, filter_sweep, loop_roll,
 207: reverb_wash, spinback, cut_transition, tempo_ramp,
 208: white_noise_sweep, vinyl_scratch_flourish, tone_play, wordplay
 209: 
 210: Based on the new knowledge, write a Python function that implements
 211: a NEW or IMPROVED transition technique. The function must:
 212: 1. Accept parameters: cur_audio, nxt_audio, sr, params
 213: 2. Return: mixed_audio (numpy array)
 214: 3. Sound good to human ears
 215: 4. Include docstring explaining the technique
 216: 
 217: Only output valid Python code, nothing else.
 218: """
 219:             response = client.chat.completions.create(
 220:                 model="gpt-4o-mini",
 221:                 messages=[{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
 222:                 max_tokens=1000
 223:             )
 224: 
 225:             return response.choices[0].message.content
 226: 
 227:         except Exception as e:
 228:             print(f"❌ Code generation failed: {e}")
 229:             return None
 230: 
 231:     def _test_in_sandbox(self, code):
 232:         """Test generated code safely"""
 233:         sandbox_file = os.path.join(self.sandbox_dir, "test_technique.py")
 234: 
 235:         # Write to sandbox
 236:         with open(sandbox_file, 'w') as f:
 237:             f.write("import numpy as np\n")
 238:             f.write("import librosa\n")
 239:             f.write(code)
 240:             f.write("\n\n# Test with dummy audio\n")
 241:             f.write("y = np.random.randn(44100)\n")
 242:             f.write("print('Syntax OK')\n")
 243: 
 244:         # Run in subprocess with timeout
 245:         try:
 246:             result = subprocess.run(
 247:                 ['python', sandbox_file],
 248:                 timeout=30,
 249:                 capture_output=True,
 250:                 text=True
 251:             )
 252:             if result.returncode == 0:
 253:                 print("✅ Sandbox test passed")
 254:                 return True
 255:             else:
 256:                 print(f"❌ Sandbox test failed: {result.stderr[:200]}")
 257:                 return False
 258:         except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
 259:             print("❌ Sandbox test timed out")
 260:             return False
 261: 
 262:     def _deploy_improvements(self, code):
 263:         """Add new technique to transition engine"""
 264:         deploy_path = "transition_engine/ai_generated_techniques.py"
 265: 
 266:         existing = ""
 267:         if os.path.exists(deploy_path):
 268:             with open(deploy_path, 'r') as f:
 269:                 existing = f.read()
 270: 
 271:         with open(deploy_path, 'w') as f:
 272:             f.write(existing)
 273:             f.write(f"\n\n# Auto-generated: {datetime.now()}\n")
 274:             f.write(code)
 275: 
 276:         print(f"✅ New technique deployed to {deploy_path}")
 277: 
 278:     def _log_improvement(self, knowledge, code):
 279:         """Log what was learned and added"""
 280:         log = []
 281:         if os.path.exists(self.improvements_log):
 282:             with open(self.improvements_log, 'r') as f:
 283:                 log = json.load(f)
 284: 
 285:         log.append({
 286:             'timestamp': str(datetime.now()),
 287:             'knowledge_items': len(knowledge),
 288:             'code_preview': code[:200] if code else None
 289:         })
 290: 
 291:         with open(self.improvements_log, 'w') as f:
 292:             json.dump(log, f, indent=2)

FILE: ai_brain\agents\transition_agent.py
================================================================================
   1: import os
   2: from typing import Dict, Tuple
   3: 
   4: class TransitionAgent:
   5:     def __init__(self, config):
   6:         self.config = config
   7:         self.history = []
   8:         self.tot_worker = None
   9:         
  10:         # Try to load Tree of Thoughts worker safely
  11:         try:
  12:             from ai_brain.local_swarm.local_llm_worker import LocalTreeOfThoughtsWorker
  13:             self.tot_worker = LocalTreeOfThoughtsWorker(model_name="deepseek-r1:8b")
  14:             print("✅ TransitionAgent using Tree of Thoughts!")
  15:         except Exception as e:
  16:             print(f"⚠️ Tree of Thoughts not available: {e}")
  17: 
  18:     def decide_transition(self, current_song: str, next_song: str, cur_ana: Dict, nxt_ana: Dict) -> Tuple[str, Dict]:
  19:         """
  20:         Decide the best transition technique.
  21:         Uses Tree of Thoughts if available and alive, otherwise falls back to fast rules.
  22:         """
  23:         # 1. Prepare rich metadata for the Tree of Thoughts LLM
  24:         track_a = {
  25:             "name": current_song,
  26:             "bpm": cur_ana.get('bpm', 120),
  27:             "key": cur_ana.get('camelot', ''),
  28:             "energy": self._energy_to_string(cur_ana.get('energy_mean', 0.5)),
  29:             "duration": cur_ana.get('duration', 180),
  30:             "phrases": str(cur_ana.get('phrases', []))
  31:         }
  32:         
  33:         track_b = {
  34:             "name": next_song,
  35:             "bpm": nxt_ana.get('bpm', 120),
  36:             "key": nxt_ana.get('camelot', ''),
  37:             "energy": self._energy_to_string(nxt_ana.get('energy_mean', 0.5)),
  38:             "duration": nxt_ana.get('duration', 180),
  39:             "phrases": str(nxt_ana.get('phrases', []))
  40:         }
  41:         
  42:         print("🎧 Checking if Local LLM is awake...")
  43:         
  44:         # 2. Check if brain is alive and execute
  45:         # Using getattr to safely check is_brain_alive just in case worker failed to boot
  46:         if self.tot_worker and getattr(self.tot_worker, 'is_brain_alive', lambda: False)():
  47:             print("🧠 Brain active. Routing to Tree of Thoughts.")
  48:             try:
  49:                 # Ask Ollama for the master plan
  50:                 plan = self.tot_worker.generate_plan(track_a=track_a, track_b=track_b)
  51:                 
  52:                 technique = plan.get('technique', 'crossfade').lower()
  53:                 print(f"🎯 Local Agent selected technique: {technique.upper()}")
  54:                 
  55:                 params = {
  56:                     "duration": 16,
  57:                     "curve": "exponential",
  58:                     "reasoning": plan.get('notes', 'ToT inference complete.'),
  59:                     "phrase_alignment": plan.get('phrase_alignment', '')
  60:                 }
  61:                 return technique, params
  62:                 
  63:             except Exception as e:
  64:                 print(f"⚠️ LangGraph Failed: {e}. Falling back to rules.")
  65:         else:
  66:             print("⚠️ Brain dead (Connection Refused). Falling back to heuristic rules immediately.")
  67:             
  68:         # 3. Rule-based Fallback
  69:         return self._fallback_decide(cur_ana, nxt_ana)
  70: 
  71:     def _energy_to_string(self, energy: float) -> str:
  72:         """Convert energy float to descriptive string"""
  73:         if energy < 0.3:
  74:             return "Low"
  75:         elif energy < 0.6:
  76:             return "Medium"
  77:         elif energy < 0.8:
  78:             return "High"
  79:         else:
  80:             return "Maximum"
  81: 
  82:     def _fallback_decide(self, cur_ana: Dict, nxt_ana: Dict) -> Tuple[str, Dict]:
  83:         """Simple rule-based fallback if LLM is offline or crashes"""
  84:         bpm_diff = abs(cur_ana.get('bpm', 120) - nxt_ana.get('bpm', 120))
  85:         
  86:         if bpm_diff <= 5:
  87:             technique = 'beatmatch_crossfade'
  88:         elif bpm_diff <= 15:
  89:             technique = 'tempo_ramp'
  90:         else:
  91:             technique = 'cut_transition'
  92:             
  93:         return technique, {'duration': 16, 'curve': 'linear'}
  94: 
  95:     def get_params(self, cur_ana: Dict, nxt_ana: Dict, technique: str) -> Dict:
  96:         """Get default parameters for a technique (Used by older scripts)"""
  97:         bpm = cur_ana.get('bpm', 120)
  98:         
  99:         return {
 100:             'crossfade_bars': 8 if bpm < 140 else 4,
 101:             'mashup_bars': 8,
 102:             'swap_bars': 8,
 103:             'duration': 16
 104:         }



================================================================================
FILE: ai_brain\agents\validation_agent.py
================================================================================
   1: import os
   2: import json
   3: import numpy as np
   4: import librosa
   5: 
   6: class ValidationAgent:
   7:     """
   8:     Judges transition quality based on:
   9:     1. Signal analysis (silence, clipping)
  10:     2. User historical feedback
  11:     3. Similarity to 'Gold Standard' transitions (YouTube data)
  12:     """
  13:     def __init__(self, config):
  14:         self.config = config
  15:         self.feedback_file = os.path.join('data', 'logs', 'feedback_weights.json')
  16:         
  17:     def score_transition(self, mix_path, technique, cur_ana, nxt_ana):
  18:         """
  19:         Returns a score from 0.0 to 1.0
  20:         """
  21:         score = 0.5 # Baseline
  22:         
  23:         try:
  24:             y, sr = librosa.load(mix_path, sr=22050, duration=60)
  25:             
  26:             # 1. Check for dead air (silence)
  27:             # If there's more than 2 seconds of silence in a 60s test clip, it's bad.
  28:             non_silent = librosa.effects.trim(y, top_db=30)[0]
  29:             if len(non_silent) < (len(y) * 0.7):
  30:                 print(f"   ⚠️ Validation: Too much silence detected! Scoring down.")
  31:                 score -= 0.3
  32:                 
  33:             # 2. Check Technique Popularity (Based on User Feedback)
  34:             if os.path.exists(self.feedback_file):
  35:                 with open(self.feedback_file, 'r') as f:
  36:                     weights = json.load(f)
  37:                     weight = weights.get(technique, 1.0)
  38:                     # Normalize weight (assuming 1.0 is neutral)
  39:                     score += (weight - 1.0) * 0.2
  40:             
  41:             # 3. Match BPM consistency
  42:             # If it's a 'Beatmatch' but the BPMs are wildly different, penalty.
  43:             if 'beatmatch' in technique:
  44:                 bpm_diff = abs(cur_ana.get('bpm', 120) - nxt_ana.get('bpm', 120))
  45:                 if bpm_diff > 10:
  46:                     score -= 0.2
  47: 
  48:             return max(0.0, min(1.0, score))
  49:             
  50:         except Exception as e:
  51:             print(f"   ❌ Validation Error: {e}")
  52:             return 0.0
  53: 
  54: if __name__ == "__main__":
  55:     from main import load_config
  56:     agent = ValidationAgent(load_config())
  57:     # Test call
  58:     # print(agent.score_transition('data/sandbox/test_mix.wav', 'beatmatch_crossfade', {}, {}))

   1: import os
   2: import json
   3: import numpy as np
   4: from visual_engine.stick_figure_gen import StickFigureGen
   5: from visual_engine.equalizer_viz import EqualizerViz
