   7: from visual_engine.waveform_display import WaveformDisplay
   8: 
   9: class VisualAgent:
  10:     """
  11:     Agent 7: Visual Director
  12:     Decides what to show on screen at any moment
  13:     Coordinates stick figures, equalizer,
  14:     waveforms, and lyric display
  15:     Outputs frames to OBS bridge
  16:     """
  17:     def __init__(self, config):
  18:         self.config = config
  19:         self.width = config['visual']['width']
  20:         self.height = config['visual']['height']
  21:         self.fps = config['visual']['fps']
  22: 
  23:         # Visual engines
  24:         self.stick_gen = StickFigureGen(config)
  25:         self.eq_viz = EqualizerViz(config)
  26:         self.lyric_display = LyricDisplay(config)
  27:         self.waveform_display = WaveformDisplay(config)
  28: 
  29:         # State
  30:         self.current_sentiment = 'neutral'
  31:         self.current_genre = 'Pop/Other'
  32:         self.has_lyrics = False
  33:         self.transition_active = False
  34:         self.transition_technique = ''
  35: 
  36:         # Sentiment keyword mappings
  37:         self.sentiment_keywords = {
  38:             'happy': [
  39:                 'happy', 'joy', 'smile', 'dance', 'party',
  40:                 'celebrate', 'fun', 'good', 'great', 'love',
  41:                 'beautiful', 'amazing', 'wonderful', 'khushi',
  42:                 'pyaar', 'rang', 'zindagi'
  43:             ],
  44:             'sad': [
  45:                 'sad', 'cry', 'tears', 'miss', 'lonely',
  46:                 'broken', 'pain', 'hurt', 'alone', 'sorry',
  47:                 'dard', 'dil', 'judaai', 'aansu'
  48:             ],
  49:             'angry': [
  50:                 'angry', 'fight', 'hate', 'war', 'kill',
  51:                 'mad', 'rage', 'fire', 'burn', 'destroy'
  52:             ],
  53:             'hype': [
  54:                 'hype', 'pump', 'go', 'run', 'fast',
  55:                 'power', 'energy', 'bounce', 'drop', 'bass',
  56:                 'money', 'rich', 'gang', 'lit', 'fire'
  57:             ],
  58:             'love': [
  59:                 'love', 'baby', 'heart', 'forever', 'together',
  60:                 'kiss', 'hold', 'feel', 'need', 'want',
  61:                 'ishq', 'mohabbat', 'dil', 'jaanu', 'saath'
  62:             ]
  63:         }
  64: 
  65:     def analyze_sentiment(self, lyrics_text):
  66:         """
  67:         Analyze lyrics sentiment
  68:         Returns sentiment string
  69:         """
  70:         if not lyrics_text:
  71:             return 'neutral'
  72: 
  73:         text_lower = lyrics_text.lower()
  74:         scores = {sentiment: 0 for sentiment in self.sentiment_keywords}
  75: 
  76:         for sentiment, keywords in self.sentiment_keywords.items():
  77:             for keyword in keywords:
  78:                 if keyword in text_lower:
  79:                     scores[sentiment] += 1
  80: 
  81:         # Return highest scoring sentiment
  82:         max_sentiment = max(scores, key=scores.get)
  83:         if scores[max_sentiment] == 0:
  84:             return 'neutral'
  85:         return max_sentiment
  86: 
  87:     def update_song(self, analysis):
  88:         """
  89:         Called when new song starts playing
  90:         Updates visual state for new song
  91:         """
  92:         self.current_genre = analysis.get('genre_hint', 'Pop/Other')
  93: 
  94:         lyrics = analysis.get('lyrics')
  95:         self.has_lyrics = (
  96:             lyrics is not None and
  97:             bool(lyrics.get('text', '').strip())
  98:         )
  99: 
 100:         if self.has_lyrics:
 101:             self.current_sentiment = self.analyze_sentiment(
 102:                 lyrics.get('text', '')
 103:             )
 104:         else:
 105:             self.current_sentiment = 'neutral'
 106: 
 107:         print(f"   🎨 Visual: genre={self.current_genre} "
 108:               f"sentiment={self.current_sentiment} "
 109:               f"lyrics={self.has_lyrics}")
 110: 
 111:     def generate_frame(self, audio_chunk, current_time,
 112:                        energy, beat_time, analysis):
 113:         """
 114:         Generate a complete video frame
 115:         Composites all visual layers
 116:         Returns PIL Image
 117:         """
 118:         from PIL import Image
 119: 
 120:         lyrics_data = analysis.get('lyrics')
 121:         timed_words = lyrics_data.get('timed_words', []) if lyrics_data else []
 122: 
 123:         # Base layer: stick figures or equalizer
 124:         if self.has_lyrics and self.current_sentiment != 'neutral':
 125:             frame = self.stick_gen.generate_frame(
 126:                 lyrics_data,
 127:                 beat_time,
 128:                 energy,
 129:                 self.current_sentiment
 130:             )
 131:         else:
 132:             frame = self.eq_viz.generate_frame(
 133:                 audio_chunk,
 134:                 self.current_genre
 135:             )
 136: 
 137:         # Overlay lyrics
 138:         if self.has_lyrics and timed_words:
 139:             from PIL import ImageDraw
 140:             draw = ImageDraw.Draw(frame)
 141:             self.lyric_display.draw_lyrics(
 142:                 draw, timed_words, current_time
 143:             )
 144: 
 145:         # Overlay transition indicator
 146:         if self.transition_active:
 147:             frame = self._draw_transition_overlay(
 148:                 frame, self.transition_technique
 149:             )
 150: 
 151:         return frame
 152: 
 153:     def _draw_transition_overlay(self, frame, technique):
 154:         """Draw transition name overlay"""
 155:         from PIL import ImageDraw
 156:         draw = ImageDraw.Draw(frame)
 157: 
 158:         text = f"▶ {technique.replace('_', ' ').upper()}"
 159: 
 160:         # Draw with glow effect
 161:         for offset in [(2, 2), (-2, -2), (2, -2), (-2, 2)]:
 162:             draw.text(
 163:                 (self.width // 2 - 200 + offset[0],
 164:                  30 + offset[1]),
 165:                 text,
 166:                 fill=(100, 80, 0)
 167:             )
 168: 
 169:         draw.text(
 170:             (self.width // 2 - 200, 30),
 171:             text,
 172:             fill=(255, 220, 50)
 173:         )
 174: 
 175:         return frame
 176: 
 177:     def set_transition(self, technique, active=True):
 178:         """Signal that a transition is happening"""
 179:         self.transition_active = active
 180:         self.transition_technique = technique
 181: 
 182:     def get_background_color(self):
 183:         """Get current background color based on genre"""
 184:         genre_colors = {
 185:             'EDM/Techno':    (5, 0, 20),
 186:             'House/Dance':   (20, 5, 0),
 187:             'Hip-Hop/Rap':   (10, 8, 0),
 188:             'R&B/Soul':      (15, 0, 10),
 189:             'Rock/Metal':    (20, 0, 0),
 190:             'Ambient/Chill': (0, 5, 20),
 191:             'Pop/Other':     (5, 0, 15),
 192:         }
 193:         return genre_colors.get(self.current_genre, (10, 10, 20))



================================================================================
FILE: ai_brain\agents\wordplay_agent.py
================================================================================
   1: import os
   2: import json
   3: import numpy as np
   4: from langdetect import detect
   5: try:
   6:     import pronouncing
   7: except:
   8:     pronouncing = None
   9: from difflib import SequenceMatcher
  10: 
  11: class WordplayAgent:
  12:     def __init__(self, config):
  13:         self.config = config
  14:         self.word_index_dir = config['paths']['word_index']
  15:         self.phoneme_dir = config['paths']['phonemes']
  16:         self.stems_dir = config['paths']['stems']
  17:         self.word_index = {}
  18:         self.same_language_bias = config['transitions'].get(
  19:             'same_language_bias', 0.3
  20:         )
  21:         os.makedirs(self.word_index_dir, exist_ok=True)
  22:         os.makedirs(self.phoneme_dir, exist_ok=True)
  23:         self._load_word_index()
  24: 
  25:     def _load_word_index(self):
  26:         index_path = os.path.join(self.word_index_dir, 'master_index.json')
  27:         if os.path.exists(index_path):
  28:             with open(index_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
  29:                 self.word_index = json.load(f)
  30:             print(f"✅ Loaded word index: {len(self.word_index)} words")
  31: 
  32:     def _save_word_index(self):
  33:         index_path = os.path.join(self.word_index_dir, 'master_index.json')
  34:         with open(index_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
  35:             json.dump(self.word_index, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
  36: 
  37:     def build_word_index(self, metadata_cache):
  38:         """
  39:         Build cross-song word/phoneme index from all songs
  40:         Finds words that appear in multiple songs for wordplay transitions
  41:         """
  42:         print("\n🗂️  Building word index...")
  43:         self.word_index = {}
  44: 
  45:         for song_id, analysis in metadata_cache.items():
  46:             lyrics_data = analysis.get('lyrics')
  47:             if not lyrics_data:
  48:                 continue
  49: 
  50:             timed_words = lyrics_data.get('timed_words', [])
  51:             language = lyrics_data.get('language', 'unknown')
  52: 
  53:             for word_entry in timed_words:
  54:                 word = word_entry['word'].lower().strip()
  55:                 word = ''.join(c for c in word if c.isalpha())
  56: 
  57:                 if len(word) < 3:
  58:                     continue
  59: 
  60:                 # Get phoneme representation
  61:                 phonemes = self._get_phonemes(word, language)
  62: 
  63:                 if word not in self.word_index:
  64:                     self.word_index[word] = []
  65: 
  66:                 # Check if we have the vocal stem clip
  67:                 vocals_stem = os.path.join(
  68:                     self.stems_dir, song_id, 'vocals.wav'
  69:                 )
  70: 
  71:                 entry = {
  72:                     'song_id': song_id,
  73:                     'timestamp': word_entry.get('start', 0),
  74:                     'end_time': word_entry.get('end', 0),
  75:                     'language': language,
  76:                     'phonemes': phonemes,
  77:                     'vocals_stem': vocals_stem if os.path.exists(
  78:                         vocals_stem
  79:                     ) else None
  80:                 }
  81: 
  82:                 self.word_index[word].append(entry)
  83: 
  84:         # Build phoneme similarity index for cross-language matching
  85:         self._build_phoneme_similarity_index()
  86: 
  87:         self._save_word_index()
  88:         print(f"✅ Word index built: {len(self.word_index)} unique words")
  89: 
  90:     def _get_phonemes(self, word, language):
  91:         """Get phoneme representation of a word"""
  92:         # Try English phoneme lookup first
  93:         phones = pronouncing.phones_for_word(word)
  94:         if phones:
  95:             return phones[0]
  96: 
  97:         # For non-English: approximate using character mapping
  98:         # This is a simplified cross-language phoneme approximation
  99:         phoneme_map = {
 100:             'a': 'AA', 'e': 'EH', 'i': 'IY', 'o': 'OW', 'u': 'UW',
 101:             'b': 'B', 'c': 'K', 'd': 'D', 'f': 'F', 'g': 'G',
 102:             'h': 'HH', 'j': 'JH', 'k': 'K', 'l': 'L', 'm': 'M',
 103:             'n': 'N', 'p': 'P', 'q': 'K', 'r': 'R', 's': 'S',
 104:             't': 'T', 'v': 'V', 'w': 'W', 'x': 'K S', 'y': 'Y',
 105:             'z': 'Z'
 106:         }
 107:         return ' '.join(phoneme_map.get(c, c.upper()) for c in word.lower())
 108: 
 109:     def _build_phoneme_similarity_index(self):
 110:         """
 111:         Find phonetically similar words across languages
 112:         e.g. 'daddy' (English) ≈ 'dadi' (Hindi)
 113:         """
 114:         phoneme_index_path = os.path.join(
 115:             self.phoneme_dir, 'similarity_index.json'
 116:         )
 117: 
 118:         similarity_pairs = []
 119:         words = list(self.word_index.keys())
 120: 
 121:         print("🔤 Computing phoneme similarities...")
 122:         for i, word_a in enumerate(words):
 123:             entries_a = self.word_index[word_a]
 124:             if not entries_a:
 125:                 continue
 126: 
 127:             phoneme_a = entries_a[0].get('phonemes', '')
 128: 
 129:             for word_b in words[i+1:]:
 130:                 entries_b = self.word_index[word_b]
 131:                 if not entries_b:
 132:                     continue
 133: 
 134:                 phoneme_b = entries_b[0].get('phonemes', '')
 135: 
 136:                 # Skip if same word
 137:                 if word_a == word_b:
 138:                     continue
 139: 
 140:                 # Calculate phoneme similarity
 141:                 sim = self._phoneme_similarity(phoneme_a, phoneme_b)
 142: 
 143:                 if sim > 0.75:
 144:                     similarity_pairs.append({
 145:                         'word_a': word_a,
 146:                         'word_b': word_b,
 147:                         'similarity': sim,
 148:                         'phoneme_a': phoneme_a,
 149:                         'phoneme_b': phoneme_b
 150:                     })
 151: 
 152:         with open(phoneme_index_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
 153:             json.dump(similarity_pairs, f, indent=2)
 154: 
 155:         print(f"✅ Found {len(similarity_pairs)} phoneme-similar word pairs")
 156: 
 157:     def _phoneme_similarity(self, phoneme_a, phoneme_b):
 158:         """Calculate similarity between two phoneme strings"""
 159:         return SequenceMatcher(None, phoneme_a, phoneme_b).ratio()
 160: 
 161:     def find_connection(self, current_analysis, next_analysis):
 162:         """
 163:         Find wordplay connection between two songs
 164:         Returns best word match or None
 165:         """
 166:         cur_id = current_analysis['song_id']
 167:         nxt_id = next_analysis['song_id']
 168: 
 169:         cur_language = current_analysis.get('lyrics', {}).get(
 170:             'language', 'unknown'
 171:         ) if current_analysis.get('lyrics') else 'unknown'
 172: 
 173:         nxt_language = next_analysis.get('lyrics', {}).get(
 174:             'language', 'unknown'
 175:         ) if next_analysis.get('lyrics') else 'unknown'
 176: 
 177:         best_match = None
 178:         best_score = 0
 179: 
 180:         # Search word index for words in both songs
 181:         for word, entries in self.word_index.items():
 182:             cur_entries = [e for e in entries if e['song_id'] == cur_id]
 183:             nxt_entries = [e for e in entries if e['song_id'] == nxt_id]
 184: 
 185:             if cur_entries and nxt_entries:
 186:                 # Exact word match found!
 187:                 score = 1.0
 188: 
 189:                 # Boost score for same language
 190:                 if cur_language == nxt_language:
 191:                     score += self.same_language_bias
 192: 
 193:                 if score > best_score:
 194:                     best_score = score
 195:                     best_match = {
 196:                         'type': 'exact',
 197:                         'word': word,
 198:                         'score': score,
 199:                         'cur_entry': cur_entries[-1],  # Use last occurrence
 200:                         'nxt_entry': nxt_entries[0],   # Use first occurrence
 201:                         'transition_time': cur_entries[-1]['timestamp'],
 202:                         'word_time_b': nxt_entries[0]['timestamp'],
 203:                         'word_clip_a': self._extract_word_clip(
 204:                             cur_entries[-1]
 205:                         ),
 206:                         'word_repeats': 2,
 207:                         'languages': f"{cur_language} → {nxt_language}"
 208:                     }
 209: 
 210:         # If no exact match, try phoneme similarity
 211:         if not best_match:
 212:             best_match = self._find_phoneme_match(
 213:                 cur_id, nxt_id, cur_language, nxt_language
 214:             )
 215: 
 216:         return best_match
 217: 
 218:     def _find_phoneme_match(self, cur_id, nxt_id, cur_lang, nxt_lang):
 219:         """Find phonetically similar words across songs"""
 220:         phoneme_index_path = os.path.join(
 221:             self.phoneme_dir, 'similarity_index.json'
 222:         )
 223: 
 224:         if not os.path.exists(phoneme_index_path):
 225:             return None
 226: 
 227:         with open(phoneme_index_path, 'r') as f:
 228:             similarity_pairs = json.load(f)
 229: 
 230:         best_match = None
 231:         best_score = 0
 232: 
 233:         for pair in similarity_pairs:
 234:             word_a = pair['word_a']
 235:             word_b = pair['word_b']
 236:             sim = pair['similarity']
 237: 
 238:             # Check if word_a is in current song and word_b in next song
 239:             entries_a_cur = [
 240:                 e for e in self.word_index.get(word_a, [])
 241:                 if e['song_id'] == cur_id
 242:             ]
 243:             entries_b_nxt = [
 244:                 e for e in self.word_index.get(word_b, [])
 245:                 if e['song_id'] == nxt_id
 246:             ]
 247: 
 248:             # Also check reverse
 249:             entries_b_cur = [
 250:                 e for e in self.word_index.get(word_b, [])
 251:                 if e['song_id'] == cur_id
 252:             ]
 253:             entries_a_nxt = [
 254:                 e for e in self.word_index.get(word_a, [])
 255:                 if e['song_id'] == nxt_id
 256:             ]
 257: 
 258:             match_found = False
 259:             cur_entry = None
 260:             nxt_entry = None
 261:             matched_words = (word_a, word_b)
 262: 
 263:             if entries_a_cur and entries_b_nxt:
 264:                 cur_entry = entries_a_cur[-1]
 265:                 nxt_entry = entries_b_nxt[0]
 266:                 match_found = True
 267:             elif entries_b_cur and entries_a_nxt:
 268:                 cur_entry = entries_b_cur[-1]
 269:                 nxt_entry = entries_a_nxt[0]
 270:                 matched_words = (word_b, word_a)
 271:                 match_found = True
 272: 
 273:             if match_found:
 274:                 score = sim
 275:                 if cur_lang == nxt_lang:
 276:                     score += self.same_language_bias
 277: 
 278:                 if score > best_score:
 279:                     best_score = score
 280:                     best_match = {
 281:                         'type': 'phoneme',
 282:                         'word_a': matched_words[0],
 283:                         'word_b': matched_words[1],
 284:                         'score': score,
 285:                         'similarity': sim,
 286:                         'cur_entry': cur_entry,
 287:                         'nxt_entry': nxt_entry,
 288:                         'transition_time': cur_entry['timestamp'],
 289:                         'word_time_b': nxt_entry['timestamp'],
 290:                         'word_clip_a': self._extract_word_clip(cur_entry),
 291:                         'word_repeats': 2,
 292:                         'languages': f"{cur_lang} → {nxt_lang}"
 293:                     }
 294: 
 295:         return best_match if best_score > 0.75 else None
 296: 
 297:     def _extract_word_clip(self, word_entry):
 298:         """
 299:         Extract just the word audio from vocals stem
 300:         Returns path to clipped audio file
 301:         """
 302:         import librosa
 303:         import soundfile as sf
 304: 
 305:         vocals_path = word_entry.get('vocals_stem')
 306:         if not vocals_path or not os.path.exists(vocals_path):
 307:             return None
 308: 
 309:         start = word_entry.get('timestamp', 0)
 310:         end = word_entry.get('end_time', start + 0.5)
 311: 
 312:         # Add small padding
 313:         start = max(0, start - 0.05)
 314:         end = end + 0.05
 315: 
 316:         clip_path = os.path.join(
 317:             self.phoneme_dir,
 318:             f"{word_entry['song_id']}_{word_entry['word'] if 'word' in word_entry else 'word'}_{start:.2f}.wav"
 319:         )
 320: 
 321:         if os.path.exists(clip_path):
 322:             return clip_path
 323: 
 324:         try:
 325:             y, sr = librosa.load(vocals_path, sr=44100,
 326:                                   offset=start, duration=end-start)
 327:             sf.write(clip_path, y, sr)
 328:             return clip_path
 329:         except Exception as e:
 330:             print(f"❌ Word clip extraction failed: {e}")
 331:             return None

  17:

  19:         self.base_path = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))
  20:         
  21:         # FIXED: Removed dead Colab agents, using LangGraph worker
  22:         self.agents = {
  23:             "LLM_WORKER": "local_llm_worker.py",      # LangGraph-based local AI
  24:             "HEALING": "local_healing_agent.py",      # Self-healing monitor
  25:             "SELENIUM": "selenium_agent.py",          # Browser automation (optional)
  26:             "UI_TESTER": "local_ui_agent.py",         # UI testing
  27:             "GIT_SYNC": "local_git_agent.py",         # Git operations
  28:             "APPROVAL": "local_approval_agent.py",    # Human approval workflow
  29:         }
  30:         
  31:         self.processes = {}
  32:         self.is_running = False
  33:     
  34:     def start_agent(self, name, script):
  35:         """Start a single agent"""
  36:         script_path = os.path.join(self.base_path, script)
  37:         
  38:         if not os.path.exists(script_path):
  39:             print(f"⚠️ Agent script not found: {script_path}")
  40:             return None
  41:         
  42:         try:
  43:             process = subprocess.Popen(
  44:                 [sys.executable, script_path],
  45:                 stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
  46:                 stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
  47:                 cwd=os.path.dirname(self.base_path)  # Run from project root
  48:             )
  49:             print(f"✅ Started {name}: PID {process.pid}")
  50:             return process
  51:         except Exception as e:
  52:             print(f"❌ Failed to start {name}: {e}")
  53:             return None
  54:     
  55:     def start_all(self):
  56:         """Start all agents"""
  57:         print("🚀 Antigravity Master starting all agents...")
  58:         self.is_running = True
  59:         
  60:         for name, script in self.agents.items():
  61:             self.processes[name] = self.start_agent(name, script)
  62:         
  63:         # Start monitor thread
  64:         threading.Thread(target=self._monitor_loop, daemon=True).start()
  65:     
  66:     def stop_all(self):
  67:         """Stop all agents"""
  68:         print("🛑 Stopping all agents...")
  69:         self.is_running = False
  70:         
  71:         for name, process in self.processes.items():
  72:             if process and process.poll() is None:
  73:                 process.terminate()
  74:                 print(f"   Stopped {name}")
  75:     
  76:     def _monitor_loop(self):
  77:         """Monitor and restart crashed agents"""
  78:         while self.is_running:
  79:             time.sleep(30)
  80:             
  81:             for name, process in self.processes.items():
  82:                 if process and process.poll() is not None:
  83:                     # Agent crashed, restart it
  84:                     print(f"⚠️ {name} crashed! Restarting...")
  85:                     self.processes[name] = self.start_agent(name, self.agents[name])
  86:     
  87:     def get_status(self):
  88:         """Get status of all agents"""
  89:         status = {}
  90:         for name, process in self.processes.items():
  91:             if process is None:
  92:                 status[name] = "NOT_STARTED"
  93:             elif process.poll() is None:
  94:                 status[name] = "RUNNING"
  95:             else:
  96:                 status[name] = f"STOPPED (code {process.returncode})"
  97:         return status
  98: 
  99: 
 100: if __name__ == "__main__":
 101:     master = AntigravityMasterAgent()
 102:     master.start_all()
 103:     
 104:     try:
 105:         while True:
 106:             time.sleep(60)
 107:             print(f"📊 Agent Status: {master.get_status()}")
 108:     except KeyboardInterrupt:
 109:         master.stop_all()

   1: import os
   2: import time
   3: import yaml
   4: import json
   5: import sys
   6: 
   7: # Configure UTF-8 for Windows 
   8: if sys.platform == 'win32':
   9:     sys.stdout.reconfigure(encoding='utf-8')
  10:     sys.stderr.reconfigure(encoding='utf-8')
  11: 
  12: from analysis.audio_analyzer import AudioAnalyzer
  13: 
  14: class LocalAudioAgent:
  15:     """
  16:     LOCAL AUDIO AGENT - Handles heavy compute audio analysis.
  17:     No LLM/Gemini credits needed.
  18:     """
  19:     def __init__(self):
  20:         with open('config.yaml', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
  21:             self.config = yaml.safe_load(f)
  22:         self.analyzer = AudioAnalyzer(self.config)
  23:         self.cache_dir = self.config['paths']['audio_cache']
  24:         self.meta_dir = 'data/metadata'
  25:         os.makedirs(self.meta_dir, exist_ok=True)
  26: 
  27:     def scan_and_analyze(self):
  28:         print("🎵 [LOCAL AUDIO AGENT] Scanning for new music...")
  29:         while True:
  30:             files = [f for f in os.listdir(self.cache_dir) if f.endswith('.mp3')]
  31:             for f in files:
  32:                 song_id = f.replace('.mp3', '')
  33:                 meta_path = os.path.join(self.meta_dir, f"{song_id}.json")
  34:                 
  35:                 if not os.path.exists(meta_path):
  36:                     print(f"🎸 Analyzing: {f}")
  37:                     try:
  38:                         audio_path = os.path.join(self.cache_dir, f)
  39:                         analysis = self.analyzer.analyze_track(audio_path, song_id)
  40:                         
  41:                         with open(meta_path, 'w') as out:
  42:                             json.dump(analysis, out)
  43:                         print(f"✅ Metadata saved for {song_id}")
  44:                     except Exception as e:
  45:                         print(f"❌ Analysis failed: {e}")
  46:                 
  47:             time.sleep(60) # Scan every minute
  48: 
  49: if __name__ == "__main__":
  50:     agent = LocalAudioAgent()
  51:     agent.scan_and_analyze()

FILE: ai_brain\local_swarm\local_git_agent.py
================================================================================
   1: import os
   2: import time
   3: import subprocess
   4: import requests
   5: import sys
   6: 
   7: # Configure UTF-8 for Windows 
   8: if sys.platform == 'win32':
   9:     sys.stdout.reconfigure(encoding='utf-8')
  10:     sys.stderr.reconfigure(encoding='utf-8')
  11: 
  12: # =================================================================
  13: # 🦖 LOCAL GIT AGENT
  14: # =================================================================
  15: # Automatically pushes code changes to GitHub to save Gemini credits.
  16: # =================================================================
  17: 
  18: UPDATE_INTERVAL = 60 # 1 minute
  19: NTFY_TOPIC = "antigravity_dj_updates"
  20: 
  21: def send_update(msg):
  22:     try:
  23:         requests.post(f"https://ntfy.sh/{NTFY_TOPIC}", data=msg)
  24:     except:
  25:         pass
  26: 
  27: def run_git_loop():
  28:     print("🐙 [LOCAL GIT AGENT] Started. Monitoring for code changes...")
  29:     
  30:     while True:
  31:         try:
  32:             # Check for changes
  33:             status = subprocess.check_output(["git", "status", "--porcelain"])
  34:             
  35:             if status:
  36:                 print("📝 Changes detected! Pushing to GitHub...")
  37:                 subprocess.run(["git", "add", "."], check=True)
  38:                 subprocess.run(["git", "commit", "-m", "🦖 Auto-sync: Innovative logic update from Antigravity"], check=True)
  39:                 subprocess.run(["git", "push", "origin", "master"], check=True)
  40:                 
  41:                 send_update("📦 Code successfully pushed to GitHub! 🦖")
  42:                 print("✅ Push complete.")
  43:             else:
  44:                 print("😴 No code changes. Sleeping.")
  45:                 
  46:         except Exception as e:
  47:             print(f"❌ Git Agent Error: {e}")
  48:             
  49:         time.sleep(UPDATE_INTERVAL)
  50: 
  51: if __name__ == "__main__":
  52:     run_git_loop()

FILE: ai_brain\local_swarm\local_healing_agent.py
================================================================================
   1: import os
   2: import time
   3: import json
   4: import traceback
   5: import subprocess
   6: import sys
   7: 
   8: # Configure UTF-8 for Windows 
   9: if sys.platform == 'win32':
  10:     sys.stdout.reconfigure(encoding='utf-8')
  11:     sys.stderr.reconfigure(encoding='utf-8')
  12: 
  13: from utils.notifier import send_notification
  14: 
  15: class LocalHealingAgent:
  16:     """
  17:     LOCAL HEALING AGENT - Monitors logs and auto-fixes common issues.
  18:     Saves Gemini credits by solving basic crashes without AI intervention.
  19:     """
  20:     def __init__(self):
  21:         self.log_dir = "data/logs"
  22:         self.error_patterns = {
  23:             "FileNotFoundError: [Errno 2] No such file or directory: 'data/": self.fix_missing_dirs,
  24:             "AttributeError: 'DJApp' object has no attribute 'metadata_cache'": self.fix_metadata_cache_duplication,
  25:             "ModuleNotFoundError": self.fix_missing_dependencies
  26:         }
  27:         os.makedirs(self.log_dir, exist_ok=True)
  28: 
  29:     def fix_missing_dirs(self, error_msg):
  30:         print("🔧 [HEALING] Attempting to fix missing directories...")
  31:         subprocess.run([sys.executable, "main.py", "--setup-dirs"], capture_output=True)
  32:         return "Re-ran directory setup."
  33: 
  34:     def fix_metadata_cache_duplication(self, error_msg):
  35:         print("🔧 [HEALING] Detected metadata_cache init error. Verifying main.py structure...")
  36:         # This usually requires a code edit, which I (the primary agent) should have fixed.
  37:         # But if it recurs, we might want to alert the user specifically.
  38:         return "Manual code check required for init structure."
  39: 
  40:     def fix_missing_dependencies(self, error_msg):
  41:         print("🔧 [HEALING] Attempting to install missing dependencies...")
  42:         try:
  43:             module_name = error_msg.split("'")[1]
  44:             subprocess.run([sys.executable, "-m", "pip", "install", module_name], check=True)
  45:             return f"Installed missing module: {module_name}"
  46:         except:
  47:             return "Failed to auto-install dependency."
  48: 
  49:     def monitor_logs(self):
  50:         print("🦖 [LOCAL HEALING AGENT] Monitoring data/logs/ for crashes...")
  51:         last_check = time.time()
  52:         
  53:         while True:
  54:             try:
  55:                 # Check for recent error logs
  56:                 error_log = os.path.join(self.log_dir, "error_log.txt")
  57:                 if os.path.exists(error_log):
  58:                     mtime = os.path.getmtime(error_log)
  59:                     if mtime > last_check:
  60:                         with open(error_log, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
  61:                             lines = f.readlines()
  62:                             if lines:
  63:                                 last_error = lines[-1]
  64:                                 print(f"🚨 [HEALING] Detected new error: {last_error.strip()}")
  65:                                 
  66:                                 # Try to find a match
  67:                                 handled = False
  68:                                 for pattern, fix_fn in self.error_patterns.items():
  69:                                     if pattern in last_error:
  70:                                         result = fix_fn(last_error)
  71:                                         send_notification(f"🩹 HEALING AGENT: Auto-fixed error.\nResult: {result}", topic='dj-agent-parth')
  72:                                         handled = True
  73:                                         break
  74:                                 
  75:                                 if not handled:
  76:                                     send_notification(f"🚨 DJ CRASHED: {last_error[:100]}", topic='dj-agent-parth')
  77:                         
  78:                         last_check = mtime
  79:             except Exception as e:
  80:                 print(f"Healing Agent Internal Error: {e}")
  81:             
  82:             time.sleep(10)
  83: 
  84: if __name__ == "__main__":
  85:     agent = LocalHealingAgent()
  86:     agent.monitor_logs()

FILE: ai_brain\local_swarm\local_llm_worker.py
================================================================================
   1: import os, json, requests
   2: from langchain_ollama import ChatOllama
   3: from langchain_core.messages import HumanMessage
   4: from pydantic import BaseModel, Field
   5: from typing import Dict, List, TypedDict, Optional
   6: from langgraph.graph import StateGraph, END
   7: 
   8: class IdeaGeneration(BaseModel):
   9:     ideas: List[Dict] = Field(description="3 transition ideas")
  10: 
  11: class FinalTransitionPlan(BaseModel):
  12:     technique: str; confidence: float; notes: str
  13: 
  14: # 🎯 NEW: Added mode and target_technique so State know if it is punishing itself
  15: class ToTState(TypedDict):
  16:     track_a_data: Dict; track_b_data: Dict; human_feedback: str; 
  17:     generated_ideas: List; critique_notes: str; final_plan: Dict;
  18:     mode: str; target_technique: Optional[str]
  19: 
  20: class LocalTreeOfThoughtsWorker:
  21:     def __init__(self, model_name="deepseek-r1:8b"):
  22:         self.generator_llm = ChatOllama(model=model_name, temperature=0.7).with_structured_output(IdeaGeneration)
  23:         self.critic_llm = ChatOllama(model=model_name, temperature=0.2)
  24:         self.selector_llm = ChatOllama(model=model_name, temperature=0.1).with_structured_output(FinalTransitionPlan)
  25:         self.workflow = self._build_graph()
  26: 
  27:     def _get_memory(self):
  28:         mem = load_json_safe('data/logs/critic_memory.json', [])[-5:]
  29:         return f"PAST FAILURES AND CRITICISM: {mem}\n"
  30: 
  31:     def _generator_node(self, state):
  32:         # 🎯 NEW: Branch logic! If Remediation, FORCE the new recipe!
  33:         if state.get('mode') == 'REMEDIATION':
  34:             tech = state['target_technique']
  35:             recipe = load_json_safe(f"data/knowledge/{tech.lower()}_recipe.json", {})
  36:             prompt = f"""
  37:             🚨 REMEDIATION MODE: You recently FAILED a {tech} transition!
  38:             Tracks: {state['track_a_data']['title']} -> {state['track_b_data']['title']}
  39:             
  40:             You went to school. Here are the exact steps you just learned to fix it:
  41:             {json.dumps(recipe.get('steps', []), indent=2)}
  42:             
  43:             Generate 3 variations of how to apply THESE SPECIFIC STEPS to these two tracks.
  44:             Do not do anything else. Just follow the newly learned steps.
  45:             """
  46:         else:
  47:             prompt = f"Tracks: {state['track_a_data']['title']} -> {state['track_b_data']['title']}\n{state['human_feedback']}\nSuggest 3 DJ techniques."
  48:             
  49:         state["generated_ideas"] = self.generator_llm.invoke([HumanMessage(content=prompt)]).ideas
  50:         return state
  51: 
  52:     def _critic_node(self, state):
  53:         mode_text = f"Ensure they follow the newly learned {state['target_technique']} recipe exactly." if state.get('mode') == 'REMEDIATION' else ""
  54:         prompt = f"Critique these ideas based on human feedback: {state['generated_ideas']}. {mode_text}"
  55:         state["critique_notes"] = self.critic_llm.invoke([HumanMessage(content=prompt)]).content
  56:         return state
  57: 
  58:     def _selector_node(self, state):
  59:         prompt = f"Pick the best idea based on this critique: {state['critique_notes']}"
  60:         res = self.selector_llm.invoke([HumanMessage(content=prompt)])
  61:         state["final_plan"] = res.model_dump()
  62:         
  63:         # 🎯 NEW: Loud, visible Remediation Monologue
  64:         print(f"\n   ========================================")
  65:         if state.get('mode') == 'REMEDIATION':
  66:             print(f"   🗣️ AI INTERNAL MONOLOGUE (Remediation Report):")
  67:             print(f"   🎯 STATUS: ATTEMPTING FIX FOR {state['target_technique']}")
  68:             print(f"   🧠 LOGIC: 'The previous attempt failed. I ingested tutorial steps.")
  69:             print(f"   The new approach: {res.notes}. Applying now.'")
  70:         else:
  71:             print(f"   🗣️ AI INTERNAL MONOLOGUE:")
  72:             print(f"   🎯 STATUS: NEW EXPLORATION")
  73:             print(f"   🧠 LOGIC: {res.notes}")
  74:         print(f"   ========================================\n")
  75:         
  76:         return state
  77: 
  78:     def _build_graph(self):
  79:         builder = StateGraph(ToTState)
  80:         builder.add_node("gen", self._generator_node); builder.add_node("crit", self._critic_node); builder.add_node("sel", self._selector_node)
  81:         builder.set_entry_point("gen"); builder.add_edge("gen", "crit"); builder.add_edge("crit", "sel"); builder.add_edge("sel", END)
  82:         return builder.compile()
  83: 
  84:     # 🎯 NEW: Updated to accept mode and technique from main engine
  85:     def generate_plan(self, a, b, mode='NORMAL', target_technique=None):
  86:         return self.workflow.invoke({
  87:             "track_a_data": a, 
  88:             "track_b_data": b, 
  89:             "human_feedback": self._get_memory(),
  90:             "mode": mode,
  91:             "target_technique": target_technique
  92:         })["final_plan"]
  93: 
  94: def load_json_safe(fp, default):
  95:     if os.path.exists(fp):
  96:         with open(fp, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: return json.load(f)
  97:     return default

  57:                 else:
  58:                     print("😴 Waiting for Factory Loop to generate mix...")
  59:                 
  60:                 time.sleep(30) # Check every 30s
  61:             except Exception as e:
  62:                 print(f"⚠️ UI Agent Error: {e}")
  63:                 time.sleep(10)
  64: 
  65: if __name__ == "__main__":
  66:     agent = LocalUIAgent()
  67:     agent.start_test_loop()

  13: from selenium import webdriver

  18: from utils.notifier import send_notification
  19: from utils.drive_manager import DriveManager
  20: 
  21: class SeleniumAgent:
  22:     def __init__(self):
  23:         with open('config.yaml', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
  24:             self.config = yaml.safe_load(f)
  25:         
  26:         self.mobile_ui_url = "http://localhost:8080"

  32:

  34:         self.chrome_options.add_argument("--headless") # Run in background
  35:         self.chrome_options.add_argument("--no-sandbox")
  36:         self.chrome_options.add_argument("--disable-dev-shm-usage")
  37:         
  38:         self.driver = None
  39:         self.last_update_time = 0
  40:         self.routine_interval = 15 * 60 # 15 minutes
  41:         self.critical_interval = 60      # 1 minute
  42:         self.last_routine_time = 0
  43:         
  44:     def init_driver(self):
  45:         # FIXED: Close old driver if it exists to stop memory leak 503s!
  46:         if self.driver:
  47:             try:
  48:                 self.driver.quit()
  49:             except:
  50:                 pass
  51:                 
  52:         service = Service(ChromeDriverManager().install())
  53:         self.driver = webdriver.Chrome(service=service, options=self.chrome_options)
  54: 
  55:     def check_mobile_ui(self):
  56:         try:
  57:             self.init_driver()
  58:             self.driver.get(self.mobile_ui_url)
  59:             time.sleep(2)
  60:             
  61:             status_text = "OFFLINE"
  62:             try:
  63:                 outgoing = self.driver.find_element(By.ID, "outgoing-title").text
  64:                 incoming = self.driver.find_element(By.ID, "incoming-title").text
  65:                 status_text = f"RUNNING: {outgoing} -> {incoming}"
  66:             except Exception:
  67:                 status_text = "UI LOADED BUT NO TASK"
  68:                 
  69:             return status_text
  70:         except Exception as e:
  71:             return f"ERROR: {str(e)[:50]}"
  72: 
  73:     def check_fleet(self):
  74:         try:
  75:             dm = DriveManager(self.config)
  76:             results = []
  77:             # FIXED: Use config drive accounts instead of hardcoded 5
  78:             accounts = self.config.get('storage', {}).get('drive_accounts', [])
  79:             for acc_id in accounts:
  80:                 try:
  81:                     service = dm.authenticate(acc_id)
  82:                     in_id = dm.get_folder_id(service, 'COLAB_INPUT')
  83:                     res_in = service.files().list(q=f"'{in_id}' in parents and trashed=false", fields='files(name)').execute()
  84:                     inputs = len(res_in.get('files', []))
  85:                     
  86:                     out_id = dm.get_folder_id(service, 'COLAB_OUTPUT')
  87:                     res_out = service.files().list(q=f"'{out_id}' in parents and trashed=false", fields='files(id, name)').execute()
  88:                     outputs = len(res_out.get('files', []))
  89:                     
  90:                     results.append(f"{acc_id}: {inputs} In / {outputs} Out")
  91:                 except Exception:
  92:                     results.append(f"{acc_id}: ERROR")
  93:             return " | ".join(results) if results else "NO ACCOUNTS CONFIGURED"
  94:         except Exception as e:
  95:             return f"Fleet check failed: {str(e)[:50]}"
  96: 
  97:     def colab_keep_alive(self):
  98:         if not self.colab_links:
  99:             return "No Colab links active."
 100:             
 101:         reports = []
 102:         for url in self.colab_links:
 103:             try:
 104:                 self.init_driver()
 105:                 self.driver.get(url)
 106:                 time.sleep(5)
 107:                 
 108:                 found_action = False
 109:                 try:
 110:                     selectors = [
 111:                         "//colab-connect-button",
 112:                         "//paper-button[@id='connect']",
 113:                         "//*[contains(text(), 'Reconnect')]",
 114:                         "//*[contains(text(), 'Connect')]"
 115:                     ]
 116:                     for s in selectors:
 117:                         elements = self.driver.find_elements(By.XPATH, s)
 118:                         if elements:
 119:                             elements[0].click()
 120:                             found_action = True
 121:                             break
 122:                             
 123:                 except Exception as e:
 124:                     print(f"Colab button error: {e}")
 125: 
 126:                 try:
 127:                     cells = self.driver.find_elements(By.CSS_SELECTOR, "div.run-button-container")
 128:                     for cell in cells:
 129:                         if "running" not in cell.get_attribute("class"):
 130:                             cell.click()
 131:                             reports.append(f"▶️ TRIGGERED CELL on {url[:20]}...")
 132:                             break 
 133:                 except Exception as e:
 134:                     print(f"Colab cell error: {e}")
 135:                     
 136:                 if found_action:
 137:                     reports.append(f"🔗 CLICKED RECONNECT on {url[:20]}...")
 138:                 elif not any("TRIGGERED CELL" in r for r in reports):
 139:                     reports.append(f"✅ Still Connected: {url[:20]}...")
 140:                     
 141:             except Exception as e:
 142:                 reports.append(f"❌ Failed {url[:20]}: {str(e)[:20]}")
 143:                 
 144:         return "\n".join(reports)

 147:         print("🐙 [SELENIUM AGENT] High-frequency monitoring started...")
 148:         while True:
 149:             try:
 150:                 now = time.time()
 151:                 
 152:                 ui_status = self.check_mobile_ui()
 153:                 fleet_status = self.check_fleet()
 154:                 
 155:                 # FIXED: Actually call colab_keep_alive! You forgot it in original!
 156:                 colab_status = self.colab_keep_alive() 
 157:                 
 158:                 actions = []
 159:                 if "ERROR" in ui_status:
 160:                     actions.append("Restart mobile_tester.py!")
 161:                 if "ERROR" in fleet_status:
 162:                     actions.append("Check Google Drive credentials!")
 163:                     
 164:                 if actions:
 165:                     alert = f"🚨 IMMEDIATE ACTION REQUIRED\n\n" + "\n".join([f"- {a}" for a in actions])
 166:                     if now - self.last_update_time > 600:
 167:                         try:
 168:                             send_notification(alert, topic='dj-agent-parth')
 169:                         except:
 170:                             pass
 171:                         self.last_update_time = now
 172:

 175:                     summary += "\n✅ EVERYTHING SMOOTH." if not actions else f"\n🚨 STILL WAITING ON: {', '.join(actions)}"
 176:                     try:
 177:                         send_notification(summary, topic='dj-agent-parth')
 178:                     except:
 179:                         pass
 180:                     self.last_routine_time = now
 181:                     
 182:                 time.sleep(self.critical_interval)
 183:                 
 184:             except Exception as e:
 185:                 print(f"Selenium Agent crash caught: {e}")
 186:                 time.sleep(30) # Prevent tight crash loops
 187: 
 188: if __name__ == "__main__":

================================================================================
FILE: ai_brain\training\auto_labeler.py
================================================================================
   1: import os
   2: import json
   3: import numpy as np
   4: import librosa
   5: from datetime import datetime
   6: 
   7: class AutoLabeler:
   8:     """
   9:     Automatically labels transition points
  10:     in DJ mix videos/audio without tutorials
  11:     Detects WHERE transitions happen and
  12:     tries to classify WHAT technique was used
  13:     """
  14:     def __init__(self, config):
  15:         self.config = config
  16:         self.training_dir = config['paths']['training_data']
  17:         self.sr = config['audio']['sample_rate']
  18:         os.makedirs(self.training_dir, exist_ok=True)
  19: 
  20:     def label_mix(self, filepath, mix_id):
  21:         """
  22:         Auto-label all transitions in a DJ mix
  23:         Returns list of labeled transition examples
  24:         """
  25:         print(f"\n🔍 Auto-labeling: {mix_id}")
  26: 
  27:         y, sr = librosa.load(filepath, sr=self.sr, mono=True)
  28: 
  29:         # Step 1: Find transition points
  30:         transition_points = self._detect_transitions(y, sr)
  31:         print(f"   Found {len(transition_points)} potential transitions")
  32: 
  33:         # Step 2: Classify each transition
  34:         labeled = []
  35:         for tp in transition_points:
  36:             technique = self._classify_transition(y, sr, tp)
  37:             features = self._extract_features_around(y, sr, tp)
  38: 
  39:             labeled.append({
  40:                 'mix_id': mix_id,
  41:                 'timestamp': tp,
  42:                 'technique': technique,
  43:                 'confidence': features.get('confidence', 0.5),
  44:                 'features': features,
  45:                 'source': 'auto_labeled',
  46:                 'labeled_at': str(datetime.now())
  47:             })
  48: 
  49:         # Save
  50:         output_path = os.path.join(
  51:             self.training_dir,
  52:             f"autolabeled_{mix_id}.json"
  53:         )
  54:         with open(output_path, 'w') as f:
  55:             json.dump(labeled, f, indent=2)
  56: 
  57:         print(f"   ✅ Labeled {len(labeled)} transitions")
  58:         return labeled
  59: 
  60:     def _detect_transitions(self, y, sr):
  61:         """
  62:         Detect transition points using:
  63:         - Spectral flux (sudden spectrum changes)
  64:         - Energy changes
  65:         - Onset detection
  66:         """
  67:         hop_length = 512
  68:         transition_points = []
  69: 
  70:         # Spectral flux
  71:         spec = np.abs(librosa.stft(y, hop_length=hop_length))
  72:         flux = np.sum(np.diff(spec, axis=1) ** 2, axis=0)
  73:         flux_times = librosa.frames_to_time(
  74:             np.arange(len(flux)), sr=sr, hop_length=hop_length
  75:         )
  76: 
  77:         # RMS energy
  78:         rms = librosa.feature.rms(y=y, hop_length=hop_length)[0]
  79:         rms_times = librosa.frames_to_time(
  80:             np.arange(len(rms)), sr=sr, hop_length=hop_length
  81:         )
  82: 
  83:         # Find peaks in spectral flux
  84:         from scipy.signal import find_peaks
  85:         flux_normalized = flux / (np.max(flux) + 1e-10)
  86: 
  87:         # Look for significant changes
  88:         peaks, properties = find_peaks(
  89:             flux_normalized,
  90:             height=0.3,
  91:             distance=sr // hop_length * 10  # Min 10 seconds apart
  92:         )
  93: 
  94:         for peak in peaks:
  95:             t = flux_times[peak]
  96: 
  97:             # Skip very beginning and end
  98:             duration = len(y) / sr
  99:             if t < 10 or t > duration - 10:
 100:                 continue
 101: 
 102:             transition_points.append(float(t))
 103: 
 104:         # Also detect energy drops/jumps
 105:         rms_diff = np.abs(np.diff(rms))
 106:         energy_peaks, _ = find_peaks(
 107:             rms_diff / (np.max(rms_diff) + 1e-10),
 108:             height=0.4,
 109:             distance=sr // hop_length * 10
 110:         )
 111: 
 112:         for peak in energy_peaks:
 113:             t = float(rms_times[min(peak, len(rms_times)-1)])
 114:             duration = len(y) / sr
 115:             if t < 10 or t > duration - 10:
 116:                 continue
 117: 
 118:             # Add if not already detected within 5 seconds
 119:             if not any(abs(t - existing) < 5 for existing in transition_points):
 120:                 transition_points.append(t)
 121: 
 122:         transition_points.sort()
 123:         return transition_points
 124: 
 125:     def _classify_transition(self, y, sr, transition_time):
 126:         """
 127:         Classify what technique was used at transition_time
 128:         Returns technique name string
 129:         """
 130:         # Extract audio windows before and after
 131:         window = int(sr * 4)
 132:         t_sample = int(transition_time * sr)
 133: 
 134:         before = y[max(0, t_sample - window):t_sample]
 135:         after = y[t_sample:min(len(y), t_sample + window)]
 136: 
 137:         if len(before) < 100 or len(after) < 100:
 138:             return 'cut_transition'
 139: 
 140:         # Feature extraction
 141:         energy_before = float(np.sqrt(np.mean(before ** 2)))
 142:         energy_after = float(np.sqrt(np.mean(after ** 2)))
 143: 
 144:         # Check for echo pattern (repeating transients)
 145:         has_echo = self._detect_echo_pattern(before)
 146: 
 147:         # Check for filter sweep (spectral centroid change)
 148:         has_filter = self._detect_filter_sweep(before, after, sr)
 149: 
 150:         # Check for reverb tail
 151:         has_reverb = self._detect_reverb_tail(before, sr)
 152: 
 153:         # Check for loop roll (repeating short segments)
 154:         has_loop = self._detect_loop_pattern(before, sr)
 155: 
 156:         # Check for hard cut (abrupt change)
 157:         is_cut = self._detect_hard_cut(before, after)
 158: 
 159:         # Decision logic
 160:         if has_loop:
 161:             return 'loop_roll'
 162:         elif has_echo:
 163:             return 'echo_out'
 164:         elif has_filter:
 165:             return 'filter_sweep'
 166:         elif has_reverb:
 167:             return 'reverb_wash'
 168:         elif is_cut:
 169:             return 'cut_transition'
 170:         elif energy_before > energy_after * 1.5:
 171:             return 'echo_out'
 172:         elif energy_after > energy_before * 1.5:
 173:             return 'filter_sweep'
 174:         else:
 175:             return 'beatmatch_crossfade'
 176: 
 177:     def _detect_echo_pattern(self, audio):
 178:         """Detect echo/delay pattern in audio"""
 179:         if len(audio) < 1000:
 180:             return False
 181:         # Autocorrelation to find repeating patterns
 182:         corr = np.correlate(audio[:4000], audio[:4000], mode='full')
 183:         corr = corr[len(corr)//2:]
 184:         corr = corr / (corr[0] + 1e-10)
 185:         # Look for secondary peaks (echoes)
 186:         from scipy.signal import find_peaks
 187:         peaks, _ = find_peaks(corr[100:2000], height=0.3)
 188:         return len(peaks) > 2
 189: 
 190:     def _detect_filter_sweep(self, before, after, sr):
 191:         """Detect spectral centroid change indicating filter sweep"""
 192:         if len(before) < 100 or len(after) < 100:
 193:             return False
 194:         centroid_before = float(np.mean(
 195:             librosa.feature.spectral_centroid(y=before, sr=sr)
 196:         ))
 197:         centroid_after = float(np.mean(
 198:             librosa.feature.spectral_centroid(y=after, sr=sr)
 199:         ))
 200:         # Large centroid change = filter sweep
 201:         return abs(centroid_after - centroid_before) > 1500
 202: 
 203:     def _detect_reverb_tail(self, audio, sr):
 204:         """Detect reverb tail (long exponential decay)"""
 205:         if len(audio) < sr:
 206:             return False
 207:         rms = librosa.feature.rms(y=audio)[0]
 208:         if len(rms) < 10:
 209:             return False
 210:         # Check if energy decays smoothly (reverb characteristic)
 211:         decay = rms[-len(rms)//3:]
 212:         is_smooth_decay = np.std(np.diff(decay)) < 0.002
 213:         return is_smooth_decay and rms[-1] < rms[0] * 0.3
 214: 
 215:     def _detect_loop_pattern(self, audio, sr):
 216:         """Detect loop roll (repeating short segments)"""
 217:         if len(audio) < sr:
 218:             return False
 219:         # Check for very regular repeating patterns
 220:         short_len = int(sr * 0.25)  # 250ms
 221:         if len(audio) < short_len * 4:
 222:             return False
 223: 
 224:         segment = audio[:short_len]
 225:         next_seg = audio[short_len:short_len * 2]
 226: 
 227:         if len(next_seg) < len(segment):
 228:             return False
 229: 
 230:         correlation = np.corrcoef(
 231:             segment[:len(next_seg)], next_seg
 232:         )[0, 1]
 233:         return correlation > 0.7
 234: 
 235:     def _detect_hard_cut(self, before, after):
 236:         """Detect hard cut transition"""
 237:         if len(before) < 100 or len(after) < 100:
 238:             return True
 239:         energy_before = np.sqrt(np.mean(before[-1000:] ** 2))
 240:         energy_after = np.sqrt(np.mean(after[:1000] ** 2))
 241:         # If energy jumps suddenly = hard cut
 242:         ratio = max(energy_before, energy_after) / (
 243:             min(energy_before, energy_after) + 1e-10
 244:         )
 245:         return ratio > 3.0
 246: 
 247:     def _extract_features_around(self, y, sr, transition_time):
 248:         """Extract audio features around transition point"""
 249:         window = int(sr * 4)
 250:         t_sample = int(transition_time * sr)
 251: 
 252:         before = y[max(0, t_sample - window):t_sample]
 253:         after = y[t_sample:min(len(y), t_sample + window)]
 254: 
 255:         features = {}
 256: 
 257:         if len(before) > 100:
 258:             features['bpm_before'] = float(
 259:                 librosa.beat.beat_track(y=before, sr=sr)[0]
 260:             )
 261:             features['energy_before'] = float(
 262:                 np.sqrt(np.mean(before ** 2))
 263:             )
 264:             features['centroid_before'] = float(
 265:                 np.mean(librosa.feature.spectral_centroid(y=before, sr=sr))
 266:             )
 267: 
 268:         if len(after) > 100:
 269:             features['bpm_after'] = float(
 270:                 librosa.beat.beat_track(y=after, sr=sr)[0]
 271:             )
 272:             features['energy_after'] = float(
 273:                 np.sqrt(np.mean(after ** 2))
 274:             )
 275:             features['centroid_after'] = float(
 276:                 np.mean(librosa.feature.spectral_centroid(y=after, sr=sr))
 277:             )
 278: 
 279:         features['confidence'] = 0.6
 280:         return features

FILE: ai_brain\training\rl_feedback.py
================================================================================
   1: import os
   2: import json
   3: import numpy as np
   4: from datetime import datetime
   5: 
   6: class RLFeedback:
   7:     """
   8:     Reinforcement Learning from user feedback
   9:     
  10:     When a transition plays:
  11:     - User gives thumbs up/down via web UI
  12:     - OR app detects skips (implicit negative feedback)
  13:     - Model updates based on what worked/didn't
  14:     
  15:     Over time the app learns:
  16:     - Which techniques work for which song combinations
  17:     - Which songs flow well together
  18:     - What the user/audience responds to
  19:     - Time-of-day preferences
  20:     - Genre sequence preferences
  21:     """
  22:     def __init__(self, config):
  23:         self.config = config
  24:         self.models_dir = config['paths']['models']
  25:         self.logs_dir = config['paths']['logs']
  26:         self.feedback_file = os.path.join(
  27:             self.logs_dir, 'feedback_log.json'
  28:         )
  29:         self.q_table_file = os.path.join(
  30:             self.models_dir, 'q_table.json'
  31:         )
  32: 
  33:         os.makedirs(self.models_dir, exist_ok=True)
  34:         os.makedirs(self.logs_dir, exist_ok=True)
  35: 
  36:         # Q-table: maps state → action → reward
  37:         # state  = (genre_a, genre_b, bpm_bucket, energy_bucket)
  38:         # action = transition technique
  39:         # reward = user feedback score
  40:         self.q_table = self._load_q_table()
  41: 
  42:         # Feedback history
  43:         self.feedback_log = self._load_feedback_log()
  44: 
  45:         # Learning parameters
  46:         self.learning_rate = 0.1
  47:         self.discount_factor = 0.9
  48:         self.epsilon = 0.15  # Exploration rate (try new things)
  49: 
  50:         # Techniques available
  51:         self.techniques = [
  52:             'beatmatch_crossfade',
  53:             'cut_transition',
  54:             'echo_out',
  55:             'filter_sweep',
  56:             'loop_roll',
  57:             'reverb_wash',
  58:             'spinback',
  59:             'tempo_ramp',
  60:             'white_noise_sweep',
  61:             'vinyl_scratch_flourish',
  62:             'tone_play',
  63:             'wordplay',
  64:             'mashup_short',
  65:             'mashup_extended',
  66:             'acapella_layer',
  67:             'drum_swap',
  68:             'bass_swap',
  69:             'stutter_glitch',
  70:             'half_time_transition',
  71:             'double_time_transition',
  72:         ]
  73: 
  74:     # ============================================================
  75:     # FEEDBACK COLLECTION
  76:     # ============================================================
  77: 
  78:     def record_transition(self, current_analysis, next_analysis,
  79:                           technique, params):
  80:         """
  81:         Record that a transition was played
  82:         Returns transition_id for later feedback
  83:         """
  84:         transition_id = f"{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}_{technique}"
  85: 
  86:         record = {
  87:             'transition_id': transition_id,
  88:             'timestamp': str(datetime.now()),
  89:             'song_a_id': current_analysis.get('song_id', ''),
  90:             'song_a_title': current_analysis.get('title', ''),
  91:             'song_b_id': next_analysis.get('song_id', ''),
  92:             'song_b_title': next_analysis.get('title', ''),
  93:             'technique': technique,
  94:             'bpm_a': current_analysis.get('bpm', 120),
  95:             'bpm_b': next_analysis.get('bpm', 120),
  96:             'genre_a': current_analysis.get('genre_hint', 'Pop/Other'),
  97:             'genre_b': next_analysis.get('genre_hint', 'Pop/Other'),
  98:             'camelot_a': current_analysis.get('camelot', ''),
  99:             'camelot_b': next_analysis.get('camelot', ''),
 100:             'energy_a': current_analysis.get('energy_mean', 0),
 101:             'energy_b': next_analysis.get('energy_mean', 0),
 102:             'feedback': None,  # To be filled in later
 103:             'was_skipped': False,
 104:             'play_duration': 0,
 105:             'state': self._get_state(current_analysis, next_analysis),
 106:         }
 107: 
 108:         self.feedback_log.append(record)
 109:         self._save_feedback_log()
 110: 
 111:         return transition_id
 112: 
 113:     def record_feedback(self, transition_id, feedback_type,
 114:                         play_duration=None):
 115:         """
 116:         Record user feedback for a transition
 117: 
 118:         feedback_type options:
 119:             'thumbs_up'    → +1.0 reward
 120:             'thumbs_down'  → -1.0 reward
 121:             'skip'         → -0.5 reward (implicit negative)
 122:             'replay'       → +0.8 reward (implicit positive)
 123:             'let_play'     → +0.3 reward (neutral positive)
 124:         """
 125:         reward_map = {
 126:             'thumbs_up':   1.0,
 127:             'thumbs_down': -1.0,
 128:             'skip':        -0.5,
 129:             'replay':       0.8,
 130:             'let_play':     0.3,
 131:         }
 132: 
 133:         reward = reward_map.get(feedback_type, 0.0)
 134: 
 135:         # Find and update the record
 136:         for record in self.feedback_log:
 137:             if record['transition_id'] == transition_id:
 138:                 record['feedback'] = feedback_type
 139:                 record['reward'] = reward
 140:                 record['was_skipped'] = (feedback_type == 'skip')
 141:                 if play_duration:
 142:                     record['play_duration'] = play_duration
 143:                 break
 144: 
 145:         self._save_feedback_log()
 146: 
 147:         # Update Q-table
 148:         self._update_q_table(transition_id, reward)
 149: 
 150:         print(f"   📊 Feedback recorded: {feedback_type} "
 151:               f"(reward={reward:+.1f})")
 152: 
 153:     def record_skip(self, transition_id, time_into_song):
 154:         """
 155:         Record that user skipped a song
 156:         Skip within 30 seconds = strong negative signal
 157:         Skip after 2 minutes = weak negative signal
 158:         """
 159:         if time_into_song < 30:
 160:             reward = -0.8
 161:             feedback_type = 'early_skip'
 162:         elif time_into_song < 60:
 163:             reward = -0.4
 164:             feedback_type = 'skip'
 165:         else:
 166:             reward = -0.1
 167:             feedback_type = 'late_skip'
 168: 
 169:         for record in self.feedback_log:
 170:             if record['transition_id'] == transition_id:
 171:                 record['feedback'] = feedback_type
 172:                 record['reward'] = reward
 173:                 record['was_skipped'] = True
 174:                 record['play_duration'] = time_into_song
 175:                 break
 176: 
 177:         self._save_feedback_log()
 178:         self._update_q_table(transition_id, reward)
 179: 
 180:         print(f"   📊 Skip recorded at {time_into_song:.0f}s "
 181:               f"(reward={reward:+.1f})")
 182: 
 183:     # ============================================================
 184:     # Q-LEARNING
 185:     # ============================================================
 186: 
 187:     def _get_state(self, analysis_a, analysis_b):
 188:         """
 189:         Convert song pair into a discrete state
 190:         for Q-table lookup
 191:         """
 192:         # BPM bucket (10 BPM increments)
 193:         bpm_diff = abs(
 194:             analysis_a.get('bpm', 120) - analysis_b.get('bpm', 120)
 195:         )
 196:         if bpm_diff < 5:
 197:             bpm_bucket = 'same'
 198:         elif bpm_diff < 15:
 199:             bpm_bucket = 'close'
 200:         elif bpm_diff < 30:
 201:             bpm_bucket = 'medium'
 202:         else:
 203:             bpm_bucket = 'far'
 204: 
 205:         # Energy bucket
 206:         energy_diff = abs(
 207:             analysis_a.get('energy_mean', 0) -
 208:             analysis_b.get('energy_mean', 0)
 209:         )
 210:         if energy_diff < 0.02:
 211:             energy_bucket = 'same'
 212:         elif energy_diff < 0.05:
 213:             energy_bucket = 'close'
 214:         else:
 215:             energy_bucket = 'different'
 216: 
 217:         # Key compatibility
 218:         c_a = analysis_a.get('camelot', '')
 219:         c_b = analysis_b.get('camelot', '')
 220:         if c_a == c_b:
 221:             key_compat = 'same'
 222:         elif c_a and c_b and c_a[:-1] == c_b[:-1]:
 223:             key_compat = 'compatible'
 224:         else:
 225:             key_compat = 'incompatible'
 226: 
 227:         genre_a = analysis_a.get('genre_hint', 'Pop/Other')
 228:         genre_b = analysis_b.get('genre_hint', 'Pop/Other')
 229:         same_genre = 'same' if genre_a == genre_b else 'diff'
 230: 
 231:         # Expanded features for advanced techniques
 232:         has_vocals_a = 'has_vocals' in analysis_a and analysis_a['has_vocals']
 233:         spectral_complexity = 'high' if analysis_a.get('spectral_centroid', 2000) > 3500 else 'low'
 234: 
 235:         state = f"{genre_a}|{genre_b}|{bpm_bucket}|{energy_bucket}|{key_compat}|{same_genre}|{'vocals' if has_vocals_a else 'no_vocals'}|{spectral_complexity}"
 236:         return state
 237: 
 238:     def _update_q_table(self, transition_id, reward):
 239:         """
 240:         Update Q-table based on received reward
 241:         Uses standard Q-learning update rule:
 242:         Q(s,a) = Q(s,a) + lr * (reward + γ * max(Q(s')) - Q(s,a))
 243:         """
 244:         # Find the record
 245:         record = None
 246:         for r in self.feedback_log:
 247:             if r['transition_id'] == transition_id:
 248:                 record = r
 249:                 break
 250: 
 251:         if not record:
 252:             return
 253: 
 254:         state = record.get('state', '')
 255:         technique = record.get('technique', '')
 256: 
 257:         if not state or not technique:
 258:             return
 259: 
 260:         # Initialize state in Q-table if needed
 261:         if state not in self.q_table:
 262:             self.q_table[state] = {
 263:                 t: 0.0 for t in self.techniques
 264:             }
 265: 
 266:         # Current Q value
 267:         current_q = self.q_table[state].get(technique, 0.0)
 268: 
 269:         # Max future Q (simplified - no next state lookahead)
 270:         max_future_q = max(self.q_table[state].values())
 271: 
 272:         # Q-learning update
 273:         new_q = current_q + self.learning_rate * (
 274:             reward + self.discount_factor * max_future_q - current_q
 275:         )
 276: 
 277:         self.q_table[state][technique] = new_q
 278:         self._save_q_table()
 279: 
 280:         print(f"   🧠 Q-table updated: "
 281:               f"technique={technique} "
 282:               f"Q: {current_q:.2f} → {new_q:.2f}")
 283: 
 284:     def get_best_technique(self, current_analysis, next_analysis):
 285:         """
 286:         Get the best technique based on learned Q-values
 287:         Uses epsilon-greedy: sometimes explores new techniques
 288:         """
 289:         state = self._get_state(current_analysis, next_analysis)
 290: 
 291:         # Explore: try random technique
 292:         if np.random.random() < self.epsilon:
 293:             technique = np.random.choice(self.techniques)
 294:             print(f"   🎲 Exploring: {technique}")
 295:             return technique, 0.0
 296: 
 297:         # Exploit: use best known technique
 298:         if state in self.q_table:
 299:             q_values = self.q_table[state]
 300: 
 301:             # Get technique with highest Q value
 302:             best_technique = max(q_values, key=q_values.get)
 303:             best_q = q_values[best_technique]
 304: 
 305:             # Only use if Q value is meaningfully positive
 306:             if best_q > 0.1:
 307:                 print(f"   🧠 RL suggests: {best_technique} "
 308:                       f"(Q={best_q:.2f})")
 309:                 return best_technique, best_q
 310: 
 311:         # No learned preference yet - return None
 312:         # (caller will use rule-based fallback)
 313:         return None, 0.0
 314: 
 315:     def get_technique_scores(self, current_analysis, next_analysis):
 316:         """
 317:         Get Q-values for all techniques for this song pair
 318:         Used to boost/penalize rule-based scores
 319:         """
 320:         state = self._get_state(current_analysis, next_analysis)
 321: 
 322:         if state not in self.q_table:
 323:             return {}
 324: 
 325:         return self.q_table[state].copy()
 326: 
 327:     # ============================================================
 328:     # ANALYTICS
 329:     # ============================================================
 330: 
 331:     def get_stats(self):
 332:         """
 333:         Get statistics about learned preferences
 334:         """
 335:         if not self.feedback_log:
 336:             return {'message': 'No feedback recorded yet'}
 337: 
 338:         total = len(self.feedback_log)
 339:         rated = [r for r in self.feedback_log if r.get('reward') is not None]
 340:         positive = [r for r in rated if r.get('reward', 0) > 0]
 341:         negative = [r for r in rated if r.get('reward', 0) < 0]
 342:         skipped = [r for r in rated if r.get('was_skipped')]
 343: 
 344:         # Best techniques by average reward
 345:         technique_rewards = {}
 346:         for record in rated:
 347:             tech = record.get('technique', '')
 348:             reward = record.get('reward', 0)
 349:             if tech not in technique_rewards:
 350:                 technique_rewards[tech] = []
 351:             technique_rewards[tech].append(reward)
 352: 
 353:         technique_avg = {
 354:             tech: float(np.mean(rewards))
 355:             for tech, rewards in technique_rewards.items()
 356:             if len(rewards) >= 3
 357:         }
 358: 
 359:         best_technique = max(technique_avg, key=technique_avg.get) \
 360:             if technique_avg else 'not enough data'
 361:         worst_technique = min(technique_avg, key=technique_avg.get) \
 362:             if technique_avg else 'not enough data'
 363: 
 364:         # Best genre pairs
 365:         genre_pair_rewards = {}
 366:         for record in rated:
 367:             pair = f"{record.get('genre_a', '')} → {record.get('genre_b', '')}"
 368:             reward = record.get('reward', 0)
 369:             if pair not in genre_pair_rewards:
 370:                 genre_pair_rewards[pair] = []
 371:             genre_pair_rewards[pair].append(reward)
 372: 
 373:         best_genre_pairs = sorted(
 374:             [
 375:                 (pair, float(np.mean(rewards)))
 376:                 for pair, rewards in genre_pair_rewards.items()
 377:                 if len(rewards) >= 2
 378:             ],
 379:             key=lambda x: x[1],
 380:             reverse=True
 381:         )[:5]
 382: 
 383:         return {
 384:             'total_transitions': total,
 385:             'rated_transitions': len(rated),
 386:             'positive_feedback': len(positive),
 387:             'negative_feedback': len(negative),
 388:             'skips': len(skipped),
 389:             'approval_rate': len(positive) / max(len(rated), 1),
 390:             'best_technique': best_technique,
 391:             'worst_technique': worst_technique,
 392:             'technique_scores': technique_avg,
 393:             'best_genre_pairs': best_genre_pairs,
 394:             'q_table_states': len(self.q_table),
 395:             'epsilon': self.epsilon,
 396:         }
 397: 
 398:     def print_stats(self):
 399:         """Print formatted statistics"""
 400:         stats = self.get_stats()
 401: 
 402:         print("\n📊 RL FEEDBACK STATISTICS")
 403:         print("=" * 50)
 404:         print(f"Total transitions:  {stats.get('total_transitions', 0)}")
 405:         print(f"Rated:              {stats.get('rated_transitions', 0)}")
 406:         print(f"Approval rate:      "
 407:               f"{stats.get('approval_rate', 0):.1%}")
 408:         print(f"Skips:              {stats.get('skips', 0)}")
 409:         print(f"\nBest technique:     {stats.get('best_technique', 'N/A')}")
 410:         print(f"Worst technique:    {stats.get('worst_technique', 'N/A')}")
 411:         print(f"\nQ-table states:     {stats.get('q_table_states', 0)}")
 412:         print(f"Exploration rate:   {stats.get('epsilon', 0):.0%}")
 413: 
 414:         if stats.get('technique_scores'):
 415:             print("\nTechnique scores:")
 416:             sorted_tech = sorted(
 417:                 stats['technique_scores'].items(),
 418:                 key=lambda x: x[1],
 419:                 reverse=True
 420:             )
 421:             for tech, score in sorted_tech:
 422:                 bar = '█' * int(abs(score) * 10)
 423:                 sign = '+' if score >= 0 else '-'
 424:                 print(f"  {tech:<30} {sign}{abs(score):.2f} {bar}")
 425: 
 426:         if stats.get('best_genre_pairs'):
 427:             print("\nBest genre transitions:")
 428:             for pair, score in stats['best_genre_pairs']:
 429:                 print(f"  {pair:<40} {score:+.2f}")
 430: 
 431:     def reduce_exploration(self):
 432:         """
 433:         Gradually reduce exploration as model learns
 434:         Called after N transitions
 435:         """
 436:         min_epsilon = 0.05
 437:         decay = 0.995
 438:         self.epsilon = max(min_epsilon, self.epsilon * decay)
 439: 
 440:     def export_training_data(self):
 441:         """
 442:         Export feedback log as training data
 443:         for transition_trainer.py
 444:         """
 445:         rated = [
 446:             r for r in self.feedback_log
 447:             if r.get('reward') is not None
 448:         ]
 449: 
 450:         training_examples = []
 451:         for record in rated:
 452:             training_examples.append({
 453:                 'technique': record['technique'],
 454:                 'features': {
 455:                     'bpm_before': record.get('bpm_a', 120),
 456:                     'bpm_after': record.get('bpm_b', 120),
 457:                     'energy_before': record.get('energy_a', 0.05),
 458:                     'energy_after': record.get('energy_b', 0.05),
 459:                     'centroid_before': 2000,
 460:                     'centroid_after': 2000,
 461:                     'confidence': abs(record.get('reward', 0))
 462:                 },
 463:                 'reward': record.get('reward', 0),
 464:                 'source': 'user_feedback',
 465:                 'timestamp': record.get('timestamp', '')
 466:             })
 467: 
 468:         output_path = os.path.join(
 469:             self.config['paths']['training_data'],
 470:             f"rl_feedback_export_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d')}.json"
 471:         )
 472:         with open(output_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
 473:             json.dump(training_examples, f, indent=2)
 474: 
 475:         print(f"✅ Exported {len(training_examples)} "
 476:               f"RL examples to {output_path}")
 477:         return output_path
 478:

 486:             try:
 487:                 with open(self.q_table_file, 'r') as f:
 488:                     return json.load(f)
 489:             except Exception:
 490:                 pass
 491:         return {}

 494:         """Save Q-table to disk"""
 495:         with open(self.q_table_file, 'w') as f:
 496:             json.dump(self.q_table, f, indent=2)
 497: 
 498:     def _load_feedback_log(self):
 499:         """Load feedback history from disk"""
 500:         if os.path.exists(self.feedback_file):
 501:             try:
 502:                 with open(self.feedback_file, 'r',
 503:                           encoding='utf-8') as f:
 504:                     return json.load(f)
 505:             except Exception:
 506:                 pass
 507:         return []
 508: 
 509:     def _save_feedback_log(self):
 510:         """Save feedback history to disk"""
 511:         with open(self.feedback_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
 512:             json.dump(
 513:                 self.feedback_log, f,
 514:                 indent=2, ensure_ascii=False
 515:             )



================================================================================
