   1: import os
   2: import json
   3: import numpy as np
   4: from datetime import datetime
   5: 
   6: class TransitionTrainer:
   7:     """
   8:     Trains the transition technique classifier
   9:     from labeled tutorial data
  10:     Input: song features of A + B
  11:     Output: best transition technique
  12:     """
  13:     def __init__(self, config):
  14:         self.config = config
  15:         self.training_dir = config['paths']['training_data']
  16:         self.models_dir = config['paths']['models']
  17:         os.makedirs(self.models_dir, exist_ok=True)
  18: 
  19:         self.model = None
  20:         self.label_encoder = None
  21:         self.feature_names = [
  22:             'bpm_a', 'bpm_b', 'bpm_diff', 'bpm_ratio',
  23:             'energy_a', 'energy_b', 'energy_diff',
  24:             'centroid_a', 'centroid_b', 'centroid_diff',
  25:             'camelot_compatible', 'same_genre',
  26:             'genre_a_encoded', 'genre_b_encoded',
  27:         ]
  28: 
  29:         self.genre_map = {
  30:             'EDM/Techno': 0, 'House/Dance': 1,
  31:             'Hip-Hop/Rap': 2, 'R&B/Soul': 3,
  32:             'Rock/Metal': 4, 'Ambient/Chill': 5,
  33:             'Pop/Other': 6, 'Drum & Bass': 7,
  34:         }
  35: 
  36:         self.technique_map = {
  37:             'beatmatch_crossfade': 0,
  38:             'cut_transition': 1,
  39:             'echo_out': 2,
  40:             'filter_sweep': 3,
  41:             'loop_roll': 4,
  42:             'reverb_wash': 5,
  43:             'spinback': 6,
  44:             'tempo_ramp': 7,
  45:             'white_noise_sweep': 8,
  46:             'wordplay': 9,
  47:             'tone_play': 10,
  48:             'mashup_short': 11,
  49:             'acapella_layer': 12,
  50:             'drum_swap': 13,
  51:             'bass_swap': 14,
  52:             'stutter_glitch': 15,
  53:             'half_time_transition': 16,
  54:             'wordplay_mashup': 17,
  55:             'phrasal_interlace': 18,
  56:             'semantic_bridge': 19,
  57:             'mashup_extended': 20,
  58:             'double_time_transition': 21,
  59:         }
  60: 
  61:     def load_training_data(self):
  62:         """Load all labeled training examples"""
  63:         all_examples = []
  64: 
  65:         for filename in os.listdir(self.training_dir):
  66:             if filename.endswith('.json'):
  67:                 filepath = os.path.join(self.training_dir, filename)
  68:                 try:
  69:                     with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
  70:                         data = json.load(f)
  71:                     if isinstance(data, list):
  72:                         all_examples.extend(data)
  73:                 except Exception as e:
  74:                     print(f"   ❌ Could not load {filename}: {e}")
  75: 
  76:         print(f"   📊 Loaded {len(all_examples)} training examples")
  77:         return all_examples
  78: 
  79:     def extract_features(self, analysis_a, analysis_b):
  80:         """
  81:         Extract feature vector from two song analyses
  82:         This is what the model uses to decide technique
  83:         """
  84:         bpm_a = analysis_a.get('bpm', 120)
  85:         bpm_b = analysis_b.get('bpm', 120)
  86:         bpm_diff = abs(bpm_a - bpm_b)
  87:         bpm_ratio = min(bpm_a, bpm_b) / max(bpm_a, bpm_b)
  88: 
  89:         energy_a = analysis_a.get('energy_mean', 0.05)
  90:         energy_b = analysis_b.get('energy_mean', 0.05)
  91:         energy_diff = abs(energy_a - energy_b)
  92: 
  93:         centroid_a = analysis_a.get('spectral_centroid', 2000)
  94:         centroid_b = analysis_b.get('spectral_centroid', 2000)
  95:         centroid_diff = abs(centroid_a - centroid_b)
  96: 
  97:         # Camelot wheel compatibility
  98:         c_a = analysis_a.get('camelot', '')
  99:         c_b = analysis_b.get('camelot', '')
 100:         camelot_compat = 1.0 if c_a == c_b else (
 101:             0.5 if c_a[:-1] == c_b[:-1] else 0.0
 102:         )
 103: 
 104:         genre_a = analysis_a.get('genre_hint', 'Pop/Other')
 105:         genre_b = analysis_b.get('genre_hint', 'Pop/Other')
 106:         same_genre = 1.0 if genre_a == genre_b else 0.0
 107: 
 108:         genre_a_enc = self.genre_map.get(genre_a, 6) / 7.0
 109:         genre_b_enc = self.genre_map.get(genre_b, 6) / 7.0
 110: 
 111:         features = np.array([
 112:             bpm_a / 200.0,
 113:             bpm_b / 200.0,
 114:             bpm_diff / 100.0,
 115:             bpm_ratio,
 116:             energy_a * 10,
 117:             energy_b * 10,
 118:             energy_diff * 10,
 119:             centroid_a / 10000.0,
 120:             centroid_b / 10000.0,
 121:             centroid_diff / 10000.0,
 122:             camelot_compat,
 123:             same_genre,
 124:             genre_a_enc,
 125:             genre_b_enc,
 126:         ], dtype=np.float32)
 127: 
 128:         return features
 129: 
 130:     def train(self):
 131:         """Train the transition classifier"""
 132:         try:
 133:             from sklearn.ensemble import RandomForestClassifier
 134:             from sklearn.model_selection import train_test_split
 135:             from sklearn.metrics import classification_report
 136:             import pickle
 137:         except ImportError:
 138:             print("❌ scikit-learn not installed")
 139:             print("   Run: pip install scikit-learn")
 140:             return False
 141: 
 142:         examples = self.load_training_data()
 143: 
 144:         if len(examples) < 10:
 145:             print("   ⚠️  Not enough training data yet")
 146:             print(f"   Need at least 10 examples, have {len(examples)}")
 147:             print("   Run dj_tutorial_scraper.py first")
 148:             return False
 149: 
 150:         # Build feature matrix
 151:         X = []
 152:         y = []
 153: 
 154:         for example in examples:
 155:             technique = example.get('technique', '')
 156:             if technique not in self.technique_map:
 157:                 continue
 158: 
 159:             features = example.get('features', {})
 160:             if not features:
 161:                 continue
 162: 
 163:             # Build feature vector from stored features
 164:             bpm_before = features.get('bpm_before', 120)
 165:             bpm_after = features.get('bpm_after', 120)
 166:             energy_before = features.get('energy_before', 0.05)
 167:             energy_after = features.get('energy_after', 0.05)
 168:             centroid_before = features.get('centroid_before', 2000)
 169:             centroid_after = features.get('centroid_after', 2000)
 170: 
 171:             feature_vec = np.array([
 172:                 bpm_before / 200.0,
 173:                 bpm_after / 200.0,
 174:                 abs(bpm_before - bpm_after) / 100.0,
 175:                 min(bpm_before, bpm_after) / max(bpm_before, bpm_after),
 176:                 energy_before * 10,
 177:                 energy_after * 10,
 178:                 abs(energy_before - energy_after) * 10,
 179:                 centroid_before / 10000.0,
 180:                 centroid_after / 10000.0,
 181:                 abs(centroid_before - centroid_after) / 10000.0,
 182:                 0.5, 0.5, 0.5, 0.5  # Unknown camelot/genre for auto-labeled
 183:             ], dtype=np.float32)
 184: 
 185:             X.append(feature_vec)
 186:             y.append(self.technique_map[technique])
 187: 
 188:         if len(X) < 10:
 189:             print("   ⚠️  Not enough valid examples after filtering")
 190:             return False
 191: 
 192:         X = np.array(X)
 193:         y = np.array(y)
 194: 
 195:         print(f"   🏋️  Training on {len(X)} examples...")
 196: 
 197:         # Split data
 198:         X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(
 199:             X, y, test_size=0.2, random_state=42
 200:         )
 201: 
 202:         # Train Random Forest
 203:         self.model = RandomForestClassifier(
 204:             n_estimators=100,
 205:             max_depth=10,
 206:             random_state=42,
 207:             class_weight='balanced'
 208:         )
 209:         self.model.fit(X_train, y_train)
 210: 
 211:         # Evaluate
 212:         y_pred = self.model.predict(X_test)
 213:         accuracy = np.mean(y_pred == y_test)
 214:         print(f"   ✅ Training accuracy: {accuracy:.2%}")
 215: 
 216:         # Save model
 217:         model_path = os.path.join(
 218:             self.models_dir, 'transition_classifier.pkl'
 219:         )
 220:         with open(model_path, 'wb') as f:
 221:             pickle.dump({
 222:                 'model': self.model,
 223:                 'technique_map': self.technique_map,
 224:                 'feature_names': self.feature_names,
 225:                 'trained_at': str(datetime.now()),
 226:                 'accuracy': accuracy,
 227:                 'n_examples': len(X)
 228:             }, f)
 229: 
 230:         print(f"   ✅ Model saved to {model_path}")
 231:         return True
 232: 
 233:     def predict(self, analysis_a, analysis_b):
 234:         """
 235:         Predict best transition technique
 236:         Returns (technique_name, confidence)
 237:         """
 238:         import pickle
 239: 
 240:         model_path = os.path.join(
 241:             self.models_dir, 'transition_classifier.pkl'
 242:         )
 243: 
 244:         if not os.path.exists(model_path):
 245:             return None, 0.0
 246: 
 247:         if self.model is None:
 248:             with open(model_path, 'rb') as f:
 249:                 saved = pickle.load(f)
 250:             self.model = saved['model']
 251:             self.technique_map = saved['technique_map']
 252: 
 253:         features = self.extract_features(analysis_a, analysis_b)
 254:         features = features.reshape(1, -1)
 255: 
 256:         prediction = self.model.predict(features)[0]
 257:         probabilities = self.model.predict_proba(features)[0]
 258:         confidence = float(np.max(probabilities))
 259: 
 260:         # Reverse map
 261:         reverse_map = {v: k for k, v in self.technique_map.items()}
 262:         technique = reverse_map.get(prediction, 'beatmatch_crossfade')
 263: 
 264:         return technique, confidence

  69:     def parse_channel(self, channel_url, max_videos=30):
  70:         """
  71:         Parse all tutorial videos from a channel
  72:         Returns list of labeled training examples
  73:         """
  74:         print(f"\n📺 Parsing channel: {channel_url}")
  75: 
  76:         # Get video list
  77:         videos = self._get_channel_videos(channel_url, max_videos)
  78:         print(f"   Found {len(videos)} videos")
  79: 
  80:         all_examples = []
  81: 
  82:         for i, video in enumerate(videos):
  83:             print(f"   [{i+1}/{len(videos)}] {video['title'][:50]}")
  84: 
  85:             try:
  86:                 examples = self._parse_video(video)
  87:                 all_examples.extend(examples)
  88:                 print(f"      → {len(examples)} training examples extracted")
  89:             except Exception as e:
  90:                 print(f"      ❌ Failed: {e}")
  91:                 continue
  92: 
  93:         # Save training data
  94:         output_path = os.path.join(
  95:             self.training_dir,
  96:             f"parsed_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.json"
  97:         )
  98:         with open(output_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
  99:             json.dump(all_examples, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
 100: 
 101:         print(f"\n✅ Saved {len(all_examples)} examples to {output_path}")
 102:         return all_examples
 103: 
 104:     def _get_channel_videos(self, channel_url, max_videos):
 105:         """Get list of videos from YouTube channel"""
 106:         ydl_opts = {
 107:             'quiet': True,
 108:             'extract_flat': True,
 109:             'playlistend': max_videos,
 110:         }
 111:         videos = []
 112:         with yt_dlp.YoutubeDL(ydl_opts) as ydl:
 113:             info = ydl.extract_info(channel_url, download=False)
 114:             for entry in info.get('entries', []):
 115:                 if entry and entry.get('duration', 0) < 1800:
 116:                     videos.append({
 117:                         'id': entry.get('id'),
 118:                         'title': entry.get('title', ''),
 119:                         'url': f"https://youtube.com/watch?v={entry.get('id')}",
 120:                         'duration': entry.get('duration', 0)
 121:                     })
 122:         return videos
 123: 
 124:     def _parse_video(self, video):
 125:         """
 126:         Parse a single tutorial video
 127:         Returns list of training examples
 128:         """
 129:         # Download audio
 130:         audio_path = self._download_audio(video)
 131:         if not audio_path:
 132:             return []
 133: 
 134:         # Transcribe
 135:         transcript_data = self._transcribe(audio_path)
 136: 
 137:         # Cleanup audio
 138:         if os.path.exists(audio_path):
 139:             os.remove(audio_path)
 140: 
 141:         if not transcript_data:
 142:             return []
 143: 
 144:         # Extract technique examples from transcript
 145:         examples = self._extract_examples(
 146:             transcript_data, video
 147:         )
 148: 
 149:         return examples
 150: 
 151:     def _download_audio(self, video):
 152:         """Download audio for transcription"""
 153:         output_path = os.path.join(
 154:             self.training_dir, f"tmp_{video['id']}.mp3"
 155:         )
 156: 
 157:         if os.path.exists(output_path):
 158:             return output_path
 159: 
 160:         ydl_opts = {
 161:             'format': 'bestaudio/best',
 162:             'outtmpl': output_path.replace('.mp3', '.%(ext)s'),
 163:             'postprocessors': [{
 164:                 'key': 'FFmpegExtractAudio',
 165:                 'preferredcodec': 'mp3',
 166:                 'preferredquality': '128',
 167:             }],
 168:             'quiet': True,
 169:         }
 170: 
 171:         try:
 172:             with yt_dlp.YoutubeDL(ydl_opts) as ydl:
 173:                 ydl.download([video['url']])
 174:             return output_path
 175:         except Exception as e:
 176:             print(f"      ❌ Download failed: {e}")
 177:             return None
 178: 
 179:     def _transcribe(self, audio_path):
 180:         """Transcribe audio with word timestamps"""
 181:         if not self.whisper_model:
 182:             print("      Loading Whisper...")
 183:             self.whisper_model = whisper.load_model("base")
 184: 
 185:         try:
 186:             result = self.whisper_model.transcribe(
 187:                 audio_path,
 188:                 word_timestamps=True
 189:             )
 190:             return result
 191:         except Exception as e:
 192:             print(f"      ❌ Transcription failed: {e}")
 193:             return None
 194: 
 195:     def _extract_examples(self, transcript_data, video):
 196:         """
 197:         Extract labeled training examples
 198:         from transcript segments
 199:         """
 200:         examples = []
 201:         segments = transcript_data.get('segments', [])
 202:         full_text = transcript_data.get('text', '').lower()
 203: 
 204:         # Check which techniques are mentioned
 205:         mentioned_techniques = []
 206:         for technique, keywords in self.technique_indicators.items():
 207:             for kw in keywords:
 208:                 if kw in full_text:
 209:                     mentioned_techniques.append(technique)
 210:                     break
 211: 
 212:         # Extract context around each technique mention
 213:         for technique in mentioned_techniques:
 214:             keywords = self.technique_indicators[technique]
 215: 
 216:             for segment in segments:
 217:                 seg_text = segment.get('text', '').lower()
 218: 
 219:                 for kw in keywords:
 220:                     if kw in seg_text:
 221:                         # Found technique mention in this segment
 222:                         context = self._get_context(
 223:                             segments,
 224:                             segment,
 225:                             window=3
 226:                         )
 227: 
 228:                         examples.append({
 229:                             'video_id': video['id'],
 230:                             'video_title': video['title'],
 231:                             'technique': technique,
 232:                             'timestamp': segment.get('start', 0),
 233:                             'text': segment.get('text', ''),
 234:                             'context': context,
 235:                             'keyword_found': kw,
 236:                             'source': 'tutorial',
 237:                         })
 238:                         break
 239: 
 240:         return examples
 241: 
 242:     def _get_context(self, segments, target_segment, window=3):
 243:         """Get surrounding segments for context"""
 244:         try:
 245:             idx = segments.index(target_segment)
 246:         except ValueError:
 247:             return target_segment.get('text', '')
 248: 
 249:         start = max(0, idx - window)
 250:         end = min(len(segments), idx + window + 1)
 251: 
 252:         context_texts = [
 253:             s.get('text', '') for s in segments[start:end]
 254:         ]
 255:         return ' '.join(context_texts)

FILE: ai_brain\training\wordplay_trainer.py
================================================================================
   1:     def score_connection(self, word_match, analysis_a, analysis_b):
   2:         """
   3:         Score how good a wordplay connection would sound
   4:         Returns float 0.0 - 1.0
   5:         """
   6:         import pickle
   7: 
   8:         model_path = os.path.join(
   9:             self.models_dir, 'wordplay_classifier.pkl'
  10:         )
  11: 
  12:         # Rule-based scoring baseline
  13:         score = 0.5
  14: 
  15:         # Exact word match bonus
  16:         if word_match.get('type') == 'exact':
  17:             score += 0.3
  18:         elif word_match.get('type') == 'phoneme':
  19:             # Partial bonus based on phoneme similarity
  20:             sim = word_match.get('similarity', 0.5)
  21:             score += 0.15 * sim
  22: 
  23:         # Same language bonus
  24:         lang_a = analysis_a.get('lyrics', {})
  25:         lang_b = analysis_b.get('lyrics', {})
  26:         if lang_a and lang_b:
  27:             la = lang_a.get('language', '')
  28:             lb = lang_b.get('language', '')
  29:             if la == lb and la not in ('', 'unknown'):
  30:                 score += 0.2
  31: 
  32:         # Key compatibility bonus
  33:         if analysis_a.get('camelot') == analysis_b.get('camelot'):
  34:             score += 0.1
  35: 
  36:         # Energy compatibility bonus
  37:         energy_diff = abs(
  38:             analysis_a.get('energy_mean', 0) -
  39:             analysis_b.get('energy_mean', 0)
  40:         )
  41:         if energy_diff < 0.02:
  42:             score += 0.05
  43: 
  44:         # Use ML model if available
  45:         if os.path.exists(model_path):
  46:             try:
  47:                 with open(model_path, 'rb') as f:
  48:                     saved = pickle.load(f)
  49:                 ml_model = saved['model']
  50: 
  51:                 lang_a_str = analysis_a.get('lyrics', {}).get(
  52:                     'language', ''
  53:                 ) if analysis_a.get('lyrics') else ''
  54:                 lang_b_str = analysis_b.get('lyrics', {}).get(
  55:                     'language', ''
  56:                 ) if analysis_b.get('lyrics') else ''
  57: 
  58:                 features = np.array([
  59:                     1.0 if lang_a_str == lang_b_str else 0.0,
  60:                     1.0 if word_match.get('type') == 'exact' else 0.5,
  61:                     analysis_a.get('energy_mean', 0.05) * 10,
  62:                     analysis_b.get('energy_mean', 0.05) * 10,
  63:                     abs(
  64:                         analysis_a.get('bpm', 120) -
  65:                         analysis_b.get('bpm', 120)
  66:                     ) / 100.0,
  67:                     1.0 if (
  68:                         analysis_a.get('camelot') ==
  69:                         analysis_b.get('camelot')
  70:                     ) else 0.0,
  71:                 ], dtype=np.float32).reshape(1, -1)
  72: 
  73:                 proba = ml_model.predict_proba(features)[0]
  74:                 ml_score = float(proba[1])
  75: 
  76:                 # Blend rule-based and ML scores
  77:                 score = (score * 0.4) + (ml_score * 0.6)
  78: 
  79:             except Exception as e:
  80:                 print(f"   ⚠️  ML scoring failed, using rules: {e}")
  81: 
  82:         return min(1.0, max(0.0, score))



================================================================================
FILE: analysis\audio_analyzer.py
================================================================================
   1: import librosa
   2: import numpy as np
   3: import json
   4: import os
   5: import warnings
   6: warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')
   7: 
   8: class AudioAnalyzer:
   9:     def __init__(self, config):
  10:         self.config = config
  11:         self.metadata_dir = config['paths']['metadata']
  12:         os.makedirs(self.metadata_dir, exist_ok=True)
  13: 
  14:         self.camelot_wheel = {
  15:             'C major': '8B',  'A minor': '8A',
  16:             'G major': '9B',  'E minor': '9A',
  17:             'D major': '10B', 'B minor': '10A',
  18:             'A major': '11B', 'F# minor': '11A',
  19:             'E major': '12B', 'C# minor': '12A',
  20:             'B major': '1B',  'G# minor': '1A',
  21:             'F# major': '2B', 'D# minor': '2A',
  22:             'C# major': '3B', 'A# minor': '3A',
  23:             'G# major': '4B', 'F minor': '4A',
  24:             'D# major': '5B', 'C minor': '5A',
  25:             'A# major': '6B', 'G minor': '6A',
  26:             'F major': '7B',  'D minor': '7A',
  27:         }
  28: 
  29:     def analyze_track(self, filepath, song_id):
  30:         cache_path = os.path.join(self.metadata_dir, f"{song_id}.json")
  31:         if os.path.exists(cache_path):
  32:             with open(cache_path, 'r') as f:
  33:                 return json.load(f)
  34: 
  35:         print(f"   🔍 Analyzing audio (fast speed-mode)...")
  36:         y, sr = librosa.load(filepath, sr=22050, duration=180.0)
  37: 
  38:         # BPM & beats
  39:         tempo_result, beats = librosa.beat.beat_track(y=y, sr=sr)
  40:       # Ensure tempo is a scalar float
  41:         if hasattr(tempo_result, '__len__'):
  42:             tempo = float(tempo_result[0]) if len(tempo_result) > 0 else 120.0
  43:         else:
  44:             tempo = float(tempo_result)
  45:         beat_times = librosa.frames_to_time(beats, sr=sr)
  46: 
  47:         # Key detection
  48:         chroma = librosa.feature.chroma_cqt(y=y, sr=sr)
  49:         chroma_mean = np.mean(chroma, axis=1)
  50:         key_index = int(np.argmax(chroma_mean))
  51:         keys = ['C','C#','D','D#','E','F','F#','G','G#','A','A#','B']
  52:         detected_key = keys[key_index]
  53:         mode = 'major'
  54:         key_full = f"{detected_key} {mode}"
  55:         camelot = self.camelot_wheel.get(key_full, 'Unknown')
  56: 
  57:         # Energy
  58:         rms = librosa.feature.rms(y=y)[0]
  59:         energy_mean = float(np.mean(rms))
  60:         energy_sections = []
  61:         section_size = max(1, len(rms) // 10)
  62:         for i in range(10):
  63:             section = rms[i*section_size:(i+1)*section_size]
  64:             energy_sections.append(float(np.mean(section)))
  65: 
  66:         # Spectral features
  67:         spectral_centroid = float(np.mean(
  68:             librosa.feature.spectral_centroid(y=y, sr=sr)
  69:         ))
  70:         zero_crossing = float(np.mean(
  71:             librosa.feature.zero_crossing_rate(y=y)
  72:         ))
  73: 
  74:         # Genre
  75:         genre_hint = self._classify_genre(
  76:             tempo, spectral_centroid, energy_mean, zero_crossing
  77:         )
  78: 
  79:         # Melody notes (simplified)
  80:         melody_notes = self._extract_melody_notes(y, sr)
  81: 
  82:         # Transition points
  83:         duration = float(len(y) / sr)
  84:         outro_time = duration * 0.8
  85:         if len(beat_times) > 0:
  86:             outro_beat = float(min(
  87:                 beat_times, key=lambda x: abs(x - outro_time)
  88:             ))
  89:         else:
  90:             outro_beat = outro_time
  91: 
  92:         analysis = {
  93:             'song_id': song_id,
  94:             'bpm': tempo,
  95:             'key': detected_key,
  96:             'mode': mode,
  97:             'key_full': key_full,
  98:             'camelot': camelot,
  99:             'duration': duration,
 100:             'energy_mean': energy_mean,
 101:             'energy_sections': energy_sections,
 102:             'spectral_centroid': spectral_centroid,
 103:             'zero_crossing_rate': zero_crossing,
 104:             'genre_hint': genre_hint,
 105:             'melody_notes': melody_notes,
 106:             'beat_times': beat_times[:20].tolist(),
 107:             'transition_points': {
 108:                 'outro_beat': outro_beat,
 109:                 'safe_transition_start': duration * 0.75,
 110:                 'emergency_cutpoint': duration * 0.95
 111:             }
 112:         }
 113: 
 114:         with open(cache_path, 'w') as f:
 115:             json.dump(analysis, f, indent=2)
 116: 
 117:         return analysis
 118: 
 119:     def load_all_metadata(self):
 120:         """Load all cached metadata"""
 121:         metadata = {}
 122:         for filename in os.listdir(self.metadata_dir):
 123:             if filename.endswith('.json') and '_phrases' not in filename \
 124:                and '_entries' not in filename:
 125:                 song_id = filename.replace('.json', '')
 126:                 filepath = os.path.join(self.metadata_dir, filename)
 127:                 with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
 128:                     metadata[song_id] = json.load(f)
 129:         print(f"✅ Loaded {len(metadata)} cached analyses")
 130:         return metadata
 131: 
 132:     def _classify_genre(self, bpm, spectral_centroid, energy, zcr):
 133:         if bpm > 140 and energy > 0.1:
 134:             return 'EDM/Techno'
 135:         elif bpm > 120 and spectral_centroid > 3000:
 136:             return 'House/Dance'
 137:         elif bpm > 130 and zcr > 0.1:
 138:             return 'Drum & Bass'
 139:         elif bpm < 80 and energy < 0.05:
 140:             return 'Ambient/Chill'
 141:         elif 85 < bpm < 110 and zcr > 0.08:
 142:             return 'Hip-Hop/Rap'
 143:         elif 60 < bpm < 100 and spectral_centroid < 2000:
 144:             return 'R&B/Soul'
 145:         elif spectral_centroid > 4000 and zcr > 0.1:
 146:             return 'Rock/Metal'
 147:         else:
 148:             return 'Pop/Other'
 149: 
 150:     def _extract_melody_notes(self, y, sr):
 151:         """Extract main melody as MIDI note numbers"""
 152:         try:
 153:             f0, voiced_flag, _ = librosa.pyin(
 154:                 y, fmin=librosa.note_to_hz('C2'),
 155:                 fmax=librosa.note_to_hz('C7')
 156:             )
 157:             voiced_f0 = f0[voiced_flag]
 158:             if len(voiced_f0) > 0:
 159:                 notes = librosa.hz_to_midi(voiced_f0[::10])
 160:                 return [int(n) for n in notes[:16] if not np.isnan(n)]
 161:         except:
 162:             pass
 163:         return [60, 62, 64, 65, 67]  # Default C major scale



================================================================================
FILE: analysis\compatibility_scorer.py
================================================================================
   1: class CompatibilityScorer:
   2:     def __init__(self, config):
   3:         self.config = config
   4:         self.compatible_camelot_pairs = self._build_camelot_pairs()
   5: 
   6:     def score(self, analysis_a, analysis_b):
   7:         """Score compatibility 0-100"""
   8:         score = 0
   9:         reasons = []
  10: 
  11:         # BPM (40 points)
  12:         bpm_diff = abs(
  13:             analysis_a.get('bpm', 120) - analysis_b.get('bpm', 120)
  14:         )
  15:         if bpm_diff < 3:
  16:             score += 40
  17:             reasons.append("✅ Perfect BPM match")
  18:         elif bpm_diff < 8:
  19:             score += 28
  20:             reasons.append("⚠️ Close BPM")
  21:         elif bpm_diff < 20:
  22:             score += 15
  23:             reasons.append("⚠️ Moderate BPM difference")
  24:         else:
  25:             score += 5
  26:             reasons.append("❌ Large BPM difference")
  27: 
  28:         # Key (35 points)
  29:         c1 = analysis_a.get('camelot', '')
  30:         c2 = analysis_b.get('camelot', '')
  31:         if c1 and c2:
  32:             if c1 == c2:
  33:                 score += 35
  34:                 reasons.append("✅ Same key")
  35:             elif (c1, c2) in self.compatible_camelot_pairs or \
  36:                  (c2, c1) in self.compatible_camelot_pairs:
  37:                 score += 25
  38:                 reasons.append("✅ Compatible keys")
  39:             else:
  40:                 score += 5
  41:                 reasons.append("❌ Incompatible keys")
  42: 
  43:         # Energy (25 points)
  44:         e_diff = abs(
  45:             analysis_a.get('energy_mean', 0) -
  46:             analysis_b.get('energy_mean', 0)
  47:         )
  48:         if e_diff < 0.02:
  49:             score += 25
  50:             reasons.append("✅ Matching energy")
  51:         elif e_diff < 0.05:
  52:             score += 15
  53:             reasons.append("⚠️ Slight energy difference")
  54:         else:
  55:             score += 5
  56:             reasons.append("⚠️ Energy shift")
  57: 
  58:         # Recommend technique
  59:         transition = self._recommend_transition(analysis_a, analysis_b, score)
  60: 
  61:         return {
  62:             'score': score,
  63:             'reasons': reasons,
  64:             'recommended_transition': transition
  65:         }
  66: 
  67:     def _recommend_transition(self, a1, a2, score):
  68:         bpm_diff = abs(a1.get('bpm', 120) - a2.get('bpm', 120))
  69:         if score >= 70:
  70:             return 'beatmatch_crossfade'
  71:         elif bpm_diff > 20:
  72:             return 'echo_out'
  73:         elif a1.get('energy_mean', 0) < a2.get('energy_mean', 0):
  74:             return 'filter_sweep'
  75:         else:
  76:             return 'reverb_wash'
  77: 
  78:     def _build_camelot_pairs(self):
  79:         pairs = set()
  80:         keys = list(range(1, 13))
  81:         for k in keys:
  82:             nxt = k % 12 + 1
  83:             pairs.add((f"{k}A", f"{nxt}A"))
  84:             pairs.add((f"{k}B", f"{nxt}B"))
  85:             pairs.add((f"{k}A", f"{k}B"))
  86:         return pairs



================================================================================
FILE: analysis\entry_point_finder.py
================================================================================
   1: import librosa
   2: import numpy as np
   3: import json
   4: import os
   5: 
   6: class EntryPointFinder:
   7:     """
   8:     Implements the Farooq Got Audio technique:
   9:     Find the most emotionally powerful entry point
  10:     rather than always starting from the beginning
  11:     """
  12:     
  13:     def __init__(self, config):
  14:         self.config = config
  15:         self.metadata_dir = config['paths']['metadata']
  16: 
  17:     def find_entry_points(self, filepath, analysis, song_id):
  18:         """
  19:         Analyze all possible entry points and rank them
  20:         """
  21:         cache_path = os.path.join(
  22:             self.metadata_dir, f"{song_id}_entries.json"
  23:         )
  24:         if os.path.exists(cache_path):
  25:             with open(cache_path, 'r') as f:
  26:                 return json.load(f)
  27: 
  28:         y, sr = librosa.load(filepath, sr=22050)
  29:         
  30:         # Get all phrase boundaries
  31:         phrases = analysis.get('phrases', {})
  32:         bar_times = analysis.get('bar_times', [])
  33:         
  34:         entry_candidates = []
  35:         
  36:         for bar_time in bar_times[::8]:  # Check every 8 bars
  37:             score = self._score_entry_point(y, sr, bar_time, analysis)
  38:             entry_candidates.append({
  39:                 'time': float(bar_time),
  40:                 'score': float(score),
  41:                 'energy': float(self._get_energy_at(y, sr, bar_time)),
  42:                 'is_standard_start': bar_time < 5.0,
  43:             })
  44:         
  45:         # Sort by score
  46:         entry_candidates.sort(key=lambda x: x['score'], reverse=True)
  47:         
  48:         result = {
  49:             'standard_start': 0.0,
  50:             'best_entry': entry_candidates[0] if entry_candidates else None,
  51:             'top_5_entries': entry_candidates[:5],
  52:             'all_candidates': entry_candidates
  53:         }
  54:         
  55:         with open(cache_path, 'w') as f:
  56:             json.dump(result, f, indent=2)
  57:         
  58:         return result
  59: 
  60:     def _score_entry_point(self, y, sr, time, analysis):
  61:         """
  62:         Score how good an entry point is
  63:         Higher = more impactful/emotional start
  64:         """
  65:         score = 0.0
  66:         sample = int(time * sr)
  67:         window = int(sr * 4)  # 4 second window
  68:         
  69:         if sample + window > len(y):
  70:             return 0.0
  71:         
  72:         segment = y[sample:sample + window]
  73:         
  74:         # Energy score (higher energy = more impactful)
  75:         rms = np.sqrt(np.mean(segment ** 2))
  76:         score += rms * 10
  77:         
  78:         # Spectral richness (more instruments = more interesting)
  79:         spec = np.abs(librosa.stft(segment))
  80:         spectral_entropy = -np.sum(
  81:             spec * np.log(spec + 1e-10)
  82:         ) / spec.size
  83:         score += spectral_entropy * 0.1
  84:         
  85:         # Onset strength (rhythmic hits = good entry)
  86:         onset_strength = np.mean(
  87:             librosa.onset.onset_strength(y=segment, sr=sr)
  88:         )
  89:         score += onset_strength * 2
  90:         
  91:         # Penalize very beginning (too common)
  92:         if time < 5.0:
  93:             score *= 0.7
  94:         
  95:         # Bonus for being in first third (avoid starting too late)
  96:         duration = len(y) / sr
  97:         if time < duration * 0.33:
  98:             score *= 1.2
  99:         
 100:         return score
 101: 
 102:     def _get_energy_at(self, y, sr, time):
 103:         sample = int(time * sr)
 104:         window = int(sr * 2)
 105:         if sample + window > len(y):
 106:             return 0.0
 107:         segment = y[sample:sample + window]
 108:         return float(np.sqrt(np.mean(segment ** 2)))



================================================================================
FILE: analysis\melody_detector.py
================================================================================
   1: import librosa
   2: import numpy as np
   3: import json
   4: import os
   5: 
   6: class MelodyDetector:
   7:     """
   8:     Detects main melody from audio
   9:     Used by tone_play transition engine
  10:     to preview incoming song's melody
  11:     using outgoing song's instrument timbre
  12:     """
  13:     def __init__(self, config):
  14:         self.config = config
  15:         self.metadata_dir = config['paths']['metadata']
  16:         self.sr = config['audio']['sample_rate']
  17:         os.makedirs(self.metadata_dir, exist_ok=True)
  18: 
  19:     def detect(self, filepath, song_id):
  20:         """
  21:         Full melody detection pipeline
  22:         Returns melody note sequence + timing
  23:         """
  24:         cache_path = os.path.join(
  25:             self.metadata_dir, f"{song_id}_melody.json"
  26:         )
  27:         if os.path.exists(cache_path):
  28:             with open(cache_path, 'r') as f:
  29:                 return json.load(f)
  30: 
  31:         print(f"   🎵 Detecting melody: {song_id}")
  32: 
  33:         y, sr = librosa.load(filepath, sr=self.sr, mono=True)
  34: 
  35:         # ---- Pitch Detection ----
  36:         f0, voiced_flag, voiced_probs = librosa.pyin(
  37:             y,
  38:             fmin=librosa.note_to_hz('C2'),
  39:             fmax=librosa.note_to_hz('C7'),
  40:             sr=sr
  41:         )
  42: 
  43:         # Get voiced (non-silent) frames
  44:         times = librosa.times_like(f0, sr=sr)
  45:         voiced_f0 = np.where(voiced_flag, f0, np.nan)
  46: 
  47:         # Convert Hz to MIDI note numbers
  48:         midi_notes = []
  49:         note_times = []
  50: 
  51:         for i, (freq, t) in enumerate(zip(voiced_f0, times)):
  52:             if not np.isnan(freq) and freq > 0:
  53:                 midi = librosa.hz_to_midi(freq)
  54:                 midi_notes.append(float(midi))
  55:                 note_times.append(float(t))
  56: 
  57:         # ---- Simplify melody (quantize to scale) ----
  58:         quantized = self._quantize_to_scale(midi_notes)
  59: 
  60:         # ---- Find melodic phrases ----
  61:         phrases = self._find_melodic_phrases(
  62:             quantized, note_times
  63:         )
  64: 
  65:         # ---- Find most memorable phrase ----
  66:         hook = self._find_hook(phrases)
  67: 
  68:         # ---- Get instrument timbre info ----
  69:         timbre = self._analyze_timbre(y, sr)
  70: 
  71:         result = {
  72:             'song_id': song_id,
  73:             'raw_notes': midi_notes[:100],
  74:             'note_times': note_times[:100],
  75:             'quantized_notes': quantized[:100],
  76:             'phrases': phrases[:10],
  77:             'hook': hook,
  78:             'timbre': timbre,
  79:             'dominant_note': int(np.median(midi_notes)) if midi_notes else 60,
  80:             'note_range': {
  81:                 'min': int(min(midi_notes)) if midi_notes else 48,
  82:                 'max': int(max(midi_notes)) if midi_notes else 72,
  83:             }
  84:         }
  85: 
  86:         with open(cache_path, 'w') as f:
  87:             json.dump(result, f, indent=2)
  88: 
  89:         return result
  90: 
  91:     def _quantize_to_scale(self, midi_notes):
  92:         """
  93:         Snap notes to nearest chromatic pitch
  94:         Removes micro-tonal variations
  95:         """
  96:         return [round(n) for n in midi_notes]
  97: 
  98:     def _find_melodic_phrases(self, notes, times, gap_threshold=0.5):
  99:         """
 100:         Group notes into phrases based on timing gaps
 101:         A gap > 0.5 seconds = new phrase
 102:         """
 103:         if not notes or not times:
 104:             return []
 105: 
 106:         phrases = []
 107:         current_phrase = {'notes': [], 'times': [], 'start': times[0]}
 108: 
 109:         for i in range(len(notes)):
 110:             if i > 0:
 111:                 gap = times[i] - times[i-1]
 112:                 if gap > gap_threshold:
 113:                     # Save current phrase
 114:                     if len(current_phrase['notes']) >= 3:
 115:                         current_phrase['end'] = times[i-1]
 116:                         current_phrase['duration'] = (
 117:                             current_phrase['end'] -
 118:                             current_phrase['start']
 119:                         )
 120:                         phrases.append(current_phrase)
 121:                     # Start new phrase
 122:                     current_phrase = {
 123:                         'notes': [],
 124:                         'times': [],
 125:                         'start': times[i]
 126:                     }
 127: 
 128:             current_phrase['notes'].append(notes[i])
 129:             current_phrase['times'].append(times[i])
 130: 
 131:         # Add last phrase
 132:         if len(current_phrase['notes']) >= 3:
 133:             current_phrase['end'] = times[-1]
 134:             current_phrase['duration'] = (
 135:                 current_phrase['end'] - current_phrase['start']
 136:             )
 137:             phrases.append(current_phrase)
 138: 
 139:         return phrases
 140: 
 141:     def _find_hook(self, phrases):
 142:         """
 143:         Find the most memorable/repeated melodic phrase
 144:         Hook = phrase that appears most often OR
 145:                has highest note variety
 146:         """
 147:         if not phrases:
 148:             return {'notes': [60, 62, 64, 65, 67], 'start': 0}
 149: 
 150:         # Score each phrase
 151:         scored = []
 152:         for phrase in phrases:
 153:             notes = phrase['notes']
 154:             # Score: note variety + length
 155:             variety = len(set(notes))
 156:             length = len(notes)
 157:             # Prefer phrases in first third of song
 158:             early_bonus = 1.5 if phrase.get('start', 0) < 60 else 1.0
 159:             score = (variety * 2 + length) * early_bonus
 160:             scored.append((score, phrase))
 161: 
 162:         scored.sort(key=lambda x: x[0], reverse=True)
 163:         return scored[0][1]
 164: 
 165:     def _analyze_timbre(self, y, sr):
 166:         """
 167:         Analyze timbral qualities to help
 168:         tone_play engine pick best instrument sound
 169:         """
 170:         # Spectral centroid (brightness)
 171:         centroid = float(np.mean(
 172:             librosa.feature.spectral_centroid(y=y, sr=sr)
 173:         ))
 174: 
 175:         # Spectral rolloff
 176:         rolloff = float(np.mean(
 177:             librosa.feature.spectral_rolloff(y=y, sr=sr)
 178:         ))
 179: 
 180:         # Zero crossing rate (noisiness)
 181:         zcr = float(np.mean(
 182:             librosa.feature.zero_crossing_rate(y=y)
 183:         ))
 184: 
 185:         # MFCCs (timbral texture)
 186:         mfccs = librosa.feature.mfcc(y=y, sr=sr, n_mfcc=13)
 187:         mfcc_means = np.mean(mfccs, axis=1).tolist()
 188: 
 189:         # Classify dominant instrument type
 190:         instrument_type = self._classify_instrument(
 191:             centroid, rolloff, zcr
 192:         )
 193: 
 194:         return {
 195:             'spectral_centroid': centroid,
 196:             'spectral_rolloff': rolloff,
 197:             'zero_crossing_rate': zcr,
 198:             'mfcc_means': mfcc_means,
 199:             'instrument_type': instrument_type,
 200:             'brightness': 'bright' if centroid > 3000 else 'warm',
 201:         }
 202: 
 203:     def _classify_instrument(self, centroid, rolloff, zcr):
 204:         """Classify dominant instrument from spectral features"""
 205:         if centroid > 5000 and zcr > 0.1:
 206:             return 'strings_or_synth'
 207:         elif centroid > 3000 and zcr < 0.05:
 208:             return 'piano_or_keys'
 209:         elif centroid < 1500:
 210:             return 'bass_or_pad'
 211:         elif zcr > 0.15:
 212:             return 'guitar_or_percussion'
 213:         else:
 214:             return 'vocal_or_mixed'
 215: 
 216:     def get_tone_play_sample(self, filepath, song_id,
 217:                               sample_duration=0.5):
 218:         """
 219:         Extract the best short audio sample to use
 220:         as the 'instrument' in tone play transitions
 221:         Returns: (audio_array, sample_rate)
 222:         """
 223:         import soundfile as sf
 224: 
 225:         melody_data = self.detect(filepath, song_id)
 226:         hook = melody_data.get('hook', {})
 227:         start_time = hook.get('start', 10.0)
 228: 
 229:         y, sr = librosa.load(
 230:             filepath,
 231:             sr=self.sr,
 232:             offset=start_time,
 233:             duration=sample_duration,
 234:             mono=True
 235:         )
 236: 
 237:         return y, sr



================================================================================
FILE: analysis\phrase_detector.py
================================================================================
   1: import librosa
   2: import numpy as np
   3: import json
   4: import os
   5: 
   6: class PhraseDetector:
   7:     def __init__(self, config):
   8:         self.config = config
   9:         self.metadata_dir = config['paths']['metadata']
  10: 
  11:     def detect_phrases(self, filepath, song_id):
  12:         """
  13:         Detect musical phrases (4, 8, 16, 32 bar boundaries)
  14:         Returns list of phrase boundary timestamps
  15:         """
  16:         cache_path = os.path.join(
  17:             self.metadata_dir, f"{song_id}_phrases.json"
  18:         )
  19:         if os.path.exists(cache_path):
  20:             with open(cache_path, 'r') as f:
  21:                 return json.load(f)
  22: 
  23:         y, sr = librosa.load(filepath, sr=22050)
  24:         
  25:         # Get beat frames
  26:         tempo, beats = librosa.beat.beat_track(y=y, sr=sr)
  27:         tempo = float(np.atleast_1d(tempo)[0]) # Ensure scalar
  28:         beat_times = librosa.frames_to_time(beats, sr=sr)
  29:         
  30:         # Group beats into bars (4 beats per bar)
  31:         bars = []
  32:         for i in range(0, len(beat_times) - 3, 4):
  33:             bars.append({
  34:                 'bar_number': len(bars) + 1,
  35:                 'start_time': float(beat_times[i]),
  36:                 'beats': beat_times[i:i+4].tolist()
  37:             })
  38:         
  39:         # Detect phrase boundaries using spectral flux
  40:         # Phrases typically change every 4, 8, or 16 bars
  41:         spectral_flux = self._compute_spectral_flux(y, sr)
  42:         
  43:         phrases = {
  44:             '4_bar': [],
  45:             '8_bar': [],
  46:             '16_bar': [],
  47:             '32_bar': []
  48:         }
  49:         
  50:         for i, bar in enumerate(bars):
  51:             if i % 4 == 0:
  52:                 phrases['4_bar'].append(bar['start_time'])
  53:             if i % 8 == 0:
  54:                 phrases['8_bar'].append(bar['start_time'])
  55:             if i % 16 == 0:
  56:                 phrases['16_bar'].append(bar['start_time'])
  57:             if i % 32 == 0:
  58:                 phrases['32_bar'].append(bar['start_time'])
  59:         
  60:         # Find HIGH ENERGY phrase boundaries (best transition points)
  61:         transition_candidates = self._find_transition_candidates(
  62:             bars, spectral_flux, sr, y
  63:         )
  64:         
  65:         result = {
  66:             'tempo': tempo,
  67:             'total_bars': len(bars),
  68:             'bar_times': [b['start_time'] for b in bars],
  69:             'phrases': phrases,
  70:             'transition_candidates': transition_candidates,
  71:             'best_transition_out': self._best_outro_phrase(
  72:                 bars, y, sr
  73:             ),
  74:             'best_transition_in': self._best_intro_phrase(
  75:                 bars, y, sr
  76:             )
  77:         }
  78:         
  79:         with open(cache_path, 'w') as f:
  80:             json.dump(result, f, indent=2)
  81:         
  82:         return result
  83: 
  84:     def _compute_spectral_flux(self, y, sr):
  85:         """Measure how much spectrum changes over time"""
  86:         hop_length = 512
  87:         spec = np.abs(librosa.stft(y, hop_length=hop_length))
  88:         flux = np.sum(np.diff(spec, axis=1) ** 2, axis=0)
  89:         return flux
  90: 
  91:     def _find_transition_candidates(self, bars, flux, sr, y):
  92:         """Find bars where energy/spectrum changes significantly"""
  93:         candidates = []
  94:         rms = librosa.feature.rms(y=y)[0]
  95:         
  96:         for i, bar in enumerate(bars[:-1]):
  97:             # Check if this is a phrase boundary (multiple of 4/8/16)
  98:             if i % 4 == 0:
  99:                 # Measure energy change at this bar
 100:                 bar_sample = int(bar['start_time'] * sr)
 101:                 window = sr * 2  # 2 second window
 102:                 
 103:                 energy_before = np.mean(rms[max(0, bar_sample//512 - 8):
 104:                                             bar_sample//512])
 105:                 energy_after = np.mean(rms[bar_sample//512:
 106:                                            bar_sample//512 + 8])
 107:                 
 108:                 energy_change = abs(energy_after - energy_before)
 109:                 
 110:                 candidates.append({
 111:                     'time': bar['start_time'],
 112:                     'bar': i + 1,
 113:                     'energy_change': float(energy_change),
 114:                     'phrase_type': '32bar' if i % 32 == 0 else
 115:                                    '16bar' if i % 16 == 0 else
 116:                                    '8bar' if i % 8 == 0 else '4bar'
 117:                 })
 118:         
 119:         # Sort by energy change
 120:         candidates.sort(key=lambda x: x['energy_change'], reverse=True)
 121:         return candidates[:10]
 122: 
 123:     def _best_outro_phrase(self, bars, y, sr):
 124:         """Find best phrase to START transitioning out"""
 125:         rms = librosa.feature.rms(y=y)[0]
 126:         duration = len(y) / sr
 127:         
 128:         # Look in last 30% of song
 129:         start_search = duration * 0.7
 130:         
 131:         for bar in reversed(bars):
 132:             if bar['start_time'] > start_search:
 133:                 # Find nearest 8-bar boundary
 134:                 bar_num = bar['bar_number']
 135:                 if bar_num % 8 == 0:
 136:                     return float(bar['start_time'])
 137:         
 138:         return float(bars[int(len(bars) * 0.75)]['start_time'])
 139: 
 140:     def _best_intro_phrase(self, bars, y, sr):
 141:         """Find best phrase to bring incoming song in on"""
 142:         # Usually bar 1 or bar 9 (after intro)
 143:         if len(bars) > 8:
 144:             return float(bars[8]['start_time'])
 145:         return float(bars[0]['start_time'])



================================================================================
FILE: analysis\vocal_analyzer.py
================================================================================
   1: import os
   2: import json
   3: import librosa
   4: import numpy as np
   5: 
   6: class VocalAnalyzer:
   7:     def __init__(self, config):
   8:         self.config = config
   9:         self.phoneme_dir = config['paths']['phonemes']
  10:         os.makedirs(self.phoneme_dir, exist_ok=True)
  11: 
  12:     def analyze(self, vocals_path, lyrics_data, song_id):
  13:         """
  14:         Analyze vocal track and match words to timestamps
  15:         Returns phoneme data for word index
  16:         """
  17:         cache_path = os.path.join(
  18:             self.phoneme_dir, f"{song_id}_phonemes.json"
  19:         )
  20:         if os.path.exists(cache_path):
  21:             with open(cache_path, 'r') as f:
  22:                 return json.load(f)
  23: 
  24:         if not vocals_path or not os.path.exists(vocals_path):
  25:             return None
  26: 
  27:         timed_words = lyrics_data.get('timed_words', [])
  28:         if not timed_words:
  29:             return None
  30: 
  31:         phoneme_data = []
  32:         y, sr = librosa.load(vocals_path, sr=22050)
  33: 
  34:         for word_entry in timed_words:
  35:             word = word_entry.get('word', '').strip().lower()
  36:             start = word_entry.get('start', 0)
  37:             end = word_entry.get('end', start + 0.3)
  38: 
  39:             if not word or len(word) < 2:
  40:                 continue
  41: 
  42:             # Extract word audio segment
  43:             start_sample = int(start * sr)
  44:             end_sample = int(end * sr)
  45:             word_audio = y[start_sample:end_sample]
  46: 
  47:             if len(word_audio) < 100:
  48:                 continue
  49: 
  50:             # Calculate word clarity (RMS energy)
  51:             clarity = float(np.sqrt(np.mean(word_audio ** 2)))
  52: 
  53:             phoneme_data.append({
  54:                 'word': word,
  55:                 'start': start,
  56:                 'end': end,
  57:                 'clarity': clarity,
  58:                 'duration': end - start
  59:             })
  60: 
  61:         result = {
  62:             'song_id': song_id,
  63:             'word_count': len(phoneme_data),
  64:             'words': phoneme_data
  65:         }
  66: 
  67:         with open(cache_path, 'w') as f:
  68:             json.dump(result, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
  69: 
  70:         return result

================================================================================
FILE: core\audio_engine.py
================================================================================
   1: """
   2: Non-blocking Audio Engine with streaming support
   3: Fixes: Memory leaks, blocking playback, no pre-buffering, THREAD FIGHTS
   4: """
   5: 
   6: import numpy as np
   7: import sounddevice as sd
   8: import threading
   9: import queue
  10: import time
  11: from collections import deque
  12: import librosa
  13: 
  14: 
  15: class AudioEngine:
  16:     """
  17:     Non-blocking audio playback engine with:
  18:     - Streaming playback (no full file in memory)
  19:     - Pre-buffering next song
  20:     - Gapless transitions
  21:     - Real-time audio chunk access (for streaming/visualization)
  22:     """
  23:     
  24:     def __init__(self, config, on_chunk_callback=None):
  25:         self.config = config
  26:         self.sr = config.get('audio', {}).get('sample_rate', 44100)
  27:         self.buffer_size = config.get('audio', {}).get('buffer_size', 2048)
  28:         
  29:         # Callback for streaming/visualization
  30:         self.on_chunk_callback = on_chunk_callback
  31:         
  32:         # Audio buffers
  33:         self.play_queue = queue.Queue(maxsize=100)
  34:         self.current_audio = None
  35:         self.current_position = 0
  36:         
  37:         # Pre-buffer for next song
  38:         self.next_audio_buffer = None
  39:         self.next_audio_ready = threading.Event()
  40:         
  41:         # State
  42:         self.is_playing = False
  43:         self.is_paused = False
  44:         self.volume = 0.85
  45:         
  46:         # FIXED: Session ID to kill old zombie threads!
  47:         self.playback_session_id = 0
  48:         
  49:         # Playback thread
  50:         self.stream = None
  51:         
  52:         # Stats
  53:         self.chunks_played = 0
  54:         self.current_time = 0.0
  55:         
  56:     def start(self):
  57:         """Start audio engine"""
  58:         if self.is_playing:
  59:             return
  60:             
  61:         self.is_playing = True
  62:         
  63:         # Open audio stream
  64:         try:
  65:             self.stream = sd.OutputStream(
  66:                 samplerate=self.sr,
  67:                 channels=2,
  68:                 dtype=np.float32,
  69:                 blocksize=self.buffer_size,
  70:                 callback=self._audio_callback,
  71:             )
  72:             self.stream.start()
  73:             print("🔊 Audio engine started")
  74:         except Exception as e:
  75:             print(f"❌ Failed to start audio stream: {e}")
  76:             self.is_playing = False
  77:         
  78:     def stop(self):
  79:         """Stop audio engine"""
  80:         self.is_playing = False
  81:         self.playback_session_id += 1 # Kill any active queue threads
  82:         
  83:         if self.stream:
  84:             try:
  85:                 self.stream.stop()
  86:                 self.stream.close()
  87:             except:
  88:                 pass
  89:             self.stream = None
  90:             
  91:         print("🔇 Audio engine stopped")
  92:         
  93:     def _audio_callback(self, outdata, frames, time_info, status):
  94:         """
  95:         Called by sounddevice for each audio chunk
  96:         NON-BLOCKING - runs in separate thread
  97:         """
  98:         if status:
  99:             pass # Suppress minor underflow warnings in console
 100:         
 101:         if not self.is_playing or self.is_paused:
 102:             outdata.fill(0)
 103:             return
 104:         
 105:         # Get next chunk from queue
 106:         try:
 107:             chunk = self.play_queue.get_nowait()
 108:             
 109:             # Apply volume
 110:             chunk = chunk * self.volume
 111:             
 112:             # Ensure correct shape
 113:             if len(chunk.shape) == 1:
 114:                 chunk = np.column_stack([chunk, chunk])
 115:             
 116:             # Fill output buffer
 117:             if len(chunk) >= frames:
 118:                 outdata[:] = chunk[:frames].reshape(-1, 2)
 119:             else:
 120:                 outdata[:len(chunk)] = chunk.reshape(-1, 2)
 121:                 outdata[len(chunk):].fill(0)
 122:             
 123:             # Callback for streaming/visualization
 124:             if self.on_chunk_callback:
 125:                 try:
 126:                     self.on_chunk_callback(chunk[:, 0])  # Mono for visualization
 127:                 except:
 128:                     pass
 129:             
 130:             self.chunks_played += 1
 131:             self.current_time += frames / self.sr
 132:             
 133:         except queue.Empty:
 134:             outdata.fill(0)
 135:     
 136:     def load_audio(self, filepath, start_time=0.0):
 137:         """
 138:         Load audio file in background thread
 139:         Returns immediately, audio loads async
 140:         """
 141:         # Increment session so old queue threads die gracefully
 142:         self.playback_session_id += 1
 143:         current_session = self.playback_session_id
 144:         
 145:         def _load():
 146:             try:
 147:                 y, sr = librosa.load(
 148:                     filepath, 
 149:                     sr=self.sr, 
 150:                     mono=False,
 151:                     offset=start_time
 152:                 )
 153:                 
 154:                 # Convert mono to stereo
 155:                 if len(y.shape) == 1:
 156:                     y = np.stack([y, y])
 157:                 
 158:                 # Transpose to (samples, channels)
 159:                 y = y.T
 160:                 
 161:                 # Abort if another song was loaded while we were decoding
 162:                 if self.playback_session_id != current_session:
 163:                     return
 164:                     
 165:                 self.current_audio = y
 166:                 self.current_position = 0
 167:                 
 168:                 # Queue initial chunks
 169:                 self._queue_chunks(current_session)
 170:                 
 171:             except Exception as e:
 172:                 print(f"❌ Audio load error: {e}")
 173:         
 174:         threading.Thread(target=_load, daemon=True).start()
 175:     
 176:     def _queue_chunks(self, session_id):
 177:         """Queue audio chunks for playback"""
 178:         if self.current_audio is None:
 179:             return
 180:         
 181:         chunk_size = self.buffer_size
 182:         
 183:         # FIXED: Check is_playing AND session_id to prevent zombie threads!
 184:         while self.current_position < len(self.current_audio) and self.is_playing:
 185:             if self.playback_session_id != session_id:
 186:                 break # A new song started, let this old thread die!
 187:                 
 188:             if self.play_queue.full():
 189:                 time.sleep(0.01)
 190:                 continue
 191:             
 192:             end = min(self.current_position + chunk_size, len(self.current_audio))
 193:             chunk = self.current_audio[self.current_position:end]
 194:             
 195:             try:
 196:                 self.play_queue.put(chunk.astype(np.float32), timeout=0.1)
 197:                 self.current_position = end
 198:             except queue.Full:
 199:                 continue
 200:     
 201:     def prebuffer_next(self, filepath, start_time=0.0):
 202:         """
 203:         Pre-load next song in background
 204:         Call this while current song is playing
 205:         """
 206:         def _prebuffer():
 207:             try:
 208:                 y, sr = librosa.load(
 209:                     filepath,
 210:                     sr=self.sr,
 211:                     mono=False,
 212:                     offset=start_time
 213:                 )
 214:                 
 215:                 if len(y.shape) == 1:
 216:                     y = np.stack([y, y])
 217:                 
 218:                 self.next_audio_buffer = y.T
 219:                 self.next_audio_ready.set()
 220:                 print("✅ Next song pre-buffered")
 221:                 
 222:             except Exception as e:
 223:                 print(f"❌ Pre-buffer error: {e}")
 224:         
 225:         self.next_audio_ready.clear()
 226:         threading.Thread(target=_prebuffer, daemon=True).start()
 227:     
 228:     def crossfade_to_next(self, crossfade_samples=44100):
 229:         """
 230:         Crossfade to pre-buffered next song
 231:         Gapless transition!
 232:         """
 233:         if self.next_audio_buffer is None:
 234:             print("⚠️ No pre-buffered audio")
 235:             return
 236:         
 237:         # Wait for pre-buffer if needed
 238:         self.next_audio_ready.wait(timeout=5)
 239:         
 240:         # FIXED: Advance session ID so old queue thread dies before we alter queue!
 241:         self.playback_session_id += 1
 242:         current_session = self.playback_session_id
 243:         
 244:         # Get remaining current audio
 245:         remaining = self.current_audio[self.current_position:]
 246:         
 247:         # Crossfade
 248:         cf_len = min(crossfade_samples, len(remaining), len(self.next_audio_buffer))
 249:         
 250:         fade_out = np.linspace(1, 0, cf_len).reshape(-1, 1)
 251:         fade_in = np.linspace(0, 1, cf_len).reshape(-1, 1)
 252:         
 253:         crossfaded = remaining[:cf_len] * fade_out + self.next_audio_buffer[:cf_len] * fade_in
 254:         
 255:         # Clear queue and add crossfade safely
 256:         while not self.play_queue.empty():
 257:             try:
 258:                 self.play_queue.get_nowait()
 259:             except:
 260:                 break
 261:         
 262:         # Queue crossfade
 263:         for i in range(0, len(crossfaded), self.buffer_size):
 264:             chunk = crossfaded[i:i + self.buffer_size]
 265:             try:
 266:                 self.play_queue.put(chunk.astype(np.float32), timeout=0.1)
 267:             except:
 268:                 break
 269:         
 270:         # Switch to next audio
 271:         self.current_audio = self.next_audio_buffer
 272:         self.current_position = cf_len
 273:         self.next_audio_buffer = None
 274:         
 275:         # Continue queueing with NEW session ID
 276:         threading.Thread(target=self._queue_chunks, args=(current_session,), daemon=True).start()
 277:     
 278:     def get_current_time(self):
 279:         """Get current playback position in seconds"""
 280:         return self.current_time
 281:     
 282:     def get_remaining_time(self):
 283:         """Get remaining time in current song"""
 284:         if self.current_audio is None:
 285:             return 0
 286:         total = len(self.current_audio) / self.sr
 287:         return max(0, total - self.current_time)
 288:     
 289:     def set_volume(self, volume):
 290:         """Set volume (0.0 to 1.0)"""
 291:         self.volume = max(0.0, min(1.0, volume))
 292:     
 293:     def pause(self):
 294:         """Pause playback"""
 295:         self.is_paused = True
 296:     
 297:     def resume(self):
 298:         """Resume playback"""
 299:         self.is_paused = False

FILE: core\cache_manager.py
