   1: """
   2: Smart Cache Manager
   3: Fixes: No cache strategy, unlimited disk usage, no LRU eviction
   4: """
   5: 
   6: import os
   7: import json
   8: import time
   9: import shutil
  10: import hashlib
  11: from pathlib import Path
  12: from dataclasses import dataclass
  13: from typing import Optional, Any, Dict
  14: from datetime import datetime, timedelta
  15: import threading
  16: 
  17: 
  18: @dataclass
  19: class CacheEntry:
  20:     key: str
  21:     path: str
  22:     size_bytes: int
  23:     created_at: float
  24:     last_accessed: float
  25:     access_count: int
  26:     metadata: dict
  27: 
  28: 
  29: class CacheManager:
  30:     """
  31:     Smart cache manager with:
  32:     - LRU eviction
  33:     - Size limits
  34:     - TTL support
  35:     - Priority-based eviction
  36:     - Disk usage monitoring
  37:     """
  38:     
  39:     def __init__(self, config):
  40:         self.config = config
  41:         
  42:         # Cache directories
  43:         self.cache_dirs = {
  44:             'audio': config['paths']['audio_cache'],
  45:             'stems': config['paths']['stems'],
  46:             'metadata': config['paths']['metadata'],
  47:             'lyrics': config['paths']['lyrics'],
  48:             'phonemes': config['paths']['phonemes'],
  49:         }
  50:         
  51:         # Limits
  52:         storage_cfg = config.get('storage', {})
  53:         self.max_cache_gb = storage_cfg.get('max_local_cache_gb', 10)
  54:         self.max_cache_bytes = self.max_cache_gb * 1024 * 1024 * 1024
  55:         
  56:         # Cache index
  57:         self.index: Dict[str, CacheEntry] = {}
  58:         self.index_file = 'data/cache_index.json'
  59:         self.lock = threading.Lock()
  60:         
  61:         # Stats
  62:         self.hits = 0
  63:         self.misses = 0
  64:         
  65:         # Load existing index
  66:         self._load_index()
  67:         
  68:         # Start cleanup thread
  69:         self.cleanup_thread = threading.Thread(
  70:             target=self._cleanup_loop,
  71:             daemon=True
  72:         )
  73:         self.cleanup_thread.start()
  74:     
  75:     def _load_index(self):
  76:         """Load cache index from disk"""
  77:         try:
  78:             if os.path.exists(self.index_file):
  79:                 with open(self.index_file, 'r') as f:
  80:                     data = json.load(f)
  81:                     for key, entry_data in data.items():
  82:                         if os.path.exists(entry_data['path']):
  83:                             self.index[key] = CacheEntry(**entry_data)
  84:         except Exception as e:
  85:             print(f"⚠️ Cache index load failed: {e}")
  86:             self.index = {}
  87:     
  88:     def _save_index(self):
  89:         """Save cache index to disk"""
  90:         try:
  91:             os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(self.index_file), exist_ok=True)
  92:             with open(self.index_file, 'w') as f:
  93:                 data = {
  94:                     key: {
  95:                         'key': entry.key,
  96:                         'path': entry.path,
  97:                         'size_bytes': entry.size_bytes,
  98:                         'created_at': entry.created_at,
  99:                         'last_accessed': entry.last_accessed,
 100:                         'access_count': entry.access_count,
 101:                         'metadata': entry.metadata,
 102:                     }
 103:                     for key, entry in self.index.items()
 104:                 }
 105:                 json.dump(data, f, indent=2)
 106:         except Exception as e:
 107:             print(f"⚠️ Cache index save failed: {e}")
 108:     
 109:     def get(self, cache_type: str, key: str) -> Optional[str]:
 110:         """
 111:         Get cached file path
 112:         Returns None if not cached
 113:         """
 114:         cache_key = f"{cache_type}:{key}"
 115:         
 116:         with self.lock:
 117:             if cache_key in self.index:
 118:                 entry = self.index[cache_key]
 119:                 
 120:                 if os.path.exists(entry.path):
 121:                     # Update access stats
 122:                     entry.last_accessed = time.time()
 123:                     entry.access_count += 1
 124:                     self.hits += 1
 125:                     return entry.path
 126:                 else:
 127:                     # File missing, remove from index
 128:                     del self.index[cache_key]
 129:         
 130:         self.misses += 1
 131:         return None
 132:     
 133:     def put(self, cache_type: str, key: str, filepath: str, 
 134:             metadata: dict = None, priority: int = 0) -> str:
 135:         """
 136:         Add file to cache
 137:         Returns cache path
 138:         """
 139:         cache_key = f"{cache_type}:{key}"
 140:         cache_dir = self.cache_dirs.get(cache_type, 'data/cache')
 141:         os.makedirs(cache_dir, exist_ok=True)
 142:         
 143:         # Get file size
 144:         size_bytes = os.path.getsize(filepath) if os.path.exists(filepath) else 0
 145:         
 146:         # Check if need to evict
 147:         self._maybe_evict(size_bytes)
 148:         
 149:         # Determine cache path
 150:         ext = os.path.splitext(filepath)[1]
 151:         cache_path = os.path.join(cache_dir, f"{key}{ext}")
 152:         
 153:         # Copy if different path
 154:         if filepath != cache_path:
 155:             shutil.copy2(filepath, cache_path)
 156:         
 157:         # Create entry
 158:         entry = CacheEntry(
 159:             key=cache_key,
 160:             path=cache_path,
 161:             size_bytes=size_bytes,
 162:             created_at=time.time(),
 163:             last_accessed=time.time(),
 164:             access_count=1,
 165:             metadata=metadata or {},
 166:         )
 167:         
 168:         with self.lock:
 169:             self.index[cache_key] = entry
 170:             self._save_index()
 171:         
 172:         return cache_path
 173:     
 174:     def exists(self, cache_type: str, key: str) -> bool:
 175:         """Check if item is cached"""
 176:         cache_key = f"{cache_type}:{key}"
 177:         
 178:         with self.lock:
 179:             if cache_key in self.index:
 180:                 entry = self.index[cache_key]
 181:                 return os.path.exists(entry.path)
 182:         
 183:         return False
 184:     
 185:     def delete(self, cache_type: str, key: str) -> bool:
 186:         """Delete cached item"""
 187:         cache_key = f"{cache_type}:{key}"
 188:         
 189:         with self.lock:
 190:             if cache_key in self.index:
 191:                 entry = self.index[cache_key]
 192:                 
 193:                 try:
 194:                     if os.path.exists(entry.path):
 195:                         os.remove(entry.path)
 196:                 except:
 197:                     pass
 198:                 
 199:                 del self.index[cache_key]
 200:                 self._save_index()
 201:                 return True
 202:         
 203:         return False
 204:     
 205:     def _maybe_evict(self, needed_bytes: int):
 206:         """Evict items if cache is full"""
 207:         current_size = self.get_total_size()
 208:         
 209:         if current_size + needed_bytes <= self.max_cache_bytes:
 210:             return
 211:         
 212:         # Need to evict
 213:         bytes_to_free = (current_size + needed_bytes) - self.max_cache_bytes
 214:         bytes_to_free = int(bytes_to_free * 1.2)  # Free 20% extra
 215:         
 216:         print(f"🧹 Cache eviction: freeing {bytes_to_free / 1024 / 1024:.1f} MB")
 217:         
 218:         with self.lock:
 219:             # Sort by LRU (least recently used first)
 220:             sorted_entries = sorted(
 221:                 self.index.values(),
 222:                 key=lambda e: (e.last_accessed, -e.access_count)
 223:             )
 224:             
 225:             freed = 0
 226:             to_delete = []
 227:             
 228:             for entry in sorted_entries:
 229:                 if freed >= bytes_to_free:
 230:                     break
 231:                 
 232:                 # Don't evict metadata (small and important)
 233:                 if 'metadata' in entry.path:
 234:                     continue
 235:                 
 236:                 to_delete.append(entry.key)
 237:                 freed += entry.size_bytes
 238:             
 239:             # Delete entries
 240:             for key in to_delete:
 241:                 entry = self.index[key]
 242:                 try:
 243:                     if os.path.exists(entry.path):
 244:                         os.remove(entry.path)
 245:                 except:
 246:                     pass
 247:                 del self.index[key]
 248:             
 249:             self._save_index()
 250:             
 251:         print(f"✅ Freed {freed / 1024 / 1024:.1f} MB")
 252:     
 253:     def get_total_size(self) -> int:
 254:         """Get total cache size in bytes"""
 255:         total = 0
 256:         for entry in self.index.values():
 257:             if os.path.exists(entry.path):
 258:                 total += entry.size_bytes
 259:         return total
 260:     
 261:     def _cleanup_loop(self):
 262:         """Background cleanup thread"""
 263:         while True:
 264:             time.sleep(3600)  # Every hour
 265:             
 266:             try:
 267:                 # Remove entries for missing files
 268:                 with self.lock:
 269:                     to_remove = []
 270:                     for key, entry in self.index.items():
 271:                         if not os.path.exists(entry.path):
 272:                             to_remove.append(key)
 273:                     
 274:                     for key in to_remove:
 275:                         del self.index[key]
 276:                     
 277:                     if to_remove:
 278:                         self._save_index()
 279:                         print(f"🧹 Cleaned {len(to_remove)} stale cache entries")
 280:                 
 281:                 # Check disk usage
 282:                 self._maybe_evict(0)
 283:                 
 284:             except Exception as e:
 285:                 print(f"⚠️ Cache cleanup error: {e}")
 286:     
 287:     def get_stats(self) -> dict:
 288:         """Get cache statistics"""
 289:         total_size = self.get_total_size()
 290:         
 291:         return {
 292:             'total_items': len(self.index),
 293:             'total_size_mb': total_size / 1024 / 1024,
 294:             'max_size_mb': self.max_cache_bytes / 1024 / 1024,
 295:             'usage_percent': (total_size / self.max_cache_bytes) * 100,
 296:             'hits': self.hits,
 297:             'misses': self.misses,
 298:             'hit_rate': self.hits / max(self.hits + self.misses, 1),
 299:         }
 300:     
 301:     def clear_all(self):
 302:         """Clear entire cache"""
 303:         with self.lock:
 304:             for entry in self.index.values():
 305:                 try:
 306:                     if os.path.exists(entry.path):
 307:                         os.remove(entry.path)
 308:                 except:
 309:                     pass
 310:             
 311:             self.index.clear()
 312:             self._save_index()
 313:         
 314:         print("🗑️ Cache cleared")



================================================================================
FILE: core\health_monitor.py
================================================================================
   1: """
   2: Health Monitor - System monitoring and auto-recovery
   3: Fixes: No health checks, no auto-restart, no alerts
   4: """
   5: 
   6: import threading
   7: import time
   8: import os
   9: import psutil
  10: from datetime import datetime, timedelta
  11: from typing import Dict, List, Callable
  12: from dataclasses import dataclass
  13: from enum import Enum
  14: 
  15: 
  16: class HealthStatus(Enum):
  17:     HEALTHY = "healthy"
  18:     WARNING = "warning"
  19:     CRITICAL = "critical"
  20:     DEAD = "dead"
  21: 
  22: 
  23: @dataclass
  24: class HealthCheck:
  25:     name: str
  26:     check_func: Callable[[], bool]
  27:     last_check: datetime = None
  28:     last_status: HealthStatus = HealthStatus.HEALTHY
  29:     consecutive_failures: int = 0
  30:     recovery_func: Callable = None
  31: 
  32: 
  33: class HealthMonitor:
  34:     """
  35:     System health monitoring with:
  36:     - Component health checks
  37:     - Auto-recovery
  38:     - Resource monitoring
  39:     - Alerting
  40:     """
  41:     
  42:     def __init__(self, config):
  43:         self.config = config
  44:         self.checks: Dict[str, HealthCheck] = {}
  45:         self.is_running = False
  46:         self.monitor_thread = None
  47:         
  48:         # Thresholds
  49:         self.cpu_warning = 80
  50:         self.cpu_critical = 95
  51:         self.memory_warning = 80
  52:         self.memory_critical = 95
  53:         self.disk_warning = 80
  54:         self.disk_critical = 95
  55:         
  56:         # Alert callbacks
  57:         self.alert_callbacks: List[Callable] = []
  58:         
  59:         # History
  60:         self.history = []
  61:         self.max_history = 1000
  62:         
  63:     def add_check(self, name: str, check_func: Callable, 
  64:                   recovery_func: Callable = None):
  65:         """Add a health check"""
  66:         self.checks[name] = HealthCheck(
  67:             name=name,
  68:             check_func=check_func,
  69:             recovery_func=recovery_func,
  70:         )
  71:     
  72:     def add_alert_callback(self, callback: Callable):
  73:         """Add callback for alerts"""
  74:         self.alert_callbacks.append(callback)
  75:     
  76:     def start(self):
  77:         """Start health monitoring"""
  78:         if self.is_running:
  79:             return
  80:         
  81:         self.is_running = True
  82:         self.monitor_thread = threading.Thread(
  83:             target=self._monitor_loop,
  84:             daemon=True
  85:         )
  86:         self.monitor_thread.start()
  87:         
  88:         print("💓 Health monitor started")
  89:     
  90:     def stop(self):
  91:         """Stop health monitoring"""
  92:         self.is_running = False
  93:         print("💔 Health monitor stopped")
  94:     
  95:     def _monitor_loop(self):
  96:         """Main monitoring loop"""
  97:         while self.is_running:
  98:             try:
  99:                 status = self._run_all_checks()
 100:                 self._log_status(status)
 101:                 
 102:                 # Alert if critical
 103:                 if status['overall'] in [HealthStatus.CRITICAL, HealthStatus.DEAD]:
 104:                     self._send_alert(status)
 105:                 
 106:             except Exception as e:
 107:                 print(f"❌ Health monitor error: {e}")
 108:             
 109:             time.sleep(30)  # Check every 30 seconds
 110:     
 111:     def _run_all_checks(self) -> dict:
 112:         """Run all health checks"""
 113:         results = {}
 114:         
 115:         # System checks
 116:         results['cpu'] = self._check_cpu()
 117:         results['memory'] = self._check_memory()
 118:         results['disk'] = self._check_disk()
 119:         
 120:         # Component checks
 121:         for name, check in self.checks.items():
 122:             try:
 123:                 is_healthy = check.check_func()
 124:                 check.last_check = datetime.now()
 125:                 
 126:                 if is_healthy:
 127:                     check.last_status = HealthStatus.HEALTHY
 128:                     check.consecutive_failures = 0
 129:                 else:
 130:                     check.consecutive_failures += 1
 131:                     
 132:                     if check.consecutive_failures >= 3:
 133:                         check.last_status = HealthStatus.CRITICAL
 134:                         
 135:                         # Try recovery
 136:                         if check.recovery_func:
 137:                             print(f"🔄 Attempting recovery for {name}")
 138:                             try:
 139:                                 check.recovery_func()
 140:                             except Exception as e:
 141:                                 print(f"❌ Recovery failed: {e}")
 142:                     else:
 143:                         check.last_status = HealthStatus.WARNING
 144:                 
 145:                 results[name] = check.last_status
 146:                 
 147:             except Exception as e:
 148:                 check.last_status = HealthStatus.DEAD
 149:                 check.consecutive_failures += 1
 150:                 results[name] = HealthStatus.DEAD
 151:                 print(f"❌ Health check '{name}' error: {e}")
 152:         
 153:         # Overall status
 154:         statuses = list(results.values())
 155:         
 156:         if HealthStatus.DEAD in statuses:
 157:             results['overall'] = HealthStatus.DEAD
 158:         elif HealthStatus.CRITICAL in statuses:
 159:             results['overall'] = HealthStatus.CRITICAL
 160:         elif HealthStatus.WARNING in statuses:
 161:             results['overall'] = HealthStatus.WARNING
 162:         else:
 163:             results['overall'] = HealthStatus.HEALTHY
 164:         
 165:         return results
 166:     
 167:     def _check_cpu(self) -> HealthStatus:
 168:         """Check CPU usage"""
 169:         try:
 170:             cpu_percent = psutil.cpu_percent(interval=1)
 171:             
 172:             if cpu_percent >= self.cpu_critical:
 173:                 return HealthStatus.CRITICAL
 174:             elif cpu_percent >= self.cpu_warning:
 175:                 return HealthStatus.WARNING
 176:             return HealthStatus.HEALTHY
 177:         except:
 178:             return HealthStatus.WARNING
 179:     
 180:     def _check_memory(self) -> HealthStatus:
 181:         """Check memory usage"""
 182:         try:
 183:             memory = psutil.virtual_memory()
 184:             
 185:             if memory.percent >= self.memory_critical:
 186:                 return HealthStatus.CRITICAL
 187:             elif memory.percent >= self.memory_warning:
 188:                 return HealthStatus.WARNING
 189:             return HealthStatus.HEALTHY
 190:         except:
 191:             return HealthStatus.WARNING
 192:     
 193:     def _check_disk(self) -> HealthStatus:
 194:         """Check disk usage"""
 195:         try:
 196:             disk = psutil.disk_usage('/')
 197:             
 198:             if disk.percent >= self.disk_critical:
 199:                 return HealthStatus.CRITICAL
 200:             elif disk.percent >= self.disk_warning:
 201:                 return HealthStatus.WARNING
 202:             return HealthStatus.HEALTHY
 203:         except:
 204:             return HealthStatus.WARNING
 205:     
 206:     def _log_status(self, status: dict):
 207:         """Log status to history"""
 208:         entry = {
 209:             'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(),
 210:             'status': {k: v.value if isinstance(v, HealthStatus) else v 
 211:                        for k, v in status.items()},
 212:         }
 213:         
 214:         self.history.append(entry)
 215:         
 216:         # Trim history
 217:         if len(self.history) > self.max_history:
 218:             self.history = self.history[-self.max_history:]
 219:     
 220:     def _send_alert(self, status: dict):
 221:         """Send alert for critical status"""
 222:         alert = {
 223:             'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(),
 224:             'status': status['overall'].value,
 225:             'details': {k: v.value if isinstance(v, HealthStatus) else v 
 226:                         for k, v in status.items()},
 227:         }
 228:         
 229:         print(f"🚨 HEALTH ALERT: {alert}")
 230:         
 231:         for callback in self.alert_callbacks:
 232:             try:
 233:                 callback(alert)
 234:             except:
 235:                 pass
 236:     
 237:     def get_status(self) -> dict:
 238:         """Get current health status"""
 239:         status = self._run_all_checks()
 240:         
 241:         # Add system info
 242:         try:
 243:             status['system'] = {
 244:                 'cpu_percent': psutil.cpu_percent(),
 245:                 'memory_percent': psutil.virtual_memory().percent,
 246:                 'disk_percent': psutil.disk_usage('/').percent,
 247:             }
 248:         except:
 249:             pass
 250:         
 251:         return {
 252:             k: v.value if isinstance(v, HealthStatus) else v 
 253:             for k, v in status.items()
 254:         }
 255:     
 256:     def get_history(self, hours: int = 24) -> List[dict]:
 257:         """Get health history"""
 258:         cutoff = datetime.now() - timedelta(hours=hours)
 259:         
 260:         return [
 261:             entry for entry in self.history
 262:             if datetime.fromisoformat(entry['timestamp']) > cutoff
 263:         ]

FILE: core\prefetcher.py
================================================================================
   1: """
   2: Smart Prefetcher - Download and analyze next songs in advance
   3: Fixes: Blocking downloads, no lookahead, cold starts, thread crashes
   4: """
   5: 
   6: import threading
   7: import queue
   8: import time
   9: from typing import Dict, List, Optional
  10: from dataclasses import dataclass
  11: from datetime import datetime
  12: 
  13: 
  14: @dataclass
  15: class PrefetchJob:
  16:     song_id: str
  17:     priority: int
  18:     requested_at: float
  19:     status: str = 'pending'  # pending, downloading, analyzing, ready, failed
  20:     filepath: Optional[str] = None
  21:     analysis: Optional[dict] = None
  22:     error: Optional[str] = None
  23: 
  24: 
  25: class Prefetcher:
  26:     """
  27:     Smart prefetcher that:
  28:     - Downloads next N songs in advance
  29:     - Pre-analyzes if not in cache
  30:     - Prioritizes based on play probability
  31:     - Cleans up after playback
  32:     """
  33:     
  34:     def __init__(self, config, downloader, analyzer, cache_manager):
  35:         self.config = config
  36:         self.downloader = downloader
  37:         self.analyzer = analyzer
  38:         self.cache = cache_manager
  39:         
  40:         # How many songs to prefetch
  41:         self.lookahead = config.get('prefetch', {}).get('lookahead', 3)
  42:         
  43:         # Jobs and Thread Safety
  44:         self.jobs: Dict[str, PrefetchJob] = {}
  45:         self.job_queue = queue.PriorityQueue()
  46:         self.jobs_lock = threading.Lock()  # FIXED: Protects dictionary from multi-thread crashes!
  47:         
  48:         # Workers
  49:         self.is_running = False
  50:         self.download_thread = None
  51:         self.analyze_thread = None
  52:         
  53:         # Currently playing
  54:         self.current_song_id = None
  55:         
  56:     def start(self):
  57:         """Start prefetcher"""
  58:         if self.is_running:
  59:             return
  60:         
  61:         self.is_running = True
  62:         
  63:         self.download_thread = threading.Thread(
  64:             target=self._download_loop,
  65:             daemon=True
  66:         )
  67:         self.download_thread.start()
  68:         
  69:         self.analyze_thread = threading.Thread(
  70:             target=self._analyze_loop,
  71:             daemon=True
  72:         )
  73:         self.analyze_thread.start()
  74:         
  75:         print("🚀 Prefetcher started")
  76:     
  77:     def stop(self):
  78:         """Stop prefetcher"""
  79:         self.is_running = False
  80:         print("⏹️ Prefetcher stopped")
  81:     
  82:     def prefetch(self, song_ids: List[str], song_metadata: Dict[str, dict]):
  83:         """
  84:         Request prefetch for list of song IDs
  85:         Called when selector picks next songs
  86:         """
  87:         for priority, song_id in enumerate(song_ids[:self.lookahead]):
  88:             with self.jobs_lock:
  89:                 if song_id in self.jobs:
  90:                     continue
  91:                 
  92:                 job = PrefetchJob(
  93:                     song_id=song_id,
  94:                     priority=priority,
  95:                     requested_at=time.time(),
  96:                 )
  97:                 self.jobs[song_id] = job
  98:             
  99:             # Check if already cached
 100:             if self.cache.exists('audio', song_id):
 101:                 with self.jobs_lock:
 102:                     self.jobs[song_id].filepath = self.cache.get('audio', song_id)
 103:                     self.jobs[song_id].status = 'analyzing'
 104:             else:
 105:                 self.job_queue.put((priority, song_id, 'download'))
 106:     
 107:     def get_ready_song(self, song_id: str) -> Optional[dict]:
 108:         """
 109:         Get prefetched song if ready
 110:         Returns {'filepath': ..., 'analysis': ...} or None
 111:         """
 112:         with self.jobs_lock:
 113:             if song_id not in self.jobs:
 114:                 return None
 115:             
 116:             job = self.jobs[song_id]
 117:             
 118:             if job.status == 'ready':
 119:                 return {
 120:                     'filepath': job.filepath,
 121:                     'analysis': job.analysis,
 122:                 }
 123:             
 124:         return None
 125:     
 126:     def wait_for_song(self, song_id: str, timeout: float = 30) -> Optional[dict]:
 127:         """
 128:         Wait for song to be ready
 129:         Returns result or None if timeout
 130:         """
 131:         start = time.time()
 132:         
 133:         while time.time() - start < timeout:
 134:             result = self.get_ready_song(song_id)
 135:             if result:
 136:                 return result
 137:             
 138:             # Check if failed
 139:             with self.jobs_lock:
 140:                 if song_id in self.jobs and self.jobs[song_id].status == 'failed':
 141:                     return None
 142:             
 143:             time.sleep(0.5)
 144:         
 145:         return None
 146:     
 147:     def set_current_song(self, song_id: str):
 148:         """
 149:         Mark song as currently playing
 150:         Cleans up older prefetched songs
 151:         """
 152:         self.current_song_id = song_id
 153:         
 154:         # Remove from jobs (no longer needed in prefetch)
 155:         with self.jobs_lock:
 156:             if song_id in self.jobs:
 157:                 del self.jobs[song_id]
 158:         
 159:         # Cleanup old jobs
 160:         self._cleanup_old_jobs()
 161:     
 162:     def _download_loop(self):
 163:         """Download worker loop"""
 164:         while self.is_running:
 165:             try:
 166:                 priority, song_id, action = self.job_queue.get(timeout=1)
 167:                 
 168:                 if action != 'download':
 169:                     continue
 170:                 
 171:                 with self.jobs_lock:
 172:                     if song_id not in self.jobs:
 173:                         continue
 174:                     job = self.jobs[song_id]
 175:                     if job.status != 'pending':
 176:                         continue
 177:                     job.status = 'downloading'
 178:                 
 179:                 try:
 180:                     # Get song URL from metadata
 181:                     url = f"https://youtube.com/watch?v={song_id}"
 182:                     
 183:                     filepath = self.downloader.download_song(url, song_id)
 184:                     
 185:                     with self.jobs_lock:
 186:                         if song_id in self.jobs:
 187:                             self.jobs[song_id].filepath = filepath
 188:                             self.jobs[song_id].status = 'analyzing'
 189:                     
 190:                     # Queue for analysis
 191:                     self.job_queue.put((priority, song_id, 'analyze'))
 192:                     
 193:                 except Exception as e:
 194:                     with self.jobs_lock:
 195:                         if song_id in self.jobs:
 196:                             self.jobs[song_id].status = 'failed'
 197:                             self.jobs[song_id].error = str(e)
 198:                     print(f"❌ Prefetch download failed for {song_id}: {e}")
 199:                 
 200:             except queue.Empty:
 201:                 continue
 202:             except Exception as e:
 203:                 print(f"❌ Prefetch download error: {e}")
 204:     
 205:     def _analyze_loop(self):
 206:         """Analysis worker loop - FIXED (Duplicate removed, lock added)"""
 207:         while self.is_running:
 208:             try:
 209:                 jobs_processed = 0
 210:                 
 211:                 # Copy jobs safely to iterate without lock blocking download thread too long
 212:                 with self.jobs_lock:
 213:                     jobs_to_check = list(self.jobs.values())
 214:                 
 215:                 # Find jobs needing analysis
 216:                 for job in jobs_to_check:
 217:                     # Double check status safely
 218:                     with self.jobs_lock:
 219:                         if job.song_id not in self.jobs:
 220:                             continue
 221:                         current_status = self.jobs[job.song_id].status
 222:                         
 223:                     if current_status != 'analyzing' or not job.filepath:
 224:                         continue
 225:                     
 226:                     jobs_processed += 1
 227:                     
 228:                     try:
 229:                         # Check cache first
 230:                         cached = self.cache.get('metadata', job.song_id)
 231:                         if cached:
 232:                             import json
 233:                             with open(cached, 'r') as f:
 234:                                 analysis_data = json.load(f)
 235:                             with self.jobs_lock:
 236:                                 if job.song_id in self.jobs:
 237:                                     self.jobs[job.song_id].analysis = analysis_data
 238:                                     self.jobs[job.song_id].status = 'ready'
 239:                             continue
 240:                         
 241:                         # Run analysis
 242:                         analysis = self.analyzer.analyze_track(
 243:                             job.filepath, job.song_id
 244:                         )
 245:                         
 246:                         with self.jobs_lock:
 247:                             if job.song_id in self.jobs:
 248:                                 self.jobs[job.song_id].analysis = analysis
 249:                                 self.jobs[job.song_id].status = 'ready'
 250:                         
 251:                         print(f"✅ Prefetched: {job.song_id}")
 252:                         
 253:                     except Exception as e:
 254:                         with self.jobs_lock:
 255:                             if job.song_id in self.jobs:
 256:                                 self.jobs[job.song_id].status = 'failed'
 257:                                 self.jobs[job.song_id].error = str(e)
 258:                         print(f"❌ Prefetch analysis failed for {job.song_id}: {e}")
 259:                 
 260:                 time.sleep(1 if jobs_processed == 0 else 0.1)
 261:                 
 262:             except Exception as e:
 263:                 print(f"❌ Prefetch analyze error: {e}")
 264:                 time.sleep(1)
 265:     
 266:     def _cleanup_old_jobs(self):
 267:         """Remove old completed/failed jobs"""
 268:         current_time = time.time()
 269:         max_age = 600  # 10 minutes
 270:         
 271:         to_remove = []
 272:         
 273:         with self.jobs_lock:
 274:             for song_id, job in self.jobs.items():
 275:                 if song_id == self.current_song_id:
 276:                     continue
 277:                 
 278:                 age = current_time - job.requested_at
 279:                 
 280:                 if age > max_age and job.status in ['ready', 'failed']:
 281:                     to_remove.append(song_id)
 282:                     
 283:                     # Delete audio file to save space
 284:                     if job.filepath and job.status == 'ready':
 285:                         try:
 286:                             self.cache.delete('audio', song_id)
 287:                         except:
 288:                             pass
 289:             
 290:             for song_id in to_remove:
 291:                 del self.jobs[song_id]
 292:     
 293:     def get_stats(self) -> dict:
 294:         """Get prefetcher statistics"""
 295:         status_counts = {}
 296:         with self.jobs_lock:
 297:             for job in self.jobs.values():
 298:                 status_counts[job.status] = status_counts.get(job.status, 0) + 1
 299:             total_jobs = len(self.jobs)
 300:             
 301:         return {
 302:             'total_jobs': total_jobs,
 303:             'queue_size': self.job_queue.qsize(),
 304:             'status_counts': status_counts,
 305:             'lookahead': self.lookahead,
 306:         }



================================================================================
FILE: core\task_queue.py
================================================================================
   1: """
   2: Async Task Queue for background processing
   3: Fixes: Blocking operations, no prioritization, no retry logic
   4: """
   5: 
   6: import threading
   7: import queue
   8: import time
   9: from enum import Enum
  10: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
  11: from typing import Callable, Any, Optional
  12: from datetime import datetime
  13: import traceback
  14: 
  15: 
  16: class TaskPriority(Enum):
  17:     CRITICAL = 0   # Must run immediately (audio playback)
  18:     HIGH = 1       # Run soon (next song download)
  19:     NORMAL = 2     # Run when possible (analysis)
  20:     LOW = 3        # Run when idle (self-improvement)
  21:     BACKGROUND = 4 # Run overnight (training)
  22: 
  23: 
  24: @dataclass(order=True)
  25: class Task:
  26:     priority: int
  27:     created_at: float = field(compare=False)
  28:     name: str = field(compare=False)
  29:     func: Callable = field(compare=False)
  30:     args: tuple = field(default=(), compare=False)
  31:     kwargs: dict = field(default_factory=dict, compare=False)
  32:     retries: int = field(default=3, compare=False)
  33:     retry_delay: float = field(default=1.0, compare=False)
  34:     timeout: Optional[float] = field(default=None, compare=False)
  35:     callback: Optional[Callable] = field(default=None, compare=False)
  36:     error_callback: Optional[Callable] = field(default=None, compare=False)
  37: 
  38: 
  39: class TaskQueue:
  40:     """
  41:     Priority-based async task queue with:
  42:     - Priority levels
  43:     - Retry logic
  44:     - Timeout handling
  45:     - Worker pool
  46:     - Health monitoring
  47:     """
  48:     
  49:     def __init__(self, num_workers=4):
  50:         self.queue = queue.PriorityQueue()
  51:         self.num_workers = num_workers
  52:         self.workers = []
  53:         self.is_running = False
  54:         
  55:         # Stats
  56:         self.tasks_completed = 0
  57:         self.tasks_failed = 0
  58:         self.tasks_pending = 0
  59:         
  60:         # Health
  61:         self.last_activity = datetime.now()
  62:         self.worker_status = {}
  63:         
  64:     def start(self):
  65:         """Start worker threads"""
  66:         if self.is_running:
  67:             return
  68:             
  69:         self.is_running = True
  70:         
  71:         for i in range(self.num_workers):
  72:             worker = threading.Thread(
  73:                 target=self._worker_loop,
  74:                 args=(i,),
  75:                 daemon=True,
  76:                 name=f"TaskWorker-{i}"
  77:             )
  78:             worker.start()
  79:             self.workers.append(worker)
  80:             self.worker_status[i] = 'idle'
  81:         
  82:         print(f"✅ Task queue started with {self.num_workers} workers")
  83:     
  84:     def stop(self):
  85:         """Stop all workers"""
  86:         self.is_running = False
  87:         
  88:         # Add poison pills to stop workers
  89:         for _ in range(self.num_workers):
  90:             self.queue.put(Task(
  91:                 priority=999,
  92:                 created_at=time.time(),
  93:                 name='__STOP__',
  94:                 func=lambda: None
  95:             ))
  96:         
  97:         # Wait for workers
  98:         for worker in self.workers:
  99:             worker.join(timeout=2)
 100:         
 101:         self.workers.clear()
 102:         print("🛑 Task queue stopped")
 103:     
 104:     def add(self, 
 105:             func: Callable,
 106:             args: tuple = (),
 107:             kwargs: dict = None,
 108:             priority: TaskPriority = TaskPriority.NORMAL,
 109:             name: str = None,
 110:             retries: int = 3,
 111:             timeout: float = None,
 112:             callback: Callable = None,
 113:             error_callback: Callable = None) -> None:
 114:         """Add task to queue"""
 115:         
 116:         task = Task(
 117:             priority=priority.value,
 118:             created_at=time.time(),
 119:             name=name or func.__name__,
 120:             func=func,
 121:             args=args,
 122:             kwargs=kwargs or {},
 123:             retries=retries,
 124:             timeout=timeout,
 125:             callback=callback,
 126:             error_callback=error_callback,
 127:         )
 128:         
 129:         self.queue.put(task)
 130:         self.tasks_pending += 1
 131:     
 132:     def add_critical(self, func, *args, **kwargs):
 133:         """Shortcut for critical priority tasks"""
 134:         self.add(func, args, kwargs, priority=TaskPriority.CRITICAL)
 135:     
 136:     def add_high(self, func, *args, **kwargs):
 137:         """Shortcut for high priority tasks"""
 138:         self.add(func, args, kwargs, priority=TaskPriority.HIGH)
 139:     
 140:     def add_low(self, func, *args, **kwargs):
 141:         """Shortcut for low priority tasks"""
 142:         self.add(func, args, kwargs, priority=TaskPriority.LOW)
 143:     
 144:     def _worker_loop(self, worker_id):
 145:         """Main worker loop"""
 146:         while self.is_running:
 147:             try:
 148:                 # Get task (blocks until available)
 149:                 task = self.queue.get(timeout=1)
 150:                 
 151:                 if task.name == '__STOP__':
 152:                     break
 153:                 
 154:                 self.worker_status[worker_id] = f'running:{task.name}'
 155:                 self.last_activity = datetime.now()
 156:                 
 157:                 # Execute task with retries
 158:                 success = self._execute_task(task, worker_id)
 159:                 
 160:                 if success:
 161:                     self.tasks_completed += 1
 162:                 else:
 163:                     self.tasks_failed += 1
 164:                 
 165:                 self.tasks_pending -= 1
 166:                 self.worker_status[worker_id] = 'idle'
 167:                 
 168:             except queue.Empty:
 169:                 continue
 170:             except Exception as e:
 171:                 print(f"❌ Worker {worker_id} error: {e}")
 172:                 self.worker_status[worker_id] = 'error'
 173:     
 174:     def _execute_task(self, task: Task, worker_id: int) -> bool:
 175:         """Execute task with retry logic"""
 176:         last_error = None
 177:         
 178:         for attempt in range(task.retries):
 179:             try:
 180:                 # Execute with timeout if specified
 181:                 if task.timeout:
 182:                     result = self._run_with_timeout(
 183:                         task.func, 
 184:                         task.args, 
 185:                         task.kwargs,
 186:                         task.timeout
 187:                     )
 188:                 else:
 189:                     result = task.func(*task.args, **task.kwargs)
 190:                 
 191:                 # Success callback
 192:                 if task.callback:
 193:                     try:
 194:                         task.callback(result)
 195:                     except:
 196:                         pass
 197:                 
 198:                 return True
 199:                 
 200:             except Exception as e:
 201:                 last_error = e
 202:                 print(f"⚠️ Task '{task.name}' attempt {attempt + 1}/{task.retries} failed: {e}")
 203:                 
 204:                 if attempt < task.retries - 1:
 205:                     time.sleep(task.retry_delay * (attempt + 1))
 206:         
 207:         # All retries failed
 208:         print(f"❌ Task '{task.name}' failed after {task.retries} attempts")
 209:         
 210:         if task.error_callback:
 211:             try:
 212:                 task.error_callback(last_error)
 213:             except:
 214:                 pass
 215:         
 216:         return False
 217:     
 218:     def _run_with_timeout(self, func, args, kwargs, timeout):
 219:         """Run function with timeout"""
 220:         result = [None]
 221:         error = [None]
 222:         
 223:         def target():
 224:             try:
 225:                 result[0] = func(*args, **kwargs)
 226:             except Exception as e:
 227:                 error[0] = e
 228:         
 229:         thread = threading.Thread(target=target)
 230:         thread.start()
 231:         thread.join(timeout=timeout)
 232:         
 233:         if thread.is_alive():
 234:             raise TimeoutError(f"Task timed out after {timeout}s")
 235:         
 236:         if error[0]:
 237:             raise error[0]
 238:         
 239:         return result[0]
 240:     
 241:     def get_stats(self):
 242:         """Get queue statistics"""
 243:         return {
 244:             'pending': self.tasks_pending,
 245:             'completed': self.tasks_completed,
 246:             'failed': self.tasks_failed,
 247:             'workers': self.worker_status.copy(),
 248:             'last_activity': self.last_activity.isoformat(),
 249:             'queue_size': self.queue.qsize(),
 250:         }
 251:     
 252:     def is_healthy(self) -> bool:
 253:         """Check if queue is healthy"""
 254:         # Check for stuck workers
 255:         if (datetime.now() - self.last_activity).seconds > 300:
 256:             return False
 257:         
 258:         # Check for error workers
 259:         if 'error' in self.worker_status.values():
 260:             return False
 261:         
 262:         return True



================================================================================
FILE: docs\WIKI.md
================================================================================
   1: # 📖 AI DJ Knowledge Wiki
   2: 
   3: Welcome to the internal knowledge base for the Autonomous AI DJ Project.
   4: 
   5: ## 📂 Navigation Index
   6: - [Architecture Diagram](../ARCHITECTURE.md)
   7: - [README (Home)](../README.md)
   8: - [Transition Techniques](#transition-techniques)
   9: - [Innovation Batching](#innovation-batching)
  10: 
  11: ### Running the Mobile Tester
  12: 1. Connect your phone to the same Wi-Fi or use the Public Cloudflare link.
  13: 2. Run `python mobile_tester.py`.
  14: 3. Open the link provided in the console.
  15: 
  16: ### Adding Music
  17: - Place `.mp3` files in the `data/library` directory.
  18: - Ensure filenames are clean (Artist - Title.mp3).
  19: - The system requires at least **2 songs** to start generating transitions.
  20: 
  21: ## 🧠 The AI Brain
  22: 
  23: ### Transition Agent
  24: The brain uses logic to pick between:
  25: - **Beatmatching**: Matching rhythms for smooth flow.
  26: - **Filter Sweeps**: Using HPF/LPF for energy shifts.
  27: - **Innovation Mode**: Creating new hybrid techniques by mutating existing rules.
  28: 
  29: ### Validation Agent
  30: Every mix is pre-checked. If the judge sees:
  31: - Long silence
  32: - Terrible beat-match
  33: - Clipping audio
  34: ...It will **delete** the mix and try again automatically.
  35: 
  36: ## 🧪 Novel Techniques & Innovation
  37: 
  38: ### Innovation Batching (Best of 10)
  39: The system continuously generates experimental transitions. To ensure you only see high-quality inventions:
  40: 1. The **Transition Agent** creates 10 "Novel" candidates.
  41: 2. The **Validation Agent** scores each one.
  42: 3. Only the **highest scoring** mix is sent to you via **ntfy** for approval.
  43: 4. The remaining 9 are logged for training but kept out of your main queue.
  44: 
  45: ## 📢 Developer Communication
  46: - **Automatic Notifications**: The AI Agent (Antigravity) will send the latest mobile links to the `ntfy` topic `dj-agent-parth` every time a file is edited. This ensures real-time access to the testing UI without needing to check the terminal.
  47: 
  48: ## 🛠️ Maintenance & Tools
  49: 
  50: ### Synchronizing Code
  51: Use `tools/sync_github.py` to push your latest changes to the remote repository.
  52: 
  53: ### Troubleshooting
  54: - **No Sound**: Check if `ffmpeg` is installed and in your System PATH.
  55: - **503 Error**: Restart the `mobile_tester.py` to refresh the Cloudflare tunnel.
  56: - **Brain Freeze**: If generation hangs, check `data/logs/error.log`.
  57: 
  58: ## 📈 Improving the System
  59: The Agent learns from your **Pass/Fail** ratings. 
  60: - **Pass**: Increases the probability of the used technique.
  61: - **Fail**: Decreases probability and triggers a retry.
  62: - **Text Feedback**: Read by the developer (and eventually the agent) to fine-tune specific behaviors.

FILE: ingestion\dj_tutorial_scraper.py
================================================================================
   1: import yt_dlp
   2: import os
   3: import json
   4: try:
   5:     import whisper
   6: except ImportError:
   7:     whisper = None
   8: 
   9: 
  10: class DJTutorialScraper:
  11:     """
  12:     Scrapes DJ tutorial channels to extract
  13:     transition techniques for AI training
  14:     """
  15:     def __init__(self, config):
  16:         self.config = config
  17:         self.training_dir = config['paths']['training_data']
  18:         os.makedirs(self.training_dir, exist_ok=True)
  19:         self.whisper_model = None
  20: 
  21:     def scrape_all_channels(self):
  22:         """Scrape all configured tutorial channels"""
  23:         channels = self.config['youtube_channels']['tutorial_sources']
  24:         all_data = []
  25: 
  26:         for channel in channels:
  27:             print(f"\n📺 Scraping: {channel}")
  28:             data = self.scrape_channel(channel)
  29:             all_data.extend(data)
  30: 
  31:         # Save training data
  32:         output_path = os.path.join(
  33:             self.training_dir, 'tutorial_data.json'
  34:         )
  35:         with open(output_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
  36:             json.dump(all_data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
  37: 
  38:         print(f"\n✅ Scraped {len(all_data)} tutorials")
  39:         return all_data
  40: 
  41:     def scrape_channel(self, channel_url, max_videos=20):
  42:         """Scrape a single channel"""
  43:         ydl_opts = {
  44:             'quiet': True,
  45:             'extract_flat': True,
  46:             'playlistend': max_videos,
  47:         }
  48: 
  49:         videos = []
  50:         with yt_dlp.YoutubeDL(ydl_opts) as ydl:
  51:             info = ydl.extract_info(channel_url, download=False)
  52:             entries = info.get('entries', [])
  53: 
  54:             for entry in entries:
  55:                 if entry:
  56:                     videos.append({
  57:                         'id': entry.get('id'),
  58:                         'title': entry.get('title'),
  59:                         'url': f"https://youtube.com/watch?v={entry.get('id')}",
  60:                         'duration': entry.get('duration', 0)
  61:                     })
  62: 
  63:         results = []
  64:         for video in videos:
  65:             # Skip very long videos (full sets)
  66:             if video['duration'] and video['duration'] > 1800:
  67:                 continue
  68: 
  69:             transcript = self._transcribe_video(video)
  70:             if transcript:
  71:                 techniques = self._extract_techniques(transcript)
  72:                 results.append({
  73:                     'video_id': video['id'],
  74:                     'title': video['title'],
  75:                     'url': video['url'],
  76:                     'transcript': transcript,
  77:                     'techniques_mentioned': techniques
  78:                 })
  79: 
  80:         return results
  81: 
  82:     def _transcribe_video(self, video):
  83:         """Download and transcribe a tutorial video"""
  84:         if not self.whisper_model:
  85:             print("   Loading Whisper model...")
  86:             self.whisper_model = whisper.load_model("base")
  87: 
  88:         audio_path = os.path.join(
  89:             self.training_dir, f"tmp_{video['id']}.mp3"
  90:         )
  91: 
  92:         try:
  93:             ydl_opts = {
  94:                 'format': 'bestaudio/best',
  95:                 'outtmpl': audio_path.replace('.mp3', '.%(ext)s'),
  96:                 'postprocessors': [{
  97:                     'key': 'FFmpegExtractAudio',
  98:                     'preferredcodec': 'mp3',
  99:                     'preferredquality': '128',
 100:                 }],
 101:                 'quiet': True,
 102:             }
 103: 
 104:             with yt_dlp.YoutubeDL(ydl_opts) as ydl:
 105:                 ydl.download([video['url']])
 106: 
 107:             result = self.whisper_model.transcribe(audio_path)
 108:             return result['text']
 109: 
 110:         except Exception as e:
 111:             print(f"   ❌ Transcription failed: {e}")
 112:             return None
 113:         finally:
 114:             if os.path.exists(audio_path):
 115:                 os.remove(audio_path)
 116: 
 117:     def _extract_techniques(self, transcript):
 118:         """Extract DJ technique mentions from transcript"""
 119:         keywords = [
 120:             'phrase', 'bar', 'beat', 'crossfade', 'beatmatch',
 121:             'filter', 'echo', 'reverb', 'loop', 'roll', 'spinback',
 122:             'scratch', 'key', 'camelot', 'harmonic', 'energy',
 123:             'drop', 'build', 'breakdown', 'transition', 'mix in',
 124:             'mix out', 'eq', 'high pass', 'low pass', 'acapella',
 125:             'stems', 'vocal', 'intro', 'outro'
 126:         ]
 127: 
 128:         found = {}
 129:         lower_transcript = transcript.lower()
 130: 
 131:         for keyword in keywords:
 132:             count = lower_transcript.count(keyword)
 133:             if count > 0:
 134:                 found[keyword] = count
 135: 
 136:         return found

FILE: ingestion\downloader.py
================================================================================
   1: import yt_dlp
   2: import os
   3: import json
   4: import signal
   5: from tqdm import tqdm
   6: 
   7: class PlaylistDownloader:
   8:     def __init__(self, config):
   9:         self.config = config
  10:         self.cache_dir = config['paths']['audio_cache']
  11:         self.metadata_dir = config['paths']['metadata']
  12:         self.playlist_cache_file = "data/playlist_cache.json"
  13:         os.makedirs(self.cache_dir, exist_ok=True)
  14:         
  15:         # Ensure cookies file exists to prevent crash
  16:         self.cookie_path = self.config.get('youtube', {}).get('cookie_file', 'data/yt_cookies.txt')
  17:         if not os.path.exists(self.cookie_path):
  18:             os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(self.cookie_path) or '.', exist_ok=True)
  19:             open(self.cookie_path, 'a').close()
  20: 
  21:     def get_playlist_metadata(self, playlist_url):
  22:         ydl_opts = {
  23:             'quiet': True,
  24:             'extract_flat': True,
  25:             'skip_download': True,
  26:             'http_headers': {
  27:                 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36',
  28:             }
  29:         }
  30:         # Only add cookiefile if it actually has data
  31:         if os.path.exists(self.cookie_path) and os.path.getsize(self.cookie_path) > 0:
  32:             ydl_opts['cookiefile'] = self.cookie_path
  33:             
  34:         try:
  35:             with yt_dlp.YoutubeDL(ydl_opts) as ydl:
  36:                 info = ydl.extract_info(playlist_url, download=False)
  37: 
  38:             songs = []
  39:             for entry in info.get('entries', []):
  40:                 if entry:
  41:                     songs.append({
  42:                         'id': entry.get('id'),
  43:                         'title': entry.get('title', 'Unknown'),
  44:                         'url': f"https://youtube.com/watch?v={entry.get('id')}",
  45:                         'duration': entry.get('duration', 0),
  46:                         'thumbnail': entry.get('thumbnail', ''),
  47:                         'cached': False,
  48:                         'analyzed': False
  49:                     })
  50: 
  51:             # Save playlist cache
  52:             with open(self.playlist_cache_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
  53:                 json.dump(songs, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
  54: 
  55:             print(f"✅ Found {len(songs)} songs")
  56:             return songs
  57:             
  58:         except Exception as e:
  59:             print(f"❌ YouTube Playlist Fetch Failed: {e}")
  60:             return []
  61: 
  62:     def load_cached_playlist(self):
  63:         if os.path.exists(self.playlist_cache_file):
  64:             try:
  65:                 with open(self.playlist_cache_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
  66:                     return json.load(f)
  67:             except:
  68:                 return []
  69:         return []
  70: 
  71:     def download_song(self, url, song_id, drive_manager=None, timeout=300):
  72:         output_path = os.path.join(self.cache_dir, f"{song_id}.mp3")
  73:         
  74:         # Check if already local
  75:         if os.path.exists(output_path):
  76:             return output_path
  77: 
  78:         # ANTI-BOT ARMOR ADDED HERE
  79:         ydl_opts = {
  80:             'format': 'bestaudio/best',
  81:             'outtmpl': os.path.join(self.cache_dir, f"{song_id}.%(ext)s"),
  82:             'cookiefile': self.cookie_path,
  83:             'http_headers': {
  84:                 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36',
  85:             },
  86:             # Add jitter to bypass anti-bot rate limits
  87:             'sleep_requests': 2,
  88:             'min_sleep_interval': 5,
  89:             'max_sleep_interval': 15,
  90:             'postprocessors': [{
  91:                 'key': 'FFmpegExtractAudio',
  92:                 'preferredcodec': 'mp3',
  93:                 'preferredquality': '192',
  94:             }],
  95:             'quiet': True,
  96:             'no_warnings': True,
  97:             'socket_timeout': 30,
  98:             'retries': 3,
  99:         }
 100:         
 101:         def timeout_handler(signum, frame):
 102:             raise TimeoutError(f"Download timed out after {timeout}s")
 103:         
 104:         # Set timeout (Unix only, must be main thread)
 105:         old_handler = None
 106:         try:
 107:             old_handler = signal.signal(signal.SIGALRM, timeout_handler)
 108:             signal.alarm(timeout)
 109:         except (AttributeError, ValueError):
 110:             pass  # Windows or running in background thread safely skips this
 111:         
 112:         try:
 113:             with yt_dlp.YoutubeDL(ydl_opts) as ydl:
 114:                 ydl.download([url])
 115:             
 116:             # Verify file actually wrote to disk
 117:             if os.path.exists(output_path):
 118:                 return output_path
 119:             else:
 120:                 return None
 121:         except Exception as e:
 122:             # FIXED: Catch crash, print error, return None instead of breaking app
 123:             print(f"❌ Download error for {song_id}: {str(e)[:100]}")
 124:             return None
 125:         finally:
 126:             try:
 127:                 if old_handler is not None:
 128:                     signal.alarm(0)
 129:                     signal.signal(signal.SIGALRM, old_handler)
 130:             except (AttributeError, ValueError):
 131:                 pass
 132: 
 133:     def _get_account_for_song(self, song_id):
 134:         """Uniformly distribute songs across all available accounts"""
 135:         accounts = self.config.get('storage', {}).get('drive_accounts', ['account_1'])
 136:         if not accounts:
 137:             accounts = ['account_1']
 138:         val = sum(ord(c) for c in song_id)
 139:         return accounts[val % len(accounts)]
 140: 
 141:     def upload_to_drive(self, song_id, drive_manager):
 142:         """Upload local MP3 to the assigned Drive account"""
 143:         # FIXED: Guard against None drive_manager
 144:         if not drive_manager:
 145:             print("❌ DriveManager not initialized")
 146:             return None
 147:             
 148:         local_path = os.path.join(self.cache_dir, f"{song_id}.mp3")
 149:         if not os.path.exists(local_path):
 150:             return None
 151:             
 152:         account_id = self._get_account_for_song(song_id)
 153:         folder_name = "AI_DJ_Library"
 154:         
 155:         print(f"☁️ Offloading {song_id} to Google Drive ({account_id})...")
 156:         try:
 157:             drive_id = drive_manager.upload_file(account_id, local_path, folder_name)
 158:             # Once uploaded, we can delete local
 159:             if drive_id:
 160:                 os.remove(local_path)
 161:                 print(f"✅ Offloaded. Saved space on disk!")
 162:             return drive_id
 163:         except Exception as e:
 164:             print(f"❌ Drive upload failed: {str(e)[:100]}")
 165:             return None
 166: 
 167:     def delete_audio(self, song_id):
 168:         filepath = os.path.join(self.cache_dir, f"{song_id}.mp3")
 169:         if os.path.exists(filepath):
 170:             try:
 171:                 os.remove(filepath)
 172:             except Exception:
 173:                 pass

================================================================================
FILE: ingestion\lyrics_fetcher.py
================================================================================
   1: import os
   2: import json
   3: import requests
   4: from langdetect import detect
   5: try:
   6:     import whisper
   7: except ImportError:
   8:     whisper = None
   9: 
  10: 
  11: class LyricsFetcher:
  12:     def __init__(self, config):
  13:         self.config = config
  14:         self.lyrics_dir = config['paths']['lyrics']
  15:         self.genius_token = os.getenv('GENIUS_API_TOKEN', '')
  16:         self.whisper_model = None
  17:         os.makedirs(self.lyrics_dir, exist_ok=True)
  18: 
  19:     def fetch(self, title, song_id, vocals_path=None):
  20:         """Try Genius first, fall back to Whisper transcription"""
  21:         cache_path = os.path.join(self.lyrics_dir, f"{song_id}.json")
  22:         
  23:         if os.path.exists(cache_path):
  24:             with open(cache_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
  25:                 return json.load(f)
  26:         
  27:         lyrics_data = None
  28:         
  29:         # Try Genius API first
  30:         if self.genius_token:
  31:             lyrics_data = self._fetch_genius(title)
  32:         
  33:         # Fall back to Whisper
  34:         if not lyrics_data and vocals_path and os.path.exists(vocals_path):
  35:             lyrics_data = self._transcribe_whisper(vocals_path)
  36:         
  37:         if lyrics_data:
  38:             # Detect language
  39:             try:
  40:                 lyrics_data['language'] = detect(lyrics_data['text'])
  41:             except:
  42:                 lyrics_data['language'] = 'unknown'
  43:             
  44:             with open(cache_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
  45:                 json.dump(lyrics_data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
  46:         
  47:         return lyrics_data
  48: 
  49:     def _fetch_genius(self, title):
  50:         """Fetch from Genius API"""
  51:         try:
  52:             headers = {'Authorization': f'Bearer {self.genius_token}'}
  53:             params = {'q': title}
  54:             r = requests.get(
  55:                 'https://api.genius.com/search',
  56:                 headers=headers, params=params, timeout=10
  57:             )
  58:             data = r.json()
  59:             hits = data.get('response', {}).get('hits', [])
  60:             if hits:
  61:                 return {
  62:                     'text': hits[0]['result'].get('full_title', ''),
  63:                     'source': 'genius',
  64:                     'timed': False
  65:                 }
  66:         except Exception as e:
  67:             print(f"Genius fetch failed: {e}")
  68:         return None
  69: 
  70:     def _transcribe_whisper(self, vocals_path):
  71:         """Transcribe vocals using Whisper AI"""
  72:         if not self.whisper_model:
  73:             print("📝 Loading Whisper model...")
  74:             self.whisper_model = whisper.load_model("base")
  75:         
  76:         try:
  77:             result = self.whisper_model.transcribe(
  78:                 vocals_path,
  79:                 word_timestamps=True,
  80:                 task="transcribe"
  81:             )
  82:             
  83:             # Extract timed words
  84:             timed_words = []
  85:             for segment in result.get('segments', []):
  86:                 for word in segment.get('words', []):
  87:                     timed_words.append({
  88:                         'word': word['word'].strip(),
  89:                         'start': word['start'],
  90:                         'end': word['end']
  91:                     })
  92:             
  93:             return {
  94:                 'text': result['text'],
  95:                 'timed_words': timed_words,
  96:                 'language': result.get('language', 'unknown'),
  97:                 'source': 'whisper',
  98:                 'timed': True
  99:             }
 100:         except Exception as e:
 101:             print(f"Whisper transcription failed: {e}")
 102:             return None



================================================================================
FILE: ingestion\playlist_watcher.py
================================================================================
   1: import json
   2: import os
   3: 
   4: class PlaylistWatcher:
   5:     def __init__(self, config):
   6:         self.config = config
   7: 
   8:     def check_for_changes(self, playlist_url, current_playlist,
   9:                           metadata_cache, app):
  10:         """
  11:         Check YouTube playlist for added/removed songs
  12:         """
  13:         print("\n🔄 Checking playlist for changes...")
  14: 
  15:         # Get current playlist from YouTube
  16:         from ingestion.downloader import PlaylistDownloader
  17:         downloader = PlaylistDownloader(self.config)
  18:         fresh_playlist = downloader.get_playlist_metadata(playlist_url)
  19: 
  20:         current_ids = {s['id'] for s in current_playlist}
  21:         fresh_ids = {s['id'] for s in fresh_playlist}
  22: 
  23:         # Find new songs
  24:         new_ids = fresh_ids - current_ids
  25:         # Find removed songs (keep files per config)
  26:         removed_ids = current_ids - fresh_ids
  27: 
  28:         if new_ids:
  29:             print(f"✨ {len(new_ids)} new songs found!")
  30:             new_songs = [s for s in fresh_playlist if s['id'] in new_ids]
  31:             self._process_new_songs(new_songs, metadata_cache, app)
  32: 
  33:         if removed_ids:
  34:             print(f"🗑️  {len(removed_ids)} songs removed from playlist")
  35:             print("   (Files kept in cache per config)")
  36: 
  37:         if not new_ids and not removed_ids:
  38:             print("✅ No changes detected")
  39: 
  40:     def _process_new_songs(self, new_songs, metadata_cache, app):
  41:         """Process and analyze new songs"""
  42:         for song in new_songs:
  43:             print(f"   Processing new song: {song['title'][:40]}")
  44:             try:
  45:                 filepath = app.downloader.download_song(
  46:                     song['url'], song['id']
  47:                 )
  48:                 analysis = app.analyzer.analyze_track(filepath, song['id'])
  49:                 analysis['title'] = song['title']
  50: 
  51:                 phrases = app.phrase_detector.detect_phrases(
  52:                     filepath, song['id']
  53:                 )
  54:                 analysis['phrases'] = phrases
  55: 
  56:                 stems = app.stem_separator.separate(filepath, song['id'])
  57:                 analysis['stems'] = stems
  58: 
  59:                 lyrics = app.lyrics_fetcher.fetch(
  60:                     song['title'], song['id'],
  61:                     stems.get('vocals')
  62:                 )
  63:                 analysis['lyrics'] = lyrics
  64: 
  65:                 if lyrics:
  66:                     phonemes = app.vocal_analyzer.analyze(
  67:                         stems.get('vocals'), lyrics, song['id']
  68:                     )
  69:                     analysis['phonemes'] = phonemes
  70: 
  71:                 metadata_cache[song['id']] = analysis
  72:                 app.playlist.append(song)
  73: 
  74:                 # Update word index with new song
  75:                 app.wordplay_agent.build_word_index(metadata_cache)
  76: 
  77:                 app.downloader.delete_audio(song['id'])
  78:                 print(f"   ✅ New song ready: {song['title'][:40]}")
  79: 
  80:             except Exception as e:
  81:                 print(f"   ❌ Failed to process {song['title']}: {e}")



================================================================================
FILE: ingestion\stem_separator.py
================================================================================
   1: import os
   2: import subprocess
   3: import shutil
   4: 
   5: class StemSeparator:
   6:     def __init__(self, config):
   7:         self.config = config
   8:         self.stems_dir = config['paths']['stems']
   9:         self.cache_dir = config['paths']['audio_cache']
  10:         os.makedirs(self.stems_dir, exist_ok=True)
  11: 
  12:     def separate(self, filepath, song_id, start_time=0):
  13:         """
  14:         Ultra-optimized local separation.
  15:         Instead of processing a 4-minute song (which takes 100% CPU for 5 mins),
  16:         we trim the audio to just 90 seconds around the transition point.
  17:         This takes only ~15 seconds on a standard laptop and needs NO cloud!
  18:         """
  19:         song_stems_dir = os.path.join(self.stems_dir, song_id)
  20:         os.makedirs(song_stems_dir, exist_ok=True)
  21: 
  22:         stems = {
  23:             'vocals': os.path.join(song_stems_dir, 'vocals.wav'),
  24:             'melody': os.path.join(song_stems_dir, 'other.wav'),
  25:             'drums': os.path.join(song_stems_dir, 'drums.wav'),
  26:             'bass': os.path.join(song_stems_dir, 'bass.wav')
  27:         }
  28: 
  29:         # If we already have the stems, skip instantly!
  30:         if all(os.path.exists(v) for v in stems.values()):
  31:             return stems
  32: 
  33:         print(f"✂️  Trimming and Separating Stems for {song_id} (Ultra-Fast Mode)...")
  34: 
  35:         # 1. Trim audio to 90 seconds (saves 90% of computer power!)
  36:         temp_trim = os.path.join(self.cache_dir, f"{song_id}_trimmed.wav").replace("\\", "/")
  37:         try:
  38:             # Safely get a start time that won't go out of bounds
  39:             safe_start = max(0, start_time - 10)
  40:             subprocess.run([
  41:                 "ffmpeg", "-y", "-i", filepath.replace("\\", "/"), 
  42:                 "-ss", str(safe_start), "-t", "90", 
  43:                 "-ac", "2", "-ar", "44100", temp_trim
  44:             ], check=True, capture_output=True)
  45:         except Exception as e:
  46:             print(f"⚠️ FFmpeg trim failed, using full file: {e}")
  47:             temp_trim = filepath
  48: 
  49:         # 2. Run Local Demucs (Extremely fast on a 90s trim!)
  50:         try:
  51:             # This runs silently in the background
  52:             subprocess.run([
  53:                 "demucs", "-n", "htdemucs",
  54:                 "--out", self.stems_dir,
  55:                 temp_trim
  56:             ], check=True, capture_output=True)
  57: 
  58:             # Demucs outputs to: stems_dir/htdemucs/song_id_trimmed/...
  59:             trim_basename = os.path.basename(temp_trim).replace(".wav", "")
  60:             out_folder = os.path.join(self.stems_dir, "htdemucs", trim_basename)
  61: 
  62:             # Move stems to our expected dictionary paths
  63:             if os.path.exists(out_folder):
  64:                 for stem_name in ['vocals', 'other', 'drums', 'bass']:
  65:                     src = os.path.join(out_folder, f"{stem_name}.wav")
  66:                     
  67:                     if stem_name == 'other': dst = stems['melody']
  68:                     else: dst = stems[stem_name]
  69:                     
  70:                     if os.path.exists(src):
  71:                         shutil.copy(src, dst)
  72: 
  73:                 # Clean up Demucs default output folder
  74:                 shutil.rmtree(os.path.join(self.stems_dir, "htdemucs"), ignore_errors=True)
  75: 
  76:             print(f"✅ Fast Stems generated locally for: {song_id}")
  77: 
  78:         except FileNotFoundError:
  79:             print("❌ Demucs not installed! Fallback to original audio.")
  80:             print("💡 FIX: Open terminal and type: pip install -U demucs")
  81:             self._create_fake_stems(temp_trim, stems)
  82:             
  83:         except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
  84:             print(f"❌ Demucs processing failed: {e}")
  85:             self._create_fake_stems(temp_trim, stems)
  86: 
  87:         # Cleanup the temporary 90s trim file
  88:         if temp_trim != filepath and os.path.exists(temp_trim):
  89:             try:
  90:                 os.remove(temp_trim)
  91:             except Exception:
  92:                 pass
  93: 
  94:         return stems
  95: 
  96:     def _create_fake_stems(self, filepath, stems):
  97:         """
  98:         Ultimate safety net: If Demucs crashes or isn't installed, 
  99:         copy the original audio as the stems so the DJ app NEVER crashes.
 100:         """
 101:         print("⚠️ Using original audio as fallback stems to prevent app crash!")
 102:         for path in stems.values():
 103:             if not os.path.exists(path):
 104:                 shutil.copy(filepath, path)

 158:             print(f"{'='*60}")
 159: 
 160:             # Skip if already completed
 161:             if self.progress.get(channel_name, {}).get('completed'):
 162:                 print(f"   ✅ Already processed - skipping")
 163:                 continue
 164: 
 165:             self._process_channel(channel_name, channel_config)
 166: 
 167:         # Final save
 168:         self._save_all_results()
 169: 
 170:         print(f"""
 171: ╔══════════════════════════════════════════╗
 172: ║     PIPELINE COMPLETE! 🎧                ║
 173: ║                                          ║
 174: ║  Training examples: {len(self.all_training_examples):<5}              ║
