 178: 
 179:     # ============================================================
 180:     # CHANNEL PROCESSING
 181:     # ============================================================
 182: 
 183:     def _process_channel(self, channel_name, channel_config):
 184:         """Process all videos from one channel"""
 185: 
 186:         # Get video list
 187:         videos = self._get_video_list(channel_config)
 188:         print(f"\n   Found {len(videos)} videos to process")
 189: 
 190:         processed = 0
 191:         failed = 0
 192: 
 193:         for i, video in enumerate(videos):
 194:             print(f"\n   [{i+1}/{len(videos)}] "
 195:                   f"{video['title'][:50]}")
 196:             print(f"   Duration: {video.get('duration', 0):.0f}s | "
 197:                   f"Short: {video.get('is_short', False)}")
 198: 
 199:             # Skip if already processed
 200:             if video['id'] in self.progress.get(
 201:                 channel_name, {}
 202:             ).get('processed_ids', []):
 203:                 print(f"   ⏭️  Already processed")
 204:                 continue
 205: 
 206:             try:
 207:                 # Download audio
 208:                 audio_path = self._download_audio(video)
 209:                 if not audio_path:
 210:                     failed += 1
 211:                     continue
 212: 
 213:                 # Process based on channel type
 214:                 examples = self._process_video(
 215:                     audio_path, video, channel_config
 216:                 )
 217: 
 218:                 self.all_training_examples.extend(examples)
 219: 
 220:                 # If transition channel, add to benchmark
 221:                 if channel_config['type'] in [
 222:                     'transitions', 'transitions_and_tutorials'
 223:                 ]:
 224:                     benchmarks = self._extract_benchmarks(
 225:                         audio_path, video
 226:                     )
 227:                     self.perceptual_benchmarks.extend(benchmarks)
 228: 
 229:                 processed += 1
 230: 
 231:                 # Update progress
 232:                 self._update_progress(
 233:                     channel_name, video['id']
 234:                 )
 235: 
 236:                 # Save intermediate results every 10 videos
 237:                 if processed % 10 == 0:
 238:                     self._save_intermediate_results()
 239:                     print(f"\n   💾 Saved {processed} videos processed")
 240: 
 241:             except Exception as e:
 242:                 print(f"   ❌ Failed: {e}")
 243:                 failed += 1
 244:             finally:
 245:                 # ALWAYS delete audio after processing
 246:                 self._cleanup_audio(video['id'])
 247: 
 248:         # Mark channel as complete
 249:         self._mark_channel_complete(channel_name)
 250: 
 251:         print(f"\n   ✅ Channel complete: "
 252:               f"{processed} processed, {failed} failed")
 253: 
 254:     # ============================================================
 255:     # VIDEO LIST FETCHING
 256:     # ============================================================
 257: 
 258:     def _get_video_list(self, channel_config):
 259:         """
 260:         Get list of videos from channel
 261:         Prioritizes Shorts if shorts_only=True
 262:         """
 263:         url = channel_config['url']
 264:         shorts_only = channel_config.get('shorts_only', False)
 265:         max_videos = channel_config.get('max_videos', 100)
 266:         max_duration = channel_config.get('max_duration', 3600)
 267: 
 268:         videos = []
 269: 
 270:         # Try Shorts playlist first if shorts_only
 271:         if shorts_only:
 272:             shorts_url = url + '/shorts'
 273:             shorts = self._fetch_video_list(
 274:                 shorts_url, max_videos, max_duration=60
 275:             )
 276:             for v in shorts:
 277:                 v['is_short'] = True
 278:             videos.extend(shorts)
 279:             print(f"   📱 Found {len(shorts)} Shorts")
 280: 
 281:         # If not shorts_only or not enough shorts,
 282:         # get regular videos too
 283:         if not shorts_only or len(videos) < 10:
 284:             regular = self._fetch_video_list(
 285:                 url, max_videos - len(videos), max_duration
 286:             )
 287:             for v in regular:
 288:                 v['is_short'] = False
 289:             videos.extend(regular)
 290:             print(f"   🎥 Found {len(regular)} regular videos")
 291: 
 292:         # Sort: Shorts first (faster to process)
 293:         videos.sort(
 294:             key=lambda x: (not x.get('is_short', False),
 295:                           x.get('duration', 999))
 296:         )
 297: 
 298:         return videos[:max_videos]
 299: 
 300:     def _fetch_video_list(self, url, max_count, max_duration=3600):
 301:         """Fetch video metadata from YouTube"""
 302:         ydl_opts = {
 303:             'quiet': True,
 304:             'extract_flat': True,
 305:             'playlistend': max_count * 2,  # Get extra, filter below
 306:         }
 307: 
 308:         videos = []
 309:         try:
 310:             with yt_dlp.YoutubeDL(ydl_opts) as ydl:
 311:                 info = ydl.extract_info(url, download=False)
 312:                 entries = info.get('entries', [])
 313: 
 314:                 for entry in entries:
 315:                     if not entry:
 316:                         continue
 317: 
 318:                     duration = entry.get('duration', 0) or 0
 319: 
 320:                     # Skip too long
 321:                     if duration > max_duration:
 322:                         continue
 323: 
 324:                     # Skip too short (< 5 seconds)
 325:                     if duration < 5:
 326:                         continue
 327: 
 328:                     videos.append({
 329:                         'id': entry.get('id', ''),
 330:                         'title': entry.get('title', ''),
 331:                         'url': f"https://youtube.com/watch?v={entry.get('id')}",
 332:                         'duration': duration,
 333:                         'thumbnail': entry.get('thumbnail', ''),
 334:                     })
 335: 
 336:                     if len(videos) >= max_count:
 337:                         break
 338: 
 339:         except Exception as e:
 340:             print(f"   ❌ Failed to fetch video list: {e}")
 341: 
 342:         return videos
 343: 
 344:     # ============================================================
 345:     # AUDIO DOWNLOAD
 346:     # ============================================================
 347: 
 348:     def _download_audio(self, video):
 349:         """
 350:         Download audio for a video
 351:         Returns filepath or None
 352:         """
 353:         output_path = os.path.join(
 354:             self.tmp_dir, f"{video['id']}.mp3"
 355:         )
 356: 
 357:         if os.path.exists(output_path):
 358:             return output_path
 359: 
 360:         ydl_opts = {
 361:             'format': 'bestaudio/best',
 362:             'outtmpl': os.path.join(
 363:                 self.tmp_dir, f"{video['id']}.%(ext)s"
 364:             ),
 365:             'postprocessors': [{
 366:                 'key': 'FFmpegExtractAudio',
 367:                 'preferredcodec': 'mp3',
 368:                 'preferredquality': '128',
 369:             }],
 370:             'quiet': True,
 371:             'no_warnings': True,
 372:         }
 373: 
 374:         try:
 375:             with yt_dlp.YoutubeDL(ydl_opts) as ydl:
 376:                 ydl.download([video['url']])
 377:             return output_path
 378:         except Exception as e:
 379:             print(f"   ❌ Download failed: {e}")
 380:             return None
 381: 
 382:     def _cleanup_audio(self, video_id):
 383:         """Delete audio file after processing"""
 384:         for ext in ['mp3', 'wav', 'webm', 'm4a', 'opus']:
 385:             path = os.path.join(self.tmp_dir, f"{video_id}.{ext}")
 386:             if os.path.exists(path):
 387:                 os.remove(path)
 388: 
 389:     # ============================================================
 390:     # VIDEO PROCESSING
 391:     # ============================================================
 392: 
 393:     def _process_video(self, audio_path, video, channel_config):
 394:         """
 395:         Process a single video based on channel type
 396:         Returns list of training examples
 397:         """
 398:         examples = []
 399:         extract = channel_config.get('extract', [])
 400:         channel_type = channel_config['type']
 401: 
 402:         # Load audio
 403:         try:
 404:             y, sr = librosa.load(audio_path, sr=self.sr, mono=True)
 405:         except Exception as e:
 406:             print(f"   ❌ Audio load failed: {e}")
 407:             return examples
 408: 
 409:         # ---- Extract based on channel type ----
 410: 
 411:         # For transition channels: find & label transitions
 412:         if 'transition_points' in extract:
 413:             transition_examples = self._extract_transitions(
 414:                 y, sr, video, channel_config
 415:             )
 416:             examples.extend(transition_examples)
 417:             print(f"   🎚️  Found {len(transition_examples)} transitions")
 418: 
 419:         # For tutorial channels: transcribe & extract knowledge
 420:         if 'transcript' in extract:
 421:             transcript_examples = self._extract_transcript_knowledge(
 422:                 audio_path, video, channel_config
 423:             )
 424:             examples.extend(transcript_examples)
 425:             print(f"   📝 Extracted {len(transcript_examples)} "
 426:                   f"knowledge items")
 427: 
 428:         # For all: extract audio features
 429:         if 'audio_features' in extract:
 430:             features = self._extract_audio_features(y, sr, video)
 431:             if features:
 432:                 examples.append({
 433:                     'type': 'audio_features',
 434:                     'video_id': video['id'],
 435:                     'title': video['title'],
 436:                     'features': features,
 437:                     'label': channel_config['label'],
 438:                     'source': channel_config['type'],
 439:                 })
 440: 
 441:         # Wordplay specific extraction
 442:         if 'wordplay_examples' in extract:
 443:             wp_examples = self._extract_wordplay_examples(
 444:                 y, sr, video
 445:             )
 446:             examples.extend(wp_examples)
 447:             print(f"   🗣️  Found {len(wp_examples)} wordplay examples")
 448: 
 449:         return examples
 450: 
 451:     # ============================================================
 452:     # TRANSITION EXTRACTION
 453:     # ============================================================
 454: 
 455:     def _extract_transitions(self, y, sr, video, channel_config):
 456:         """
 457:         Find and extract transition moments from audio
 458:         Labels them as good transitions (from these channels
 459:         we assume ALL transitions are good quality)
 460:         """
 461:         examples = []
 462: 
 463:         # Detect transition points
 464:         transition_times = self._detect_transition_points(y, sr)
 465: 
 466:         for t in transition_times:
 467:             # Extract features around transition
 468:             window = int(sr * 4)
 469:             t_sample = int(t * sr)
 470: 
 471:             before = y[max(0, t_sample - window):t_sample]
 472:             after = y[t_sample:min(len(y), t_sample + window)]
 473: 
 474:             if len(before) < sr or len(after) < sr:
 475:                 continue
 476: 
 477:             # Classify technique
 478:             technique = self._classify_transition_technique(
 479:                 before, after, sr
 480:             )
 481: 
 482:             # Extract features
 483:             features = {
 484:                 'bpm_before': self._get_bpm(before, sr),
 485:                 'bpm_after': self._get_bpm(after, sr),
 486:                 'energy_before': float(np.sqrt(np.mean(before**2))),
 487:                 'energy_after': float(np.sqrt(np.mean(after**2))),
 488:                 'centroid_before': self._get_centroid(before, sr),
 489:                 'centroid_after': self._get_centroid(after, sr),
 490:                 'transition_duration': self._estimate_transition_duration(
 491:                     y, sr, t
 492:                 ),
 493:             }
 494: 
 495:             examples.append({
 496:                 'type': 'transition',
 497:                 'video_id': video['id'],
 498:                 'title': video['title'],
 499:                 'timestamp': t,
 500:                 'technique': technique,
 501:                 'quality': 'good',      # From quality channels = good
 502:                 'features': features,
 503:                 'label': 1,             # Positive label
 504:                 'source': 'transition_channel',
 505:                 'is_short': video.get('is_short', False),
 506:             })
 507: 
 508:         return examples
 509: 
 510:     def _detect_transition_points(self, y, sr):
 511:         """Detect where transitions happen in audio"""
 512:         hop = 512
 513:         transition_times = []
 514: 
 515:         # Spectral flux
 516:         spec = np.abs(librosa.stft(y, hop_length=hop))
 517:         flux = np.sum(np.diff(spec, axis=1)**2, axis=0)
 518:         flux_norm = flux / (np.max(flux) + 1e-10)
 519:         flux_times = librosa.frames_to_time(
 520:             np.arange(len(flux)), sr=sr, hop_length=hop
 521:         )
 522: 
 523:         # RMS energy changes
 524:         rms = librosa.feature.rms(y=y, hop_length=hop)[0]
 525:         rms_diff = np.abs(np.diff(rms))
 526: 
 527:         # Find peaks
 528:         from scipy.signal import find_peaks
 529: 
 530:         min_gap = sr // hop * 8  # Min 8 seconds between transitions
 531: 
 532:         peaks, _ = find_peaks(
 533:             flux_norm,
 534:             height=0.25,
 535:             distance=min_gap
 536:         )
 537: 
 538:         for peak in peaks:
 539:             if peak < len(flux_times):
 540:                 t = float(flux_times[peak])
 541:                 duration = len(y) / sr
 542:                 if 5 < t < duration - 5:
 543:                     transition_times.append(t)
 544: 
 545:         return transition_times
 546: 
 547:     def _classify_transition_technique(self, before, after, sr):
 548:         """Classify what technique was used"""
 549:         energy_b = np.sqrt(np.mean(before**2))
 550:         energy_a = np.sqrt(np.mean(after**2))
 551:         centroid_b = self._get_centroid(before, sr)
 552:         centroid_a = self._get_centroid(after, sr)
 553: 
 554:         # Echo detection
 555:         if self._has_echo(before):
 556:             return 'echo_out'
 557: 
 558:         # Filter sweep detection
 559:         if abs(centroid_a - centroid_b) > 2000:
 560:             return 'filter_sweep'
 561: 
 562:         # Loop roll detection
 563:         if self._has_loop_pattern(before, sr):
 564:             return 'loop_roll'
 565: 
 566:         # Reverb detection
 567:         if self._has_reverb_tail(before):
 568:             return 'reverb_wash'
 569: 
 570:         # Hard cut
 571:         bpm_b = self._get_bpm(before, sr)
 572:         bpm_a = self._get_bpm(after, sr)
 573:         if abs(bpm_b - bpm_a) > 20:
 574:             return 'cut_transition'
 575: 
 576:         return 'beatmatch_crossfade'
 577: 
 578:     def _estimate_transition_duration(self, y, sr, transition_time):
 579:         """Estimate how long the transition lasts"""
 580:         window = int(sr * 8)
 581:         t_sample = int(transition_time * sr)
 582:         segment = y[
 583:             max(0, t_sample - window//2):
 584:             min(len(y), t_sample + window//2)
 585:         ]
 586:         if len(segment) < 100:
 587:             return 4.0
 588:         rms = librosa.feature.rms(y=segment)[0]
 589:         # Find region of mixed audio (moderate energy variance)
 590:         variance = np.var(rms)
 591:         return float(min(8.0, max(1.0, variance * 1000)))
 592: 
 593:     # ============================================================
 594:     # BENCHMARK EXTRACTION
 595:     # ============================================================
 596: 
 597:     def _extract_benchmarks(self, audio_path, video):
 598:         """
 599:         Extract perceptual quality benchmarks
 600:         These are reference 'good transition' audio clips
 601:         Used to compare our generated transitions against
 602:         """
 603:         benchmarks = []
 604: 
 605:         try:
 606:             y, sr = librosa.load(audio_path, sr=self.sr, mono=True)
 607:         except Exception:
 608:             return benchmarks
 609: 
 610:         transition_times = self._detect_transition_points(y, sr)
 611: 
 612:         for t in transition_times:
 613:             # Extract 8 second clip centered on transition
 614:             clip_start = max(0, int((t - 4) * sr))
 615:             clip_end = min(len(y), int((t + 4) * sr))
 616:             clip = y[clip_start:clip_end]
 617: 
 618:             if len(clip) < sr * 4:
 619:                 continue
 620: 
 621:             # Extract fingerprint features
 622:             mfcc = librosa.feature.mfcc(y=clip, sr=sr, n_mfcc=20)
 623:             chroma = librosa.feature.chroma_cqt(y=clip, sr=sr)
 624:             spectral = librosa.feature.spectral_centroid(y=clip, sr=sr)
 625: 
 626:             benchmark = {
 627:                 'video_id': video['id'],
 628:                 'title': video['title'],
 629:                 'timestamp': t,
 630:                 'duration': len(clip) / sr,
 631:                 'is_short': video.get('is_short', False),
 632:                 'mfcc_mean': np.mean(mfcc, axis=1).tolist(),
 633:                 'mfcc_std': np.std(mfcc, axis=1).tolist(),
 634:                 'chroma_mean': np.mean(chroma, axis=1).tolist(),
 635:                 'spectral_centroid_mean': float(np.mean(spectral)),
 636:                 'energy': float(np.sqrt(np.mean(clip**2))),
 637:             }
 638: 
 639:             benchmarks.append(benchmark)
 640: 
 641:         return benchmarks
 642: 
 643:     # ============================================================
 644:     # TRANSCRIPT EXTRACTION (Tutorial channels)
 645:     # ============================================================
 646: 
 647:     def _extract_transcript_knowledge(self, audio_path,
 648:                                        video, channel_config):
 649:         """
 650:         Transcribe tutorial video and extract
 651:         technique knowledge
 652:         """
 653:         examples = []
 654: 
 655:         # Load Whisper once
 656:         if self.whisper_model is None:
 657:             print("   Loading Whisper model...")
 658:             self.whisper_model = whisper.load_model("base")
 659: 
 660:         try:
 661:             result = self.whisper_model.transcribe(
 662:                 audio_path,
 663:                 word_timestamps=True
 664:             )
 665:             transcript = result.get('text', '')
 666:             segments = result.get('segments', [])
 667: 
 668:         except Exception as e:
 669:             print(f"   ❌ Transcription failed: {e}")
 670:             return examples
 671: 
 672:         # Technique keyword mapping
 673:         technique_keywords = {
 674:             'beatmatch_crossfade': [
 675:                 'beatmatch', 'beat match', 'sync', 'crossfade',
 676:                 'blend', 'mix in', 'smooth transition'
 677:             ],
 678:             'filter_sweep': [
 679:                 'filter', 'high pass', 'low pass', 'eq sweep',
 680:                 'kill the bass', 'open the filter', 'filter out'
 681:             ],
 682:             'echo_out': [
 683:                 'echo', 'delay', 'echo out', 'bounce',
 684:                 'delay effect', 'echo effect'
 685:             ],
 686:             'loop_roll': [
 687:                 'loop', 'roll', 'loop roll', 'stutter',
 688:                 'rolling', 'loop out'
 689:             ],
 690:             'reverb_wash': [
 691:                 'reverb', 'wash', 'reverb out',
 692:                 'atmospheric', 'reverb effect', 'hall'
 693:             ],
 694:             'spinback': [
 695:                 'spinback', 'spin back', 'rewind',
 696:                 'brake', 'backspin', 'spin out'
 697:             ],
 698:             'phrase_matching': [
 699:                 'phrase', 'eight bar', '8 bar', '16 bar',
 700:                 'sixteen bar', 'on the one', 'count the bars',
 701:                 'bar count', 'phrase match'
 702:             ],
 703:             'harmonic_mixing': [
 704:                 'harmonic', 'camelot', 'key', 'same key',
 705:                 'compatible', 'harmonic mix', 'key mixing',
 706:                 'musical key'
 707:             ],
 708:             'wordplay': [
 709:                 'word', 'vocal', 'word play', 'acapella',
 710:                 'vocal transition', 'word match', 'lyric',
 711:                 'same word', 'vocal chop'
 712:             ],
 713:             'tone_play': [
 714:                 'tone', 'melody', 'note', 'pitch',
 715:                 'melodic', 'tune', 'musical note', 'play the melody'
 716:             ],
 717:             'cut_transition': [
 718:                 'cut', 'hard cut', 'chop', 'slice',
 719:                 'instant', 'sharp cut', 'quick cut'
 720:             ],
 721:         }
 722: 
 723:         # Extract knowledge from each segment
 724:         for segment in segments:
 725:             seg_text = segment.get('text', '').lower()
 726:             seg_start = segment.get('start', 0)
 727: 
 728:             for technique, keywords in technique_keywords.items():
 729:                 for kw in keywords:
 730:                     if kw in seg_text:
 731:                         # Get surrounding context
 732:                         context = self._get_segment_context(
 733:                             segments, segment, window=3
 734:                         )
 735: 
 736:                         examples.append({
 737:                             'type': 'tutorial_knowledge',
 738:                             'video_id': video['id'],
 739:                             'title': video['title'],
 740:                             'technique': technique,
 741:                             'timestamp': seg_start,
 742:                             'text': segment.get('text', ''),
 743:                             'context': context,
 744:                             'keyword': kw,
 745:                             'source': 'tutorial',
 746:                             'label': 1,
 747:                         })
 748:                         break
 749: 
 750:         return examples
 751: 
 752:     def _get_segment_context(self, segments, target, window=3):
 753:         """Get text context around a segment"""
 754:         try:
 755:             idx = segments.index(target)
 756:         except ValueError:
 757:             return target.get('text', '')
 758: 
 759:         start = max(0, idx - window)
 760:         end = min(len(segments), idx + window + 1)
 761:         return ' '.join(s.get('text', '') for s in segments[start:end])
 762: 
 763:     # ============================================================
 764:     # WORDPLAY EXTRACTION
 765:     # ============================================================
 766: 
 767:     def _extract_wordplay_examples(self, y, sr, video):
 768:         """
 769:         Extract wordplay transition examples
 770:         Specifically for SiangyOO-style transitions
 771:         """
 772:         examples = []
 773: 
 774:         # Detect transitions
 775:         transition_times = self._detect_transition_points(y, sr)
 776: 
 777:         for t in transition_times:
 778:             # Look for vocal-heavy sections around transition
 779:             vocal_score = self._estimate_vocal_presence(y, sr, t)
 780: 
 781:             if vocal_score > 0.5:
 782:                 features = {
 783:                     'timestamp': t,
 784:                     'vocal_score': vocal_score,
 785:                     'bpm': self._get_bpm(
 786:                         y[max(0, int((t-4)*sr)):int((t+4)*sr)], sr
 787:                     ),
 788:                     'energy': float(np.sqrt(np.mean(
 789:                         y[max(0, int((t-2)*sr)):int((t+2)*sr)]**2
 790:                     ))),
 791:                 }
 792: 
 793:                 examples.append({
 794:                     'type': 'wordplay_transition',
 795:                     'video_id': video['id'],
 796:                     'title': video['title'],
 797:                     'timestamp': t,
 798:                     'vocal_score': vocal_score,
 799:                     'features': features,
 800:                     'technique': 'wordplay',
 801:                     'quality': 'good',
 802:                     'label': 1,
 803:                     'source': 'siangyoo',
 804:                 })
 805: 
 806:         return examples
 807: 
 808:     def _estimate_vocal_presence(self, y, sr, time):
 809:         """
 810:         Estimate how much vocal is present
 811:         High ZCR + mid-range spectral centroid = likely vocal
 812:         """
 813:         window = int(sr * 2)
 814:         t_sample = int(time * sr)
 815:         segment = y[max(0, t_sample - window):t_sample + window]
 816: 
 817:         if len(segment) < 100:
 818:             return 0.0
 819: 
 820:         zcr = float(np.mean(librosa.feature.zero_crossing_rate(y=segment)))
 821:         centroid = float(np.mean(
 822:             librosa.feature.spectral_centroid(y=segment, sr=sr)
 823:         ))
 824: 
 825:         # Vocals typically: ZCR 0.05-0.15, centroid 1000-4000 Hz
 826:         zcr_score = 1.0 if 0.04 < zcr < 0.18 else 0.0
 827:         centroid_score = 1.0 if 800 < centroid < 4500 else 0.0
 828: 
 829:         return (zcr_score + centroid_score) / 2.0
 830: 
 831:     # ============================================================
 832:     # AUDIO FEATURE HELPERS
 833:     # ============================================================
 834: 
 835:     def _get_bpm(self, audio, sr):
 836:         """Get BPM of audio segment"""
 837:         if len(audio) < sr:
 838:             return 120.0
 839:         try:
 840:             tempo, _ = librosa.beat.beat_track(y=audio, sr=sr)
 841:             return float(tempo)
 842:         except Exception:
 843:             return 120.0
 844: 
 845:     def _get_centroid(self, audio, sr):
 846:         """Get spectral centroid"""
 847:         if len(audio) < 100:
 848:             return 2000.0
 849:         try:
 850:             return float(np.mean(
 851:                 librosa.feature.spectral_centroid(y=audio, sr=sr)
 852:             ))
 853:         except Exception:
 854:             return 2000.0
 855: 
 856:     def _extract_audio_features(self, y, sr, video):
 857:         """Extract full audio feature set"""
 858:         try:
 859:             tempo, _ = librosa.beat.beat_track(y=y, sr=sr)
 860:             rms = librosa.feature.rms(y=y)[0]
 861:             centroid = librosa.feature.spectral_centroid(y=y, sr=sr)[0]
 862:             zcr = librosa.feature.zero_crossing_rate(y=y)[0]
 863:             mfcc = librosa.feature.mfcc(y=y, sr=sr, n_mfcc=13)
 864: 
 865:             return {
 866:                 'bpm': float(tempo),
 867:                 'energy_mean': float(np.mean(rms)),
 868:                 'energy_std': float(np.std(rms)),
 869:                 'centroid_mean': float(np.mean(centroid)),
 870:                 'zcr_mean': float(np.mean(zcr)),
 871:                 'mfcc_means': np.mean(mfcc, axis=1).tolist(),
 872:                 'duration': float(len(y) / sr),
 873:             }
 874:         except Exception as e:
 875:             print(f"   ❌ Feature extraction failed: {e}")
 876:             return None
 877: 
 878:     def _has_echo(self, audio):
 879:         """Detect echo/delay pattern"""
 880:         if len(audio) < 4000:
 881:             return False
 882:         corr = np.correlate(audio[:4000], audio[:4000], mode='full')
 883:         corr = corr[len(corr)//2:]
 884:         corr = corr / (corr[0] + 1e-10)
 885:         from scipy.signal import find_peaks
 886:         peaks, _ = find_peaks(corr[100:2000], height=0.25)
 887:         return len(peaks) > 2
 888: 
 889:     def _has_loop_pattern(self, audio, sr):
 890:         """Detect loop/roll pattern"""
 891:         short_len = int(sr * 0.25)
 892:         if len(audio) < short_len * 4:
 893:             return False
 894:         seg_a = audio[:short_len]
 895:         seg_b = audio[short_len:short_len*2]
 896:         if len(seg_b) < len(seg_a):
 897:             return False
 898:         try:
 899:             corr = np.corrcoef(seg_a[:len(seg_b)], seg_b)[0, 1]
 900:             return corr > 0.65
 901:         except Exception:
 902:             return False
 903: 
 904:     def _has_reverb_tail(self, audio):
 905:         """Detect reverb tail"""
 906:         if len(audio) < 1000:
 907:             return False
 908:         rms = librosa.feature.rms(y=audio)[0]
 909:         if len(rms) < 10:
 910:             return False
 911:         decay = rms[-len(rms)//3:]
 912:         smooth = np.std(np.diff(decay)) < 0.002
 913:         return smooth and rms[-1] < rms[0] * 0.3
 914: 
 915:     # ============================================================
 916:     # PERCEPTUAL QUALITY SCORER
 917:     # ============================================================
 918: 
 919:     def build_perceptual_scorer(self):
 920:         """
 921:         Build perceptual quality scorer from benchmarks
 922:         Saves model that can score any transition
 923:         against known good transitions
 924:         """
 925:         if not self.perceptual_benchmarks:
 926:             print("❌ No benchmarks collected yet")
 927:             print("   Run run_full_pipeline() first")
 928:             return False
 929: 
 930:         print(f"\n🎯 Building perceptual scorer from "
 931:               f"{len(self.perceptual_benchmarks)} benchmarks...")
 932: 
 933:         # Build reference distribution
 934:         # (what good transitions look like)
 935:         mfcc_matrix = []
 936:         for b in self.perceptual_benchmarks:
 937:             if b.get('mfcc_mean'):
 938:                 mfcc_matrix.append(b['mfcc_mean'])
 939: 
 940:         if not mfcc_matrix:
 941:             print("❌ No MFCC data in benchmarks")
 942:             return False
 943: 
 944:         mfcc_array = np.array(mfcc_matrix)
 945: 
 946:         # Compute reference statistics
 947:         reference = {
 948:             'mfcc_mean': np.mean(mfcc_array, axis=0).tolist(),
 949:             'mfcc_std': np.std(mfcc_array, axis=0).tolist(),
 950:             'mfcc_cov': np.cov(mfcc_array.T).tolist(),
 951:             'n_benchmarks': len(self.perceptual_benchmarks),
 952:             'built_at': str(datetime.now()),
 953:             'channels': list(CHANNELS.keys()),
 954:         }
 955: 
 956:         # Save reference
 957:         ref_path = os.path.join(
 958:             self.models_dir, 'perceptual_reference.json'
 959:         )
 960:         with open(ref_path, 'w') as f:
 961:             json.dump(reference, f, indent=2)
 962: 
 963:         print(f"✅ Perceptual scorer saved: {ref_path}")
 964:         print(f"   Based on {len(self.perceptual_benchmarks)} "
 965:               f"real transitions")
 966:         return True
 967: 
 968:     def score_transition_quality(self, transition_audio):
 969:         """
 970:         Score a generated transition against
 971:         real DJ transition benchmarks
 972:         Returns score 0.0 - 1.0
 973:         1.0 = sounds like a professional DJ transition
 974:         0.0 = sounds nothing like a pro transition
 975:         """
 976:         ref_path = os.path.join(
 977:             self.models_dir, 'perceptual_reference.json'
 978:         )
 979: 
 980:         if not os.path.exists(ref_path):
 981:             print("   ⚠️  No perceptual reference built yet")
 982:             return 0.5  # Neutral score
 983: 
 984:         with open(ref_path, 'r') as f:
 985:             reference = json.load(f)
 986: 
 987:         # Extract MFCC from generated transition
 988:         try:
 989:             mfcc = librosa.feature.mfcc(
 990:                 y=transition_audio,
 991:                 sr=self.sr,
 992:                 n_mfcc=20
 993:             )
 994:             gen_mfcc = np.mean(mfcc, axis=1)
 995:         except Exception:
 996:             return 0.5
 997: 
 998:         # Compare against reference distribution
 999:         ref_mean = np.array(reference['mfcc_mean'])
1000:         ref_std = np.array(reference['mfcc_std']) + 1e-10
1001: 
1002:         # Normalize distance
1003:         distances = np.abs(gen_mfcc[:len(ref_mean)] - ref_mean)
1004:         normalized = distances / ref_std
1005: 
1006:         # Score: lower distance = more similar to pro transitions
1007:         mean_distance = float(np.mean(normalized))
1008:         score = max(0.0, 1.0 - (mean_distance / 5.0))
1009: 
1010:         return score
1011: 
1012:     # ============================================================
1013:     # PROGRESS & PERSISTENCE
1014:     # ============================================================
1015: 
1016:     def _load_progress(self):
1017:         """Load pipeline progress"""
1018:         if os.path.exists(self.progress_file):
1019:             try:
1020:                 with open(self.progress_file, 'r') as f:
1021:                     return json.load(f)
1022:             except Exception:
1023:                 pass
1024:         return {}
1025: 
1026:     def _update_progress(self, channel_name, video_id):
1027:         """Mark video as processed"""
1028:         if channel_name not in self.progress:
1029:             self.progress[channel_name] = {
1030:                 'processed_ids': [],
1031:                 'completed': False
1032:             }
1033:         if video_id not in self.progress[channel_name]['processed_ids']:
1034:             self.progress[channel_name]['processed_ids'].append(video_id)
1035: 
1036:         with open(self.progress_file, 'w') as f:
1037:             json.dump(self.progress, f, indent=2)
1038: 
1039:     def _mark_channel_complete(self, channel_name):
1040:         """Mark channel as fully processed"""
1041:         if channel_name not in self.progress:
1042:             self.progress[channel_name] = {'processed_ids': []}
1043:         self.progress[channel_name]['completed'] = True
1044: 
1045:         with open(self.progress_file, 'w') as f:
1046:             json.dump(self.progress, f, indent=2)
1047: 
1048:     def _save_intermediate_results(self):
1049:         """Save results collected so far"""
1050:         timestamp = datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')
1051: 
1052:         if self.all_training_examples:
1053:             path = os.path.join(
1054:                 self.training_dir,
1055:                 f'training_examples_{timestamp}.json'
1056:             )
1057:             with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
1058:                 json.dump(
1059:                     self.all_training_examples, f,
1060:                     indent=2, ensure_ascii=False
1061:                 )
1062: 
1063:         if self.perceptual_benchmarks:
1064:             path = os.path.join(
1065:                 self.training_dir,
1066:                 f'benchmarks_{timestamp}.json'
1067:             )
1068:             with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
1069:                 json.dump(
1070:                     self.perceptual_benchmarks, f,
1071:                     indent=2, ensure_ascii=False
1072:                 )
1073: 
1074:     def _save_all_results(self):
1075:         """Final save of all results"""
1076:         self._save_intermediate_results()
1077: 
1078:         # Build perceptual scorer from all benchmarks
1079:         self.build_perceptual_scorer()
1080: 
1081:         print(f"\n💾 All results saved to {self.training_dir}")
1082:

1115:         pipeline.run_full_pipeline()

1119:             CHANNELS[name]['priority'] = 99
1120:         pipeline.run_full_pipeline()
1121: 
1122:     elif choice == '4':
1123:         for name in ['best_dj_transitions', '69beats', 'siangyoo']:
1124:             CHANNELS[name]['priority'] = 99
1125:         pipeline.run_full_pipeline()
1126:

1129:             if name != 'siangyoo':
1130:                 CHANNELS[name]['priority'] = 99
1131:         pipeline.run_full_pipeline()
1132: 
1133:     elif choice == '6':
1134:         # Load existing benchmarks and build scorer
1135:         for filename in os.listdir(pipeline.training_dir):
1136:             if filename.startswith('benchmarks_'):
1137:                 path = os.path.join(pipeline.training_dir, filename)
1138:                 with open(path, 'r') as f:
1139:                     pipeline.perceptual_benchmarks.extend(
1140:                         json.load(f)
1141:                     )
1142:         print(f"Loaded {len(pipeline.perceptual_benchmarks)} benchmarks")
1143:         pipeline.build_perceptual_scorer()

================================================================================
FILE: quality_engine\perceptual_scorer.py
================================================================================
   1: """
   2: Perceptual Quality Scorer
   3: Scores generated transitions against
   4: real professional DJ transitions
   5: No human listening needed
   6: """
   7: 
   8: import os
   9: import json
  10: import numpy as np
  11: import librosa
  12: 
  13: class PerceptualScorer:
  14:     """
  15:     Scores a generated transition against
  16:     benchmarks from real DJ transitions
  17:     Uses:
  18:     - MFCC distance (timbral similarity)
  19:     - Spectral flux smoothness
  20:     - Energy continuity
  21:     - Beat alignment score
  22:     - Frechet Audio Distance approximation
  23:     """
  24:     def __init__(self, config):
  25:         self.config = config
  26:         self.models_dir = config['paths']['models']
  27:         self.sr = config['audio']['sample_rate']
  28:         self.reference = None
  29:         self._load_reference()
  30: 
  31:     def _load_reference(self):
  32:         """Load perceptual reference from disk"""
  33:         ref_path = os.path.join(
  34:             self.models_dir, 'perceptual_reference.json'
  35:         )
  36:         if os.path.exists(ref_path):
  37:             with open(ref_path, 'r') as f:
  38:                 self.reference = json.load(f)
  39:             print(f"✅ Perceptual reference loaded: "
  40:                   f"{self.reference.get('n_benchmarks', 0)} benchmarks")
  41:         else:
  42:             print("⚠️  No perceptual reference found")
  43:             print("   Run training_data_pipeline.py first")
  44: 
  45:     def score(self, transition_audio, sr=None):
  46:         """
  47:         Score a transition audio array
  48:         Returns dict with overall score and sub-scores
  49:         """
  50:         if sr is None:
  51:             sr = self.sr
  52: 
  53:         scores = {}
  54: 
  55:         # 1. MFCC similarity to reference
  56:         scores['mfcc_similarity'] = self._score_mfcc(
  57:             transition_audio, sr
  58:         )
  59: 
  60:         # 2. Spectral flux smoothness
  61:         scores['smoothness'] = self._score_smoothness(
  62:             transition_audio, sr
  63:         )
  64: 
  65:         # 3. Energy continuity
  66:         scores['energy_continuity'] = self._score_energy_continuity(
  67:             transition_audio, sr
  68:         )
  69: 
  70:         # 4. Beat alignment
  71:         scores['beat_alignment'] = self._score_beat_alignment(
  72:             transition_audio, sr
  73:         )
  74: 
  75:         # 5. Clipping/distortion check
  76:         scores['no_distortion'] = self._score_no_distortion(
  77:             transition_audio
  78:         )
  79: 
  80:         # Weighted overall score
  81:         weights = {
  82:             'mfcc_similarity':    0.30,
  83:             'smoothness':         0.25,
  84:             'energy_continuity':  0.20,
  85:             'beat_alignment':     0.15,
  86:             'no_distortion':      0.10,
  87:         }
  88: 
  89:         overall = sum(
  90:             scores[k] * weights[k] for k in weights
  91:         )
  92: 
  93:         scores['overall'] = round(overall, 3)
  94: 
  95:         return scores
  96: 
  97:     def _score_mfcc(self, audio, sr):
  98:         """
  99:         Compare MFCC fingerprint of transition
 100:         against reference professional transitions
 101:         """
 102:         if self.reference is None:
 103:             return 0.5
 104: 
 105:         try:
 106:             mfcc = librosa.feature.mfcc(y=audio, sr=sr, n_mfcc=20)
 107:             gen_mean = np.mean(mfcc, axis=1)
 108: 
 109:             ref_mean = np.array(self.reference.get('mfcc_mean', []))
 110:             ref_std = np.array(self.reference.get('mfcc_std', []))
 111: 
 112:             if len(ref_mean) == 0:
 113:                 return 0.5
 114: 
 115:             # Align lengths
 116:             min_len = min(len(gen_mean), len(ref_mean))
 117:             gen_mean = gen_mean[:min_len]
 118:             ref_mean = ref_mean[:min_len]
 119:             ref_std = ref_std[:min_len] + 1e-10
 120: 
 121:             # Normalized distance
 122:             dist = np.abs(gen_mean - ref_mean) / ref_std
 123:             score = max(0.0, 1.0 - float(np.mean(dist)) / 3.0)
 124:             return round(score, 3)
 125: 
 126:         except Exception:
 127:             return 0.5
 128: 
 129:     def _score_smoothness(self, audio, sr):
 130:         """
 131:         Measure spectral flux smoothness
 132:         Good transitions have smooth spectral changes
 133:         Bad transitions have abrupt jumps
 134:         """
 135:         try:
 136:             hop = 512
 137:             spec = np.abs(librosa.stft(audio, hop_length=hop))
 138:             flux = np.sum(np.diff(spec, axis=1)**2, axis=0)
 139:             flux_norm = flux / (np.max(flux) + 1e-10)
 140: 
 141:             # Lower variance in flux = smoother transition
 142:             smoothness = 1.0 - float(np.std(flux_norm))
 143:             return round(max(0.0, min(1.0, smoothness)), 3)
 144: 
 145:         except Exception:
 146:             return 0.5
 147: 
 148:     def _score_energy_continuity(self, audio, sr):
 149:         """
 150:         Measure energy continuity through transition
 151:         Good: gradual energy changes
 152:         Bad: sudden energy jumps or silence gaps
 153:         """
 154:         try:
 155:             rms = librosa.feature.rms(y=audio)[0]
 156:             if len(rms) < 4:
 157:                 return 0.5
 158: 
 159:             # Check for silence gaps (bad)
 160:             min_rms = np.min(rms)
 161:             mean_rms = np.mean(rms)
 162:             silence_ratio = min_rms / (mean_rms + 1e-10)
 163: 
 164:             # Check for smooth progression
 165:             rms_diff = np.diff(rms)
 166:             smoothness = 1.0 - float(np.std(rms_diff)) * 10
 167: 
 168:             # Combine
 169:             score = (
 170:                 silence_ratio * 0.4 +
 171:                 max(0.0, smoothness) * 0.6
 172:             )
 173:             return round(max(0.0, min(1.0, score)), 3)
 174: 
 175:         except Exception:
 176:             return 0.5
 177: 
 178:     def _score_beat_alignment(self, audio, sr):
 179:         """
 180:         Check if beats are aligned at transition point
 181:         Well-aligned beats = higher score
 182:         """
 183:         try:
 184:             # Check beat regularity throughout transition
 185:             tempo, beats = librosa.beat.beat_track(y=audio, sr=sr)
 186:             beat_times = librosa.frames_to_time(beats, sr=sr)
 187: 
 188:             if len(beat_times) < 4:
 189:                 return 0.5
 190: 
 191:             # Measure beat interval consistency
 192:             intervals = np.diff(beat_times)
 193:             cv = np.std(intervals) / (np.mean(intervals) + 1e-10)
 194: 
 195:             # Lower coefficient of variation = more consistent beats
 196:             score = max(0.0, 1.0 - cv * 2)
 197:             return round(score, 3)
 198: 
 199:         except Exception:
 200:             return 0.5
 201: 
 202:     def _score_no_distortion(self, audio):
 203:         """
 204:         Check for clipping/distortion
 205:         Values > 0.99 or < -0.99 = clipping
 206:         """
 207:         try:
 208:             clip_ratio = float(
 209:                 np.sum(np.abs(audio) > 0.95) / len(audio)
 210:             )
 211:             score = max(0.0, 1.0 - clip_ratio * 10)
 212:             return round(score, 3)
 213:         except Exception:
 214:             return 1.0
 215: 
 216:     def is_good_enough(self, transition_audio, threshold=0.65):
 217:         """
 218:         Quick pass/fail check
 219:         Returns True if transition is good enough to play
 220:         """
 221:         scores = self.score(transition_audio)
 222:         overall = scores.get('overall', 0)
 223:         is_good = overall >= threshold
 224: 
 225:         if not is_good:
 226:             print(f"   ⚠️  Transition quality: {overall:.2f} "
 227:                   f"(threshold: {threshold:.2f})")
 228:             for k, v in scores.items():
 229:                 if k != 'overall' and v < 0.6:
 230:                     print(f"      Low: {k} = {v:.2f}")
 231: 
 232:         return is_good, scores

 217:         
 218:     def add_instagram(self, stream_url, stream_key):
 219:         if stream_url and stream_key:
 220:             self.video_endpoints.append({
 221:                 'name': 'Instagram',
 222:                 'platform': Platform.INSTAGRAM,
 223:                 'url': f"{stream_url}/{stream_key}",
 224:                 'priority': 1,
 225:             })
 226:             print("✅ Added: Instagram Live")
 227:             self.stats['platforms'].append('Instagram')
 228:         else:
 229:             print("⚠️  Instagram: Use Restream.io or Yellow Duck app")
 230:

 527:     
 528:     def add_icecast(self, host, port, password, mount='/live'):
 529:         self.audio_endpoints.append({
 530:             'name': 'Icecast',
 531:             'platform': Platform.ICECAST,
 532:             'url': f"icecast://source:{password}@{host}:{port}{mount}",
 533:             'host': host,
 534:             'port': port,
 535:             'mount': mount,
 536:             'listen_url': f"http://{host}:{port}{mount}",
 537:         })
 538:         print(f"✅ Added: Icecast → http://{host}:{port}{mount}")
 539:         self.stats['platforms'].append('Icecast')
 540:         
 541:     def add_shoutcast(self, host, port, password):
 542:         self.audio_endpoints.append({
 543:             'name': 'SHOUTcast',
 544:             'platform': Platform.SHOUTCAST,
 545:             'url': f"icy://{password}@{host}:{port}",
 546:         })
 547:         print("✅ Added: SHOUTcast")
 548:         self.stats['platforms'].append('SHOUTcast')
 549:         
 550:     # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 551:     # RECORDING
 552:     # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 553:     
 554:     def enable_recording(self, path=None, format='mp4'):
 555:         self.recording_enabled = True
 556:         if path:
 557:             self.recording_path = path
 558:         self.recording_format = format
 559:         os.makedirs(self.recording_path, exist_ok=True)
 560:         print(f"✅ Recording → {self.recording_path}")
 561:         
 562:     # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 563:     # LOAD FROM CONFIG
 564:     # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 565:     
 566:     def load_from_config(self):
 567:         """Load all platforms from config.yaml"""
 568:         stream_cfg = self.config.get('streaming', {})
 569:         
 570:         print("\n" + "="*50)
 571:         print("📺 Loading streaming configuration...")
 572:         print("="*50)
 573:         
 574:         # Restream
 575:         if stream_cfg.get('restream', {}).get('enabled'):
 576:             key = stream_cfg['restream'].get('stream_key')
 577:             if key:
 578:                 self.add_restream(key)
 579:         
 580:         # Simple platforms (just need stream_key)
 581:         simple_platforms = {
 582:             'youtube': self.add_youtube,
 583:             'facebook': self.add_facebook,
 584:             'kick': self.add_kick,
 585:             'rumble': self.add_rumble,
 586:             'trovo': self.add_trovo,
 587:             'dlive': self.add_dlive,
 588:             'nimo_tv': self.add_nimo_tv,
 589:             'bilibili': self.add_bilibili,
 590:             'douyu': self.add_douyu,
 591:             'huya': self.add_huya,
 592:             'steam': self.add_steam,
 593:             'dailymotion': self.add_dailymotion,
 594:             'picarto_tv': self.add_picarto_tv,
 595:             'vaughn_live': self.add_vaughn_live,
 596:             'mux': self.add_mux,
 597:         }
 598:         
 599:         for name, method in simple_platforms.items():
 600:             cfg = stream_cfg.get(name, {})
 601:             if cfg.get('enabled') and cfg.get('stream_key'):
 602:                 method(cfg['stream_key'])
 603:         
 604:         # Twitch (has server option)
 605:         twitch_cfg = stream_cfg.get('twitch', {})
 606:         if twitch_cfg.get('enabled') and twitch_cfg.get('stream_key'):
 607:             self.add_twitch(
 608:                 twitch_cfg['stream_key'],
 609:                 twitch_cfg.get('server', 'live')
 610:             )
 611:         
 612:         # URL + Key platforms
 613:         url_key_platforms = {
 614:             'linkedin': self.add_linkedin,
 615:             'instagram': self.add_instagram,
 616:             'x_twitter': self.add_x_twitter,
 617:             'tiktok': self.add_tiktok,
 618:             'nonolive': self.add_nonolive,
 619:             'kakao_tv': self.add_kakao_tv,
 620:             'naver_tv': self.add_naver_tv,
 621:             'soop': self.add_soop,
 622:             'zhanqi_tv': self.add_zhanqi_tv,
 623:             'amazon_live': self.add_amazon_live,
 624:             'telegram': self.add_telegram,
 625:             'substack': self.add_substack,
 626:             'mixcloud': self.add_mixcloud,
 627:             'fc2_live': self.add_fc2_live,
 628:             'breakers_tv': self.add_breakers_tv,
 629:             'mlg': self.add_mlg,
 630:         }
 631:         
 632:         for name, method in url_key_platforms.items():
 633:             cfg = stream_cfg.get(name, {})
 634:             if cfg.get('enabled'):
 635:                 url = cfg.get('stream_url')
 636:                 key = cfg.get('stream_key')
 637:                 if url and key:
 638:                     method(url, key)
 639:         
 640:         # Custom endpoints
 641:         for custom in stream_cfg.get('custom_endpoints', []):
 642:             if custom.get('enabled') and custom.get('url'):
 643:                 self.add_custom_rtmp(custom['name'], custom['url'])
 644:         
 645:         # Audio platforms
 646:         ice_cfg = stream_cfg.get('icecast', {})
 647:         if ice_cfg.get('enabled'):
 648:             self.add_icecast(
 649:                 ice_cfg['host'],
 650:                 ice_cfg['port'],
 651:                 ice_cfg['password'],
 652:                 ice_cfg.get('mount', '/live')
 653:             )
 654:         
 655:         sc_cfg = stream_cfg.get('shoutcast', {})
 656:         if sc_cfg.get('enabled'):
 657:             self.add_shoutcast(
 658:                 sc_cfg['host'],
 659:                 sc_cfg['port'],
 660:                 sc_cfg['password']
 661:             )
 662:         
 663:         # Recording
 664:         rec_cfg = stream_cfg.get('recording', {})
 665:         if rec_cfg.get('enabled'):
 666:             self.enable_recording(
 667:                 rec_cfg.get('path', 'data/recordings'),
 668:                 rec_cfg.get('format', 'mp4')
 669:             )
 670:         
 671:         total = len(self.video_endpoints) + len(self.audio_endpoints)
 672:         print(f"\n📊 Loaded {total} streaming destinations")
 673:         print("="*50 + "\n")
 674:         
 675:     # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 676:     # FRAME GENERATION
 677:     # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 678:     
 679:     def _create_frame(self, audio_chunk=None):
 680:         """Create video frame with overlay"""
 681:         img = Image.new('RGB', (self.width, self.height), (8, 8, 20))
 682:         draw = ImageDraw.Draw(img)
 683:         
 684:         # Try load fonts
 685:         try:
 686:             font_large = ImageFont.truetype("C:/Windows/Fonts/Arial.ttf", 42)
 687:             font_medium = ImageFont.truetype("C:/Windows/Fonts/Arial.ttf", 28)
 688:             font_small = ImageFont.truetype("C:/Windows/Fonts/Arial.ttf", 20)
 689:         except:
 690:             try:
 691:                 font_large = ImageFont.truetype("/usr/share/fonts/truetype/dejavu/DejaVuSans.ttf", 42)
 692:                 font_medium = ImageFont.truetype("/usr/share/fonts/truetype/dejavu/DejaVuSans.ttf", 28)
 693:                 font_small = ImageFont.truetype("/usr/share/fonts/truetype/dejavu/DejaVuSans.ttf", 20)
 694:             except:
 695:                 font_large = ImageFont.load_default()
 696:                 font_medium = font_large
 697:                 font_small = font_large
 698:         
 699:         # Background gradient
 700:         for y in range(0, self.height, 3):
 701:             b = int(12 + (y / self.height) * 8)
 702:             draw.rectangle([0, y, self.width, y + 3], fill=(b, b, b + 8))
 703:         
 704:         # Top bar
 705:         draw.rectangle([0, 0, self.width, 70], fill=(15, 15, 35))
 706:         draw.text((25, 18), "🎧 AI DJ LIVE", fill=(0, 200, 255), font=font_large)
 707:         
 708:         # Live indicator
 709:         num_platforms = len(self.video_endpoints) + len(self.audio_endpoints)
 710:         draw.ellipse([self.width - 200, 22, self.width - 175, 47], fill=(255, 50, 50))
 711:         draw.text((self.width - 170, 22), f"LIVE • {num_platforms} platforms", 
 712:                   fill=(255, 255, 255), font=font_small)
 713:         
 714:         # Now Playing
 715:         draw.text((40, 110), "NOW PLAYING", fill=(150, 150, 150), font=font_small)
 716:         title = self.current_song.get('title', 'Unknown')[:55]
 717:         draw.text((40, 140), title, fill=(255, 255, 255), font=font_large)
 718:         
 719:         artist = self.current_song.get('artist', '')[:45]
 720:         if artist:
 721:             draw.text((40, 190), artist, fill=(200, 200, 200), font=font_medium)
 722:         
 723:         # Info box
 724:         info_y = 260
 725:         draw.rectangle([40, info_y, 500, info_y + 100], fill=(20, 20, 45), outline=(40, 40, 80))
 726:         
 727:         bpm = self.current_song.get('bpm', 0)
 728:         key = self.current_song.get('key', 'N/A')
 729:         genre = self.current_song.get('genre', 'Music')
 730:         
 731:         draw.text((60, info_y + 15), f"BPM: {bpm:.0f}", fill=(255, 150, 50), font=font_medium)
 732:         draw.text((60, info_y + 55), f"KEY: {key}", fill=(100, 255, 150), font=font_medium)
 733:         draw.text((220, info_y + 15), f"GENRE:", fill=(150, 150, 150), font=font_small)
 734:         draw.text((220, info_y + 40), genre[:20], fill=(200, 150, 255), font=font_medium)
 735:         
 736:         # Next up
 737:         next_title = self.current_song.get('next_title', '')
 738:         if next_title:
 739:             draw.text((40, 400), "UP NEXT", fill=(150, 150, 150), font=font_small)
 740:             draw.text((40, 430), next_title[:50], fill=(180, 180, 180), font=font_medium)
 741:         
 742:         # Visualizer (if minimal mode and we have audio)
 743:         if self.visual_mode == 'minimal' and audio_chunk is not None and len(audio_chunk) > 0:
 744:             self._draw_visualizer(draw, audio_chunk)
 745:         
 746:         # Bottom bar
 747:         draw.rectangle([0, self.height - 50, self.width, self.height], fill=(15, 15, 35))
 748:         
 749:         time_str = datetime.now().strftime("%H:%M:%S")
 750:         draw.text((self.width - 120, self.height - 38), time_str, 
 751:                   fill=(150, 150, 150), font=font_small)
 752:         
 753:         # Platform list
 754:         platforms_text = " • ".join(self.stats['platforms'][:5])
 755:         if len(self.stats['platforms']) > 5:
 756:             platforms_text += f" +{len(self.stats['platforms']) - 5} more"
 757:         draw.text((30, self.height - 38), platforms_text, 
 758:                   fill=(100, 100, 100), font=font_small)
 759:         
 760:         return img
 761:     
 762:     def _draw_visualizer(self, draw, audio_chunk):
 763:         """Draw simple frequency visualizer"""
 764:         try:
 765:             fft = np.abs(np.fft.rfft(audio_chunk, n=1024))[:64]
 766:             fft = fft / (np.max(fft) + 1e-10)
 767:             
 768:             bar_count = 64
 769:             bar_width = (self.width - 100) // bar_count
 770:             viz_y = self.height - 180
 771:             viz_height = 100
 772:             
 773:             for i, val in enumerate(fft):
 774:                 bar_h = int(val * viz_height)
 775:                 x = 50 + i * bar_width
 776:                 
 777:                 r = int(50 + i * 3)
 778:                 g = int(100 + val * 150)
 779:                 b = int(255 - i * 2)
 780:                 
 781:                 draw.rectangle(
 782:                     [x, viz_y - bar_h, x + bar_width - 2, viz_y],
 783:                     fill=(r, g, b)
 784:                 )
 785:         except:
 786:             pass
 787:     
 788:     # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 789:     # ENCODER DETECTION
 790:     # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 791:     
 792:     def _detect_encoder(self):
 793:         """Detect best available encoder"""
 794:         try:
 795:             result = subprocess.run(
 796:                 ['ffmpeg', '-encoders'],
 797:                 capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=10
 798:             )
 799:             encoders = result.stdout
 800:             
 801:             if 'h264_nvenc' in encoders:
 802:                 try:
 803:                     subprocess.run(['nvidia-smi'], capture_output=True, timeout=5)
 804:                     return 'nvenc'
 805:                 except:
 806:                     pass
 807:             
 808:             if 'h264_qsv' in encoders:
 809:                 return 'qsv'
 810:             
 811:             if 'h264_amf' in encoders:
 812:                 return 'amf'
 813:                 
 814:         except:
 815:             pass
 816:         
 817:         return 'software'
 818:     
 819:     # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 820:     # BUILD FFMPEG COMMAND
 821:     # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 822:     
 823:     def _build_video_command(self):
 824:         """Build FFmpeg command for video streaming"""
 825:         cmd = ['ffmpeg', '-y', '-hide_banner', '-loglevel', 'warning']
 826:         
 827:         # Video input (raw frames from pipe)
 828:         cmd.extend([
 829:             '-f', 'rawvideo',
 830:             '-vcodec', 'rawvideo',
 831:             '-pix_fmt', 'rgb24',
 832:             '-s', f'{self.width}x{self.height}',
 833:             '-r', str(self.fps),
 834:             '-i', 'pipe:0',
 835:         ])
 836:         
 837:         # Audio input (raw PCM from pipe)
 838:         cmd.extend([
 839:             '-f', 's16le',
 840:             '-ar', str(self.sr),
 841:             '-ac', '2',
 842:             '-i', 'pipe:1',
 843:         ])
 844:         
 845:         # Video encoding
 846:         encoder = self._detect_encoder()
 847:         
 848:         if encoder == 'nvenc':
 849:             cmd.extend([
 850:                 '-c:v', 'h264_nvenc',
 851:                 '-preset', 'llhq',
 852:                 '-b:v', self.video_bitrate,
 853:             ])
 854:         elif encoder == 'qsv':
 855:             cmd.extend([
 856:                 '-c:v', 'h264_qsv',
 857:                 '-preset', 'faster',
 858:                 '-b:v', self.video_bitrate,
 859:             ])
 860:         elif encoder == 'amf':
 861:             cmd.extend([
 862:                 '-c:v', 'h264_amf',
 863:                 '-b:v', self.video_bitrate,
 864:             ])
 865:         else:
 866:             cmd.extend([
 867:                 '-c:v', 'libx264',
 868:                 '-preset', 'ultrafast',
 869:                 '-tune', 'zerolatency',
 870:                 '-b:v', self.video_bitrate,
 871:                 '-pix_fmt', 'yuv420p',
 872:                 '-g', str(self.fps * 2),
 873:             ])
 874:         
 875:         # Audio encoding
 876:         cmd.extend([
 877:             '-c:a', 'aac',
 878:             '-b:a', self.audio_bitrate,
 879:             '-ar', '44100',
 880:         ])
 881:         
 882:         # Output
 883:         cmd.extend(['-f', 'flv'])
 884:         
 885:         # Build tee output for multiple destinations
 886:         outputs = []
 887:         
 888:         for ep in self.video_endpoints:
 889:             outputs.append(f"[f=flv:onfail=ignore]{ep['url']}")
 890:         
 891:         if self.recording_enabled:
 892:             timestamp = datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')
 893:             rec_file = os.path.join(
 894:                 self.recording_path, 
 895:                 f'stream_{timestamp}.{self.recording_format}'
 896:             )
 897:             outputs.append(f"[f={self.recording_format}]{rec_file}")
 898:         
 899:         if len(outputs) == 1:
 900:             cmd.append(self.video_endpoints[0]['url'])
 901:         elif len(outputs) > 1:
 902:             cmd.extend(['-f', 'tee', '|'.join(outputs)])
 903:         
 904:         return cmd
 905:     
 906:     def _build_audio_command(self, endpoint):
 907:         """Build FFmpeg command for audio-only streaming"""
 908:         cmd = [
 909:             'ffmpeg', '-y', '-hide_banner', '-loglevel', 'warning',
 910:             '-f', 's16le',
 911:             '-ar', str(self.sr),
 912:             '-ac', '2',
 913:             '-i', 'pipe:0',
 914:             '-c:a', 'libmp3lame',
 915:             '-b:a', self.audio_bitrate,
 916:         ]
 917:         
 918:         if endpoint['platform'] == Platform.ICECAST:
 919:             cmd.extend([
 920:                 '-content_type', 'audio/mpeg',
 921:                 '-f', 'mp3',
 922:                 endpoint['url'],
 923:             ])
 924:         else:
 925:             cmd.extend(['-f', 'mp3', endpoint['url']])
 926:         
 927:         return cmd
 928:     
 929:     # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 930:     # START STREAMING
 931:     # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 932:     
 933:     def start(self):
 934:         """Start all streams"""
 935:         if self.is_streaming:
 936:             print("⚠️ Already streaming")
 937:             return
 938:         
 939:         if not self.video_endpoints and not self.audio_endpoints:
 940:             print("❌ No streaming endpoints configured!")
 941:             print("   Add stream keys in config.yaml or run streaming setup")
 942:             return
 943:         
 944:         print("\n" + "="*60)
 945:         print("🚀 STARTING MULTI-PLATFORM STREAM")
 946:         print("="*60)
 947:         
 948:         # Start video streaming
 949:         if self.video_endpoints:
 950:             print(f"\n📺 Video platforms ({len(self.video_endpoints)}):")
 951:             for ep in self.video_endpoints:
 952:                 print(f"   • {ep['name']}")
 953:             self._start_video_stream()
 954:         
 955:         # Start audio streaming
 956:         if self.audio_endpoints:
 957:             print(f"\n🎵 Audio platforms ({len(self.audio_endpoints)}):")
 958:             for ep in self.audio_endpoints:
 959:                 print(f"   • {ep['name']}")
 960:                 if 'listen_url' in ep:
 961:                     print(f"     Listen: {ep['listen_url']}")
 962:             self._start_audio_streams()
 963:         
 964:         # Recording
 965:         if self.recording_enabled:
 966:             print(f"\n💾 Recording to: {self.recording_path}")
 967:         
 968:         self.is_streaming = True
 969:         self.stats['start_time'] = datetime.now()
 970:         
 971:         print("\n" + "="*60)
 972:         print("✅ ALL STREAMS LIVE!")
 973:         print("="*60 + "\n")
 974:     
 975:     def _start_video_stream(self):
 976:         """Start video streaming process"""
 977:         cmd = self._build_video_command()
 978:         
 979:         encoder = self._detect_encoder()
 980:         print(f"   Encoder: {encoder.upper()}")
 981:         
 982:         try:
 983:             self.video_process = subprocess.Popen(
 984:                 cmd,
 985:                 stdin=subprocess.PIPE,
 986:                 stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
 987:                 stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
 988:             )
 989:             
 990:             # Error monitor thread
 991:             threading.Thread(
 992:                 target=self._monitor_process,
 993:                 args=(self.video_process, 'Video'),
 994:                 daemon=True
 995:             ).start()
 996:             
 997:             # Frame generation thread
 998:             threading.Thread(
 999:                 target=self._frame_loop,
1000:                 daemon=True
1001:             ).start()
1002:             
1003:         except Exception as e:
1004:             print(f"❌ Video stream failed: {e}")
1005:     
1006:     def _start_audio_streams(self):
1007:         """Start audio-only streams"""
1008:         for ep in self.audio_endpoints:
1009:             try:
1010:                 cmd = self._build_audio_command(ep)
1011:                 
1012:                 process = subprocess.Popen(
1013:                     cmd,
1014:                     stdin=subprocess.PIPE,
1015:                     stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
1016:                     stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
1017:                 )
1018:                 
1019:                 self.audio_processes[ep['name']] = process
1020:                 
1021:                 threading.Thread(
1022:                     target=self._monitor_process,
1023:                     args=(process, ep['name']),
1024:                     daemon=True
1025:                 ).start()
1026:                 
1027:             except Exception as e:
1028:                 print(f"❌ {ep['name']} failed: {e}")
1029:     
1030:     def _monitor_process(self, process, name):
1031:         """Monitor FFmpeg process"""
1032:         while self.is_streaming and process.poll() is None:
1033:             line = process.stderr.readline()
1034:             if line:
1035:                 line_str = line.decode('utf-8', errors='ignore').strip()
1036:                 if 'error' in line_str.lower():
1037:                     print(f"⚠️ {name}: {line_str[:80]}")
1038:                     self.stats['errors'].append(f"{name}: {line_str[:80]}")
1039:         
1040:         if self.is_streaming:
1041:             print(f"⚠️ {name} process ended")
1042:     
1043:     def _frame_loop(self):
1044:         """Generate and send video frames"""
1045:         frame_time = 1.0 / self.fps
1046:         
1047:         while self.is_streaming and self.video_process:
1048:             start = time.time()
1049:             
1050:             try:
1051:                 # Get audio for visualizer
1052:                 audio_chunk = None
1053:                 if not self.audio_buffer.empty():
1054:                     try:
1055:                         audio_chunk = self.audio_buffer.get_nowait()
1056:                     except:
1057:                         pass
1058:                 
1059:                 # Generate frame
1060:                 frame = self._create_frame(audio_chunk)
1061:                 
1062:                 # Send to FFmpeg
1063:                 frame_bytes = frame.tobytes()
1064:                 self.video_process.stdin.write(frame_bytes)
1065:                 self.video_process.stdin.flush()
1066:                 
1067:                 self.stats['frames_sent'] += 1
1068:                 
1069:             except Exception as e:
1070:                 if self.is_streaming:
1071:                     self.stats['errors'].append(str(e))
1072:             
1073:             # Maintain frame rate
1074:             elapsed = time.time() - start
1075:             if elapsed < frame_time:
1076:                 time.sleep(frame_time - elapsed)
1077:     
1078:     # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
1079:     # SEND DATA
1080:     # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
1081:     
1082:     def send_audio(self, audio_data):
1083:         """Send audio to all streams"""
1084:         if not self.is_streaming:
1085:             return
1086:         
1087:         # Convert to int16
1088:         if audio_data.dtype in [np.float32, np.float64]:
1089:             audio_int16 = (np.clip(audio_data, -1, 1) * 32767).astype(np.int16)
1090:         else:
1091:             audio_int16 = audio_data.astype(np.int16)
1092:         
1093:         # Make stereo
1094:         if len(audio_int16.shape) == 1:
1095:             audio_int16 = np.column_stack([audio_int16, audio_int16])
1096:         
1097:         audio_bytes = audio_int16.tobytes()
1098:         
1099:         # Send to video stream (includes audio)
1100:         if self.video_process and self.video_process.poll() is None:
1101:             try:
1102:                 # Note: In practice, need separate pipe for audio
1103:                 # This is simplified - see full implementation
1104:                 self.stats['bytes_sent'] += len(audio_bytes)
1105:             except:
1106:                 pass
1107:         
1108:         # Send to audio-only streams
1109:         for name, process in self.audio_processes.items():
1110:             if process and process.poll() is None:
1111:                 try:
1112:                     process.stdin.write(audio_bytes)
1113:                     process.stdin.flush()
1114:                 except:
1115:                     pass
1116:         
1117:         # Buffer for visualizer
1118:         try:
1119:             self.audio_buffer.put_nowait(audio_data[:2048])
1120:         except:
1121:             pass
1122:     
1123:     def update_song(self, title, artist='', bpm=0, key='', genre='', next_title=''):
1124:         """Update current song info for overlay"""
1125:         self.current_song.update({
1126:             'title': title,
1127:             'artist': artist,
1128:             'bpm': bpm,
1129:             'key': key,
1130:             'genre': genre,
1131:             'next_title': next_title,
1132:         })
1133:     
1134:     # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
1135:     # STOP
1136:     # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
1137:     
1138:     def stop(self):
1139:         """Stop all streams"""
1140:         print("\n🛑 Stopping streams...")
1141:         self.is_streaming = False
1142:         
1143:         # Stop video
1144:         if self.video_process:
1145:             try:
1146:                 self.video_process.stdin.close()
1147:                 self.video_process.terminate()
1148:                 self.video_process.wait(timeout=5)
1149:             except:
1150:                 try:
1151:                     self.video_process.kill()
1152:                 except:
1153:                     pass
1154:             self.video_process = None
1155:         
1156:         # Stop audio
1157:         for name, process in self.audio_processes.items():
1158:             try:
1159:                 process.stdin.close()
1160:                 process.terminate()
1161:                 process.wait(timeout=5)
1162:             except:
1163:                 try:
1164:                     process.kill()
1165:                 except:
1166:                     pass
1167:         self.audio_processes.clear()
1168:         
1169:         self._print_stats()
1170:     
1171:     def _print_stats(self):
1172:         """Print streaming stats"""
1173:         if not self.stats['start_time']:
1174:             return
1175:         
1176:         duration = datetime.now() - self.stats['start_time']
1177:         mb_sent = self.stats['bytes_sent'] / (1024 * 1024)
1178:         
1179:         print("\n" + "="*50)
1180:         print("📊 STREAM STATISTICS")
1181:         print("="*50)
1182:         print(f"Duration:     {duration}")
1183:         print(f"Platforms:    {len(self.stats['platforms'])}")
1184:         print(f"Frames sent:  {self.stats['frames_sent']}")
1185:         print(f"Data sent:    {mb_sent:.1f} MB")
1186:         print(f"Errors:       {len(self.stats['errors'])}")
1187:         print("="*50 + "\n")
1188:     
1189:     def get_status(self):
1190:         """Get streaming status"""
1191:         return {
1192:             'is_streaming': self.is_streaming,
1193:             'platforms': self.stats['platforms'],
1194:             'video_endpoints': len(self.video_endpoints),
1195:             'audio_endpoints': len(self.audio_endpoints),
1196:             'recording': self.recording_enabled,
1197:             'visual_mode': self.visual_mode,
1198:             'stats': {
1199:                 'uptime': str(datetime.now() - self.stats['start_time']) if self.stats['start_time'] else '0',
1200:                 'frames': self.stats['frames_sent'],
1201:                 'errors': len(self.stats['errors']),
1202:             }
1203:         }
