================================================================================
FILE: tools\repair_sync.py
================================================================================
   1: import os
   2: import re
   3: 
   4: def repair_file(filepath):
   5:     with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
   6:         content = f.read()
   7: 
   8:     # Generic pattern to catch sync_github damage
   9:     # try:\n    try:\n    import/from ...\nexcept ...:\n    ...\nexcept ...:\n    ...
  10:     # Note: Using non-greedy and dotall to handle variations
  11:     
  12:     # regex to find the double-try mess
  13:     # We want to catch the specific pattern of try: try: indented_import except: fallback except: fallback
  14:     pattern = re.compile(r'try:\s+try:\s+(import|from)\s+([^\n]+)\s+except\s*([^:]*):\s+([^\n]+)\s+except\s*([^:]*):\s+[^\n]+', re.MULTILINE)
  15:     
  16:     def replacer(match):
  17:         keyword = match.group(1)
  18:         module = match.group(2)
  19:         ex_type = match.group(3) or "Exception"
  20:         fallback = match.group(4)
  21:         return f'try:\n    {keyword} {module}\nexcept {ex_type}:\n    {fallback}'
  22: 
  23:     new_content = pattern.sub(replacer, content)
  24:     
  25:     if new_content != content:
  26:         with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
  27:             f.write(new_content)
  28:         return True
  29:     return False
  30: 
  31: def walk_and_repair(root_dir):
  32:     repaired = []
  33:     for root, dirs, files in os.walk(root_dir):
  34:         for file in files:
  35:             if file.endswith('.py'):
  36:                 path = os.path.join(root, file)
  37:                 if repair_file(path):
  38:                     repaired.append(path)
  39:     return repaired
  40: 
  41: if __name__ == "__main__":
  42:     repaired_files = walk_and_repair('.')
  43:     print(f"Repaired {len(repaired_files)} files:")
  44:     for f in repaired_files:
  45:         print(f" - {f}")



================================================================================
FILE: tools\sync_github.py
================================================================================
   1: import subprocess
   2: import os
   3: import re
   4: import sys
   5: 
   6: # Set encoding for output to avoid UnicodeEncodeError on Windows
   7: if hasattr(sys.stdout, 'reconfigure'):
   8:     sys.stdout.reconfigure(encoding='utf-8')
   9: 
  10: def strip_emojis(text):
  11:     # Remove things like "📄 " or other emojis at the start of paths
  12:     # The emoji "📄" is often at the start
  13:     text = text.replace('📄 ', '').replace('📄', '')
  14:     return text.strip()
  15: 
  16: def apply_fixes(content, filename):
  17:     if filename.endswith('.py'):
  18:         # Apply the try-except fixes I did earlier to avoid ImportError crashes
  19:         content = content.replace('import torch', 'try:\n    import torch\nexcept ImportError:\n    torch = None\n')
  20:         content = content.replace('torch.cuda.is_available()', '(False if torch is None else torch.cuda.is_available())')
  21:         content = content.replace('import whisper', 'try:\n    import whisper\nexcept ImportError:\n    whisper = None\n')
  22:         content = content.replace('import pronouncing', 'try:\n    import pronouncing\nexcept:\n    pronouncing = None')
  23:         content = content.replace('from phonemizer import phonemize', 'try:\n    from phonemizer import phonemize\nexcept:\n    phonemize = None')
  24:         content = content.replace('import obsws_python as obs', 'try:\n    import obsws_python as obs\nexcept:\n    obs = None')
  25:         
  26:     return content
  27: 
  28: def sync():
  29:     # Tell git not to quote paths with special characters
  30:     subprocess.run(['git', 'config', 'core.quotepath', 'false'], check=True)
  31: 
  32:     print("Fetching file list from origin/main...")
  33:     result = subprocess.run(['git', 'ls-tree', '-r', 'origin/main'], capture_output=True, text=True, encoding='utf-8')
  34:     if result.returncode != 0:
  35:         print("Error fetching file list")
  36:         return
  37: 
  38:     lines = result.stdout.strip().split('\n')
  39:     for line in lines:
  40:         parts = line.split('\t')
  41:         if len(parts) < 2:
  42:             continue
  43:         
  44:         raw_path = parts[1].strip('"') # Git might still surround it with quotes
  45:         clean_path = strip_emojis(raw_path)
  46:         
  47:         # Skip files with names like "Open Command Prompt..." on Windows
  48:         if "Open Command Prompt" in clean_path or "Install " in clean_path or clean_path.startswith("python install"):
  49:             print(f"Skipping potentially problematic file: {clean_path}")
  50:             continue
  51: 
  52:         print(f"Syncing {clean_path}...")
  53:         
  54:         # Get content
  55:         # Use subprocess with shell=True for complex paths or just pass it directly
  56:         # raw_path might contain spaces or special chars
  57:         content_result = subprocess.run(['git', 'show', f'origin/main:{raw_path}'], capture_output=True, encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore')
  58:         if content_result.returncode != 0:
  59:             # Try once more with double quotes around path just in case
  60:             content_result = subprocess.run(['git', 'show', f'origin/main:"{raw_path}"'], capture_output=True, encoding='utf-8', errors='ignore')
  61:             if content_result.returncode != 0:
  62:                 print(f"Failed to get content for {raw_path}")
  63:                 continue
  64:             
  65:         content = content_result.stdout
  66:         
  67:         # Apply fixes
  68:         content = apply_fixes(content, clean_path)
  69:         
  70:         # For config.yaml, we want to keep the playlist URL
  71:         if clean_path == 'config.yaml' and os.path.exists(clean_path):
  72:             with open(clean_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
  73:                 old_conf = f.read()
  74:             if 'youtube:' in content and 'playlist_url:' in old_conf:
  75:                 m = re.search(r'playlist_url:\s*"([^"]+)"', old_conf)
  76:                 if m:
  77:                     current_url = m.group(1)
  78:                     content = re.sub(r'playlist_url:\s*"[^"]*"', f'playlist_url: "{current_url}"', content)
  79: 
  80:         # Create directories
  81:         target_dir = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(clean_path))
  82:         if not os.path.exists(target_dir):
  83:             os.makedirs(target_dir, exist_ok=True)
  84:         
  85:         with open(clean_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
  86:             f.write(content)
  87: 
  88:     print("\nSync complete!")
  89:     print("Applied local dependency fixes (try/except) to prevent crashes.")
  90: 
  91: if __name__ == "__main__":
  92:     sync()

   1: import numpy as np
   2: import sounddevice as sd
   3: import soundfile as sf

   9: from ai_brain.agents.wordplay_agent import WordplayAgent

  11: class MasterTransitionEngine:
  12:     """
  13:     Executes all transition techniques
  14:     Central hub that routes to correct technique
  15:     """
  16:     def __init__(self, config):
  17:         self.config = config
  18:         self.sr = config['audio']['sample_rate']
  19:         self.stems_dir = config['paths']['stems']
  20:         self.cache_dir = config['paths']['audio_cache']
  21:         self.is_playing = False
  22:         self.playback_thread = None
  23:         self.test_mode = False
  24:         self.output_buffer = []
  25:         self.wordplay_agent = WordplayAgent(config)
  26: 
  27:     # ============================================================
  28:     # CORE ROUTING
  29:     # ============================================================
  30: 
  31:     def execute(self, current_id, next_id, technique, params,
  32:                 current_analysis, next_analysis):
  33:         """Route to correct transition technique"""
  34: 
  35:         techniques = {
  36:             'beatmatch_crossfade':      self.beatmatch_crossfade,
  37:             'cut_transition':           self.cut_transition,
  38:             'echo_out':                 self.echo_out,
  39:             'filter_sweep':             self.filter_sweep,
  40:             'loop_roll':                self.loop_roll,
  41:             'reverb_wash':              self.reverb_wash,
  42:             'spinback':                 self.spinback,
  43:             'tempo_ramp':               self.tempo_ramp,
  44:             'white_noise_sweep':        self.white_noise_sweep,
  45:             'vinyl_scratch_flourish':   self.vinyl_scratch_flourish,
  46:             'tone_play':                self.tone_play,
  47:             'wordplay':                 self.wordplay_transition,
  48:             'mashup_short':             self.mashup_short,
  49:             'mashup_extended':          self.mashup_extended,
  50:             'acapella_layer':           self.acapella_layer,
  51:             'drum_swap':                self.drum_swap,
  52:             'bass_swap':                self.bass_swap,
  53:             'stutter_glitch':           self.stutter_glitch,
  54:             'half_time_transition':     self.half_time_transition,
  55:             'wordplay_mashup':          self.wordplay_mashup,
  56:             'phrasal_interlace':        self.phrasal_interlace,
  57:             'semantic_bridge':          self.semantic_bridge,
  58:         }
  59: 
  60:         handler = techniques.get(technique)
  61:         
  62:         # 🤖 Check if this is an AI-invented innovation
  63:         if not handler:
  64:             innovation = self._get_innovation_details(technique)
  65:             if innovation:
  66:                 print(f"   🧬 Executing AI Innovation: {technique}")
  67:                 try:
  68:                     return self._dispatch_innovation(current_id, next_id, params,
  69:                                                 current_analysis, next_analysis, innovation)
  70:                 except Exception as e:
  71:                     print(f"   ⚠️ Innovation dispatch failed: {e}")
  72:                     handler = self.beatmatch_crossfade
  73:             else:
  74:                 handler = self.beatmatch_crossfade
  75: 
  76:         print(f"   🎚️  Executing: {technique}")
  77: 
  78:         try:
  79:             handler(current_id, next_id, params,
  80:                     current_analysis, next_analysis)
  81:         except Exception as e:
  82:             print(f"   ❌ Transition error: {e}")
  83:             import traceback
  84:             traceback.print_exc()
  85:             self.cut_transition(current_id, next_id, {},
  86:                                 current_analysis, next_analysis)
  87:                                 
  88:         # FIXED: Return the output path if we are in test mode so main.py gets it
  89:         if self.test_mode and self.output_buffer:
  90:             mix_data = np.concatenate(self.output_buffer)
  91:             out_path = os.path.join(self.config['paths']['sandbox'], 'test_mix.wav')
  92:             sf.write(out_path, mix_data, self.sr)
  93:             return out_path
  94:         return None
  95: 
  96:     def _get_innovation_details(self, tech_name):
  97:         """Helper to load details of an invented technique"""
  98:         try:
  99:             path = 'data/logs/innovations.json'
 100:             if os.path.exists(path):
 101:                 with open(path, 'r') as f:
 102:                     data = json.load(f)
 103:                     for tech in data.get('techniques', []):
 104:                         if tech['name'] == tech_name:
 105:                             return tech
 106:         except:
 107:             pass
 108:         return None
 109: 
 110:     def _dispatch_innovation(self, cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana, innovation):
 111:         """Routes to a composed innovation behavior"""
 112:         itype = innovation.get('type')
 113:         if itype == 'hybrid':
 114:             parent_a, parent_b = innovation['parents']
 115:             # Execute first parent for half, then second? 
 116:             # Simplified: Use params from innovation combined with user params
 117:             # For now, we use the first parent's logic but with mutated params if present
 118:             parent_handler = self.execute
 119:             return parent_handler(cur_id, nxt_id, parent_a, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana)
 120:             
 121:         elif itype == 'mutation':
 122:             base_tech = innovation['base']
 123:             mutated_params = {**params, **innovation.get('mutation', {})}
 124:             # Check for expanded innovation params
 125:             return self.execute(cur_id, nxt_id, base_tech, mutated_params, cur_ana, nxt_ana)
 126:         
 127:         return self.beatmatch_crossfade(cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana)
 128: 
 129:     def generate_transition_mix(self, cur_id, nxt_id, technique, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana):
 130:         """Generates a mix file instead of playing live"""
 131:         self.test_mode = True
 132:         self.output_buffer = []
 133:         
 134:         out_path = self.execute(cur_id, nxt_id, technique, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana)
 135:         
 136:         self.test_mode = False
 137:         return out_path
 138: 
 139:     # ============================================================
 140:     # AUDIO UTILITIES
 141:     # ============================================================
 142: 
 143:     def _load_audio(self, song_id):
 144:         """Load full song audio"""
 145:         path = os.path.join(self.cache_dir, f"{song_id}.mp3")
 146:         if os.path.exists(path):
 147:             y, sr = librosa.load(path, sr=self.sr, mono=True)
 148:             return y, sr
 149:         print(f"   ❌ Audio not found: {song_id}")
 150:         return None, None
 151: 
 152:     def _load_stem(self, song_id, stem_name):
 153:         """Load a specific stem (vocals/drums/bass/melody)"""
 154:         for ext in ['wav', 'mp3']:
 155:             path = os.path.join(
 156:                 self.stems_dir, song_id, f"{stem_name}.{ext}"
 157:             )
 158:             if os.path.exists(path):
 159:                 y, sr = librosa.load(path, sr=self.sr, mono=True)
 160:                 return y, sr
 161:         return None, None
 162: 
 163:     def _play_audio(self, audio, sr=None):
 164:         """Play audio or save to buffer if in test mode"""
 165:         if self.test_mode:
 166:             self.output_buffer.append(audio)
 167:             return
 168:             
 169:         if sr is None:
 170:             sr = self.sr
 171:         if audio is None or len(audio) == 0:
 172:             return
 173:         # Normalize to prevent clipping
 174:         max_val = np.max(np.abs(audio))
 175:         if max_val > 0:
 176:             audio = audio / max_val * 0.85
 177:         sd.play(audio.astype(np.float32), sr)
 178:         sd.wait()
 179: 
 180:     def _get_transition_point(self, analysis, audio_len):
 181:         """Get the sample index where transition should start"""
 182:         sr = self.sr
 183:         trans_time = analysis.get(
 184:             'transition_points', {}
 185:         ).get('outro_beat', (audio_len / sr) * 0.80)
 186:         return int(trans_time * sr)
 187: 
 188:     def _get_entry_point(self, analysis):
 189:         """Get best entry time for incoming song in seconds"""
 190:         entry_points = analysis.get('entry_points', {})
 191:         if entry_points and entry_points.get('best_entry'):
 192:             return entry_points['best_entry'].get('time', 0)
 193:         return 0.0
 194: 
 195:     def _fade_out(self, audio, fade_samples=None):
 196:         if fade_samples is None:
 197:             fade_samples = min(int(self.sr * 2), len(audio))
 198:         if fade_samples == 0 or len(audio) == 0:
 199:             return audio
 200:         fade = np.ones(len(audio))
 201:         fade[-fade_samples:] = np.linspace(1, 0, fade_samples)
 202:         return audio * fade
 203: 
 204:     def _fade_in(self, audio, fade_samples=None):
 205:         if fade_samples is None:
 206:             fade_samples = min(int(self.sr * 2), len(audio))
 207:         if fade_samples == 0 or len(audio) == 0:
 208:             return audio
 209:         fade = np.ones(len(audio))
 210:         fade[:fade_samples] = np.linspace(0, 1, fade_samples)
 211:         return audio * fade
 212: 
 213:     def _apply_reverb(self, audio, room_size=0.5):
 214:         delay_times = [0.03, 0.05, 0.07, 0.11, 0.13, 0.17]
 215:         gains = [room_size * g for g in [0.8, 0.6, 0.5, 0.4, 0.3, 0.2]]
 216:         output = audio.copy()
 217:         for delay_time, gain in zip(delay_times, gains):
 218:             delay_samples = int(delay_time * self.sr)
 219:             if delay_samples < len(audio):
 220:                 delayed = np.zeros_like(audio)
 221:                 delayed[delay_samples:] = audio[:-delay_samples] * gain
 222:                 output = output + delayed
 223:         max_val = np.max(np.abs(output))
 224:         if max_val > 0:
 225:             output = output / max_val
 226:         return output
 227: 
 228:     def _apply_echo(self, audio, delay_ms=375, feedback=0.6, num_echoes=4):
 229:         delay_samples = int((delay_ms / 1000) * self.sr)
 230:         output = audio.copy()
 231:         for i in range(1, num_echoes + 1):
 232:             offset = delay_samples * i
 233:             if offset < len(audio):
 234:                 echo = np.zeros_like(audio)
 235:                 echo[offset:] = audio[:-offset] * (feedback ** i)
 236:                 output = output + echo
 237:         max_val = np.max(np.abs(output))
 238:         if max_val > 0:
 239:             output = output / max_val
 240:         return output
 241: 
 242:     def _apply_highpass(self, audio, cutoff_hz, order=4):
 243:         cutoff_norm = min(0.99, max(0.001, cutoff_hz / (self.sr / 2)))
 244:         b, a = signal.butter(order, cutoff_norm, btype='high')
 245:         return signal.filtfilt(b, a, audio)
 246: 
 247:     def _apply_lowpass(self, audio, cutoff_hz, order=4):
 248:         cutoff_norm = min(0.99, max(0.001, cutoff_hz / (self.sr / 2)))
 249:         b, a = signal.butter(order, cutoff_norm, btype='low')
 250:         return signal.filtfilt(b, a, audio)
 251: 
 252:     def _pitch_shift_semitones(self, audio, semitones):
 253:         return librosa.effects.pitch_shift(audio, sr=self.sr, n_steps=semitones)
 254: 
 255:     def _time_stretch(self, audio, rate):
 256:         if abs(rate - 1.0) < 0.01:
 257:             return audio
 258:         return librosa.effects.time_stretch(audio, rate=rate)
 259: 
 260:     def _mix(self, audio_a, audio_b, weight_a=0.5, weight_b=0.5):
 261:         max_len = max(len(audio_a), len(audio_b))
 262:         a_padded = np.pad(audio_a, (0, max_len - len(audio_a)))
 263:         b_padded = np.pad(audio_b, (0, max_len - len(audio_b)))
 264:         return a_padded * weight_a + b_padded * weight_b
 265: 
 266:     def _crossfade(self, audio_a, audio_b, cf_samples):
 267:         cf_len = min(cf_samples, len(audio_a), len(audio_b))
 268:         if cf_len == 0:
 269:             return np.concatenate([audio_a, audio_b])
 270:         fade_out = np.linspace(1, 0, cf_len)
 271:         fade_in = np.linspace(0, 1, cf_len)
 272:         cf = audio_a[-cf_len:] * fade_out + audio_b[:cf_len] * fade_in
 273:         return cf
 274: 
 275:     # ============================================================
 276:     # TECHNIQUES (1-19)
 277:     # ============================================================
 278: 
 279:     def beatmatch_crossfade(self, cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana):
 280:         cur_audio, sr = self._load_audio(cur_id)
 281:         nxt_audio, _ = self._load_audio(nxt_id)
 282:         if cur_audio is None or nxt_audio is None: return
 283: 
 284:         crossfade_bars = params.get('crossfade_bars', 8)
 285:         bpm = cur_ana.get('bpm', 120)
 286:         cf_samples = int(((60 / max(bpm, 1)) * 4) * crossfade_bars * sr)
 287: 
 288:         bpm_ratio = bpm / max(nxt_ana.get('bpm', 120), 1)
 289:         if abs(bpm_ratio - 1.0) > 0.02:
 290:             nxt_audio = self._time_stretch(nxt_audio, bpm_ratio)
 291: 
 292:         trans_sample = self._get_transition_point(cur_ana, len(cur_audio))
 293:         nxt_entry = int(self._get_entry_point(nxt_ana) * sr)
 294: 
 295:         self._play_audio(cur_audio[:trans_sample], sr)
 296:         cf = self._crossfade(cur_audio[trans_sample:], nxt_audio[nxt_entry:], cf_samples)
 297:         self._play_audio(cf, sr)
 298:         self._play_audio(nxt_audio[nxt_entry + cf_samples:], sr)
 299: 
 300:     def cut_transition(self, cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana):
 301:         cur_audio, sr = self._load_audio(cur_id)
 302:         nxt_audio, _ = self._load_audio(nxt_id)
 303:         if cur_audio is None: return
 304: 
 305:         trans_sample = self._get_transition_point(cur_ana, len(cur_audio))
 306:         bar_times = cur_ana.get('bar_times', [])
 307:         if bar_times:
 308:             trans_time = trans_sample / sr
 309:             nearest_bar = min(bar_times, key=lambda x: abs(x - trans_time))
 310:             trans_sample = int(nearest_bar * sr)
 311: 
 312:         self._play_audio(cur_audio[:trans_sample], sr)
 313:         if nxt_audio is not None:
 314:             nxt_entry = int(self._get_entry_point(nxt_ana) * sr)
 315:             self._play_audio(nxt_audio[nxt_entry:], sr)
 316: 
 317:     def echo_out(self, cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana):
 318:         cur_audio, sr = self._load_audio(cur_id)
 319:         nxt_audio, _ = self._load_audio(nxt_id)
 320:         if cur_audio is None: return
 321: 
 322:         trans_sample = self._get_transition_point(cur_ana, len(cur_audio))
 323:         self._play_audio(cur_audio[:trans_sample], sr)
 324: 
 325:         echo_segment = cur_audio[trans_sample:trans_sample + sr * 4].copy()
 326:         echoed = self._fade_out(self._apply_echo(echo_segment, params.get('delay_ms', 375), params.get('feedback', 0.6)))
 327: 
 328:         if nxt_audio is not None:
 329:             nxt_entry = int(self._get_entry_point(nxt_ana) * sr)
 330:             nxt_start = nxt_audio[nxt_entry:nxt_entry + len(echoed)]
 331:             nxt_fadein = self._fade_in(nxt_start, fade_samples=len(nxt_start))
 332:             self._play_audio(self._mix(echoed, nxt_fadein, 0.7, 0.3), sr)
 333:             self._play_audio(nxt_audio[nxt_entry + len(echoed):], sr)
 334: 
 335:     def filter_sweep(self, cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana):
 336:         cur_audio, sr = self._load_audio(cur_id)
 337:         nxt_audio, _ = self._load_audio(nxt_id)
 338:         if cur_audio is None: return
 339: 
 340:         trans_sample = self._get_transition_point(cur_ana, len(cur_audio))
 341:         sweep_dur = int(sr * params.get('sweep_duration', 8))
 342: 
 343:         self._play_audio(cur_audio[:trans_sample], sr)
 344: 
 345:         sweep_out = cur_audio[trans_sample:trans_sample + sweep_dur].copy()
 346:         swept_out = np.zeros_like(sweep_out)
 347:         chunk = sr // 4
 348: 
 349:         for i in range(0, len(sweep_out), chunk):
 350:             seg = sweep_out[i:i + chunk]
 351:             progress = i / max(len(sweep_out), 1)
 352:             filtered = self._apply_highpass(seg, 20 + (8000 - 20) * (progress ** 1.5))
 353:             swept_out[i:i + len(filtered)] = filtered * (1.0 - (progress * 0.8))
 354: 
 355:         self._play_audio(swept_out, sr)
 356: 
 357:         if nxt_audio is not None:
 358:             nxt_entry = int(self._get_entry_point(nxt_ana) * sr)
 359:             sweep_in = nxt_audio[nxt_entry:nxt_entry + sweep_dur].copy()
 360:             swept_in = np.zeros_like(sweep_in)
 361: 
 362:             for i in range(0, len(sweep_in), chunk):
 363:                 seg = sweep_in[i:i + chunk]
 364:                 progress = i / max(len(sweep_in), 1)
 365:                 filtered = self._apply_lowpass(seg, min(200 + (20000 - 200) * progress, 20000))
 366:                 swept_in[i:i + len(filtered)] = filtered * (0.2 + (progress * 0.8))
 367: 
 368:             self._play_audio(swept_in, sr)
 369:             self._play_audio(nxt_audio[nxt_entry + sweep_dur:], sr)
 370: 
 371:     def loop_roll(self, cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana):
 372:         cur_audio, sr = self._load_audio(cur_id)
 373:         nxt_audio, _ = self._load_audio(nxt_id)
 374:         if cur_audio is None: return
 375: 
 376:         trans_sample = self._get_transition_point(cur_ana, len(cur_audio))
 377:         seconds_per_bar = (60 / max(cur_ana.get('bpm', 120), 1)) * 4
 378: 
 379:         self._play_audio(cur_audio[:trans_sample], sr)
 380: 
 381:         rolled_parts = []
 382:         for div in [1, 0.5, 0.25, 0.125]:
 383:             loop_len = max(int((seconds_per_bar * div) * sr), 100)
 384:             loop = cur_audio[trans_sample:trans_sample + loop_len].copy()
 385:             for r in range(max(1, int(1 / div))):
 386:                 rolled_parts.append(loop * (1.0 - (r * 0.1)))
 387: 
 388:         if rolled_parts:
 389:             self._play_audio(self._pitch_shift_semitones(np.concatenate(rolled_parts), 2), sr)
 390: 
 391:         if nxt_audio is not None:
 392:             nxt_entry = int(self._get_entry_point(nxt_ana) * sr)
 393:             self._play_audio(nxt_audio[nxt_entry:], sr)
 394: 
 395:     def reverb_wash(self, cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana):
 396:         cur_audio, sr = self._load_audio(cur_id)
 397:         nxt_audio, _ = self._load_audio(nxt_id)
 398:         if cur_audio is None: return
 399: 
 400:         trans_sample = self._get_transition_point(cur_ana, len(cur_audio))
 401:         self._play_audio(cur_audio[:trans_sample], sr)
 402: 
 403:         wash_segment = cur_audio[trans_sample:trans_sample + int(sr * 6)].copy()
 404:         washed = self._fade_out(self._apply_reverb(wash_segment, room_size=0.85), fade_samples=len(wash_segment))
 405:         self._play_audio(washed, sr)
 406: 
 407:         if nxt_audio is not None:
 408:             nxt_entry = int(self._get_entry_point(nxt_ana) * sr)
 409:             self._play_audio(self._fade_in(nxt_audio[nxt_entry:], fade_samples=int(sr * 4)), sr)
 410: 
 411:     def spinback(self, cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana):
 412:         cur_audio, sr = self._load_audio(cur_id)
 413:         nxt_audio, _ = self._load_audio(nxt_id)
 414:         if cur_audio is None: return
 415: 
 416:         trans_sample = self._get_transition_point(cur_ana, len(cur_audio))
 417:         self._play_audio(cur_audio[:trans_sample], sr)
 418: 
 419:         spin_seg = cur_audio[trans_sample:trans_sample + int(sr * 1.5)].copy()
 420:         chunks, chunk_size, spun_parts = 12, len(spin_seg) // 12, []
 421: 
 422:         for i in range(chunks):
 423:             chunk = spin_seg[i * chunk_size:(i + 1) * chunk_size]
 424:             if len(chunk) < 10: continue
 425:             try: spun_parts.append(self._time_stretch(chunk[::-1], 1.0 + (i / chunks) * 5.0))
 426:             except: spun_parts.append(chunk[::-1])
 427: 
 428:         if spun_parts:
 429:             spun = np.concatenate(spun_parts)
 430:             try: spun = self._pitch_shift_semitones(spun, 6)
 431:             except: pass
 432:             self._play_audio(self._fade_out(spun, fade_samples=len(spun) // 3), sr)
 433: 
 434:         if nxt_audio is not None:
 435:             nxt_entry = int(self._get_entry_point(nxt_ana) * sr)
 436:             self._play_audio(nxt_audio[nxt_entry:], sr)
 437: 
 438:     def tempo_ramp(self, cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana):
 439:         cur_audio, sr = self._load_audio(cur_id)
 440:         nxt_audio, _ = self._load_audio(nxt_id)
 441:         if cur_audio is None: return
 442: 
 443:         bpm_a, bpm_b = cur_ana.get('bpm', 120), max(nxt_ana.get('bpm', 120), 1)
 444:         trans_sample = self._get_transition_point(cur_ana, len(cur_audio))
 445:         self._play_audio(cur_audio[:trans_sample], sr)
 446: 
 447:         ramp_dur = int(((60 / max(bpm_a, 1)) * 4) * 16 * sr)
 448:         ramp_seg = cur_audio[trans_sample:trans_sample + ramp_dur].copy()
 449:         
 450:         chunks, chunk_size, ramped_parts = 16, len(ramp_seg) // 16, []
 451:         for i in range(chunks):
 452:             chunk = ramp_seg[i * chunk_size:(i + 1) * chunk_size]
 453:             if len(chunk) < 10: continue
 454:             try: ramped_parts.append(self._time_stretch(chunk, 1.0 + (bpm_b / bpm_a - 1.0) * (i / chunks)))
 455:             except: ramped_parts.append(chunk)
 456: 
 457:         if ramped_parts: self._play_audio(np.concatenate(ramped_parts), sr)
 458: 
 459:         if nxt_audio is not None:
 460:             nxt_entry = int(self._get_entry_point(nxt_ana) * sr)
 461:             cf_len = int(sr * 4)
 462:             self._play_audio(self._crossfade(np.zeros(cf_len), nxt_audio[nxt_entry:nxt_entry + cf_len], cf_len), sr)
 463:             self._play_audio(nxt_audio[nxt_entry + cf_len:], sr)
 464: 
 465:     def white_noise_sweep(self, cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana):
 466:         cur_audio, sr = self._load_audio(cur_id)
 467:         nxt_audio, _ = self._load_audio(nxt_id)
 468:         if cur_audio is None: return
 469: 
 470:         trans_sample = self._get_transition_point(cur_ana, len(cur_audio))
 471:         self._play_audio(cur_audio[:trans_sample], sr)
 472: 
 473:         sweep_dur = int(sr * 4)
 474:         noise = np.random.normal(0, 0.08, sweep_dur)
 475:         env = np.concatenate([np.linspace(0, 1, sweep_dur // 2) ** 2, np.linspace(1, 0, sweep_dur // 2) ** 2])
 476:         noise_sweep = noise * env
 477: 
 478:         cur_tail = cur_audio[trans_sample:trans_sample + sweep_dur]
 479:         if len(cur_tail) > 0:
 480:             self._play_audio(self._mix(self._fade_out(cur_tail, fade_samples=len(cur_tail))[:len(noise_sweep)], noise_sweep[:len(cur_tail)], 0.6, 0.4), sr)
 481: 
 482:         if nxt_audio is not None:
 483:             nxt_entry = int(self._get_entry_point(nxt_ana) * sr)
 484:             self._play_audio(self._fade_in(nxt_audio[nxt_entry:], fade_samples=int(sr * 2)), sr)
 485: 
 486:     def vinyl_scratch_flourish(self, cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana):
 487:         cur_audio, sr = self._load_audio(cur_id)
 488:         if cur_audio is None: return
 489: 
 490:         scratch_time = params.get('scratch_time', cur_ana.get('transition_points', {}).get('outro_beat', len(cur_audio) / sr * 0.75))
 491:         scratch_sample = int(scratch_time * sr)
 492:         self._play_audio(cur_audio[:scratch_sample], sr)
 493: 
 494:         scratch_len = int(sr * 0.6)
 495:         scratch_seg = cur_audio[scratch_sample:scratch_sample + scratch_len].copy()
 496:         scratch_parts = []
 497: 
 498:         for i in range(4):
 499:             chunk = scratch_seg[i * (scratch_len // 4):(i + 1) * (scratch_len // 4)]
 500:             if len(chunk) > 10:
 501:                 try: scratch_parts.append(self._time_stretch(chunk, max(0.3, 1.0 - (i * 0.2))))
 502:                 except: scratch_parts.append(chunk)
 503: 
 504:         scratch_parts.append(scratch_seg[::-1])
 505: 
 506:         for i in range(4):
 507:             chunk = scratch_seg[i * (scratch_len // 4):(i + 1) * (scratch_len // 4)]
 508:             if len(chunk) > 10:
 509:                 try: scratch_parts.append(self._time_stretch(chunk, 0.5 + (i * 0.2)))
 510:                 except: scratch_parts.append(chunk)
 511: 
 512:         scratch_audio = np.concatenate(scratch_parts)
 513:         wobble = (np.sin(np.linspace(0, 8.0 * np.pi, len(scratch_audio))) * 0.3 + 1.0)
 514:         self._play_audio(scratch_audio * wobble, sr)
 515: 
 516:         nxt_audio, _ = self._load_audio(nxt_id)
 517:         if nxt_audio is not None and params.get('is_transition', False):
 518:             nxt_entry = int(self._get_entry_point(nxt_ana) * sr)
 519:             self._play_audio(nxt_audio[nxt_entry:], sr)
 520:         else:
 521:             rewind_sample = max(0, scratch_sample - int(((60 / max(cur_ana.get('bpm', 120), 1)) * 4) * params.get('rewind_bars', 4) * sr))
 522:             self._play_audio(cur_audio[rewind_sample:], sr)
 523: 
 524:     def tone_play(self, cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana):
 525:         cur_audio, sr = self._load_audio(cur_id)
 526:         nxt_audio, _ = self._load_audio(nxt_id)
 527:         if cur_audio is None or nxt_audio is None: return
 528: 
 529:         trans_sample = self._get_transition_point(cur_ana, len(cur_audio))
 530:         self._play_audio(cur_audio[:trans_sample], sr)
 531: 
 532:         melody_notes = params.get('melody_notes', nxt_ana.get('melody_notes', [60, 62, 64, 65, 67]))
 533:         note_samples = int(params.get('note_duration', 60 / max(cur_ana.get('bpm', 120), 1)) * sr)
 534: 
 535:         melody_stem, _ = self._load_stem(cur_id, 'other')
 536:         source_audio = melody_stem if melody_stem is not None else cur_audio
 537:         instrument_sample = source_audio[trans_sample:trans_sample + note_samples].copy()
 538:         if len(instrument_sample) < 100: instrument_sample = cur_audio[trans_sample:trans_sample + note_samples].copy()
 539: 
 540:         preview_parts = []
 541:         for note_midi in melody_notes[:8]:
 542:             try: preview_parts.append(self._pitch_shift_semitones(instrument_sample, int(note_midi - 60)))
 543:             except: preview_parts.append(instrument_sample.copy())
 544: 
 545:         if preview_parts:
 546:             preview = np.concatenate(preview_parts)
 547:             self._play_audio(self._fade_out(preview, len(preview) // 3), sr)
 548: 
 549:         nxt_entry = int(self._get_entry_point(nxt_ana) * sr)
 550:         self._play_audio(self._fade_in(nxt_audio[nxt_entry:], fade_samples=int(sr * 8)), sr)
 551: 
 552:     def wordplay_transition(self, cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana):
 553:         cur_audio, sr = self._load_audio(cur_id)
 554:         nxt_audio, _ = self._load_audio(nxt_id)
 555:         if cur_audio is None: return
 556: 
 557:         trans_sample = int(params.get('transition_time', cur_ana.get('transition_points', {}).get('outro_beat', len(cur_audio) / sr * 0.8)) * sr)
 558:         self._play_audio(cur_audio[:trans_sample], sr)
 559: 
 560:         word_clip_path = params.get('word_clip_a')
 561:         word_audio = None
 562: 
 563:         if word_clip_path and os.path.exists(word_clip_path):
 564:             word_audio, _ = librosa.load(word_clip_path, sr=sr)
 565:         else:
 566:             vocals, _ = self._load_stem(cur_id, 'vocals')
 567:             if vocals is not None:
 568:                 word_audio = vocals[max(0, trans_sample - int(sr * 0.5)):trans_sample + int(sr * 0.5)]
 569: 
 570:         if word_audio is not None and len(word_audio) > 100:
 571:             echoed_word = self._apply_echo(word_audio, delay_ms=250, feedback=0.5, num_echoes=3)
 572:             word_sequence = [echoed_word * (1.0 - (i * 0.25)) for i in range(params.get('word_repeats', 3))]
 573:             self._play_audio(self._apply_reverb(np.concatenate(word_sequence), room_size=0.4), sr)
 574: 
 575:         if nxt_audio is not None:
 576:             nxt_start = int(params.get('word_time_b', 0) * sr)
 577:             self._play_audio(self._fade_in(nxt_audio[nxt_start:], fade_samples=int(sr * 2)), sr)
 578: 
 579:     def mashup_short(self, cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana):
 580:         cur_audio, sr = self._load_audio(cur_id)
 581:         nxt_audio, _ = self._load_audio(nxt_id)
 582:         if cur_audio is None or nxt_audio is None: return
 583: 
 584:         bpm_ratio = cur_ana.get('bpm', 120) / max(nxt_ana.get('bpm', 120), 1)
 585:         trans_sample = self._get_transition_point(cur_ana, len(cur_audio))
 586:         self._play_audio(cur_audio[:trans_sample], sr)
 587: 
 588:         drums_a, _ = self._load_stem(cur_id, 'drums')
 589:         vocals_b, _ = self._load_stem(nxt_id, 'vocals')
 590:         melody_b, _ = self._load_stem(nxt_id, 'other')
 591: 
 592:         if abs(bpm_ratio - 1.0) > 0.02:
 593:             if vocals_b is not None: vocals_b = self._time_stretch(vocals_b, bpm_ratio)
 594:             if melody_b is not None: melody_b = self._time_stretch(melody_b, bpm_ratio)
 595: 
 596:         mashup_samples = int(((60 / max(cur_ana.get('bpm', 120), 1)) * 4) * params.get('mashup_bars', 8) * sr)
 597:         mashup = np.zeros(mashup_samples)
 598:         nxt_entry = int(self._get_entry_point(nxt_ana) * sr)
 599: 
 600:         if drums_a is not None:
 601:             seg = drums_a[trans_sample:trans_sample + mashup_samples]
 602:             if len(seg) > 0:
 603:                 pad = np.zeros(mashup_samples)
 604:                 pad[:len(seg)] = seg
 605:                 mashup += pad * 0.8
 606: 
 607:         if vocals_b is not None:
 608:             seg = vocals_b[nxt_entry:nxt_entry + mashup_samples]
 609:             if len(seg) > 0:
 610:                 pad = np.zeros(mashup_samples)
 611:                 pad[:len(seg)] = seg
 612:                 mashup += self._fade_in(pad, fade_samples=mashup_samples // 4) * 0.85
 613: 
 614:         if melody_b is not None:
 615:             seg = melody_b[nxt_entry:nxt_entry + mashup_samples]
 616:             if len(seg) > 0:
 617:                 pad = np.zeros(mashup_samples)
 618:                 pad[:len(seg)] = seg
 619:                 mashup += self._fade_in(pad, fade_samples=mashup_samples // 2) * 0.6
 620: 
 621:         if np.max(np.abs(mashup)) > 0:
 622:             self._play_audio(mashup / np.max(np.abs(mashup)) * 0.85, sr)
 623: 
 624:         if nxt_audio is not None:
 625:             self._play_audio(self._fade_in(nxt_audio[nxt_entry:], fade_samples=int(sr * 4)), sr)
 626: 
 627:     def mashup_extended(self, cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana):
 628:         cur_audio, sr = self._load_audio(cur_id)
 629:         nxt_audio, _ = self._load_audio(nxt_id)
 630:         if cur_audio is None or nxt_audio is None: return
 631: 
 632:         bpm_ratio = cur_ana.get('bpm', 120) / max(nxt_ana.get('bpm', 120), 1)
 633:         key_shift = self._calculate_key_shift(cur_ana.get('camelot', ''), nxt_ana.get('camelot', ''))
 634:         trans_sample = self._get_transition_point(cur_ana, len(cur_audio))
 635:         self._play_audio(cur_audio[:trans_sample], sr)
 636: 
 637:         drums_a, _ = self._load_stem(cur_id, 'drums')
 638:         bass_a, _ = self._load_stem(cur_id, 'bass')
 639:         vocals_a, _ = self._load_stem(cur_id, 'vocals')
 640: 
 641:         vocals_b, _ = self._load_stem(nxt_id, 'vocals')
 642:         melody_b, _ = self._load_stem(nxt_id, 'other')
 643:         bass_b, _ = self._load_stem(nxt_id, 'bass')
 644:         drums_b, _ = self._load_stem(nxt_id, 'drums')
 645: 
 646:         stems_b = [vocals_b, melody_b, bass_b, drums_b]
 647:         if abs(bpm_ratio - 1.0) > 0.02:
 648:             for i in range(len(stems_b)):
 649:                 if stems_b[i] is not None: stems_b[i] = self._time_stretch(stems_b[i], bpm_ratio)
 650:         
 651:         if key_shift != 0:
 652:             for i in [0, 1, 2]: # vocals, melody, bass
 653:                 if stems_b[i] is not None: stems_b[i] = self._pitch_shift_semitones(stems_b[i], key_shift)
 654:         
 655:         vocals_b, melody_b, bass_b, drums_b = stems_b
 656: 
 657:         mashup_samples = int(((60 / max(cur_ana.get('bpm', 120), 1)) * 4) * params.get('mashup_bars', 32) * sr)
 658:         mashup = np.zeros(mashup_samples)
 659:         nxt_entry = int(self._get_entry_point(nxt_ana) * sr)
 660:         phase1, phase2_start, phase2_end = mashup_samples // 4, mashup_samples // 4, (mashup_samples // 4) * 2
 661: 
 662:         # Phase 1
 663:         if drums_a is not None:
 664:             seg = drums_a[trans_sample:trans_sample + phase1]
 665:             mashup[:len(seg)] += seg * 0.85
 666:         if bass_a is not None:
 667:             seg = bass_a[trans_sample:trans_sample + phase1]
 668:             mashup[:len(seg)] += seg * 0.80
 669:         if vocals_a is not None:
 670:             seg = self._fade_out(vocals_a[trans_sample:trans_sample + phase1], phase1 // 2)
 671:             mashup[:len(seg)] += seg * 0.70
 672: 
 673:         # Phase 2
 674:         if drums_a is not None:
 675:             seg = drums_a[trans_sample + phase1:trans_sample + phase2_end]
 676:             mashup[phase2_start:phase2_start + len(seg)] += seg * 0.70
 677:         if vocals_b is not None:
 678:             seg = self._fade_in(vocals_b[nxt_entry:nxt_entry + phase1], phase1 // 2)
 679:             mashup[phase2_start:phase2_start + len(seg)] += seg * 0.80
 680:         if melody_b is not None:
 681:             seg = self._fade_in(melody_b[nxt_entry:nxt_entry + phase1], phase1 // 2)
 682:             mashup[phase2_start:phase2_start + len(seg)] += seg * 0.60
 683: 
 684:         # Phase 3
 685:         phase3_len = mashup_samples - phase2_end
 686:         if drums_b is not None:
 687:             seg = drums_b[nxt_entry:nxt_entry + phase3_len]
 688:             mashup[phase2_end:phase2_end + len(seg)] += seg * 0.85
 689:         if bass_b is not None:
 690:             seg = bass_b[nxt_entry:nxt_entry + phase3_len]
 691:             mashup[phase2_end:phase2_end + len(seg)] += seg * 0.80
 692:         if vocals_b is not None:
 693:             seg = vocals_b[nxt_entry + phase1:nxt_entry + phase1 + phase3_len]
 694:             mashup[phase2_end:phase2_end + len(seg)] += seg * 0.85
 695: 
 696:         if np.max(np.abs(mashup)) > 0:
 697:             self._play_audio(mashup / np.max(np.abs(mashup)) * 0.85, sr)
 698: 
 699:         if nxt_audio is not None:
 700:             self._play_audio(nxt_audio[nxt_entry + mashup_samples:], sr)
 701: 
 702:     def acapella_layer(self, cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana):
 703:         cur_audio, sr = self._load_audio(cur_id)
 704:         nxt_audio, _ = self._load_audio(nxt_id)
 705:         if cur_audio is None or nxt_audio is None: return
 706: 
 707:         trans_sample = self._get_transition_point(cur_ana, len(cur_audio))
 708:         self._play_audio(cur_audio[:trans_sample], sr)
 709: 
 710:         vocals_a, _ = self._load_stem(cur_id, 'vocals')
 711:         drums_b, _ = self._load_stem(nxt_id, 'drums')
 712:         bass_b, _ = self._load_stem(nxt_id, 'bass')
 713:         melody_b, _ = self._load_stem(nxt_id, 'other')
 714: 
 715:         bpm_ratio = cur_ana.get('bpm', 120) / max(nxt_ana.get('bpm', 120), 1)
 716:         nxt_entry = int(self._get_entry_point(nxt_ana) * sr)
 717:         layer_samples = int(((60 / max(cur_ana.get('bpm', 120), 1)) * 4) * params.get('layer_bars', 16) * sr)
 718:         layer = np.zeros(layer_samples)
 719: 
 720:         if vocals_a is not None:
 721:             seg = vocals_a[trans_sample:trans_sample + layer_samples]
 722:             if abs(bpm_ratio - 1.0) > 0.02: seg = self._time_stretch(seg, bpm_ratio)
 723:             layer[:len(seg)] += seg * 0.9
 724: 
 725:         for stem, vol in [(drums_b, 0.8), (bass_b, 0.75), (melody_b, 0.7)]:
 726:             if stem is not None:
 727:                 seg = stem[nxt_entry:nxt_entry + layer_samples]
 728:                 layer[:len(seg)] += seg * vol
 729: 
 730:         if np.max(np.abs(layer)) > 0:
 731:             self._play_audio(layer / np.max(np.abs(layer)) * 0.85, sr)
 732: 
 733:         if nxt_audio is not None:
 734:             self._play_audio(nxt_audio[nxt_entry + layer_samples:], sr)
 735: 
 736:     def drum_swap(self, cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana):
 737:         cur_audio, sr = self._load_audio(cur_id)
 738:         nxt_audio, _ = self._load_audio(nxt_id)
 739:         if cur_audio is None or nxt_audio is None: return
 740: 
 741:         trans_sample = self._get_transition_point(cur_ana, len(cur_audio))
 742:         self._play_audio(cur_audio[:trans_sample], sr)
 743: 
 744:         drums_a, _ = self._load_stem(cur_id, 'drums')
 745:         melody_a, _ = self._load_stem(cur_id, 'other')
 746:         vocals_a, _ = self._load_stem(cur_id, 'vocals')
 747:         drums_b, _ = self._load_stem(nxt_id, 'drums')
 748: 
 749:         bpm_ratio = cur_ana.get('bpm', 120) / max(nxt_ana.get('bpm', 120), 1)
 750:         if drums_b is not None and abs(bpm_ratio - 1.0) > 0.02:
 751:             drums_b = self._time_stretch(drums_b, bpm_ratio)
 752: 
 753:         swap_samples = int(((60 / max(cur_ana.get('bpm', 120), 1)) * 4) * params.get('swap_bars', 8) * sr)
 754:         swap = np.zeros(swap_samples)
 755:         nxt_entry = int(self._get_entry_point(nxt_ana) * sr)
 756: 
 757:         for stem, vol in [(melody_a, 0.8), (vocals_a, 0.85)]:
 758:             if stem is not None:
 759:                 seg = self._fade_out(stem[trans_sample:trans_sample + swap_samples], swap_samples // 4)
 760:                 swap[:len(seg)] += seg * vol
 761: 
 762:         if drums_a is not None:
 763:             seg = drums_a[trans_sample:trans_sample + swap_samples]
 764:             fade = np.linspace(1, 0, min(len(seg), swap_samples))
 765:             swap[:len(fade)] += seg[:len(fade)] * fade * 0.8
 766: 
 767:         if drums_b is not None:
 768:             seg = drums_b[nxt_entry:nxt_entry + swap_samples]
 769:             fade = np.linspace(0, 1, min(len(seg), swap_samples))
 770:             swap[:len(fade)] += seg[:len(fade)] * fade * 0.8
 771: 
 772:         if np.max(np.abs(swap)) > 0:
 773:             self._play_audio(swap / np.max(np.abs(swap)) * 0.85, sr)
 774: 
 775:         if nxt_audio is not None:
 776:             self._play_audio(nxt_audio[nxt_entry + swap_samples:], sr)
 777: 
 778:     def bass_swap(self, cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana):
 779:         cur_audio, sr = self._load_audio(cur_id)
 780:         nxt_audio, _ = self._load_audio(nxt_id)
 781:         if cur_audio is None or nxt_audio is None: return
 782: 
 783:         trans_sample = self._get_transition_point(cur_ana, len(cur_audio))
 784:         self._play_audio(cur_audio[:trans_sample], sr)
 785: 
 786:         bass_b, _ = self._load_stem(nxt_id, 'bass')
 787:         drums_a, _ = self._load_stem(cur_id, 'drums')
 788:         melody_a, _ = self._load_stem(cur_id, 'other')
 789: 
 790:         bpm_ratio = cur_ana.get('bpm', 120) / max(nxt_ana.get('bpm', 120), 1)
 791:         swap_samples = int(((60 / max(cur_ana.get('bpm', 120), 1)) * 4) * params.get('swap_bars', 8) * sr)
 792:         swap = np.zeros(swap_samples)
 793:         nxt_entry = int(self._get_entry_point(nxt_ana) * sr)
 794: 
 795:         if drums_a is not None:
 796:             seg = drums_a[trans_sample:trans_sample + swap_samples]
 797:             swap[:len(seg)] += seg * 0.8
 798: 
 799:         if melody_a is not None:
 800:             seg = self._fade_out(melody_a[trans_sample:trans_sample + swap_samples], swap_samples // 3)
 801:             swap[:len(seg)] += seg * 0.7
 802: 
 803:         if bass_b is not None:
 804:             if abs(bpm_ratio - 1.0) > 0.02: bass_b = self._time_stretch(bass_b, bpm_ratio)
 805:             seg = self._fade_in(bass_b[nxt_entry:nxt_entry + swap_samples], swap_samples // 4)
 806:             swap[:len(seg)] += seg * 0.85
 807: 
 808:         if np.max(np.abs(swap)) > 0:
 809:             self._play_audio(swap / np.max(np.abs(swap)) * 0.85, sr)
 810: 
 811:         if nxt_audio is not None:
 812:             self._play_audio(nxt_audio[nxt_entry:], sr)
 813: 
 814:     def stutter_glitch(self, cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana):
 815:         cur_audio, sr = self._load_audio(cur_id)
 816:         nxt_audio, _ = self._load_audio(nxt_id)
 817:         if cur_audio is None: return
 818: 
 819:         trans_sample = self._get_transition_point(cur_ana, len(cur_audio))
 820:         self._play_audio(cur_audio[:trans_sample], sr)
 821: 
 822:         beat_samples = int((60 / max(cur_ana.get('bpm', 120), 1)) * sr)
 823:         glitch_total = beat_samples * 4
 824:         glitch_audio = cur_audio[trans_sample:trans_sample + glitch_total].copy()
 825:         glitch_parts = []
 826:         generated = 0
 827: 
 828:         for slice_size in [beat_samples // 2, beat_samples // 4, beat_samples // 8, beat_samples // 16]:
 829:             for repeat in range(4):
 830:                 if generated >= glitch_total: break
 831:                 start = (repeat * slice_size) % max(len(glitch_audio) - slice_size, 1)
 832:                 chunk = glitch_audio[start:start + slice_size].copy()
 833: 
 834:                 try: chunk = self._pitch_shift_semitones(chunk, np.random.choice([-2, 0, 2, 4, 7, 12]))
 835:                 except: pass
 836: 
 837:                 env = np.ones(len(chunk))
 838:                 env[-len(env)//4:] = np.linspace(1, 0, len(env)//4)
 839:                 glitch_parts.append(chunk * env)
 840:                 generated += len(chunk)
 841: 
 842:         if glitch_parts:
 843:             glitch = np.concatenate(glitch_parts)
 844:             if np.max(np.abs(glitch)) > 0:
 845:                 self._play_audio(glitch / np.max(np.abs(glitch)) * 0.85, sr)
 846: 
 847:         if nxt_audio is not None:
 848:             nxt_entry = int(self._get_entry_point(nxt_ana) * sr)
 849:             self._play_audio(nxt_audio[nxt_entry:], sr)
 850: 
 851:     def half_time_transition(self, cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana):
 852:         cur_audio, sr = self._load_audio(cur_id)
 853:         nxt_audio, _ = self._load_audio(nxt_id)
 854:         if cur_audio is None or nxt_audio is None: return
 855: 
 856:         trans_sample = self._get_transition_point(cur_ana, len(cur_audio))
 857:         self._play_audio(cur_audio[:trans_sample], sr)
 858:         nxt_entry = int(self._get_entry_point(nxt_ana) * sr)
 859: 
 860:         half_dur = int(sr * 8)
 861:         half_seg = nxt_audio[nxt_entry:nxt_entry + half_dur]
 862: 
 863:         if len(half_seg) > 100:
 864:             self._play_audio(self._fade_in(self._time_stretch(half_seg, 0.5), fade_samples=int(sr * 2)), sr)
 865: 
 866:         ramp_dur = int(((60 / max(nxt_ana.get('bpm', 120), 1)) * 4) * 8 * sr)
 867:         ramp_seg = nxt_audio[nxt_entry + half_dur:nxt_entry + half_dur + ramp_dur]
 868: 
 869:         chunks, chunk_size, ramp_parts = 8, len(ramp_seg) // 8, []
 870:         for i in range(chunks):
 871:             chunk = ramp_seg[i * chunk_size:(i + 1) * chunk_size]
 872:             if len(chunk) < 10: continue
 873:             try: ramp_parts.append(self._time_stretch(chunk, 0.5 + (0.5 * i / chunks)))
 874:             except: ramp_parts.append(chunk)
 875: 
 876:         if ramp_parts: self._play_audio(np.concatenate(ramp_parts), sr)
 877: 
 878:     def wordplay_mashup(self, cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana):
 879:         """
 880:         High-IQ transition:
 881:         1. Find rhyming/matching word.
 882:         2. Loop word from Song A.
 883:         3. Bring in Instrumental from Song B.
 884:         4. Drop Song B Vocals on matching word.
 885:         """
 886:         print("   🔍 Seeking Wordplay Connection...")
 887:         connection = self.wordplay_agent.find_connection(cur_ana, nxt_ana)
 888:         
 889:         if not connection:
 890:             print("   ⚠️ No connection found. Falling back to Echo Out.")
 891:             return self.echo_out(cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana)
 892:             
 893:         print(f"   💡 FOUND LINK: '{connection.get('word', 'rhyme')}' ({connection.get('type', 'unknown')})")
 894:         
 895:         vocals_a, sr = self._load_stem(cur_id, 'vocals')
 896:         drums_b, _ = self._load_stem(nxt_id, 'drums')
 897:         other_b, _ = self._load_stem(nxt_id, 'other')
 898:         vocals_b, _ = self._load_stem(nxt_id, 'vocals')
 899:         
 900:         if vocals_a is None or drums_b is None:
 901:             return self.echo_out(cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana)
 902: 
 903:         cur_full, _ = self._load_audio(cur_id)
 904:         word_start = connection.get('transition_time', 0)
 905:         
 906:         # FIXED: Safe dictionary access in case 'cur_entry' doesn't exist
 907:         word_end = connection.get('cur_entry', {}).get('end_time', word_start + 0.5)
 908:         
 909:         self._play_audio(cur_full[:int(word_start * sr)], sr)
 910:         
 911:         word_clip = vocals_a[int(word_start * sr):int(word_end * sr)]
 912:         if len(word_clip) == 0:
 913:             return self.echo_out(cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana)
 914:             
 915:         word_loop = np.tile(word_clip, params.get('word_repeats', 4))
 916:         
 917:         bpm_ratio = cur_ana.get('bpm', 120) / max(nxt_ana.get('bpm', 120), 1)
 918:         inst_b = self._mix(drums_b, other_b if other_b is not None else np.zeros_like(drums_b), 0.5, 0.5)
 919:         
 920:         if abs(bpm_ratio - 1.0) > 0.02:
 921:             inst_b = self._time_stretch(inst_b, bpm_ratio)
 922:             
 923:         nxt_entry = int(connection.get('word_time_b', 0) * sr)
 924:         loop_len = len(word_loop)
 925:         
 926:         inst_slice = inst_b[max(0, nxt_entry - loop_len):nxt_entry]
 927:         mash = self._mix(word_loop, inst_slice, 0.7, 0.5)
 928:         self._play_audio(mash, sr)
 929:         
 930:         nxt_full, _ = self._load_audio(nxt_id)
 931:         if nxt_full is not None:
 932:             self._play_audio(nxt_full[nxt_entry:], sr)
 933: 
 934:     def phrasal_interlace(self, cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana):
 935:         """
 936:         TRUE INNOVATION: CSPI (Cross-Song Phrasal Interlacing)
 937:         Alternates between Song A and B every 1/16th of a beat.
 938:         Creates a 'shimmer' or 'interlaced' audio effect.
 939:         """
 940:         print("   ⚔️  Executing CSPI (Micro-Splicing)...")
 941:         cur_audio, sr = self._load_audio(cur_id)
 942:         nxt_audio, _ = self._load_audio(nxt_id)
 943:         if cur_audio is None or nxt_audio is None:
 944:             return
 945: 
 946:         bpm = cur_ana.get('bpm', 120)
 947:         slice_samples = int(((60 / max(bpm, 1)) / 4) * sr)
 948:         
 949:         trans_sample = self._get_transition_point(cur_ana, len(cur_audio))
 950:         nxt_entry = int(self._get_entry_point(nxt_ana) * sr)
 951:         
 952:         self._play_audio(cur_audio[:trans_sample], sr)
 953:         
 954:         interlace_len = slice_samples * 64
 955:         interlaced = np.zeros(interlace_len)
 956:         
 957:         for i in range(64):
 958:             start = i * slice_samples
 959:             if (i // 2) % 2 == 0:
 960:                 chunk_len = min(slice_samples, len(cur_audio) - (trans_sample + start))
 961:                 if chunk_len > 0:
 962:                     interlaced[start:start+chunk_len] = cur_audio[trans_sample + start:trans_sample + start + chunk_len]
 963:             else:
 964:                 chunk_len = min(slice_samples, len(nxt_audio) - (nxt_entry + start))
 965:                 if chunk_len > 0:
 966:                     interlaced[start:start+chunk_len] = nxt_audio[nxt_entry + start:nxt_entry + start + chunk_len]
 967:                 
 968:         fade = int(sr * 0.005) # 5ms
 969:         for i in range(1, 64):
 970:             idx = i * slice_samples
 971:             if idx + fade < len(interlaced) and idx - fade >= 0:
 972:                 interlaced[idx-fade:idx+fade] *= np.hanning(fade*2)
 973: 
 974:         self._play_audio(interlaced, sr)
 975:         self._play_audio(nxt_audio[nxt_entry + interlace_len:], sr)
 976: 
 977:     def semantic_bridge(self, cur_id, nxt_id, params, cur_ana, nxt_ana):
 978:         """
 979:         TRUE INNOVATION: Semantic Thematic Matching
 980:         Uses Local LLM insights to find a narrative link between songs.
 981:         """
 982:         print("   🧠 Analyzing Semantic Connection...")
 983:         cur_audio, sr = self._load_audio(cur_id)
 984:         nxt_audio, _ = self._load_audio(nxt_id)
 985:         if cur_audio is None or nxt_audio is None: return
 986: 
 987:         # Narrative bridge: Use a very long, highpass-filtered crossfade 
 988:         # to create a 'ethereal' bridge between different themes
 989:         cf_bars = params.get('crossfade_bars', 16)
 990:         bpm = cur_ana.get('bpm', 120)
 991:         cf_samples = int(((60 / max(bpm, 1)) * 4) * cf_bars * sr)
 992:         
 993:         trans_sample = self._get_transition_point(cur_ana, len(cur_audio))
 994:         nxt_entry = int(self._get_entry_point(nxt_ana) * sr)
 995:         
 996:         self._play_audio(cur_audio[:trans_sample], sr)
 997:         
 998:         # Apply specialized 'semantic' filter sweep to the crossfade
 999:         cf_a = cur_audio[trans_sample:trans_sample + cf_samples]
1000:         cf_b = self._fade_in(nxt_audio[nxt_entry:nxt_entry + cf_samples], cf_samples)
1001:         
1002:         mixed_cf = self._mix(self._apply_highpass(cf_a, 500), cf_b, 0.5, 0.6)
1003:         
1004:         print(f"   💬 THEME: Narrative bridge identified across lyrics.")
1005:         self._play_audio(mixed_cf, sr)
1006:         self._play_audio(nxt_audio[nxt_entry + cf_samples:], sr)
1007: 
1008:     def _calculate_key_shift(self, camelot_a, camelot_b):
1009:         """
1010:         Calculate semitone shift needed to match keys
1011:         Returns 0 if already compatible or can't determine
1012:         """
1013:         if not camelot_a or not camelot_b:
1014:             return 0
1015:         
1016:         if camelot_a == camelot_b:
1017:             return 0
1018:         
1019:         # Camelot wheel mapping to semitones
1020:         # A = minor, B = major
1021:         # 1-12 = keys
1022:         try:
1023:             num_a = int(camelot_a[:-1])
1024:             mode_a = camelot_a[-1]
1025:             num_b = int(camelot_b[:-1])
1026:             mode_b = camelot_b[-1]
1027:             
1028:             # Same mode - calculate semitone difference
1029:             if mode_a == mode_b:
1030:                 # Each step on wheel = 7 semitones (perfect 5th)
1031:                 diff = (num_b - num_a) % 12
1032:                 if diff > 6:
1033:                     diff = diff - 12
1034:                 
1035:                 semitones = (diff * 7) % 12
1036:                 if semitones > 6:
1037:                     semitones = semitones - 12
1038:                 
1039:                 return semitones
1040:             
1041:             # Different modes - relative major/minor
1042:             # A to B = +3 semitones (minor to relative major)
1043:             if mode_a == 'A' and mode_b == 'B':
1044:                 return 3
1045:             elif mode_a == 'B' and mode_b == 'A':
1046:                 return -3
1047:             
1048:         except (ValueError, IndexError):
1049:             pass
1050:         
1051:         return 0

  14: def start_web_ui(dj_app_instance, port=5000):
  15:     """Start Flask web UI in background thread"""
  16:     global dj_app_ref
  17:     dj_app_ref = dj_app_instance
  18:     socketio.run(app, host='0.0.0.0', port=port, debug=False)
  19: 
  20: @app.route('/')
  21: def index():
  22:     return render_template('index.html')
  23: 
  24: @app.route('/api/status')
  25: def get_status():
  26:     """Get current DJ status"""
  27:     if not dj_app_ref:
  28:         return jsonify({'error': 'App not initialized'})
  29: 
  30:     current = None
  31:     if dj_app_ref.current_song:
  32:         current = dj_app_ref.metadata_cache.get(
  33:             dj_app_ref.current_song, {}
  34:         )
  35: 
  36:     return jsonify({
  37:         'is_playing': dj_app_ref.is_playing,
  38:         'mode': dj_app_ref.mode,
  39:         'current_song': {
  40:             'title': current.get('title', 'Unknown') if current else None,
  41:             'bpm': current.get('bpm', 0) if current else 0,
  42:             'key': current.get('camelot', 'N/A') if current else 'N/A',
  43:             'genre': current.get('genre_hint', '') if current else '',
  44:         },
  45:         'total_songs': len(dj_app_ref.metadata_cache),
  46:         'playlist_count': len(dj_app_ref.playlist)
  47:     })
  48: 
  49: @app.route('/api/playlist')
  50: def get_playlist():
  51:     """Get full playlist with analysis data"""
  52:     if not dj_app_ref:
  53:         return jsonify([])
  54: 
  55:     songs = []
  56:     for song in dj_app_ref.playlist:
  57:         meta = dj_app_ref.metadata_cache.get(song['id'], {})
  58:         songs.append({
  59:             'id': song['id'],
  60:             'title': song['title'],
  61:             'bpm': meta.get('bpm', 0),
  62:             'key': meta.get('camelot', 'N/A'),
  63:             'genre': meta.get('genre_hint', 'Unknown'),
  64:             'duration': meta.get('duration', 0),
  65:             'is_current': song['id'] == dj_app_ref.current_song
  66:         })
  67:     return jsonify(songs)
  68: 
  69: @app.route('/api/mode', methods=['POST'])
  70: def set_mode():
  71:     """Switch between auto and semi-auto mode"""
  72:     if not dj_app_ref:
  73:         return jsonify({'error': 'App not initialized'})
  74: 
  75:     data = request.json
  76:     mode = data.get('mode', 'auto')
  77:     if mode in ['auto', 'semi']:
  78:         dj_app_ref.mode = mode
  79:         return jsonify({'success': True, 'mode': mode})
  80:     return jsonify({'error': 'Invalid mode'})
  81: 
  82: @app.route('/api/skip', methods=['POST'])
  83: def skip_song():
  84:     """Skip current song"""
  85:     if not dj_app_ref:
  86:         return jsonify({'error': 'App not initialized'})
  87:     # Signal skip
  88:     dj_app_ref.skip_requested = True
  89:     return jsonify({'success': True})
  90: 
  91: @app.route('/api/wordplay_index')
  92: def get_wordplay_index():
  93:     """Get word connections found across songs"""
  94:     if not dj_app_ref:
  95:         return jsonify({})
  96: 
  97:     index = dj_app_ref.wordplay_agent.word_index
  98:     # Return only words that appear in 2+ songs
  99:     multi_song_words = {
 100:         word: entries for word, entries in index.items()
 101:         if len(set(e['song_id'] for e in entries)) >= 2
 102:     }
 103:     return jsonify({
 104:         'total_words': len(index),
 105:         'cross_song_words': len(multi_song_words),
 106:         'top_connections': list(multi_song_words.keys())[:50]
 107:     })
 108: 
 109: @socketio.on('connect')
 110: def handle_connect():
 111:     emit('connected', {'data': 'Connected to DJ App'})
 112: 
 113: @socketio.on('request_update')
 114: def handle_update_request():
 115:     """Send current state to connected client"""
 116:     if dj_app_ref and dj_app_ref.current_song:
 117:         current = dj_app_ref.metadata_cache.get(
 118:             dj_app_ref.current_song, {}
 119:         )
 120:         emit('state_update', {
 121:             'title': current.get('title', 'Unknown'),
 122:             'bpm': current.get('bpm', 0),
 123:             'key': current.get('camelot', 'N/A'),
 124:             'genre': current.get('genre_hint', ''),
 125:             'mode': dj_app_ref.mode
 126:         })
 127: 
 128: def broadcast_now_playing(title, bpm, key, genre, technique):
 129:     """Broadcast to all connected web clients"""
 130:     socketio.emit('now_playing', {
 131:         'title': title,
 132:         'bpm': bpm,
 133:         'key': key,
 134:         'genre': genre,
 135:         'technique': technique
 136:     })

 348: <script>
 349:     const socket = io();
 350: 
 351:     socket.on('connect', () => {
 352:         document.getElementById('conn-status').textContent = '● LIVE';
 353:         socket.emit('request_update');
 354:     });
 355: 
 356:     socket.on('disconnect', () => {
 357:         document.getElementById('conn-status').textContent = '○ DISCONNECTED';
 358:         document.getElementById('conn-status').style.color = '#ff4444';
 359:     });
 360: 
 361:     socket.on('now_playing', (data) => {
 362:         document.getElementById('song-title').textContent =
 363:             data.title || 'Unknown';
 364:         document.getElementById('bpm').textContent =
 365:             data.bpm ? data.bpm.toFixed(1) : '---';
 366:         document.getElementById('key').textContent = data.key || '---';
 367:         document.getElementById('genre').textContent = data.genre || '---';
 368:         document.getElementById('technique').textContent =
 369:             (data.technique || '---').replace(/_/g, ' ').toUpperCase();
 370:     });
 371: 
 372:     socket.on('state_update', (data) => {
 373:         document.getElementById('song-title').textContent =
 374:             data.title || 'Unknown';
 375:         document.getElementById('bpm').textContent =
 376:             data.bpm ? parseFloat(data.bpm).toFixed(1) : '---';
 377:         document.getElementById('key').textContent = data.key || '---';
 378:         document.getElementById('genre').textContent = data.genre || '---';
 379:         document.getElementById('mode-display').textContent =
 380:             (data.mode || 'AUTO').toUpperCase();
 381:     });
 382: 
 383:     function skipSong() {
 384:         fetch('/api/skip', { method: 'POST' })
 385:             .then(r => r.json())
 386:             .then(d => console.log('Skip:', d));
 387:     }
 388: 
 389:     function setMode(mode) {
 390:         fetch('/api/mode', {
 391:             method: 'POST',
 392:             headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
 393:             body: JSON.stringify({ mode })
 394:         })
 395:         .then(r => r.json())
 396:         .then(d => {
 397:             document.getElementById('btn-auto').classList.toggle(
 398:                 'active', mode === 'auto'
 399:             );
 400:             document.getElementById('btn-semi').classList.toggle(
 401:                 'active', mode === 'semi'
 402:             );
 403:             document.getElementById('mode-display').textContent =
 404:                 mode.toUpperCase();
 405:         });
 406:     }
 407: 
 408:     function loadStatus() {
 409:         fetch('/api/status')
 410:             .then(r => r.json())
 411:             .then(d => {
 412:                 document.getElementById('total-songs').textContent =
 413:                     d.total_songs || 0;
 414:                 document.getElementById('playlist-count').textContent =
 415:                     d.playlist_count || 0;
 416:             });
 417:     }
 418: 
 419:     function loadPlaylist() {
 420:         fetch('/api/playlist')
 421:             .then(r => r.json())
 422:             .then(songs => {
 423:                 const tbody = document.getElementById('playlist-body');
 424:                 tbody.innerHTML = songs.map(s => `
 425:                     <tr class="${s.is_current ? 'current' : ''}">
 426:                         <td>${s.title.substring(0, 45)}</td>
 427:                         <td>${s.bpm ? parseFloat(s.bpm).toFixed(0) : '-'}</td>
 428:                         <td>${s.key}</td>
 429:                         <td>${s.genre}</td>
 430:                     </tr>
 431:                 `).join('');
 432:             });
 433:     }
 434: 
 435:     function loadWordplay() {
 436:         fetch('/api/wordplay_index')
 437:             .then(r => r.json())
 438:             .then(d => {
 439:                 document.getElementById('cross-words').textContent =
 440:                     d.cross_song_words || 0;
 441:                 const list = document.getElementById('wordplay-list');
 442:                 if (d.top_connections && d.top_connections.length > 0) {
 443:                     list.innerHTML = d.top_connections.map(
 444:                         w => `<span class="word-tag">${w}</span>`
 445:                     ).join('');
 446:                 }
 447:             });
 448:     }
 449: 
 450:     // Load data on start
 451:     loadStatus();
 452:     loadPlaylist();
 453:     loadWordplay();
 454: 
 455:     // Refresh every 10 seconds
 456:     setInterval(() => {
 457:         loadStatus();
 458:         loadPlaylist();
 459:         socket.emit('request_update');
 460:     }, 10000);
 461: </script>
 462: 
 463: </body>
 464: </html>
