FILE: utils\drive_manager.py
================================================================================
   1: """
   2: Google Drive Manager - 5 Account Round Robin with Smart Indexing
   3: Stores MP3s, stems, transitions on Drive to save local space.
   4: Tracks which account has what data!
   5: """
   6: 
   7: import os
   8: import io
   9: import json
  10: import threading
  11: from google.auth.transport.requests import Request
  12: from google.oauth2.credentials import Credentials
  13: from google_auth_oauthlib.flow import InstalledAppFlow
  14: from googleapiclient.discovery import build
  15: from googleapiclient.http import MediaFileUpload, MediaIoBaseDownload
  16: 
  17: class DriveManager:
  18:     SCOPES = ['https://www.googleapis.com/auth/drive.file']
  19: 
  20:     def __init__(self, config):
  21:         self.config = config
  22:         self.credentials_path = 'data/credentials.json'
  23:         self.tokens_dir = 'data/tokens'
  24:         self.index_path = 'data/drive_index.json'
  25:         os.makedirs(self.tokens_dir, exist_ok=True)
  26:         
  27:         # Thread-safe service cache
  28:         self._local = threading.local()
  29:         
  30:         # Load account index (tracks which account has what)
  31:         self.index = self._load_index()
  32:         
  33:         # Get accounts from config
  34:         self.accounts = config.get('storage', {}).get('drive_accounts', ['account_1'])
  35:         
  36:         # Storage limit per account (15GB free, use 14GB to be safe)
  37:         self.max_bytes_per_account = 14 * 1024 * 1024 * 1024  # 14GB
  38: 
  39:     def _load_index(self):
  40:         """Load index tracking which account has what files"""
  41:         if os.path.exists(self.index_path):
  42:             try:
  43:                 with open(self.index_path, 'r') as f:
  44:                     return json.load(f)
  45:             except:
  46:                 pass
  47:         return {
  48:             'files': {},           # file_id -> {account, path, size}
  49:             'account_usage': {},   # account_id -> bytes_used
  50:             'current_account_idx': 0
  51:         }
  52:     
  53:     def _save_index(self):
  54:         """Save index to disk"""
  55:         os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(self.index_path), exist_ok=True)
  56:         with open(self.index_path, 'w') as f:
  57:             json.dump(self.index, f, indent=2)
  58:     
  59:     def _get_best_account(self, file_size_bytes: int) -> str:
  60:         """Get the best account to store a file (round robin with space check)"""
  61:         # Start from current index
  62:         start_idx = self.index.get('current_account_idx', 0)
  63:         
  64:         for i in range(len(self.accounts)):
  65:             idx = (start_idx + i) % len(self.accounts)
  66:             account_id = self.accounts[idx]
  67:             
  68:             # Check usage
  69:             usage = self.index.get('account_usage', {}).get(account_id, 0)
  70:             
  71:             if usage + file_size_bytes < self.max_bytes_per_account:
  72:                 # This account has space!
  73:                 self.index['current_account_idx'] = (idx + 1) % len(self.accounts)
  74:                 self._save_index()
  75:                 return account_id
  76:         
  77:         # All accounts full! Use the one with most space
  78:         min_usage = float('inf')
  79:         best_account = self.accounts[0]
  80:         for account_id in self.accounts:
  81:             usage = self.index.get('account_usage', {}).get(account_id, 0)
  82:             if usage < min_usage:
  83:                 min_usage = usage
  84:                 best_account = account_id
  85:         
  86:         print(f"⚠️ All accounts nearly full! Using {best_account}")
  87:         return best_account
  88: 
  89:     def authenticate(self, account_id):
  90:         """Authenticate and return a thread-safe service instance"""
  91:         if not hasattr(self._local, 'services'):
  92:             self._local.services = {}
  93:             
  94:         if account_id in self._local.services:
  95:             return self._local.services[account_id]
  96: 
  97:         token_path = os.path.join(self.tokens_dir, f'token_{account_id}.json')
  98:         creds = None
  99:         
 100:         if os.path.exists(token_path):
 101:             try:
 102:                 creds = Credentials.from_authorized_user_file(token_path, self.SCOPES)
 103:             except Exception as e:
 104:                 print(f"⚠️ Token corrupt for {account_id}: {e}")
 105:             
 106:         if not creds or not creds.valid:
 107:             if creds and creds.expired and creds.refresh_token:
 108:                 try:
 109:                     creds.refresh(Request())
 110:                 except Exception as e:
 111:                     print(f"⚠️ Token refresh failed: {e}")
 112:                     creds = None
 113:                     
 114:             if not creds:
 115:                 if not os.path.exists(self.credentials_path):
 116:                     raise FileNotFoundError(f"Missing {self.credentials_path}")
 117:                 
 118:                 print(f"🛑 WAITING FOR BROWSER AUTH: {account_id}")
 119:                 flow = InstalledAppFlow.from_client_secrets_file(self.credentials_path, self.SCOPES)
 120:                 creds = flow.run_local_server(port=0)
 121:             
 122:             with open(token_path, 'w') as token:
 123:                 token.write(creds.to_json())
 124:         
 125:         service = build('drive', 'v3', credentials=creds)
 126:         self._local.services[account_id] = service
 127:         return service
 128: 
 129:     def get_folder_id(self, service, folder_name):
 130:         """Find or create a folder on Drive"""
 131:         query = f"name = '{folder_name}' and mimeType = 'application/vnd.google-apps.folder' and trashed = false"
 132:         try:
 133:             results = service.files().list(q=query, fields="files(id)").execute()
 134:             files = results.get('files', [])
 135:             
 136:             if files:
 137:                 return files[0]['id']
 138:             else:
 139:                 file_metadata = {
 140:                     'name': folder_name,
 141:                     'mimeType': 'application/vnd.google-apps.folder'
 142:                 }
 143:                 folder = service.files().create(body=file_metadata, fields='id').execute()
 144:                 return folder.get('id')
 145:         except Exception as e:
 146:             print(f"❌ Drive folder error: {e}")
 147:             raise
 148: 
 149:     def upload_file(self, account_id, local_path, drive_folder_name):
 150:         """Upload a local file to a specific Drive account"""
 151:         service = self.authenticate(account_id)
 152:         folder_id = self.get_folder_id(service, drive_folder_name)
 153:         
 154:         filename = os.path.basename(local_path)
 155:         file_size = os.path.getsize(local_path)
 156:         
 157:         file_metadata = {
 158:             'name': filename,
 159:             'parents': [folder_id]
 160:         }
 161:         
 162:         media = MediaFileUpload(local_path, resumable=True)
 163:         
 164:         try:
 165:             # Check if file already exists
 166:             query = f"name = '{filename}' and '{folder_id}' in parents and trashed = false"
 167:             results = service.files().list(q=query, fields="files(id)").execute()
 168:             existing_files = results.get('files', [])
 169:             
 170:             if existing_files:
 171:                 file = service.files().update(fileId=existing_files[0]['id'], media_body=media).execute()
 172:                 file_id = existing_files[0]['id']
 173:             else:
 174:                 file = service.files().create(body=file_metadata, media_body=media, fields='id').execute()
 175:                 file_id = file.get('id')
 176:             
 177:             # Update index
 178:             self.index['files'][file_id] = {
 179:                 'account': account_id,
 180:                 'folder': drive_folder_name,
 181:                 'filename': filename,
 182:                 'size': file_size
 183:             }
 184:             
 185:             # Update account usage
 186:             if account_id not in self.index['account_usage']:
 187:                 self.index['account_usage'][account_id] = 0
 188:             self.index['account_usage'][account_id] += file_size
 189:             
 190:             self._save_index()
 191:             return file_id
 192:             
 193:         except Exception as e:
 194:             print(f"❌ Drive upload error: {e}")
 195:             return None
 196: 
 197:     def upload_auto(self, local_path, drive_folder_name):
 198:         """
 199:         AUTO-UPLOAD: Picks the best account automatically!
 200:         Uses round-robin with space checking.
 201:         """
 202:         file_size = os.path.getsize(local_path)
 203:         account_id = self._get_best_account(file_size)
 204:         
 205:         print(f"☁️ Auto-uploading to {account_id}...")
 206:         return self.upload_file(account_id, local_path, drive_folder_name)
 207: 
 208:     def upload_transition(self, local_path):
 209:         """Upload a transition mix for mobile testing and AI learning"""
 210:         if not os.path.exists(local_path):
 211:             print("❌ Mix file not found for upload!")
 212:             return None
 213:             
 214:         try:
 215:             file_size = os.path.getsize(local_path)
 216:             account_id = self._get_best_account(file_size)
 217:             
 218:             service = self.authenticate(account_id)
 219:             folder_id = self.get_folder_id(service, 'DJ_Agent_Transitions')
 220:             
 221:             filename = os.path.basename(local_path)
 222:             file_metadata = {
 223:                 'name': filename,
 224:                 'parents': [folder_id]
 225:             }
 226:             
 227:             media = MediaFileUpload(local_path, mimetype='audio/wav', resumable=True)
 228:             file = service.files().create(
 229:                 body=file_metadata, 
 230:                 media_body=media, 
 231:                 fields='id, webViewLink'
 232:             ).execute()
 233:             
 234:             file_id = file.get('id')
 235:             
 236:             # Make public for mobile access
 237:             permission = {'type': 'anyone', 'role': 'reader'}
 238:             service.permissions().create(fileId=file_id, body=permission).execute()
 239:             
 240:             # Update index
 241:             self.index['files'][file_id] = {
 242:                 'account': account_id,
 243:                 'folder': 'DJ_Agent_Transitions',
 244:                 'filename': filename,
 245:                 'size': file_size
 246:             }
 247:             if account_id not in self.index['account_usage']:
 248:                 self.index['account_usage'][account_id] = 0
 249:             self.index['account_usage'][account_id] += file_size
 250:             self._save_index()
 251:             
 252:             return file.get('webViewLink')
 253:             
 254:         except Exception as e:
 255:             print(f"❌ Failed to upload transition: {e}")
 256:             return None
 257: 
 258:     def download_file(self, account_id, drive_file_id, local_path):
 259:         """Download a file from Drive"""
 260:         try:
 261:             service = self.authenticate(account_id)
 262:             request = service.files().get_media(fileId=drive_file_id)
 263:             fh = io.BytesIO()
 264:             downloader = MediaIoBaseDownload(fh, request)
 265:             done = False
 266:             while not done:
 267:                 status, done = downloader.next_chunk()
 268:             
 269:             with open(local_path, 'wb') as f:
 270:                 f.write(fh.getvalue())
 271:             return local_path
 272:         except Exception as e:
 273:             print(f"❌ Drive download error: {e}")
 274:             return None
 275: 
 276:     def find_file(self, filename):
 277:         """Find which account has a specific file"""
 278:         for file_id, info in self.index.get('files', {}).items():
 279:             if info.get('filename') == filename:
 280:                 return {
 281:                     'file_id': file_id,
 282:                     'account': info['account'],
 283:                     'folder': info['folder']
 284:                 }
 285:         return None
 286: 
 287:     def get_storage_report(self):
 288:         """Get storage usage report for all accounts"""
 289:         report = []
 290:         for account_id in self.accounts:
 291:             usage = self.index.get('account_usage', {}).get(account_id, 0)
 292:             usage_gb = usage / (1024 * 1024 * 1024)
 293:             percent = (usage / self.max_bytes_per_account) * 100
 294:             report.append({
 295:                 'account': account_id,
 296:                 'used_gb': round(usage_gb, 2),
 297:                 'percent': round(percent, 1)
 298:             })
 299:         return report

FILE: utils\json_utils.py
================================================================================
   1: import numpy as np
   2: 
   3: def make_serializable(obj):
   4:     """
   5:     Recursively convert any non-serializable objects (like numpy types) 
   6:     into standard Python types for JSON serialization.
   7:     """
   8:     if isinstance(obj, dict):
   9:         return {k: make_serializable(v) for k, v in obj.items()}
  10:     elif isinstance(obj, (list, tuple)):
  11:         return [make_serializable(v) for v in obj]
  12:     elif isinstance(obj, np.integer):
  13:         return int(obj)
  14:     elif isinstance(obj, np.floating):
  15:         return float(obj)
  16:     elif isinstance(obj, np.ndarray):
  17:         return obj.tolist()
  18:     elif hasattr(obj, '__dict__'):
  19:         return make_serializable(obj.__dict__)
  20:     return obj

  12:                           "Tags": "musical_note,headphones"

  15:     except Exception as e:

================================================================================
FILE: visual_engine\equalizer_viz.py
================================================================================
   1: import numpy as np
   2: from PIL import Image, ImageDraw
   3: import librosa
   4: import math
   5: 
   6: class EqualizerViz:
   7:     """
   8:     Real-time frequency equalizer visualizer
   9:     Analyzes actual audio being played
  10:     """
  11:     def __init__(self, config):
  12:         self.config = config
  13:         self.width = config['visual']['width']
  14:         self.height = config['visual']['height']
  15:         self.sr = config['audio']['sample_rate']
  16:         self.bar_count = 128
  17:         self.smoothed_bars = np.zeros(self.bar_count)
  18:         self.decay = 0.85
  19: 
  20:     def generate_frame(self, audio_chunk, genre_hint='Pop/Other'):
  21:         """
  22:         Generate equalizer frame from audio chunk
  23:         Returns PIL Image
  24:         """
  25:         img = Image.new('RGB', (self.width, self.height), (5, 5, 15))
  26:         draw = ImageDraw.Draw(img)
  27: 
  28:         # Get frequency data from audio chunk
  29:         if audio_chunk is not None and len(audio_chunk) > 0:
  30:             bars = self._compute_fft_bars(audio_chunk)
  31:         else:
  32:             bars = np.zeros(self.bar_count)
  33: 
  34:         # Smooth bars with decay
  35:         self.smoothed_bars = (
  36:             np.maximum(bars, self.smoothed_bars * self.decay)
  37:         )
  38: 
  39:         # Get color scheme from genre
  40:         color_scheme = self._genre_colors(genre_hint)
  41: 
  42:         self._draw_bars(draw, self.smoothed_bars, color_scheme)
  43:         self._draw_peak_dots(draw, bars, self.smoothed_bars)
  44:         self._draw_reflection(draw, self.smoothed_bars, color_scheme)
  45: 
  46:         return img
  47: 
  48:     def _compute_fft_bars(self, audio_chunk):
  49:         """Compute FFT and map to bar heights"""
  50:         # FFT
  51:         fft = np.abs(np.fft.rfft(audio_chunk, n=2048))
  52:         fft = fft[:len(fft)//2]
  53: 
  54:         # Map FFT bins to bar_count bars (logarithmic)
  55:         bars = np.zeros(self.bar_count)
  56:         fft_len = len(fft)
  57: 
  58:         for i in range(self.bar_count):
  59:             # Log scale: more bars for low frequencies
  60:             start = int((i / self.bar_count) ** 2 * fft_len)
  61:             end = int(((i + 1) / self.bar_count) ** 2 * fft_len)
  62:             end = max(end, start + 1)
  63:             end = min(end, fft_len)
  64: 
  65:             if start < fft_len:
  66:                 bars[i] = np.mean(fft[start:end])
  67: 
  68:         # Normalize
  69:         max_val = np.max(bars)
  70:         if max_val > 0:
  71:             bars = bars / max_val
  72: 
  73:         return bars
  74: 
  75:     def _genre_colors(self, genre_hint):
  76:         """Get color gradient based on genre"""
  77:         schemes = {
  78:             'EDM/Techno':   [(0, 200, 255), (150, 0, 255)],
  79:             'House/Dance':  [(255, 100, 0), (255, 0, 150)],
  80:             'Hip-Hop/Rap':  [(255, 200, 0), (255, 80, 0)],
  81:             'R&B/Soul':     [(200, 0, 100), (100, 0, 200)],
  82:             'Rock/Metal':   [(255, 50, 0), (200, 0, 0)],
  83:             'Ambient/Chill':[(0, 150, 200), (0, 50, 150)],
  84:             'Pop/Other':    [(100, 0, 255), (255, 0, 150)],
  85:         }
  86:         return schemes.get(genre_hint, schemes['Pop/Other'])
  87: 
  88:     def _draw_bars(self, draw, bars, colors):
  89:         """Draw main equalizer bars"""
  90:         bar_width = self.width // self.bar_count
  91:         max_height = int(self.height * 0.7)
  92:         base_y = int(self.height * 0.85)
  93: 
  94:         for i, bar_val in enumerate(bars):
  95:             bar_height = int(bar_val * max_height)
  96:             if bar_height < 2:
  97:                 bar_height = 2
  98: 
  99:             x = i * bar_width
 100: 
 101:             # Interpolate color based on position
 102:             progress = i / self.bar_count
 103:             r = int(colors[0][0] + (colors[1][0] - colors[0][0]) * progress)
 104:             g = int(colors[0][1] + (colors[1][1] - colors[0][1]) * progress)
 105:             b = int(colors[0][2] + (colors[1][2] - colors[0][2]) * progress)
 106: 
 107:             # Brighter at top
 108:             brightness = 0.5 + (bar_val * 0.5)
 109:             color = (
 110:                 min(255, int(r * brightness)),
 111:                 min(255, int(g * brightness)),
 112:                 min(255, int(b * brightness))
 113:             )
 114: 
 115:             draw.rectangle(
 116:                 [x + 1, base_y - bar_height,
 117:                  x + bar_width - 1, base_y],
 118:                 fill=color
 119:             )
 120: 
 121:     def _draw_peak_dots(self, draw, current_bars, smoothed_bars):
 122:         """Draw peak indicator dots above bars"""
 123:         bar_width = self.width // self.bar_count
 124:         max_height = int(self.height * 0.7)
 125:         base_y = int(self.height * 0.85)
 126: 
 127:         for i, bar_val in enumerate(smoothed_bars):
 128:             peak_y = base_y - int(bar_val * max_height) - 5
 129:             x = i * bar_width + bar_width // 2
 130:             draw.ellipse(
 131:                 [x - 2, peak_y - 2, x + 2, peak_y + 2],
 132:                 fill=(255, 255, 255)
 133:             )
 134: 
 135:     def _draw_reflection(self, draw, bars, colors):
 136:         """Draw mirrored reflection below bars"""
 137:         bar_width = self.width // self.bar_count
 138:         max_height = int(self.height * 0.15)
 139:         base_y = int(self.height * 0.85)
 140: 
 141:         for i, bar_val in enumerate(bars):
 142:             bar_height = int(bar_val * max_height)
 143: 
 144:             x = i * bar_width
 145:             progress = i / self.bar_count
 146:             r = int(colors[0][0] + (colors[1][0] - colors[0][0]) * progress)
 147:             g = int(colors[0][1] + (colors[1][1] - colors[0][1]) * progress)
 148:             b = int(colors[0][2] + (colors[1][2] - colors[0][2]) * progress)
 149: 
 150:             # Dimmer reflection
 151:             color = (r // 4, g // 4, b // 4)
 152: 
 153:             draw.rectangle(
 154:                 [x + 1, base_y,
 155:                  x + bar_width - 1, base_y + bar_height],
 156:                 fill=color
 157:             )

FILE: visual_engine\lyric_display.py
================================================================================
   1: from PIL import Image, ImageDraw, ImageFont
   2: import os
   3: import math
   4: 
   5: class LyricDisplay:
   6:     """
   7:     Karaoke-style lyric display
   8:     Highlights current word as it's sung
   9:     """
  10:     def __init__(self, config):
  11:         self.config = config
  12:         self.width = config['visual']['width']
  13:         self.height = config['visual']['height']
  14:         self.current_line = ""
  15:         self.next_line = ""
  16:         self.current_word_idx = 0
  17: 
  18:         # Try to load a font
  19:         self.font_large = self._load_font(52)
  20:         self.font_small = self._load_font(36)
  21: 
  22:     def _load_font(self, size):
  23:         """Load font with fallback"""
  24:         font_paths = [
  25:             "C:/Windows/Fonts/Arial.ttf",
  26:             "C:/Windows/Fonts/arialbd.ttf",
  27:             "/usr/share/fonts/truetype/dejavu/DejaVuSans.ttf",
  28:         ]
  29:         for path in font_paths:
  30:             if os.path.exists(path):
  31:                 try:
  32:                     return ImageFont.truetype(path, size)
  33:                 except Exception:
  34:                     pass
  35:         return ImageFont.load_default()
  36: 
  37:     def update(self, timed_words, current_time):
  38:         """
  39:         Update display state based on current playback time
  40:         Returns (current_word, line_of_words)
  41:         """
  42:         if not timed_words:
  43:             return None, []
  44: 
  45:         current_word = None
  46:         visible_words = []
  47: 
  48:         for i, word_entry in enumerate(timed_words):
  49:             start = word_entry.get('start', 0)
  50:             end = word_entry.get('end', start + 0.3)
  51: 
  52:             # Show words in a 5 second window
  53:             if current_time - 2 <= start <= current_time + 3:
  54:                 visible_words.append({
  55:                     'word': word_entry['word'],
  56:                     'start': start,
  57:                     'end': end,
  58:                     'active': start <= current_time <= end
  59:                 })
  60: 
  61:             if start <= current_time <= end:
  62:                 current_word = word_entry['word']
  63: 
  64:         return current_word, visible_words
  65: 
  66:     def draw_lyrics(self, draw, timed_words, current_time):
  67:         """
  68:         Draw karaoke-style lyrics on frame
  69:         Active word is highlighted/larger
  70:         """
  71:         if not timed_words:
  72:             return
  73: 
  74:         current_word, visible_words = self.update(timed_words, current_time)
  75: 
  76:         if not visible_words:
  77:             return
  78: 
  79:         # Build display line
  80:         lyric_y = int(self.height * 0.82)
  81:         total_width = 0
  82:         word_positions = []
  83: 
  84:         # Measure total width
  85:         for entry in visible_words:
  86:             font = self.font_large if entry['active'] else self.font_small
  87:             try:
  88:                 bbox = draw.textbbox((0, 0), entry['word'] + " ", font=font)
  89:                 w = bbox[2] - bbox[0]
  90:             except Exception:
  91:                 w = len(entry['word']) * 20
  92: 
  93:             word_positions.append((entry, w))
  94:             total_width += w
  95: 
  96:         # Center the line
  97:         start_x = (self.width - total_width) // 2
  98:         current_x = start_x
  99: 
 100:         for entry, w in word_positions:
 101:             word = entry['word']
 102:             is_active = entry['active']
 103: 
 104:             if is_active:
 105:                 color = (255, 255, 100)  # Yellow highlight
 106:                 font = self.font_large
 107:                 # Draw glow effect
 108:                 for offset in [(1,0),(-1,0),(0,1),(0,-1)]:
 109:                     draw.text(
 110:                         (current_x + offset[0], lyric_y + offset[1]),
 111:                         word + " ",
 112:                         font=font,
 113:                         fill=(200, 150, 0)
 114:                     )
 115:             else:
 116:                 color = (200, 200, 200)  # White
 117:                 font = self.font_small
 118: 
 119:             draw.text(
 120:                 (current_x, lyric_y),
 121:                 word + " ",
 122:                 font=font,
 123:                 fill=color
 124:             )
 125:             current_x += w

FILE: visual_engine\obs_bridge.py
================================================================================
   1: import json
   2: import time
   3: import threading
   4: try:
   5:     import obsws_python as obs
   6: except:
   7:     obs = None
   8: 
   9: class OBSBridge:
  10:     """
  11:     Controls OBS Studio for YouTube livestream
  12:     Updates overlays in real-time
  13:     """
  14:     def __init__(self, config):
  15:         self.config = config
  16:         self.ws = None
  17:         self.connected = False
  18:         self.port = config['visual']['obs_websocket_port']
  19:         self.password = config['visual']['obs_websocket_password']
  20: 
  21:     def connect(self):
  22:         """Connect to OBS WebSocket"""
  23:         try:
  24:             self.ws = obs.ReqClient(
  25:                 host='localhost',
  26:                 port=self.port,
  27:                 password=self.password,
  28:                 timeout=3
  29:             )
  30:             self.connected = True
  31:             print("✅ Connected to OBS")
  32:         except Exception as e:
  33:             print(f"⚠️  OBS not connected: {e}")
  34:             print("   App will run without OBS integration")
  35:             self.connected = False
  36: 
  37:     def update_display(self, current_analysis, next_analysis, technique):
  38:         """Update all OBS overlays"""
  39:         if not self.connected:
  40:             return
  41: 
  42:         try:
  43:             # Update song info text
  44:             self._update_text_source(
  45:                 'current_song',
  46:                 f"NOW: {current_analysis.get('title', 'Unknown')[:40]}"
  47:             )
  48: 
  49:             self._update_text_source(
  50:                 'next_song',
  51:                 f"NEXT: {next_analysis.get('title', 'Unknown')[:40]}"
  52:             )
  53: 
  54:             self._update_text_source(
  55:                 'bpm_display',
  56:                 f"BPM: {current_analysis.get('bpm', 0):.0f}"
  57:             )
  58: 
  59:             self._update_text_source(
  60:                 'key_display',
  61:                 f"KEY: {current_analysis.get('camelot', 'N/A')}"
  62:             )
  63: 
  64:             self._update_text_source(
  65:                 'technique_display',
  66:                 f"TECHNIQUE: {technique.replace('_', ' ').upper()}"
  67:             )
  68: 
  69:         except Exception as e:
  70:             print(f"⚠️  OBS update error: {e}")
  71: 
  72:     def _update_text_source(self, source_name, text):
  73:         """Update a text source in OBS"""
  74:         if not self.connected:
  75:             return
  76:         try:
  77:             self.ws.set_input_settings(
  78:                 name=source_name,
  79:                 settings={'text': text},
  80:                 overlay=True
  81:             )
  82:         except Exception:
  83:             pass
  84: 
  85:     def trigger_scene_change(self, scene_name):
  86:         """Switch OBS scene"""
  87:         if not self.connected:
  88:             return
  89:         try:
  90:             self.ws.set_current_program_scene(scene_name)
  91:         except Exception as e:
  92:             print(f"⚠️  Scene change failed: {e}")



================================================================================
FILE: visual_engine\stick_figure_gen.py
================================================================================
   1: import numpy as np
   2: from PIL import Image, ImageDraw, ImageFont
   3: import os
   4: import json
   5: import math
   6: 
   7: class StickFigureGen:
   8:     """
   9:     Generates stick figure animations based on
  10:     lyric sentiment and song story
  11:     Switches to equalizer for instrumentals
  12:     """
  13:     def __init__(self, config):
  14:         self.config = config
  15:         self.width = config['visual']['width']
  16:         self.height = config['visual']['height']
  17:         self.frame_count = 0
  18:         self.bg_color = (10, 10, 20)
  19:         self.figure_color = (255, 255, 255)
  20: 
  21:     def generate_frame(self, lyrics_data, beat_time,
  22:                        energy, sentiment, current_word=None):
  23:         """
  24:         Generate a single animation frame
  25:         Returns PIL Image
  26:         """
  27:         img = Image.new('RGB', (self.width, self.height), self.bg_color)
  28:         draw = ImageDraw.Draw(img)
  29: 
  30:         has_lyrics = (
  31:             lyrics_data is not None and
  32:             lyrics_data.get('text', '').strip() != ''
  33:         )
  34: 
  35:         if has_lyrics:
  36:             self._draw_stick_scene(
  37:                 draw, sentiment, energy, beat_time, current_word
  38:             )
  39:         else:
  40:             self._draw_equalizer(draw, energy, beat_time)
  41: 
  42:         # Always draw beat pulse overlay
  43:         self._draw_beat_pulse(draw, energy, beat_time)
  44: 
  45:         self.frame_count += 1
  46:         return img
  47: 
  48:     def _draw_stick_scene(self, draw, sentiment, energy,
  49:                            beat_time, current_word):
  50:         """Draw scene based on song sentiment"""
  51: 
  52:         if sentiment == 'happy':
  53:             self.bg_color = (20, 15, 5)
  54:             self.figure_color = (255, 220, 50)
  55:         elif sentiment == 'sad':
  56:             self.bg_color = (5, 10, 25)
  57:             self.figure_color = (150, 180, 255)
  58:         elif sentiment == 'angry':
  59:             self.bg_color = (25, 5, 5)
  60:             self.figure_color = (255, 80, 50)
  61:         elif sentiment == 'hype':
  62:             self.bg_color = (15, 5, 25)
  63:             self.figure_color = (200, 50, 255)
  64:         elif sentiment == 'love':
  65:             self.bg_color = (20, 5, 15)
  66:             self.figure_color = (255, 100, 180)
  67:         else:
  68:             self.bg_color = (10, 10, 20)
  69:             self.figure_color = (255, 255, 255)
  70: 
  71:         # Redraw background with new color
  72:         draw.rectangle(
  73:             [0, 0, self.width, self.height],
  74:             fill=self.bg_color
  75:         )
  76: 
  77:         # Draw ground line
  78:         ground_y = int(self.height * 0.75)
  79:         draw.line(
  80:             [(0, ground_y), (self.width, ground_y)],
  81:             fill=(80, 80, 80), width=2
  82:         )
  83: 
  84:         # Beat-synced bounce
  85:         bounce = int(
  86:             math.sin(beat_time * math.pi * 2) * 10 * energy * 5
  87:         )
  88: 
  89:         if sentiment == 'happy':
  90:             self._draw_dancing_figure(
  91:                 draw, self.width // 3,
  92:                 ground_y + bounce,
  93:                 self.figure_color, beat_time
  94:             )
  95:             self._draw_dancing_figure(
  96:                 draw, 2 * self.width // 3,
  97:                 ground_y + bounce,
  98:                 self.figure_color, beat_time + 0.5
  99:             )
 100: 
 101:         elif sentiment == 'sad':
 102:             self._draw_sad_figure(
 103:                 draw, self.width // 2,
 104:                 ground_y, self.figure_color
 105:             )
 106:             self._draw_rain(draw)
 107: 
 108:         elif sentiment == 'love':
 109:             self._draw_dancing_figure(
 110:                 draw, self.width // 2 - 80,
 111:                 ground_y, self.figure_color, beat_time
 112:             )
 113:             self._draw_dancing_figure(
 114:                 draw, self.width // 2 + 80,
 115:                 ground_y, (255, 150, 200), beat_time
 116:             )
 117:             self._draw_hearts(draw, beat_time)
 118: 
 119:         elif sentiment == 'hype':
 120:             for i, x in enumerate([
 121:                 self.width // 5,
 122:                 2 * self.width // 5,
 123:                 3 * self.width // 5,
 124:                 4 * self.width // 5
 125:             ]):
 126:                 jump = int(abs(math.sin(
 127:                     beat_time * math.pi * 2 + i * 0.5
 128:                 )) * 80 * energy * 3)
 129:                 self._draw_dancing_figure(
 130:                     draw, x, ground_y - jump,
 131:                     self.figure_color,
 132:                     beat_time + i * 0.25
 133:                 )
 134:         else:
 135:             self._draw_dancing_figure(
 136:                 draw, self.width // 2,
 137:                 ground_y + bounce,
 138:                 self.figure_color, beat_time
 139:             )
 140: 
 141:     def _draw_stick_figure(self, draw, cx, ground_y, color,
 142:                             arm_angle=0, leg_angle=0):
 143:         """Draw a basic stick figure at position cx, ground_y"""
 144:         scale = 60
 145: 
 146:         # Head
 147:         head_r = scale // 3
 148:         head_cx = cx
 149:         head_cy = ground_y - scale * 2 - head_r
 150:         draw.ellipse(
 151:             [head_cx - head_r, head_cy - head_r,
 152:              head_cx + head_r, head_cy + head_r],
 153:             outline=color, width=3
 154:         )
 155: 
 156:         # Body
 157:         body_top = head_cy + head_r
 158:         body_bot = ground_y - scale
 159:         draw.line(
 160:             [(cx, body_top), (cx, body_bot)],
 161:             fill=color, width=3
 162:         )
 163: 
 164:         # Arms
 165:         arm_y = body_top + scale // 2
 166:         arm_len = scale * 0.8
 167:         draw.line([
 168:             (int(cx - arm_len * math.cos(arm_angle)),
 169:              int(arm_y - arm_len * math.sin(arm_angle))),
 170:             (cx, arm_y),
 171:             (int(cx + arm_len * math.cos(arm_angle)),
 172:              int(arm_y + arm_len * math.sin(arm_angle)))
 173:         ], fill=color, width=3)
 174: 
 175:         # Legs
 176:         draw.line([
 177:             (cx, body_bot),
 178:             (int(cx - scale * 0.6 * math.sin(leg_angle)),
 179:              ground_y)
 180:         ], fill=color, width=3)
 181:         draw.line([
 182:             (cx, body_bot),
 183:             (int(cx + scale * 0.6 * math.sin(leg_angle)),
 184:              ground_y)
 185:         ], fill=color, width=3)
 186: 
 187:     def _draw_dancing_figure(self, draw, cx, ground_y,
 188:                               color, beat_time):
 189:         """Stick figure dancing with beat"""
 190:         arm_angle = (
 191:             0.5 + math.sin(beat_time * math.pi * 4) * 0.8
 192:         )
 193:         leg_angle = (
 194:             0.3 + abs(math.sin(beat_time * math.pi * 2)) * 0.6
 195:         )
 196:         self._draw_stick_figure(
 197:             draw, cx, ground_y, color, arm_angle, leg_angle
 198:         )
 199: 
 200:     def _draw_sad_figure(self, draw, cx, ground_y, color):
 201:         """Sad drooping stick figure"""
 202:         self._draw_stick_figure(
 203:             draw, cx, ground_y, color,
 204:             arm_angle=-0.3,
 205:             leg_angle=0.1
 206:         )
 207: 
 208:     def _draw_rain(self, draw):
 209:         """Draw rain drops"""
 210:         import random
 211:         random.seed(self.frame_count // 3)
 212:         for _ in range(50):
 213:             x = random.randint(0, self.width)
 214:             y = random.randint(0, self.height)
 215:             draw.line(
 216:                 [(x, y), (x - 2, y + 15)],
 217:                 fill=(100, 150, 255), width=1
 218:             )
 219: 
 220:     def _draw_hearts(self, draw, beat_time):
 221:         """Draw floating hearts between figures"""
 222:         pulse = abs(math.sin(beat_time * math.pi * 2))
 223:         size = int(20 + pulse * 15)
 224:         cx = self.width // 2
 225:         cy = int(self.height * 0.5)
 226: 
 227:         for dx in range(-size, size):
 228:             for dy in range(-size, size):
 229:                 if (dx*dx + dy*dy) < size*size // 2:
 230:                     draw.point(
 231:                         (cx + dx, cy + dy),
 232:                         fill=(255, 50, 100)
 233:                     )
 234: 
 235:     def _draw_equalizer(self, draw, energy, beat_time):
 236:         """Draw frequency equalizer bars for instrumentals"""
 237:         draw.rectangle(
 238:             [0, 0, self.width, self.height],
 239:             fill=self.bg_color
 240:         )
 241: 
 242:         bar_count = 64
 243:         bar_width = self.width // bar_count
 244:         center_y = self.height // 2
 245: 
 246:         for i in range(bar_count):
 247:             freq_factor = math.sin(
 248:                 i * 0.3 + beat_time * 5
 249:             ) * 0.5 + 0.5
 250:             height = int(energy * freq_factor * self.height * 0.8)
 251: 
 252:             r = int(50 + (i / bar_count) * 200)
 253:             g = int(20)
 254:             b = int(200 - (i / bar_count) * 100)
 255:             color = (r, g, b)
 256: 
 257:             x = i * bar_width
 258:             draw.rectangle(
 259:                 [x, center_y - height // 2,
 260:                  x + bar_width - 2, center_y + height // 2],
 261:                 fill=color
 262:             )
 263: 
 264:     def _draw_beat_pulse(self, draw, energy, beat_time):
 265:         """Subtle beat pulse overlay on edges"""
 266:         pulse = abs(math.sin(beat_time * math.pi * 2))
 267:         alpha = int(pulse * energy * 100)
 268:         if alpha > 10:
 269:             draw.rectangle(
 270:                 [0, 0, self.width, 5],
 271:                 fill=(alpha, alpha // 2, alpha * 2)
 272:             )
 273:             draw.rectangle(
 274:                 [0, self.height - 5, self.width, self.height],
 275:                 fill=(alpha, alpha // 2, alpha * 2)
 276:             )



================================================================================
FILE: visual_engine\waveform_display.py
================================================================================
   1: import numpy as np
   2: from PIL import Image, ImageDraw
   3: import librosa
   4: 
   5: class WaveformDisplay:
   6:     """
   7:     DJ-style dual waveform display
   8:     Shows current and incoming song waveforms
   9:     with playhead position
  10:     """
  11:     def __init__(self, config):
  12:         self.config = config
  13:         self.width = config['visual']['width']
  14:         self.height = config['visual']['height']
  15:         self.waveform_height = 80
  16:         self.waveform_a = None
  17:         self.waveform_b = None
  18: 
  19:     def load_waveform(self, filepath, song_id):
  20:         """Pre-compute waveform data for display"""
  21:         try:
  22:             y, sr = librosa.load(filepath, sr=8000, mono=True, duration=300)
  23:             # Downsample to width pixels
  24:             chunk_size = max(1, len(y) // self.width)
  25:             waveform = []
  26:             for i in range(0, len(y) - chunk_size, chunk_size):
  27:                 chunk = y[i:i + chunk_size]
  28:                 waveform.append(float(np.max(np.abs(chunk))))
  29:             return waveform[:self.width]
  30:         except Exception:
  31:             return [0.1] * self.width
  32: 
  33:     def draw_waveforms(self, draw, waveform_a, waveform_b,
  34:                        progress_a, bpm_a, bpm_b, technique):
  35:         """
  36:         Draw dual waveform display at bottom of screen
  37:         """
  38:         panel_y = self.height - 180
  39:         panel_height = 170
  40:         panel_color = (15, 15, 25)
  41: 
  42:         # Background panel
  43:         draw.rectangle(
  44:             [0, panel_y, self.width, self.height],
  45:             fill=panel_color
  46:         )
  47: 
  48:         # Divider line
  49:         draw.line(
  50:             [(0, panel_y), (self.width, panel_y)],
  51:             fill=(60, 60, 80), width=1
  52:         )
  53: 
  54:         # Waveform A (current song) - top half of panel
  55:         wf_a_y = panel_y + 10
  56:         self._draw_single_waveform(
  57:             draw,
  58:             waveform_a,
  59:             wf_a_y,
  60:             self.waveform_height,
  61:             progress_a,
  62:             color=(0, 200, 255),
  63:             played_color=(0, 80, 120),
  64:             label=f"NOW PLAYING | BPM: {bpm_a:.0f}"
  65:         )
  66: 
  67:         # Waveform B (next song) - bottom half
  68:         wf_b_y = panel_y + self.waveform_height + 25
  69:         self._draw_single_waveform(
  70:             draw,
  71:             waveform_b,
  72:             wf_b_y,
  73:             self.waveform_height,
  74:             0,  # Next song hasn't started
  75:             color=(255, 100, 50),
  76:             played_color=(100, 40, 20),
  77:             label=f"NEXT UP | BPM: {bpm_b:.0f}"
  78:         )
  79: 
  80:         # Technique indicator
  81:         draw.text(
  82:             (self.width // 2 - 150, panel_y + 65),
  83:             f"▶ {technique.replace('_', ' ').upper()}",
  84:             fill=(200, 200, 50)
  85:         )
  86: 
  87:     def _draw_single_waveform(self, draw, waveform, y_start,
  88:                                height, progress, color,
  89:                                played_color, label):
  90:         """Draw a single waveform"""
  91:         if not waveform:
  92:             waveform = [0.1] * self.width
  93: 
  94:         center_y = y_start + height // 2
  95:         playhead_x = int(progress * self.width)
  96: 
  97:         for x, amp in enumerate(waveform[:self.width]):
  98:             bar_height = int(amp * height * 0.9)
  99:             bar_height = max(2, bar_height)
 100: 
 101:             c = played_color if x < playhead_x else color
 102:             draw.rectangle(
 103:                 [x, center_y - bar_height // 2,
 104:                  x + 1, center_y + bar_height // 2],
 105:                 fill=c
 106:             )
 107: 
 108:         # Playhead line
 109:         draw.line(
 110:             [(playhead_x, y_start), (playhead_x, y_start + height)],
 111:             fill=(255, 255, 0), width=2
 112:         )
 113: 
 114:         # Label
 115:         draw.text((10, y_start), label, fill=(180, 180, 180))
